rus kyi rnam dbye/ (5)rgyal rabs kun gyi mchog gyur rgya gar rgyal rabs/ (10)bcom ldan 'das kyi rnam thar las 'phags pa'i mdzad pa bcu gnyis bstan tshul/ (15)ston pa'i
sku tshab bzhengs tshul/ (32)bstan pa'i gtad rabs/ (35)bstan pa'i gnas tshad/ (37)bka' bsdu rim pa gsum du mdzad tshul/ (38)

[A:toc-2]'phags yul bal po'i rgyal rabs/ (51)blo ldan rgya nag rgyal rabs/ (62)dpa' bo mi nyag gi rgyal rabs/ (74)chos rgyal bod kyi rgyal rabs/ (77)bod kyi blon chen mdzangs

byon tshul/ (187)

[A:toc-3]dbus gtsang dpon chen dang / sa skya nang chen rim pa'i byon tshul/ (191)khri skor mchog gyur zha lu ba'i byung tshul dang / myang yul chags lugs/ (196)lha dbang sprul
pa dpal ldan shar dga'i byung tshul/ (201)ma sangs sprul pa stag sna rdzong pa'i byung tshul/ (213)gnod sbyin sprul pa rnam rgyal gling pa'i byon tshul/ (225)bod du
bstan pa phyi dar dang / mkhas grub sde dgon byung tshul/ (233)jo bo rje'i slob rgyud dang / bka' gdams pa'i byon tshul/ (238)rngog lo khu dbon gyi slob rgyud dang / bshad
grwa dar tshul/ (242)smad 'dul gyi bshad rgyud/ (247)

[A:toc-4]bod du bla chen mkhan rgyud dang / spu tsho mkhan rgyud/ paN chen mkhan rgyud rnams byon tshul/ (249)tshogs pa sde bzhir gyes tshul/ (251)dgas po bka' brgyud byon
tshul/ (253)phag mo gru pa'i chos rgyud dang / bla rabs byon tshul/ (264)dpal phag mo gru pa'i dpon rabs byon tshul/ (267)lha pa'i bla rabs chos rgyud byon tshul/ (272)shangs
pa bka' brgyud rin chen bdun byon tshul/ (274)chos rgyal 'phags pa'i shes bya rab gsal las/ snod bcud kyi chags tshul mdor bsdus/ (282)yig tshang gi mdzad byang dang
smon lam/ (290)

mchod brjod dang rtsom pa dam bca' ba// bla ma dang mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /chos kyi rgyal po skyabs gsum 'dus pa'i sku/ /chos kyi dbang phyug
khams gsum 'dren pa'i mchog /chos kyi 'byor pas stong gsum dbul ba sel/ /chos rje bla ma dus gsum mkhyen la 'dud/ /bskal bzang 'di la srid pa gsum gyi mgon/ /mtshan bzang
dpe byad brgyad cu'i gzi 'od 'bar/ /rigs bzang zas gtsang sras po lha'i lha/ /blo bzang kun mkhyen rgyal po'i zhabs la 'dud/ /byams pa'i thugs kyis log pa'i lta ba 'joms/
/snyan dbyangs gsung gi 'gro la chos char 'bebs/ /smra ba'i phyogs la mi 'jigs seng ge yi/ /spobs pa mchog stsol rgyal sras sku la 'dud/ /bstan pa yun ring gnas phyir
ston pa yis/ /bstan 'dzin skyes bu'i mthun rkyen sgrub pa dang / /bstan la gnod byed dgra bgegs tshar gcod pa'i/ /bstan srung lha chen dpal 'bar rgyal gyur cig/de ltar mchod
par brjod nas/ dam pa rnams dgyes pa'i 'bel gtam mkhas rmongs dbye ba'i gzhi/ /rgya gar rgya nag ge sar stag gzig dang / /bal po hor sog mi nyag rgyal rabs dang / khyad
par bod yul gangs can khrod 'di ru/ bstan pa'i gsal byed lo paN khu dbon sogs/ /mkhas grub du mas dka' ba brgya phrag gis/ /dge 'dun sde btsugs bshad sgrub bskyangs tshul
dang / /de'i

sbyin bdag sde dpon byams ldan rnams/ /rim par byon nas bstan pa'i bya ba dang / /rang gzhan phan bde'i dpal la bkod tshul gyi/ /yig tshang ngo mtshar 'phreng ba mtha' yas
rnams/ /bdag rmongs blo yis srad bur brgyus la nus/ /'on kyang bstan la gus zhing mkhas pa yi/ /phyag srol mthong la blo mos che ba dang / /gong ma'i rnam thar dam pa'i gleng
'os rnams/ /brjed du phangs nas sangs rgyas 'jig rten 'dir/ /byon pa'i tshul dang bka' chems bka' khol dang / /rgyal rabs rkyang khugs blon po'i zhal gdams dang / /sba
bzhed yar lung jo bo tshal pa dang / /bu ston gyis mdzad chos 'byung chen mo sogs/ /yig tshang sna tshogs legs bsdus brjed byang dang / /blo gsal mdzes pa'i rgyan la phan
phyir du/ /mdor bsdus don gsal 'di nyid bdag gis bris/ /mkhas pa'i tshogs kyis bzod pa mdzad par rigs/ /rgya bod kyi yig tshang mkhas pa dga' bar byed pa'i mchod brjod
dang gleng gzhi bstan pa phyogs dus thams cad du dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig/ //

'dzam bu gling pa'i rgyal rabs spyi byings kyi stong thun zur tsam bzhugs so/ / oM swa sti/ sngon bsags bsod nams du mas rgyu byas zhing / /rigs rus cho 'brang ldan pas rkyen
byas te/ /rgyu rkyen rten 'brel 'dzoms pas gling bzhi la/ /'khor lo'i sgyur rgyal rnams la'ang bstod par bgyi/ /spyi ru lha mi'i rjer gyur rgyal rigs la/ /rgyas par phye
na sum brgya drug cu yod/ /de las bsdus na rnam pa gnyis bshad de/ /dag pa sangs rgyas rje dang ma dag sems can rje/ /sangs rgyas rje ni sku gsum 'gro don mdzad/ /sems
can rje la rnam pa lngar dbye nas/ /stong gsum dbang byed spyi phud rgyal po dang / /sa 'dzin rgyal po phyogs skyong rgyal po dang / /rigs drug rgyal po 'dzam gling rgyal
po dang / /lnga po de yang 'dzam gling sog kha'i rgyal po la/ /bskos dang gdung rgyud glo bur rgyal por bshad/ /rgyal po de gsum 'khor los sgyur rgyal rkyen/ /de la spyi
phud rgyal po tshangs pa dang / /sa 'dzin brgya byin phyogs skyong rgyal chen bzhi/ /rigs drug rgyal po gshin rje chos rgyal dang / /'dzam gling gdung rgyud rgyal po mang
bkur rgyud/ /'khor lo sgyur rgyal spyi bo skyes la sogs/ /gser dngul zangs lcags dbang sgyur rgyal po yin/ /bod kyi rgyal po glo bur rgyal por grags/ /bskos pa'i rgyal
po phyogs bzhi'i rgyal po yin/ /rgya gar chos kyi rgyal por bsko ba ni/ /

byin rlabs bum pa glang chen snas bzung nas/ /de yis su la dbang bskur de la bkod/ /rgya nag gtsug lag rgyal por bsko ba ni/ /rgya'i khang pa shin tu mtho ba la| /shel gyi
skas btsugs su thar de la bsko/ /ge sar dmag gi rgyal por bsko ba ni/ /dpag chen bzhis mda' bzhi char phyogs bzhir 'phangs/ mda' bzhi dus su zin na de la bsko ba yin/ /stag
gzig nor gyi rgyal por bsko ba ni/ /rin chen gling nas nor bu sus lon gyis/ /nor gyi bdag po de la bsko ba yin/ /bskos pa'i rgyal po bzhi'i ston pa ni/ /rgya gar rgyal
po sngon sbyangs las 'phro can/ /sangs rgyas chos kyi snod du rung bas na/ /rgyal ba shAkya thub pas ston pa mdzad/ /rgya nag gtsug lag dpyad kyis 'dul gzigs nas/ /mkhyen
rab bdag po 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyis/ /gab tse sum brgya drug cu ston par mdzad/ /ge sar dmag gi 'dul bar gzigs nas su/ /lha mo panytsi ka yi bu lnga brgya po/ /de 'dra
dmag tu sprul nas ston pa mdzad/ /stag gzig nor gyi 'dul bar gzigs nas su/ /'phags pa nor 'dzin sku sprul ston pa mdzad/ /rgya gar chos rgyal ma rig mun pa sel/ /rgya nag
rgyal po legs nyes me long ston/ /ge sar rgyal po dmag gis dgra dpung 'dul/ / stag gzig rgyal pos dbul ba'i sdug bsngal sel/ /zhes bshad pa rnams rgyal rabs spyi yi stong
thun zur tsam mo// //

'dzam bu gling pa'i yul khams dang mi rigs rus rnam dbye bzhugs so/ / oM swa sti/ srid pa'i gter kha bang mdzod 'dzoms pa'i mthus/ /mi srid bya ba gang yang med pa'i phyir/
/khams gsum gling bzhi khyad par rgya bod na/ /yul grangs mi rigs rnam 'gyur 'di ltar snang / /de'ang lho 'dzam bu gling pa yul gru che chung dang / mtha' dbus kyi ngos
'dzin/ mi rigs/ skad rigs kyi rnam dbye mang du bstan cing / khyad par dam pa'i chos kyi 'byung khungs/ yul gyi dbus rgya gar rdo rje gdan la ngos 'dzin pa mang la/ mdo rgyud
nas kyang bshad pa ni chos dar sa yin pa la dgongs so/ /'dzam bu gling gi sa tshad dang yul khams kyi dbye gnas bstan pa lugs gcig la/ 'dzam gling sog kha 'di dbyibs
shing rta lta bu sog pa'i yu ba lcags ri'i ngos la bstan pa la dpag tshad phyed dang bzhi dang / gzhan phyogs gsum la dpag tshad stong phrag gnyis gnyis so/ /de'i shar gyi
gling g.yog rnga yab na/ ljon pa rta mgo can gyi rgyal khams yod cing / nub kyi rnga yab gzhan la/ yaksha srin po'i rgyal khams yod de/ gling g.yog gnyis po'ang dbyibs
gong dang 'dra zhing / rgya ni gling che ba'i phyed ma'i tshad do/ /'dzam gling 'di la yul gru chen po dgu yod par 'dod de/ shar na rgya nag dang khri bstan/ lho na rgya
gar dang kha che/ nub na stag sde dang / gzig 'phan/ byang na khrom dang /

ge sar gnyis/ dbus na bod yul gangs kyi ra ba dang dgu zer ste/ 'dzam gling gi sa tshad kyi lte ba/ bod gangs can 'di yin par 'dod pa ni/ sa mtho/ ri mang / gangs chags/ chu
bo thams cad 'di nas phyi mtha' rnams la babs pa'i phyir gyis/ 'di nyid sa'i dbus lte ba yin par 'dod do/ /bod kha ba can gyi rgyal khams dang / phyogs bzhi'i rgyal khams
kyi mtshams na/ srid pas bskos pa'i rdo ring chen po bzhi yod de/ shar phyogs rgya nag po dang bod kyi sa mtshams sha phud gangs dkar lha'i yul na/ 'gron bu dung gi rdo
ring btsugs pa yan chad/ lho phyogs rgya dkar po dang / bod kyi so mtshams nyug ma bu khur srin gyi mthing shun/ g.yu'i rdo ring btsugs pa tshun chod/ nub phyogs stag gzig
dang bod kyi so tshams/ skang ma skang gcig klu'i yul na/ sha tshe dngul gyi rdo ring btsugs pa man chad/ byang phyogs khrom ge sar dang bod kyi so mtshams ma sma'i lu
rgyud sman gyi yul na/ ra gan gser gyi rdo ring btsugs pa tshun chad/ de rnams bod kha ba can gyi sa tshad du rtogs par byed cing / rdo ring bzhi po de la/ sbom phra pho
'dom lnga bcu'i 'khor dang / dpangs la pho 'dom gnyis brgya re yod par byed do/ /bod la yul gru chen po gsum yod pa ni/ stod mnga' ris skor gsum gangs dang g.ya'i ra ba
rdzing dang 'dra ba la yul gru chen po gcig smad lha ri chu drug la/ nags dang ne'u ljongs zhing dang 'dra ba la yul gru chen po gcig bar dbus gtsang ru bzhi brag dang chu
'thab pa yur ba dang 'dra ba la yul gru chen po gcig te/ de gsum mo/ /dang po bod kha ba can gyi rgyal khams zer zhing / bar skabs su lha srin mang po'i 'dzin pa'i dus
na/ gdong dmar can gyi yul zer

ba'ang byung / de rting bod rgyal gri gum btsan po'i sras/ bar pa bya khris/ spu bo brag thog tu byon/ spu bo'i rje mdzad/ rting la yar gdan drangs/ spu de gung rgyal bya bar
mtshan gsol/ bod kyi rgyal por bskos/ de'i mnga' zhabs su gyur phyin na/ spur rgyal bod kyi yul bya ba 'di byung bar gda'o/ /rgya dkar po'i yul de/ dar dkar gyi yol ba
brkyangs pa dang 'dra/ rgya nag po'i yul/ mkhris pa gcong la bskyur ba dang 'dra/ bal po'i yul gzhong pa dang 'dra ba/ zhang zhung yul bshang kha'i sbubs 'dra/ lho kha bzhi
ra skor 'dra/ kong po'i yul bre 'dra/ bod zal mo'i sgang 'dra ba zer ba rgyal rabs khugs pa thugs rje chen po'i yang tig las gsungs so/ /'dzam bu gling na rgyal khams
che chung bcu gsum yod pa'i/ mi dngos can gyi 'dzin pa lnga ni/ rgya gar chos kyi rgyal khams/ rgya nag rtsis kyi rgyal khams/ stag gzig nor gyi rgyal khams/ khrom ge sar
dmag gi rgyal khams/ bod yul kha ba can gyi rgyal khams dang lnga'o/ /mi ma yin pas 'dzin pa'i rgyal khams brgyad ni/ og ma sbal 'byar rgyal khams/ the rings mig gis rgyal
khams/ skyer chab sme sha can gyi rgyal khams/ sog po spre'u lag can gyi rgyal khams/ rgya mo khyi khyo can gyi rgyal khams/ tshe tshe ra mgo can gyi rgyal khams/ sna
bo che bong bu'i rgyal khams/ tsu ta rkang gcig pa'i rgyal khams dang brgyad do/ /zhib par phye na/ 'dzam bu gling pa la/ mi rigs mi 'dra ba sum brgya drug cu/ skad rigs
mi gcig pa bdun brgya nyi shu/ lus kyi rnam 'gyur mi 'dra ba bcu bdun/ rus pa lces 'gyur tshad gcig ming kha nas thon tshad gcig yod

par bshad na'ang / rus kyi phyi mo bcu gnyis tsam la bsdus so/ /de la rgyal rigs rnams che ba/ rje rigs rnams mthun pa/ bram ze'i rigs rnams gtsang ba| dmangs rigs rnams mang
ba dang bzhi las/ spyi'i rigs bzhi zer te/ 'dzam bu gling pa'i mi rigs thams cad 'di bzhir 'dus so/ /bar gyi rigs bzhi ni/ rgya gar ba lha las chad pas/ saMskri ta lha'i
skad du smra/ rgya nag pa klu las chad pas/ na ga tri ta klu'i skad du smra/ hor lha ma yin las chad pas/ a su tri ta lha ma yin gyi skad du smra/ bod spre'u dang brag
srin mo las chad pa ni/ a wa bhraM sha tri ta 'dre'i skad du smra ba dang bzhi'o/ /nang gi rigs bzhi ni/ stong dang / ldong dang / se dang / dmu rnams te/ 'di bzhi las bod
mi phal che ba gyes par bshad pas/ 'di rnams la rus kyi phyi mo bcu gnyis zhes grags/ yang lugs gcig la/ phyi'i mi'u rigs bzhi ni/ spang phug gi phyi ba dang / ko kyong
gi sbal pa dang / spra dang / spre'u de bzhi'o/ /nang gi mi'u rigs bzhi ni/ gam shang rgya dang / gyim shang hor/ kha le mon/ spu rgyal bod dang bzhi'o/ /de'i nang nas/
rgya la grol cha gnyis su gyes pa ni/ dmu rus dang / ke la'o/ /hor la yang gnyis su gyes pa ni/ srin tsha dang / lha tsha'o/ /mon la rigs gsum byung ba ni/ mon rang rgyud
pa dang / rgya bod mtshams kyi mi nyag kong po dang gsum mo/ /bod la mi'u gdung drug tu grol te/ de yang bod khams pa'i lugs la/ sngon yul rma kha shu g.yag shur bya ba'i
gong khar/ srid pa rgya lu thing ge zhes pa la bu gsum byung ba la rgya bod hor gsur du gyes pa'i/ bod mi khri tho chen po bya ba de la bu drug byung ba ni/ dbra 'bru
ldong gsum lga dang bzhi/ nu bo was dha gnyis dang drug

bod kyi mi bu gdung drug des/ rma kha shu ras ldebs stag bya ba der/ bod ma gsum bu drug sa bgos byas/ dbra'i phra mo rab phra thob/ 'bru'i 'bru mo khrom khrom thob/ ldong
gi pa ma le sang thob/ sga'i sga mo me po thob/ dbra sdes rgya bod so mtshams su/ mtshams kyi mda' ra gong ma bzung / de la che rgyud gong nas ma shor ba/ pho bo ldong gi
bu rgyud yin/ mthu chen dam tshig ma nyams pa/ se khyung dbra'i bu rgyud yin/ dpa' rgya stag mche sder ma nyams pa/ a lcags 'bru'i bu rgyud yin/ phyugs g.yang mo'i mkhal
tshil ma zhu ba/ rmu tsha sga'i bu rgyud yin/ /pho bo ldong la che drug yod/ stod na pa tshab 'bring g.yas gnyis/ /bar na ro che rag shi gnyis/ /smad na mi nyag gyi then
gnyis/ /che drug 'chan gyi btsun drug de/ /gi ri mdo dang gling pa gnyis/ /ro rje phu dang 'da' ba gnyis/ /gyi than rgyas bsdus che chung gnyis/ /de che btsun spel ma bcu
gnyis yin/ /se khyung dbra la 'chad drug yod// stod na zhang zhung khyung po gnyis/ /bar na mar pa spu rang gnyis/ /smad na re khe nyag le gnyis// 'chad drug 'chan gyi
btsun drug de/ /ki la rme sha rme tshan gnyis/ /brag ru la gu rdo nye gnyis/ /nyag le kho bo kho 'dre gnyis/ /che btsun spel ma bcu gnyis yin/ khri zam 'bru'i che drug de/
/shar na king dang rong po gnyis/ /lho na bhe dang ri thog gnyis/ /smad na 'grom dang ngo gro gnyis/ /'chad drug 'chan gyi btsun drug de/ /a dang spos dang tsha khrom gsum/
/zhugs pa bstod nye nyer gre gsum/ /che btsun spel ma bcu gnyis yin/ /rmu tsha sga'i 'chad drug de/ /thod rus stag tu stod na yod/ /bya can khrab tsan stod na yod/ /bya
che span ston stod na yod/ /'chad drug 'chan gyi btsun drug de/ /sga la gyes pa yul sa gnyis/ /bstan rus yul stag 'grog sta gnyis/ / dba'as la che skor chung skor gnyis/
/ che btsun spel ma bcu gnyis yod// //

rgyal rabs kun gyi mchog gyur rgya gar rgyal rabs bzhugs so/ /na ma sarba buddha bo dhi satwa bhe/ kun mkhyen kun la mkhas pa'i zas gtsang sras/ /lha'i lhar gyur srid pa gsum
gyi mgon/ khams gsum mun pa'i smag rum sel mdzad pa/ /bu ram shing pa'i gdung 'dzin zhabs la 'dud/ /'dren mchog de yis mi mjed 'jig rten 'dir/ /gzigs pa lnga yis 'gro
ba'i don la byon/ /rgyal ba'i zhing mchog rgya gar rgyal rabs 'di/ /rgyal rabs kun gyi rtse mor 'bri bar bya/ /thog mar 'dzam gling 'di na mchog gyur pa/ /zas bzhi ming drug
tha dad rnam gsum gyi/ /kun nas 'byor pa sngon med mi yi bdag/mang pos bkur ba'i zhabs la phyag 'chal lo/ /de yang sngon rabs dang da ltar byung ba'i lo rgyus/ kha dog
sna tshogs pa las/ dang po rgyal po mang pos bkur ba'i gdung rabs 'di/ sngon la bshad par bya ba yin te/ 'dzam bu gling 'di dang po byung ba dang / mchog tu gyur pa'i phyir
ro/ /dang po stong gsum 'jig rten gyi khams 'di chags pa na/ /'dzam bu gling 'di chus rgya mtsho chen po'i steng du/ rlung gis bsrubs pa'i spris ma mar gsar lta bu'i
sa chen po 'di chags zhing / 'od gsal gyi lha 'ga' zhig tshe 'phos nas der mir skyes nas/ rang 'od kyis rang gsal zhing mkha' la 'gro la/ dga'

bde'i zas kyi 'tsho zhing / tshe lo dpag tu med pa thub par byung ngo / /de'i tshe gza' skar dus tshes pho mo'i dbye ba gang yang med do/ /der mi gcig gis sa'i bcud ro bzang
po dang ldan pa zhig rnyed/ de myangs pas thams cad rim gyi kha zas za zhing / sgyu lus lci ba dang 'od kyang nub/ nyi zla gza' skar dus tshigs nyi nub la sogs pa byung
ngo / /sa'i bcud de nub nas rim gyi dman te/ bdud rtsi sa'i zhag myu gu'i tshal ma rmos pa'i lo thog byung ba rnams rim par zos pas pho mo'i dbang po byung ste/ 'khrig pa
spyod pa byung ngo / /de yi ngo tsha skyobs pa la khang pa byung / de'i sngon lo thog la gsog 'jog dang dbang ris med cing / nam dgos dus su len/ brngas ma thag skye ba
la mi gcig gis gsog 'jog byas pas/ 'bru ngan cing phub sog can du gyur/ gcig gis ma byin par blangs pas kun bgros nas gzugs dang spyod pa phun sum tshogs pa'i mi gcig rgyal
por skos/ de la zhing pa kun gyi lo tog gi drug cha re phul bas/ rgyal po sa'i drug cha dbang zer ba de nas byung zhing / mang pos bkur ba'i rgyal po zhes bya bar grags
la/ lho 'dzam bu gling pa'i rgyal po'i thog ma yin no/ /mang bkur rgyal po de'i yab lha chen po/ de'i yab lha rgyal ba nas yar la/ rim pa bzhin/ lha gzigs ldan bkra shis/
lha dbang po lag pa/ 'khor ba dung skyong / dri med dpung mdzes/ bshad can nam bshad dang bdun no/ /yar 'ded kyi lha bdun zer ste/ lung gsal po mi 'dug na'ang / 'di ni
bsam gtan bzhi pa'i gnas nas chad pa yin zer ro/ /mang pos bkur ba'i bu rgyud rim pa bzhin/ 'od mdzes/ dge ba/dge mchog gso sbyong 'phags rnams sngon gyi rgyal po sde lnga'o/
/'di rnams kyi

ring la/ mi'i ming la rim pa bzhin/ sems can/ tshur shog rme ba can/ sprin mgrin/ ta li skang ngo / /gso sbyong 'phags kyi spyi bo'i lba ba rdol ba las skyes pa/ rgyal po nga
las nu ni gling bzhi dang / rgyal chen rigs bzhi dang / sum cu rtsa gsum man la gser gyi 'khor los dbang bsgyur ro/ /de nas mi'i ming mi zhes bya ba 'di byung ngo / /nga
las nu'i brla g.yas pa las skyes pa mdzes pa/ de'i brla las nyer mdzes/ de'i brla las mdzes can/ de'i brla las mdzes ldan rnams 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po lnga te/
rim pa bzhin du/ gling bzhi dang / gsum/ gnyis/ gcig la/ gser dngul zangs lcags kyi 'khor los dbang bsgyur ro/ /de'i dus su bskal ba rdzogs ldan skye dgu'i tshe lo bzhi
khri pa/ bram ze'i rigs kyi sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig 'jig rten du byung ngo / /de'i bstan pa dam pa'i chos ni lo brgyad khri'i bar du gnas par bshad/ mdzes ldan bu ni bzang
po nas/ bu rgyud rim pa bzhin rgyal rabs sum cu'i mthar/ kun nas 'od zer zhes bya ba'i rgyal rabs brgya tham pa yul gru 'dzin du byung / de nas rim par rgyud de/ yul
dmag gi mi tshugs pa la sogs pa'i yul chen po bcu drug dang / sangs rgyas de'i bstan pa'i ring la rgyal rabs drug 'bum gcig khri drug stong nyis brgya dang gsum byung ngo
/ /de nas bskal ba gsum ldan tshe lo gsum khri pa'i dus su/ bram ze'i rigs kyi sangs rgyas gser thub byon/ de'i dam pa'i chos lo lnga stong gnas par bshad do/ /de nas yul
dmag gis mi tshugs pa la sogs pa yul chen bzhi/ sangs rgyas de'i bstan pa'i ring la/ rgyal rabs nyis 'bum drug khri chig stong brgya dang lnga bcu byung ba'i tha ma rgyal
po

kri kri yin ste/ bskal ba gnyis ldan tshe lo nyi khri pa/ rgyal rigs kyi sangs rgyas 'od srung byon/ de'i dam pa'i chos tshe lo brgyad khri gnas par bshad do/ /kri'i kri'i
bu rgyud brgya tham pa yul gru 'dzin du byung ba tha ma rna ba can no/ /de la bu go'u ta ma dang / bha ra dhwa dza gnyis las/ nu bos rgyal srid bzung ngo / /go'u ta mas nags
na bsam gtan sgom/ de'i skabs su g.yon chen padma'i rtsa lag gis/smad 'tshong ma 'gro ba bzang mo bsad pa'i nyes pa go'u ta ma la dkris pas/ bha ra dhwa dzas rang gi
phu bo yin pa dang / nyes pa med par ma shes/ go'u ta ma khrims las bsgral/ de 'chi khar rang gi mkhan po mdog nag dang 'phrad nas/ bden pa brjod pas/ mkhan po gser mdog
tu gyur/ des tshul bzhin ma yin pa chags pa yid la byas/ sa bon zags pa las sgo nga'i nang nas khye'u byung ba mkhan pos/ bu ram shing gi tshal du nyi ma la bskyangs pas/
ming nyi ma'i gnyen dang / bu ram shing par btags so/ /phyis bha ra dhwa dza bu med par shi go'u ta ma btsal bas ma rnyed/ sngar gyi lo rgyus zhus pas thams cad mya ngan
du gyur/ khye'u gnyis po blangs nas rim par rgyal sar bskos so/ /'di la bu ram shing pa'i steng zer ro/ /de'i bu rgyud brgya tham pa yul gru 'dzin du byung ba'i tha ma/
'phags skyes po/ de la bu rgyud gsum skyes/ ma de shi nas/ rgyal rigs dbang chen nyi 'og rgyal po zhes bya ba'i bu mo khab tu blangs/ de la bu byung na rgyal sar 'don pa'i
chad byas pas/ bu byung ba rgyal srid dgar ming btags rgyal por bskos/ phu bo gsum po rang rang gi sring mo dang bcas te spyugs pas chu bo skal ldan shing rta'i 'gram du/
ri dwags gsod cing lang tsho rgyas pa dang / drang srong

gis gnang ba byin nas/ mas dben pa'i ming sring 'grogs pas rgyud mang du 'phel ste/ ser skya dang lhas ldan du grong khyer chen po mang du byung ste/ yab kyis de'i rgyu mtshan
tshor nas/ de bzhin phod pa phod pa byas pas/ shAkya shAkya zhes grags so/ /'di la shAkya'i rigs kyi ya mtshan zer te/ rigs phal pa ma 'dres pa'i phyir ro/ /phyis rgyal
srid dgar la bu med par shi phu bo rnams rim par rgyal sar bskos pas/ che rgyud la shAkya chen po/ 'bring rgyud la shAkya ri brag pa/ chung rgyud shAkya li tsa byi'i rgyud
zhes pa grags shing / rgyal po dka' thub can gyi rgyud lnga khri lnga stong / ser skyar byung ba'i tha ma shing rta bcu pa'o/ /de rnams kyi rgyud pa bcu gcig gis tha
ma gzhu brtan la sras seng ge 'gram dang / seng ge sgra'o/ /phu bo'i sras zas gtsang / zas dkar/ bre'o zas/ tshad med zas so/ /zas gtsang gi sras rgyal po don grub dang
/ gcung dga' bo/ zas dkar la/ rgyal ba dang bzang ldan/ bre'o zas la/ ming chen dang ma 'gag pa/ tshad med zas la/ kun dga' bo dang / lhas sbyin no/ /rgyal po don grub kyi
sras sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po yin te/ 'di yan gyi shAkya chen po'i rgyud bar ma chad zer de/ rgyal po zas gtsang yan/ sangs rgyas 'od srung gi bstan pa'i ring la/ rgyal
rabs lnga khri lnga stong nyis brgya nyi shu rtsa gcig byung ngo / /de'i rting du rgyal bu don grub dang / sras sgra can 'dzin bzang po yan nas/ mang pos bkur ba'i rgyal
po man kun dril bas rgyal rabs dgu 'bum sum khri nyis stong bdun brgya bcu gsum byung ngo / /rgya gar chos rgyal rgyal rabs 'di bris pas/ /dge ba'i chos lugs lugs bzhin
dar ba dang / /bshes gnyen chos mdzad mdzad 'phrin rab rgyas zhing / /zhing 'dir thub bstan bstan pa gnas par shog /dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig/ / /

bcom ldan 'das kyi rnam thar las 'phags pa'i mdzad pa bcu gnyis bstan tshul/ dang por rgyal po don grub mi mjed 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir byon pa ste/ nyan thos pa na re/ skye
ba dpag tu med pa'i sngon nas tshogs gnyis bsags pa'i skyes bu rang rgyud pa gcig rgyal po zas gtsang gi sras su 'khrungs pa yin zer/ byang sems pa rnams ni/ 'di so so
skye bo yang ma yin/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang ma yin zer/ gsang sngags pa rnams ni sngon bskal ba me long gi 'byung gnas zhes bya ba la/ lam lnga/ sa bcu
bgrod nas sangs rgyas tshar ba de'i sprul pa yin zer/ gang ltar yang dang po byang chub mchog tu thugs bskyed/ bskal ba grangs med gsum du tshogs bsags/ sgrib pa sbyangs
pa'i mthar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par thams cad mthun pas/ de yang thugs bskyed lugs mdo sde snying rje pad dkar las/ 'di dang po bram ze rgya mtsho'i rdul du
gyur tshe thugs bskyed ces pa dang / bskal bzang las/ sman par gyur tshe thugs bskyed/ drin lan gsab par dmyal ba'i lcags bsregs kyi thang la/ shing rta 'dren pa'i gyad
du 'khrungs tshe thugs bskyed/ phung po gsum par tshong dpon gyi bu sngon dgar gyur tshe'am/ yang na rdza mkhan gyi khye'u snang byed du gyur tshe/ sangs rgyas thub pa chen
po'i drung du 'khar ba'i bum pa

gcig dang / dkar sha pa ni rdog po lnga/ mchil lham zung gcig /gdugs gcig rnams phul nas/ bde bar gshegs pa khyed sku ci 'dra dang / /'khor dang sku tshe'i tshad dang zhing
khams dang / khyed kyi mtshan mchog bzang po ci 'dra ba/ /de 'dra kho nar bdag sogs 'gyur bar shog /ces pa'i smon lam btab nas thugs bskyed par bshad do/ /de rting bskal
ba grangs med gsum du tshogs bsags par/ sangs rgyas rin chen gtsug tor can yan gyis grangs med dang po rdzogs/ sangs rgyas mar me mdzad yan gyis grangs med gnyis pa rdzogs/
rnam gzigs yan gyi grangs med gsum pa rdzogs par bshad de/ rnam gzigs mar me rin chen gtsug /grangs med gsum gyi tha mar byung / /dang po shAkya thub pa'o/ /zhes pa ltar
'dod do/ /grangs med kyi ngos 'dzin nyan thos pa'i lugs la mdzad nas dang po rdzogs pa lung las/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa nas/ /'dren pa yul 'khor skyong gi bar/ /bdun
khri lnga stong tshang ba yis/ /sangs rgyas rnams ni ngas mchod do/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa rdzogs pa lung las/ sangs rgyas legs mdzad nas bzung te/ /dbang po rgyal mtshan
thug gi bar/ /bdun khri drug stong tshang ba yis/ /sangs rgyas rnams ni ngas mchod do/ /zhesaso/ /gsum pa rdzogs pa lung las/ sangs rgyas mar me mdzad nas ni/ /sangs rgyas
'od srung bar dag tu/ /bdun khri bdun stong tshang ba yi/ /sangs rgyas rnams ni ngas mchod do/ /zhes so/ /theg pa chen po'i lugs la/ gong ltar khyi'u snang byed kyi thugs
bskyed pa nas bzung ste/ sa dang po ma thob kyi bar la bskal ba grangs med dang po/ de'i dus so so skye bo'i lus grangs med blangs rting tshogs kyi lam du zhugs nas/
dge ba spel ba dang / sbyor lam las 'bras la nges shes skyes te/ de'i bar la sangs rgyas bdun khri lnga stong la bsnyen bkur byas pa'i tha ma la/ sangs rgyas rin chen gtsug
tor can yin

no/ de ltar sa dang po rab tu dga' ba thob nas/ mthong lam chos nyid bden pa rdzogs te/ sa gnyis pa dri ma med pa nas/ sgom lam la zhugs/ sa gsum pa 'od byed pa/ bzhi pa 'od
'phro ba/ lnga pa spyangs dka' ba/ drug pa mngon du gyur pa/ bdun pa ring du song ba'i sa thob pa man la/ grangs med gnyis pa'o/ /de'i bar la sangs rgyas bdun khri drug
stong la bsnyen bkur byas pa'i tha ma la/ sangs rgyas mar me mdzad yin no/ /de'i rting la sa brgyad pa mi g.yo ba/ dgu pa legs pa'i blo gros/ bcu pa chos kyi sprin thob
pa'i dus su/ byang chub sems dpa' dam pa tog dkar por gyur cing / de man gyi grangs med gsum du tshogs bsags nas/ de'i ring la sangs rgyas bdun khri bdun stong la bsnyen
bkur byas pa'i tha ma la/ sangs rgyas rnam gzigs yin no/ /de ltar bskal pa grangs med gsum du tshogs bsags nas/ sa bcu non cing / sa gnyis pa nas bcu'i bar la/ sgom lam la
sgom pa 'phel ste/ sa bcu gcig pa kun tu 'od dang / bcu gnyis pa ma chags padma can dang / bcu gsum pa rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sa sangs rgyas kyi go 'phangs brnyes pa'i tshul
'og nas bshad pa ltar ro/ /thub pa'i mdzad pa bcu gnyis dngos la/ 'jig rten pa'i mdzad pa lnga la lhum su zhugs pa/ sku bltams pa/ gzhon nu rol rtsed mdzad pa/ btsun mo
khab tu bzhes pa/ rgyal srid bzung ba rnams so/ /'jig rten las 'das pa'i mdzad pa lnga ni/ rab tu byung ba/ dka' ba spyad pa/ chos 'khor skor ba/ cho 'phrul bstan pa/ bdud
btul cing sangs rgyas pa rnams so/ khyad par can gyi mdzad pa gnyis ni/ rtag tu re ba rnams sun 'byin pa'i phyir/ mya ngan 'das pa'i tshul bstan pa dang / phyi rabs spro
ba skyed pa'i phyir/ sku gdung ring bsrel cha brgyad du bgos pa dang / byin rlabs 'byung ba'i mdzad pa'o/ /de ltar mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi dang po/ dam pa tog dkar por
gyur ste/ dga' ldan du bzhugs

pa'i dus su/ mi mjed 'jig rten gyi khams su snyigs ma lnga bdo bar ni/ sems can tshe dang / nyon mongs dang / lta ba dang / dus kyi snyigs ma rnams la dgongs nas/ dus kyi snyigs
ma ni pha dang bur 'thab pa/ tshe'i snyigs ma ni tshe lo brgya pa/ nyon mongs pa'i snyigs ma dug lnga rags pa / las kyi snyigs ma dge ba chung du spyod pa/ lta ba'i
snyigs ma log par spyod pa'o/ /gdul bya dus la babs par shes nas/ rtsod ldan gyi dus/ 'jam bu gling pa'i mi rnams tshe lo brgya pa'i skabs su/ dga' ldan du rgyal tshab byams
pa la dbang bskur nas/ 'dzam bu gling du gzigs pa lnga'i sgo nas/'byon par chas pa ni/ gnas dang rigs rgyud yab yum dus dang lnga la gzigs nas/ yul ni ser skya la sogs
pa grong khyer drug la gzigs/ rigs rgyal rigs la gzigs/ yab zas gtsang ma la gzigs/ yum sgyu ma lha mdzes la gzigs/ dus yum gso sbyong mdzad pa'i dus la gzigs/ nga ni
'dzam bu gling du chos ston pa la 'gro'o gsungs pas/ lha thams cad ma dga' ste/ thabs sna tshogs pa'i gshol btabs kyang ma thebs pa dang / lha'i bu gzi brjid dam pas de ltar
na/ glang po che'i gzugs su sprul nas byon na/ don che'o zer ba ltar/glang chen thal dkar mche ba drug ldan gcig tu sprul nas byon/ grong khyer ser skya'i pho brang na/
rgyal po zas gtsang ma yab yur rgyal srid skyong gin bzhugs pa'i tshes bco lnga'i zla ba nya gang ba la/ yur lha mo sgyu 'phrul ma gso sbyong la gnas pa'i spyi bo nas
glang chen thims par rmis te/ lhums su zhugs nas yum la dga' bde'i ting nge 'dzin mang po thugs la 'khrungs par gyur to/ /de'ang jo bo rjes bzhed pa'i/ sangs rgyas shing
pho byi ba'i dbyar 'bring po'i nya la lhums su zhugs/ glang lo dpyid tha chung gi tshes brgyad la sku bltams/ sa mo phag la sangs rgyas/ shing pho spre'u lo mya ngan 'das
par bshad cing / chos rje sa skya paNDi ta ni me mo yos la lhums su zhugs par bzhed cing /sa pho 'brug la sku bltams/ spyir zla tha chung skar ma sa ga'i nya ba'i tshes

bco lnga'i yang gcig na dbo zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi'i nyin zer rgyal phur 'dzoms dus chu pho stag la sangs rgyas/ me mo smin drug zla ba'i tshes brgyad kyi zla ba ri mgo la
yol ba dang mya ngan las 'das phag la mya ngan las 'das par bzhed/ dpyid tha'i tshes brgyad skar ma rgyal la bltams par mthun no so/ /rgyal bu lhums su zhugs pa'i mdzad
pa de dang po'o/ /de ltar lhums su zla ba dgu ngo bcu bzhugs nas/ lum bi ni'i tshal du yum gyi phyag g.yas pas shing nya gro ta'i yal ga la 'jus pa'i 'og rtsib ma'i bar nas
sku bltams/ lhas me tog gtor/ brgya byin dang tshangs pas bstan/ lha klu thams cad kyi mchod pa phul/ dga' bo dang nyer dga' bo la sogs pas sku khrus gsol/ sku las 'od
zer 'phros bltams 'phral la phyogs bzhir gom pa bdun bdun bor bas/ zhabs rjes la padma re re byung cing / dge mtshan che ba'i tshigs su bcad pa re re gsung dus yab kyis/
gang tshe rkang gnyis gtso bo khyod bltams tshe/ /sa chen sogs bstod pa ni thub pa'i bstod pa'i thog ma'o/ /ston pa dang dus mnyam du yul dbus su rgyal po tshangs byin dang
/ padma chen po dang / dmag rgyal/ rtsib gyi mu khyud mtha' yas dang bzhi po la/ bu bzhi btsas pa ni/ gsal rgyal/ gzugs can snying po/ shar pa/ gtum po rab snang rnams
yin no/ /byang sems sku bltams nas zhag bdun nas yum 'das te/ sum cu rtsa gsum du skyes/ sru mo skye dgu'i bdag mos 'go byas/ ma ma brgyad la gtad nas 'phel skyed shin
du che'o/ /rgyal bu bltams pa'i mdzad pa ste gnyis pa'o/ /gsum pa ni de'i dus ri bo gru 'dzin na/ drang srong nyon mongs med ces pa/ 'jig rten chags 'jig la mkhas pa gcig
yod pa des/ 'od zer gyi snang ba

de mthong nas/ sangs rgyas sku bltams par shes shing / gzhan yang mtshan ltas mkhan rnams na re/ 'di ni rgyal srid bskyangs na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur zhing /
rab tu byung na 'jig rten gsum gyi mgon du nges par 'gyur ro/ / zhes sogs mtshan ltas shin du bzang bar bcad te/ /mtshan yang rgyal po don grub tu gsol lo/ /yang drang srong
na re/ da lta rtsod ldan tshe lo brgya pa'i dus/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mi 'byung bas/ 'di ni da ste lo sum cu rtsa lnga nas mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya
ba la the tshom mi za zhing / bdag ni rgas pas 'di'i chos mi thob par 'chi'o/ /zhes zer nas mya ngan byed la/ tsha bo mes sbyin la rgyal po 'di sangs rgyas dus khyed rab
tu byung zhig zer ba ltar byas pas/ mes byin dgra bcom pa thob pa'i mtshan ni 'phags pa ka ta ya na'o/ /shAkya'i rigs rnams kyi lha gnod sbyin shAkya 'phel gyi drung du rgyal
bu byon pas/ lha'i lhas phyag byas byung bas/ becom ldan lha'i lha'o zhes pa dang / de'i lam na shAkya'i rigs gdug pa can thams cad la 'tshe ba gcig yod pa des kyang
btud pas shAkya thub pa zhes grags so/ /de nas gzhon nu nyid nas yig dpon srin po'i go bya las 'bri klog dang / shAkya'i srid sgrub las rtsis dang / blon po lhar bcas las
'phongs dang / byang sems bzang po len las glang po che'i gnya' bar bzhon pa sogs/ rgyal po'i bya ba rnams slob par brtsam pa tsam gyis mkhyen te/ lhas byin la sogs rgyal
phran rnams dang / angga mangga dhar sgyu rtsal 'gran dus/ zhabs kyi mthe bong gi glang po che'i ro dpag tshad gcig gi bar la skyur bas/ sa gshong nge song ba ser skya
grong khyer gyi phyi rol na glang po gshong bya

ba yod do/ /mda'i rtsal 'gran pas/ shing rta la bdun lcags kyi phag pa bdun dang bcas pa phug nas/ mda' zug pa'i rjes na mda' chu khron pa skyes zer ba/ yan lag brgyad ldan
gyi chu yod do/ /gzhan yang rkyal dang shing sdong gcod pa la sogs pa rtsal sna gang la yang sus kyang 'gran par mi nus pas gzhon nu rol rtsed kyi mdzad pa ste gsum pa'o/
/bzhi pa de nas rgyal po'i dgung lo bcu bdun bzhes pa'i dus su/ shAkya lag na be con gyi bu mo grags 'dzin ma dang / dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa'i dus/ shAkya du legs
kyi bu mo sa mtsho ma dang / nyi shu rtsa dgu bzhes dus shAkya dril bu sgra'i bu mo/ shAkya bza' ri dwags skyes ma rnams 'khor nyi khri nyi khri dang bcas pa khab tu blangs
pa ni/ btsun mo khab tu bzhes pa'i mdzad pa ste bzhi pa'o/ /lnga pa de ltar lo nyi shu rtsa dgu'i bar la ni/ rgyal srid tshul dang mthun pa bskyangs shing / yab kyis
rgyal bu chos las yengs nas/ 'jig rten gyi bya ba la blo 'brid pa'i phyir/ zhing pa'i mtha' rtogs su bcug pa'i che/ ngo mtshar ba'i ltas mthong nas/ gang tshe thub chen
zhing pa'i gong bzhud tshe/ /zhes pa'i sras la bstod pa mdzad do/ /der rting rgyal po chibs pa ngang pa gser ldan la chibs/ 'dun pas sna khrid de grong khyer gyi shar lho
nub rnams su/ nyin re byon pas na rgas 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal 'dun pas brda sbyar/ byang phyogs su byon nyin/ sprul pa'i dge slong dang mjal/ bzhon pa las babs te phyag byas/
bdag kyang 'di ltar rab tu byung ngo gsungs/ pho brang du log rab tu byung lugs ji ltar legs

bsam pa kho na sems kyin bzhugs pas/ yab dang 'khor 'bangs thams cad kyis bslu brid dang / yengs thabs sna tshogs byed cing / mtshan mkhan na re/ da ste zhag bdun la rgyal
bu rab tu ma byung na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur ro zer bas/ yab dang khu bo mes po 'khor bcas thams cad kyis pho brang gi phyogs mtshams thams cad dpung dang bcas
nas bsrungs/ btsun mo rnams kyis nang du glu gar dang bkur sti la sogs pas thugs yengs thabs byed do/ /de nas zhag bdun pa'i srod la/ rgyal po'i dgongs pa la/ bdag gi
btsun mo drug khri blang pa la gcig dang yang ma 'grogs na/ zas gtsang gi sras kyis bud med bsten ma nus pas dbang med du rab tu byung ba yin no zer ba'i yal ga yong bsam/
de spangs pa'i phyir/ de nub btsun mo dam pa grags 'dzin ma dang lhan cig gzims so/ /sras sgra can 'dzin lhums su zhugs so/ /tho rangs kyi cha zin pa dang / brgya byin
gyis skul nas/ rta ngang pa gser ldan la chibs yab rgyal po mnal du song ba la bskor ba byas/ phyi phyag btsal nas/ 'dun pas kyang rta gsham du bzhon pa dang / lha'i bu
bzhis rta'i rmig pa re re nas btegs nas/ dka' thub kyi nags la gtad de/ nam mkha' la myur bar byon no/ /rgyal srid chos bzhin bskyangs pa'i mdzad pa ste lnga pa'o/ /drug
pa ni/ der rgyal bu nam mkha' la byon pa la/ gzugs khams kyi lha man chad/ tshangs pa dang brgya byin la sogs pas bsus shing spro ba skyed pas/ nam thun gcig na dka' thub
kyi nags mchod rten rnam dag drung du brtol nas/ rang nyid kyi dbu skra rang nyid kyi gzhar ste/ rab du byung / 'dun pa la rta dang rgyan

cha rnams bskur te/ ser skyar slog btang bas/ smre sngags 'don cing phyin pas zhag bdun la slebs tsam byung zhing / blon 'bangs rnams kyi rta la 'ju zhing ngus pas/ gser ldan
de nyid du shi nas/ grong khyer sgra can du bram ze las drug la mkhas pa gcig tu skyes so/ /rgyal po rab tu byung ba'i dbu skra dang / ka shi ka'i na bza' rnams brgya
byin gyis khyer nas/ sum cu rtsa gsum na rin po che las gru ba pa'i dbu skra'i mchod rten dang / na bza'i mchod rten bya ba bzhengs yod do/ /grong khyer dpe med kyi khyim
bdag gi bus bzhag pa'i na bza'/ ngur smig brgya byin gyi lag nas phul ba gsol te/ rang byung du bsnyen par rdzogs par gyur to/ /de nas yab dang rgyal po legs par rab gsal
kyi rgyal bu gcig pur nags la 'dug ces pa thos nas/ 'khor lnga brgya btang bas/ lnga nyar gzhan rnams phyir slog btang ngo / /rab tu byung ba'i mdzad pa ste drug pa'o/
/bdun pa ni/ de nas 'khor lnga po yang khrid de chu bo na ra dzA ra'i 'gram du byon nas/ /lo drug tu dka' thub mdzad par zhing pa'i bu mo gnyis kyis 'o ma'i nying khu la/
lha'i bu gnyis kyi gzi brjid skyed pa'i sman btab nas drangs pa gsol bas/ sku lus gser btso ma'i mdog lta bur gyur nas/ de'i tshe 'khor lnga po yang ma dad par gyur nas/
rang re tsho wa ra Na sir 'gro zer song ngo / /dka' ba spyad pa'i mdzad pa ste bdun po'o/ /brgyad pa ni/ de nas byang sems kyis sangs rgya bar bzhed de/ 'od gsal gyi lha'i
tshig bzhin rdo rje gdan la phyin pa'i lam du/ tshong dpon ga gon dang / bzang pos 'bras chan drangs pas/ gsol ba'i zhal phor la lha'i bu'i lhung bzed gsum phul ba gcig
tu byin gyis brlabs nas gsol/ tshong dpon gyi lam gyi bar chad bsrung ba'i phyir lha'i bkra shis don grub bya ba gsungs/ de

nas yang gshegs pa'i lam du/ rtswa tshong bkra shis kyis phul ba'i rtswa rdo rje gdan gyi spo la byang chub kyi shing drung du gdan la bting nas/ ji srid zag med ma thob bar/
de srid skyil krung gshig mi bya/ /gsungs nas/ srod la lha'i bu'i bdud btul/ nam gung rab mtha'i ting nge 'dzin mngon du mdzad/ tho rangs mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas
so/ /gsang sngags bla med pa rnams kyis byang sems kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi ngang de las 'og min du byon nas/ mngon par byang chub lnga'i stong pa nyid las byang chub pa/
gdan pad nyi las byang chub pa/ gsung yig 'bru las byang chub pa/ thugs phyag mtshan las byang chub pa/ sku yongs rdzogs las byang chub pa'o/ /gdams pa zhus ma thag tu
de ltar sgom pa dang / sa bcu gcig pa/ bcu gnyis pa/ bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sa thob ste sangs rgyas skad/ 'di ni rdo rje gdan du sangs rgyas zer ba dang yang mi 'gal
lo/ /nges par 'og min du sangs rgyas pa ni/ stug po bkod pa'i mdo las/ sangs rgyas thams cad 'og min du/ /sangs rgyas par ni ma gyur na/ /'dod khams gzugs khams rnams su
ni/ /sangs rgyas par ni mi mdzad do/ /zhes bshad pa bzhin no/ /mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i mdzad pa ste brgyad pa'o/ /dgu pa ni/ de ltar sangs rgyas ma thag tu/
'dul dka' ba'i skye bos zab mo'i chos zab zhi spros bral 'od gsal 'dus ma byas/ /bdud rtsi lta bu'i chos zhig kho bos brnyes/ /su la bstan kyang go bar mi 'dug pas/ /mi
smra nags kyi nang du gnas par byed/ /ces gsung nas chos ma gsungs/go dka' la/ rang nyams su blang bar bya'o dgongs nas/ zhag bzhi bcu zhe dgu'i bar la chos ma gsungs so/
/de'i rjes lha tshangs pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba btab pas/ gnang te 'khor rnams bsdu ba'i phyir/ ghaNDi brdung ba'i sgra la/ sangs rgyas slob mar gyur pa
gang su dag/

deng 'dir ston pas chos kyi char 'bebs kyis/ /gang dag nyan par 'dod rnams 'dir byon la/ /zab mo rgyal ba'i bka' la nyon cig ang / /zhes pa'i skad gsal bar byung zhing / thog
mar wA ra Na sir 'khor lnga sde bzang po la sags theg dman gyi gang zag rnams la/ chu stod zla ba'i tshes bzhi nas/bden pa bzhi'i chos kyi 'khor lo rim pa gsum du bskor
ro/ /gsum ni dang po sgrub pa'i 'khor lo/ /bar du chad pas bcad pa'i 'khor lo/ tha ma rung mthun gyi 'khor lo'o/ /'khor lnga sde po/ ye shes khong chud kyi bsnyen par rdzogs
par gyur cing / kun shes kauNDi nyas dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob/ gzhan bzhi po yang zag pa las sems grol lo/ /'khor lnga kun shes kauNDi nya/ rta thul/ ming chen/
glang po/ bzang ldan no/ /pos chos gos ldum po gon ma shes pa 'od gsal gyi lhas brda bstan to/ /chos 'khor gnyis pa/ bya rgod phung po'i ri la/ rab 'byor dang / sha ri'i
bu la sogs pa/ 'khor dgra bcom pa dang / byang sems mang po la/ theg pa thun mong ma yin pa'i mtshan nyid med pa'i chos kyi 'khor la bskor ro/ /chos 'khor gsum pa/ ri ma
la ya dang / yangs pa can la sogs par/ don dam yang dag 'phags la sogs/ 'khor rnam bzhi'i byang sems bsam gyis mi khyab pa la/ theg pa thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/
don dam rnam par nges pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ro/ /de'i skabs shig tu/ yab rgyal po zas gtsang yang dge ba la bskul ba'i dus la babs par mkhyen nas/ tshe dang ldan
pa 'char ka yab rgyal po'i drung dru btang / brda sbyar te/ shing nya gro ta'i kun dga' ra bar/ yab sras mjal nas/ 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams la chos bstan cing / yab kyi rgyang
nas gus pa'i phyag 'tshal/

dad pas bstod pa ni/ de yang 'di dang khyod la lan gsum du/ /thub pa khyod kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thugs rje che mnga' lha yi mchod pa'i gtso/ khyod 'dra 'jig rten ma
mchis lta ci smos/ /mtshan ni don grub lags zhes mngon brjod pa/ /pha dang ma yi bsam ste btags pa lags/ khyod kyi bsam rdzogs bdud rtsi brnyes pas na/ /don grub legs par
nga don bdag gi 'tshal/ /zhes pas bstod cing / yab rgyal po'ang sangs rgyas kyi zhal mthong / chos thos pas zag pa las sems rnam par grol lo/ /ston pa'i zhal nas dge slong
'char kas yab rgyal po dge ba la bskul ba'i bsod nams kyi phung po de la/ gal te gzugs yod na 'jig rten gyi khams/ gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed du mi shong ste/ bsod
nams kyi tshogs shin du rgya chen po gsungs so/ /de ltar chos 'khor rim pa gsum du bskor ba'i ring la/ lo bdun du zhag bzhi bcu zhe dgu ma tshang ba song bar byed cing
/ ston pa sangs rgyas nas lo bdun lon pa'i dus sum cu rtsa gsum du yum la chos gsung ba la byon/ zhag dgu bcu bzhugs pa de'i bar la/ lha tshangs pa dang / gza' khyab 'jug
lha'i dbang po brgya byin gsum gyis ston pa'i sku tshab re bzhengs par gsol ba btabs pas gnang ste/ tshangs pas lha'i rin po che las chos sku'i rten/ bum pa zlum por byas
pa/ dpal reg pa med pa du ba lta bu'i mchod rten bzhengs pa'i tshad tshangs pa'i mtho gang ngo / /de mkha' 'gros gdan drangs o rgyan gyi yul he ru ka'i rgyal khams na
bar snang la bzhugs te/ dpa' bo mkha' 'gro mi ma yin rnams kyi mchod pa'i rten byed/ mchog gi dngos grub ster ro/ khyab 'jug gi klu'i rin po che la/ longs sku'i

rten rnam snang gangs can mtsho'i sku dpag tshad bcu gnyis yod pa gcig bzhengs/ de phyis rgya mtsho na bzhugs te/ klu dang gza' rnams kyi mchod pa'i rten byed do/ /brgya byin
gyi lha mi'i rin po che sna tshogs dang / 'ching bu lnga bcu rtsa gcig la sprul sku'i rten/ sangs rgyas dgung lo brgyad pa dang / bcu gnyis pa dang / nyi shu rtsa lnga'i
sku tshad gsum bzhengs nas/ che ba de brgya byin rang gi yid dam mdzad/ chung ba gnyis rgya gar du rgyal po gsal rgyal gyi yi dam mdzad/ bar skabs nas rgya nag dang bal
yul du phebs/ mthar bod du 'gro don la phebs par lung bstan pa bzhin da lta lha sa 'phrul snang dang / ra mo che na bzhugs pa'i jo bo mched gnyis yin no/ sku tshab rnams
kyi rab gnas sangs rgyas nyid rang gis mdzad cing / lha bzo ba bi shwa karma dang / sku gnyer byams pa/ bka' srung phyag rdor dang dpal mgon bdun cu rtsa lngas byas shing
byed par dam bcas so/ /yang ston pa lha yul du bzhugs ring la rgyal po u tra ya na/ sems shin du skyo nas/ mo'u 'gal gyi bu la bskul nas/ tsan dan ga shirSha la ston pa'i
sku tshab lha yul du bzhengs rab gnas zhus te/ mi yul du spyan drangs/ phyis rgya nag tu phebs nas/ tsan dan jo bor grags pa yod/ paN chen shAkya shri ltar na/ tha skar
gyi zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la lha las babs pa'i dus chen yod par bzhed/ smin drug zla ba'i ches bzhi la/ sum cu rtsa gsum nas mi yul du phebs pa ni/ dpal lha las babs
pa'i dus mchod zhes bya'o/ /de ltar theg pa chung ngu'i chos rnams ni/ gang la gang 'tsham par bstan zin gyis/ theg chen bla med kyi chos rnams/ 'dzam bu gling gi mi rnams
la gsal bar ston pa'i dus skabs la ma

slebs par dgongs nas/ sprul pas gsungs pa ni/ 'khor los sgyur rgyal du sprul nas/ dur khrod bsil ba tshal du bya ba'i rgyud gsungs/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed du spyod pa'i rgyud
gsungs/ 'og min du rnal 'byor gyi rgyud gsungs/rgya gar lho phyogs shri dharma pha la chos kyi 'byung gnas su byon/ rdo gru gsum snol ba'i steng du/ rnal 'byor bla na
med pa'i rgyud rnams ni/ dpa' bo mkha' 'gro dang / mi ma yin rnams la gsungs pa'o/ /de rnams chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i mdzad pa ste dgu pa'o/ /bcu pa ni/ de dag gi skabs
su ston pa la tho mtshams zhing bar du gcod pa brtsam par 'dod pa'i bdud dang mu stegs rnams pham par mdzad pa ni/ 'khor mo 'jigs pa'i yul du bdud btul ba'i dus na/ gzhan
'phrul dbang byed nas bdud rje dga' rab dbang phyug kho yang / lha'i bu'i bdud dgu khris bskor nas byung te/ go'u ta ma khyod kyi bskal ba grangs med gsum du tshogs
bsags zer ba'i rdzun gtong bar 'dug pa/ de'i dpang por su yod zer ba la/ ston pas/ sa 'di 'gro ba kun gyi rten yin te/ /rgyu dang mi rgyu mnyam shing nye ring med/ /de ring
khyod kyi gzu dang dpang mdzod shig /gsungs pa dang / sa'i lha mo bstan ma byung nas lus phyed tsam pa steng du bton/ thal mo sbyar nas/ de nges par bden no zer bas/ bdud
rje skyengs te dpa' bkong zhing / bdud kyi sde rnams pham par gyur to/ /der rting gnyan yod du mu stegs kyi ston pa chen po rdzogs byed dang / gnag lhas kyi bu ka ti
dang / rnam par smra ba'i bu kun tu rgyal ba dang / mi pham skra'i lwa ba can dang / ka ta'i bu nog can dang / gcer bu

gnyen gyi bu ste rtog ge pa drug po bram ze rgyus rgyal dang bram ze rnam rdeg dang / bram ze bzang ldan dang / bram ze tshangs pa'i ched/ bram ze padma'i snying po dang/ bram
ze dmar po ste rjes su snyeg pa drug dang / rengs byed kyi bu lhag gcod dang / sgyu rtsal can gyi bu rings 'phur dang / kun tu rgyu rab bzang dang / bram ze bu kun rgyal
dang / drang srong nyon mongs med dang / steng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can te/ snyom par 'jug pa drug ste/ ston pa drug gsum bco brgyad kyi ma rung bar bgyis pas/ gshegs
pa'i skabs ma legs zhes gsol bas/ nyi ma'i 'od dang 'od gzhan ltar/ de dag chos dang ma 'dres shing / de dag nga nyid kyis zil gyi mnan nus so zhes gsung / 'khor dang
bcas pa rnams/ rta'i zla ba'i tshes gcig nas/ bco lnga'i bar nyin re bzhin cho 'phrul bstan nas/ bdud dang mu stegs thams cad tshar bcad nas nang pa'i sgor bcug pa ni/ bstan
pa rgyas par mdzad pa ste bcu pa'o/ /ston pa sangs rgyas nyid ni bskal pa'i bar du bzhugs na'ang dbang thob te/ bdud kyi gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ mya ngan las 'da' bar
zhal gyi bzhes tshar ba da nga / rtag 'dzin can rnams mi rtag pa la bskul ba'i ched du/ mya ngan las 'da' bar bzhed de/ grong khyer rtswa mchog tu chos kyi tha ma gsungs
pa'i dus na/'khor gyi nang nas rig 'dzin gyi rgyal po kun dza ra bya ba stan las langs/ pus mo btsugs nas bcom ldan 'das khyed kyi chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bstan
tshar ro gsungs mod kyang / bstan pa'i snying po zab mo'i lam gsang sngags bla na med pa'i theg pa dag 'dzam gling 'dir ma gsungs so zhes zhus pa'i lan du/ nga ni 'di
nas ma snang nas/ /lo ni brgya dang bcu gnyis nas/ /lha gnas gsum du grags pa'i sar/ /bstan pa'i snying po dam pa zhig/'dzam gling

shar lho'i phyogs mtshams su/ /mi lha skal ldan grags ma byed/ /rgyal po dza zhes bya ba la/ /sngon du ltas rnams snang gyur te/ /drag shul can zhes bya ba'i rtse/ /grogs kyi
sems la dag pa'i lus/ /lang ka'i bdag po la sogs la/ /phyag na rdo rjes ston par 'gyur/ /zhes lung bstan to/ /der 'khor thams cad mya ngan dang smre sngags 'don pa la/
'di skad ces bka' bstsal to/ /nga ni nges par mya ngan las 'da' bas/ lus gser mdog 'di la yang yang ltos/ phyis mya ngan ma byed cig 'dus byas thams cad 'di dang 'dra'o

la/ de ltar na cis kyang bzhugs par gsol ba btabs pas/ sa steng 'jig rten gang na yang / /skyes nas 'chi bar ma gyur tam/ /gang zhig khyod kyi ma mthong ngam/ /'on te mthong
na'ang the tshom za/ /nga yi mya ngan khyod byed na/ khyod kyi mya ngan sus byed pa/ de la 'bras bu gang yang med/ /gsungs pa de ni chos kyi phyi ma'o/ /der dbu nub tu
bstan/ zhal lhor gzigs/ zhabs shar la brkyang / phyag g.yas 'og tu bcug phyag g.yon brla'i steng du bskyal nas/ dgung la brgyad cu tham pa bzhes pa'i sa ga'i zla ba'i tshes

po bkod pa'i

zhing du gshegs so/ /sku gdung ni bka' bzhin dri bzang pos byugs ras yug stong dang / 'bru mar gyi dril nas/ zhag bdun nas zhugs la 'bul snyam par/ /ston pa nyid rang gi thugs

pa'i mdzad pa ste bcu gnyis pa'o/ // /

ston pa'i sku tshab bzhengs tshul/ yang sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das pa'i phyi lo'i dbyar de 'phags pa drug sdes/ 'dod khams kyi lha'i gnang ba dang bstun nas/ sangs rgyas
kyi sku tshab khru bcu drug pa mya ngan 'das chung bya ba dang / gzugs khams pa'i gnang ba dang bstun nas/ sku tshab khru sum cu rtsa gnyis pa mya ngan 'das chen bya ba
bzhengs so/ /de nas shrI seng has rten de gnyis la byang chub kyi shing gi ra bas bskor nas mchod pa chen po byas so/ /de nas lo nyi shu tsam nas/ bram ze ma hA pas la bya
bas khyim bdag chen po gcig gi bu che ba ma hA sam be ri bo gangs can gyi rgyud yul wa ra Na sir/ drang srong lhung ba ri dwags kyi nags bden bzhi'i chos 'khor skor sar/

bya ka lan dha ka skad 'don pa mtshan nyid med pa'i chos 'khor bskor sar/ gnas chen brgyad kyi byang chub snying po'i shing gi lo ma la rgyu byas nas sku tshab gcig bzhengs
pa'i mtshan/ bhe mu wan zhes grags so/ /bu chung ba ma la sam bhes/ ma'i ngag bzhin dbus 'gyur rdo rje gdan gyi steng/ byang chub kyi shing gi shar/ ston pa'i sku rgyab
bstan nas/ sangs rgyas sa der/ nang lha khang dang / phyi mchod rten du yod pa'i ghanno la'i dkyil du/ sangs rgyas dgung lo

sum cu ba'i sku tshad bzhengs pa de'i rgyu ni/ chu bo gang gA'i 'gram/ ston pa sku khrus mdzad pa'i rdzing bu na/ tsan dan go shirSha'i sdong po/ 'gyel ba brdar nas lde khu

gnyis ni/ tshong dpon gyi bu la klu'i rgyal pos byin pa'i rin po che mar gad cung gzhogs yod pa/ khru gang la dum bu gnyis byas nas phul ba de bcug yod pas nyin mtshan med
par 'od gsal lo/ /sku de bzhengs pa la zla ba drug zhag drug dgos rgyu la bram ze mas zhag gcig gi lta ba sngas pas sku'i zhabs g.yas pa'i the chung ma tshang bar byed
cing / mo na re sku 'di la sangs rgyas dngos dang mi 'dra ba'i mtshan rtags brgyad 'dug de min khyad mi 'dug phyis sku 'di la yon tan brgyad 'char bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes gleng
bar byed de/ lha mi'i ston pa shAkya thub pas/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir dgung lo brgyad cu'i bar la/ gnas gang du bzhugs dang / mya ngan las 'das khar bstan pa su la gtad/

brtan pa'i gtad rabs/ bcom ldan 'das kyi lung rim par bstan te/ bstan pa gtad pa ni/ ston pas 'od srung chen po la gtad/ de nas rim bzhin du/ kun dga' bo dang / shA na'i gos
can/ nyer sbas/ dhi dhi ka btsun pa buddha nanti la/ buddha mi tra la/ des slob ma dge slong rtsib la/ des su na sha ta la/ des rta skad la/ des ma shi ba la/ des klu sgrub

pa lags so/ /sangs rgyas shAkya thub pas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa'i zhing khams kyi

ming / stong gsum mi mjed 'jig rten zer la/ stong gsur gyi dbye ba ni/ ri rab gling bzhi/ gling phran nyi zla/ lcags ri khor yug tshang ba gcig nas bgrang ba'i cha stong la
stong chung yang zer la/ stong spyi phud gcig go / de stong la stong gnyis pa bar ma'o/ /de stong la stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams zer ro/ /de rnams
re re bgrangs na/ ri rab ling bzhi'i tshangs ris man chad bye ba phrag brgya ste/ dung phyur gcig go /mi mjed ces bya ba ni/ bzod pa'i ming ste/ pad dkar las nyon mongs
pa dug gsum gyi mi phrogs shing bzod la/ snying rje pad dkar las/ ci phyir 'jig rten gyi khams de ni mi mjed ces bya zhe na/ sems can de dag 'dod chags la mi mjed pa dang

bstan pa'i gnas tshad/ thub pa'i bstan pa gnas tshad la/ mdo sde bskal bzang las/ dam pa'i chos ni lo lnga brgya dang gzugs brnyan lnga brgya ste/ lo stong du gnas zer ba dang
/mdo rgyud mang po nas lo grangs mi gcig pa du ma zhig bshad na'ang / de rnams ni drang don dgongs pa can re yin la/ 'bum TIka 'grel pa gnod 'joms nas bshad pa 'di ni
sgra ji bzhin pa yin par mkhas pa rnams bzhed do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'bum TIka nas bstan pa lo lnga stong du gnas pa/ lnga brgya phrag bcur phye bas le'u bcu tham par
'gyur la/ le'u dang po la dgra bcom pa'i le'u/ gnyis pa la phyir mi 'ongs pa'i le'u/ gsum pa la rgyun du zhugs pa'i le'u rnams la khongs du chud pa'i le'u gsum zhes bya'o/
/bzhi pa lhag mthong gi le'u/lnga pa ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u/ drug pa tshul khrims gyi le'u rnams la sgrub pa'i le'u gsum zer/ bdun pa mngon pa/ brgyad pa mdo sde/ dgu
pa 'dul ba'i le'u rnams la lung gi le'u gsum zer/ lnga brgya ba phrag bcu pa la rab tu byung ba'i rtags tsam las/ lta spyod rnal ma dag mi ldan pas/ rtags tsam 'dzin pa'i
le'u ste/ 'di la lnga brgya tha ma zhes bya'o/ /bstan pa lo lnga stong du gnas rgyu'i steng nas/ sngar ji tsam 'das/ da lo grangs ji tsam gnas ni/ 'di thog nas zhib tu
brtsi'o/ / / /

bka' bsdu rim pa gsum du mdzad tshul/ sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas/ dgra bcom pa chos kyi spyan dang ldan pa rnams kyis/ bka' bsdu rim pa gsum du mdzad pa'i tshul ni/
de mtshams shA ri'i bu la sogs pa'i dgra bcom pa shas che ba yang mya ngan las 'das 'das gang po e yin tshul bstan 'khor thams cad ston pa gshegs pa'i mya ngan gyis/ chos
khrims lhod par gyur pa la lha rnams 'phya bar byed pa/ 'phags pa 'od srung gis gsan nas/ bka' bsdu bar dgongs te/ dang po bskul nas gaNDi brdungs pas/ dgra bcom pa lnga
brgyar gcig gis chad pa 'dus/ der kun dga' bo'i rgyud la dgra bcom pa ma thob par mkhyen nas/ 'od srung gi rtsod pa rnam pa brgyad kyi sgo nas nyes pa'i tshul shing gtad
pa ni/ kun dga' bo khyod kyis skye dgu'i bdag mo rab tu byung ba'i zhu sna byas pa dang / ston pa la chu snyog ma can drangs pa dang / na bza' 'tshem dus pus mo'i 'og tu
mnan pa dang / mya ngan las 'da' gsungs dus bzhugs par ma zhus pa dang / dris lan log par btab pa dang / so thar sdom pa'i gnad ston par bzhed pa la/ ched gnyer ma zhus
pa dang / mya ngan las 'da' khar sku gser mdog gzhan la bstan pa dang / sku'i gsang gnas sbubs su nub pa bud med rnams la bstan pa dang / brgyad po des nyes pa'i tshul shing
len du

bcug tshogs nas phud pa dgra bcom pa spong byed kyi bskul nas bsam gtan bsgoms pas zhag bdun nas dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob nas/ rgyal po'i khab tu byon nas/ snam sbyar lnga
brgya'i khri thog tu bzhugs nas bka' bsnga mdzad pa'o/ / bka' dang po don rnam pa bdun gyi sgo nas bsdus ste/ dus ni sangs rgyas mya ngan 'das pa'i phyi lo'i dbyar ro/
/gnas ni rgyal po'i khab/ a su gsang ba'i brag khung ngam/ rdo bcag pa'i phug go /sbyin bdag ni rgyal po ma skyes dgra'o/ /tshogs pa ni dgra bcom lnga brgya'o/ /gang zag
sus thugs rgyud la bsdus pa ni/ 'phags pa 'od srung gis bskul nas/ kun dga' bos mdo sde/ nye bar 'khor gyi 'dul ba/ 'od srung gi mngon pa'i sde snod rnams/ dbyar zla 'bring
po'i tshes bcu drug nas brtsams te bsdus pa'o/ /bsdu ba'i dngos gzhi ni sangs rgyas kyi bka' sde snod gsum mo/ /dgos byed sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che dar zhing
rgyas par bya ba dang / lha rnams kyi 'phya ba bsal bar bya ba'i phyir bsdus pa dang bdun no/ /bka' bsdu bar pa la don bdun te/ dus ni sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas
lo brgya dang bcu nas so/ /gnas yangs pa can gyi gtsug lag khang du'o/ /sbyin bdag rgyal po dharma a sho ka'o/ /tshogs pa dgra bcom bdun brgya'o/ /gang zag dgra bcom pa
grags pas gsol ba btab nas gnas brtan thams cad 'don gyi thugs rgyud las so/ /bsdu bya sde snod gsum mo/ /dgos pa bstan pa dar zhing rgyas pa dang / rgyal po nyi ma bcu
pa'i mchod gnas

dge slong lha chen pos chos log brtsams pa 'gog pa'i phyir du brtsams pa dang bdun no/ /de ltar bka' bsdu gnyis po'i dus su/ ston pas gsung tshad kyi sde snod rnams mi brjed
pa'i gzungs thob cing / mngon par shes pa dang ldan pa'i dgra bcom pa rnams tshogs nas dran bsdur zhu dag ma nor bar byas pa yin gyis/ po ti glegs bam dang yi ger bkod
pa ni tshig 'bru gcig kyang med par bzhed do/ /bka' bsdu gsum pa'i don bdun ni/ dus ni sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas lo gsum brgya lon nas/ gnas shrI dza lan dha ra'i
gtsug lag khang /sbyin bdag rgyal po ki na la/ tshogs pa dgra bcom pa lnga brgya/ byang chub sems dpa' lnga brgya/ so so skye bo'i paNDi ta khri drug stong rnams so/ /gang
zag dgra bcom pa pur ni kas gsol ba btab nas/ skye ba tha ma'i byang chub sems dpa' su mu tri ta'i thugs rgyud las so/ /dngos po ni sde snod gsum mo/ /dgos pa ni sangs
rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas par bya ba'i phyir dang / rgyal ba'i bka' la phyi rabs kyi gang zag rnams kyis lhag chad nor 'khrul du
'don pa dang / sgo skur spangs pa'i phyir dag par bsdus pa dang bdun no/ /bka' bsdu gsum pa de'i dus su/ sde snod gsum la gtogs tshad thams cad gzhung du bkod cing / bka'
shog tu btab nas bam po dang / le'u rnams grangs gsal bar byas pa'o/ /bka' bsdu rim pa gsum po 'di ni theg pa chung ngu'i bsdu'o/ /

chen po'i bka' bsdu ba ni/ rgyal po'i khab kyi lho phyogs/ bi ma la swa bha wa zhes bya ba'i ri la/ rgyal sras 'bum phrag bcu 'dus te/ 'jam dpal gyis mngon pa/ byams pas 'dul
ba/ phyag rdor gyis mdo sde rnams bsdus zhes grags shing / gsang sngags kyi chos rnams ni/ ston pas lung bstan pa bzhin rgyal po dza'i khang steng du byin gyis brlabs
pa las/ char ltar 'bebs par byed do/ /sde snod gsum po'i bka' bsdu tshar na'ang / thams cad po ti glegs bam la bkod pa'i skabs su/ lha ma srin sde brgyad pos gsungs rab kyi
zhabs tog dang / bdag 'dzin la ma 'chams par thob khyer byas pas/ khri brgyad stong pa lhas thob/ shes rab khri pa lha mi gnyis/ nyi khri mis/ lang kar gshegs pa srin
pos/ tog gzungs bdud kyi/ gzungs ma mos/ 'bum klus thob ste/ khyab 'jug skal ba chad pas/ khos 'thab rtsod byas nas gzhan thams cad mi yul du lus/ 'bum klu'i yul nas ma lon
pa'i skabs su/ klu'i rgyal po shAkya bya ba nad tsi tsi dzwa las thebs pa sus kyang 'chos ma thub ste/ sman pa 'tsho byed gzhon nu'i bu/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis bcos
pa'i gtang rags la/ 'bum phul nas mi yul rgya gar lho phyogs su rim par dar te/ rgya mo tsha ba rong du slebs pa chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi rlangs khams pa ga
cha gdan 'dren du btang bas/ bsam yas su phebs nas/ bod khams spyi khyab tu dar zhing rgyas par gyur pas rgyas pa 'bum zhes grags so/ /'bum la sho lo ka 'bum yod pas 'bum
zhes zer cing / le'u bdun cu rtsa gnyis bam po gsum brgya/ shad bzhi khri bzhi 'bum/ tsheg bye ba bzhi khri yod/ gzhan yang bka' thams cad la

'di bzhin gyi rgyas btab yod cing / mdor na skabs chen brgyad/ skabs chung bdun cu tham pa ni/ rgyas pa 'bum nas bsdus pa yi ge gcig ma yan la tshang ngo / /'bum bod yul du
sgyur ba po snga ma ni/ mkhas pa bai ro tsa na yin no/ /da lta sho lo ka 'bum ma tshang ba ni/ mtha' dum klu'i yul du lus par byed na'ang / chos nyid mi 'gyur ba'i le'us
'jug bsdus pas/ don la tshang bar ka cog zhang gsum la sogs la paN mkhas pa thams cad bzhed pa mthun no/ /yang 'bum sde lngar grags pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i
'bum ni/ rgyas pa 'bum la zer te/ zab cing rgya che ba sho lo ka 'bum yod pas 'bum zhes bya'o/ /dkon brtsegs la smon lam 'bum yod pas 'bum zhes bya/ phal po che na sangs
rgyas kyi mtshan 'bum yod pas 'bum zhes bya'o/ /mtshan dgu brgya ma tshang ba 'phags pa glang ru lung bstan na yod pas tshang ngo / /lang kar gshegs pa'i mdo na/ srin
po 'dul ba'i rnam grangs 'bum yod pas 'bum zhes bya'o/ /mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'bum ni/ ston pa mya ngan las 'da' khar zhal chems gsungs pa 'bum yod pas 'bum zhes bya ba
rnams so/ /gsungs rab yan lag bcu gnyis ni/ brgyad stong 'grel pa snying po don mchog las/ mdo sde dbyangs snyad lung du bstan/ /tshigs bcad mchod brjod gleng gzhi dang /
/rtogs brjod de lta bu byung dang / /skyes rabs shin du rgyas pa dang / /rmad byung gtan la phab pa dang / /gsung rab yan lag bcu gnyis yin/ /bka' bsdu gsum pa dgos pa'i
nyer len ni/ de'i dus na nyan thos

dge 'dun gyi tshogs thams cad/ ston pa sangs rgyas kyi rjes su slob par 'dod pa mthun cing / lta ba ma log pa sha stag yin na'ang / gang zag dbang po rab 'bring mtha' gsum
gyis/ ston pas gsungs pa'i drang don/ nges don/ ldem dgongs la sogs rnams la dgongs yul tha dad du bzung / de'i tshig gi phyogs la zhen nas/ so sor gyes pas sde pa bco brgyad
du grags pa byung ba de dus dge 'dun la 'gyed pa'i phyir rtsod pa byung ba ste/ gzhi yod par smra ba tshang la sde pa re re bzhin/ nged kyi 'di bka' dngos can yin gyi
gzhan ma rnams de ltar ma yin no zer ba sogs kyi rtsod pa byung ngo / /de la yang rtsa ba'i sde pa bzhi/ de las gyes pa'i bco brgyad yod de/ rtsa ba bzhi ni/ thams cad
yod par smra ba/ phal chen pa/ mang pos bkur ba/ gnas brtan pa'i sde ba dang bzhi'o/ /thams cad yod smra ba la gyes pa bdun ni/ gzhi kun pa'i sde ba/ 'od srung pa'i/ sa ston
pa'i/ chos srung pa'i/ gos dmar can/ rnam par phye te smra ba/ mang du thos pa la sbyangs pa'i sde pa rnams so/ /paNDi ta dha na shI las/ sde pa tha dad klog pa'i 'khor
lo las/ gzhi kun pa dang 'od srung sde/ /sa ston sde dang chos srung sde/ /mang thos gos dmar slob ma'i sde/ /rnam par phye te smra ba'i sde/ /thams cad yod par smra ba
yin zhis gsungs/ de dag gi skad ni/ saM skri ta'i chos ston no/ /rigs rgyal rigs/ sras sgra gcan 'dzin gyi slob rgyud/ bslab pa la gus pa'i mchog go /mkho ba'i yo byed
bcu gsum ni/ snam sbyar/ bla gos/ mthang gos/ sham thabs/ sham thabs kyi gzan/ rngul gzan/ de'i yang

gzan/ yang na/ khrus zo/ gdong phyis/ rnag gzan/ g.yan pa dgab pa/ skra bzed/ gding ba/ dbyar gyi gos ras chen dang bcu gsum mo/ /de la snam sbyar ni rab kyi rab la snam phran
nyer lnga 'bring la nyer gsum/ /tha ma la nyer gcig glegs bu phyed lnga'o/ /'bring gi gsum po la snam phran bcu dgu/ bcu bdun/ bco lnga/ glegs bu phyed dang bzhi'o/ /tha
ma'i gsum po la snam phran bcu gsum bcu gcig dgu pa'o/ /glegs bu phyed dang gsum pa'o/ /yod smra ba la rtags/ utpal la/ rin po che/ shing lo ris/ 'khor lo'am/ padma'o/
/phal chen sde pa la gyes pa lnga ni/ shar gyi ri la gnas pa/ nub kyi ri la/ gangs kyi ri la/ 'jig rten las 'das par smra ba/ rnam par brtags te smra ba'i sde pa rnams
so/ /zhes gsungs so/ /shar nub ri dang gangs rir gnas/ /'jig rten 'das par smra ba dang / /rtag par smra ba'i sde pa ste/ lnga tshan dge 'dun phal chen pa zhes gsungs/ phal
chen pa ni/ skad pra kr-i ta rang bzhin gyi skad/ rigs bram ze/ 'phags pa 'od srung gi slob rgyud/ sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa'i mchog go/ snam sbyar 'dra/ rtags
dpal be'am/ g.yung drung ris so/ /mang pos bkur ba la gyes pa gsum ni/ sa sgrog rigs kyi sde/ srung ba po'i sde/ gnas ma bu'i sde rnams so/ /sa sgrog rigs dang chen srung
ba pa/ /gnas ma bu yi sde rnams ni/ /kun gyi bkur ba rnams pa gsum/ /zhes gsungs so/ /skad be sha tri tas ston/ zur chag gi skad/ rigs 'breg mkhan/ 'phags pa nye bar 'khor
gyi slob rgyud/ 'dul ba 'dzin pa'i mchog go/ snam

sbyar 'dra/ rtags dung ngo / /gnas brtan pa'i sde pa las gyes pa gsum ni/ gtsug lag khang chen po'i sde pa/ rgyal byed tshal na gnas pa'i sde pa/ 'jig med ri la gnas pa'i sde
pa rnams so/ /de nyid las/ rgyal byed tshal gnas 'jig med gnas/ /gtsug lag khang chen gnas brtan pa/ /zhes gsungs so/ /skad a ba bhraM sha tas ston no sha za'i skad/ rigs
brag gor sde'i gdol ba/ ka tyA ya na'i slob rgyud/ mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i mchog snam sbyar 'dra/ rtags bum pa'o/ /de rnams kyi log rtog dgag cing / gcig gis gcig la chos
ma yin zer ba bsal ba'i phyir du/ bsdu ba gsum pa mdzad pa yin te/ thub pa'i bstan pa la sde pa bco brgyad du gyes pa yong ba'i snga ltas/ sngon rgyal po kri kri'i rmi
lam du byung ba/ sangs rgyas 'od srung la zhus pas ma 'ongs pa na/ 'di ltar 'byung ngo zhes lung bstan pa yod do/ /rmi ltas bcu ni glang gnyis/ sprel gnyis/ khron/ chu che/
ldum ra/ tsan dan/ 'thab ras/ kri kri'i rmi lam bcu yin/ spyir chos thams cad bsdu na/ bka' bstan bcos gnyis su 'dus te/ dbyig gnyen gyis rnam bshad rig pa las/ chos
rnams thams cad mdor bsdus na bka' dang bstan bcos gnyis su 'dus te/ /legs par gsungs dang de yi dgongs 'grel dang / /de yi dbang gis shAkya'i bstan pa 'di/ /'jig rten khams
'dir yun ring gnas par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs la/ bka' dang bstan bcos kyi khyad par ni/ ston pa bzhugs pa'i zhal nas gsungs pa dang / cho 'phrul gyi chos kyi sgra bsgrags
pa thams cad ston pa'i bka' yin no/ /ston pa gshegs nas da lta'i bar la mdzad pa thams cad

bstan bcos yin no/ /ston pa rang gi dngos su gsungs pa dang 'jam dpal mtshan brjod la sogs pa rnams ni/ zhal nas gsung pa'i bka'o/ /gang zag gzhan bskul nas gsungs pa rnams
ni byin gyis brlabs pa'i bka'o/ /mdo'i gleng gzhi dang / chos kyi sdom dang / bka' bsdu gyis shig gsungs pa rnams/ rjes su gnang ba'i bka'o/ /sher snying la bka' gsum ga
tshang bar byed pa ni/ zab pa'i phyir ro/ /de ltar na/ bka' gsum po 'chad par 'dod na/ ston pa dang 'khor dang / gnas dang chos dang / dus dang / phun sum tshogs pa lnga'i
sgo nas 'chad pa yin na no/ /bka' phal che ba'i zhu ba po brgyad ni/ sha ri'i bu/ rab 'byor/ kau shi ka ste brgya byin/ byams pa/ 'od srung / gang po/ gang gA'i lha mo/
kun dga' bo rnams so/ /bstan bcos rtsom pa snga ba la rgya gar du/ bka' bsdu gsum pa'i dus su tshogs pa rnams zhal mthun par bye brag bshad mdzod chen mo bya ba rtsom pa/
phal che ba bod du ma 'gyur bar byed do/ /bstan bcos 'chad par 'dod na/ don rnam pa gnyis te/ lo rgyus kyi don dang / dngos gzhi'i don no/ /dang po la bka' dang bstan
bcos gang la bshad nyan byed kyang / bar chad gnyis spong rgyu ni/ lung dang mngon par rtogs pa'i bar chad do/ /'du shes bzhi sgom pa ni/ 'phel bar byed pa longs spyod kyi
'du shes sgom pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i nad zhi bar byed pa sman pa'i 'du shes dang / dgos 'dod 'byung ba yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i 'du shes dang / mi zad pa'i don 'byung
bas na/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'du shes bsgoms pa'i ngang nas/ 'chad pa dang nyan par bya'o/ /dman

pa'ii chos kyi sgor zhugs nas sa lam rim kyi bgrod/ rgyu'i sdom pa gsum gyi rnam grangs ni/ dang po so sor thar pa'i sdom pa/ nyan thos kyi dge slong gi 'dul khrims nyis brgya
lnga bcu rtsa gsum la/ sdom tshig ltung ba sde lnga bya ba gsungs ste/ sdom pa gcod par byed pa pham pa'i sde bzhi/ gsol ba dge 'dun la rag las pas/ dge 'dun lhag ma'i
sde bcu gsum/ ma mthol ma bshags ngan song du skyur ba spangs ltung gi sde sum cu/ ltung byed 'ba' zhig pa dgu bcu/ mthol zhing bshags pa la ming gi btags pa so sor bshags
pa bzhi/ chos phun sum tshogs pa la bslab cing goms par byed pa bslab bya nyes byas kyi sde la/ brgya dang bcu gnyis/ dril bas 'dul khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum
yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa la/ smon pa sems bskyed dang / 'jug pa sems bskyed gnyis/ gsang sngags kyi dam tshig ni/ gsang sngags nang pa/ theg chen bla med pa/
a ti yo ga rnams la dam tshig sa ma ya 'bum sde'i rgyud nas bshad pa ltar na/ dam tshig phra rags bsrung rgyu 'bum phrag gcig go/ nyan thos dge 'dun gyi tshogs rnams la
mig gi 'bras bu ltar bcas pa'i bslab pa gsum ni/ lhag pa tshul khrims gyis bslab pa dang / lhag pa byang sems la bstan pa'i bslab pa dang / lhag pa shes rab kyi bslab pa
dang gsum mo/ /bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po la gsum te/ sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po dang / tshul khrims las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po
dang / sgom pa

las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po dang gsum mo/ /sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas lo brgya dang bcu skor na/ chos rgyal mya ngan med ces bya bas/ 'dzam bu gling mtha'
dag gi rgyal po byas so/ /de nas rim gyis rgyal sar/ tsandra bdun byung ba ni/ ha ri tsandra/ shrI tsandra/ a khe tsandra/ dharma tsandra/ karma tsandra/ bi kra ma tsandra/
ga mi tsandra rnams so/ /go mi ni dza lan dha ra'i slob ma yin cing / de'i phyag rgya mo klu mo gcig gi nub re la rgyal bu re zos pas/ klu ma de rgyal po go mi las
btul lo/ /de nas rgyal sar pA la bdun byung ste/ go pA la/ dharma pA la/ bi kh'a pA la/ ra ma pA la/ hi ma pA la/ mo pA la/ ne pA la rnams so/ /ne pA la'i dus su blon pos
ngo log byas nas/ pA la'i bang so nub bo/ /de nas se na bzhi byung ste/ ba na se na/ ke pa se na/ ma ni tra se na/ ma hwan se na'o/ /tsandra bdun dang / pA la bdun/ lha
mo tsuddhas byin pa'i dngos grub yin no/ /pA la na bdun po'i ring la/ mkhas grub thams cad byon no/ /dharma pA la rgya gar na bzhugs dus/ bod na rgyal po sad na legs mjing
yon yod par/ yar klungs bang so'i rdo ring la yi ge yod ces grub thob u rgyan pas bris 'dug go/ mi mjed 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa/
lo lnga stong lnga brgya gnas rgyu dang / sku tshes dgung lo brgya thub rgyu/ skye dgu'i bdag mo sogs bud med rab tu byung ba'i skyon gyis/ bstan pa lo lnga brgya dang
/ sku tshe lo nyi shu bri bas ston pa dgung lo brgyad cu la gshegs shing / bstan pa lo lnga stong du nub par bshad la/ lnga stong gi steng nas sngar lo du 'das/ da lo grangs
ji tsam yod brtsi ba ni/ chos rje sa skya pas bzhed pa ltar/ thub pa sa pho 'brug lo

bar byas pa'i lugs kyi/ de nas chu pho khyi lo la ti shri kun blo ba/ bod du bsnyen par rdzogs par byon pa'i lo yan la/ lo sum stong bzhi brgya lnga bcu rtsa lnga 'das/ rtsa
drug pa'i steng na yod cing / da lo stong dang lnga brgya bzhi bcu zhe lnga lhag mar yod ces gsung 'dug pa/ lhag ma de'i steng nas yang / da lan shing pho stag lo/ srog
rme rgya gar dbus na yod pa 'di yan la lo brgya dang nyi shu rtsa dgu song 'dug pa/ yar rgyab pas sngar 'das kun dril/ lo sum stong lnga brgya brgyad cu gya lnga song /
gya lnga ba'i steng na yod cing 'bras bu dang / sgrub pa dang /lung gi dus dang / mngon pa'i dus rnams/ mdo sde'i steng nas kyang lo brgyad cu gya bzhi tsam song bas na/
da bstan pa dngos la/ mdo sde'i lo bzhi brgya bcu drug dang / 'dul ba'i lo lnga brgya yod cing / der steng rtags tsam 'dzin pa lnga brgya rnams dril bas/ lo stong dang bzhi
brgya bcu drug yod par/ mkhas pa rnams bzhed do/ /byams mgon gyi sprul pa dang / bstan pa dngos ji tsam la 'byon ni/ yong su grags par/ tshe lo bcu pa'i las kyi 'bras
bu yongs su rdzogs pa'i skabs su/ mi gzhan las lus gzugs dang gzi brjid che ba yod pas/ de byams pa'i sprul par byon pa byed cing / de nas tshe lo yar 'phel ste/ brgyad khri'i
bar du'o/ /zhes bshad cing / byams pa mgon po'i bstan pa dngos ni/ 'dul ba tsandra gar bha dang / 'dul ba dar ma bya bar sangs rgyas kyi lung bstan yod pa/ tsandra
gar bha'i nang na/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo bye ba phrag lnga bcu rtsa bdun song ba dang / rgyal ba byams pa mgon po 'jig

rten du sems can gyi don la 'byon par gsungs so/ /mdo sde bskal bzang las/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshogs can gtso bo zhes pa/ yab yum sras rim gro ba mchog gnyis la sogs cha tshang
ba la/ sku tshe'i tshad ni nyi ma gcig ste/ de'i bar la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bcu gnyis rdzogs par bshad cing/ dam pa'i chos ni lo dung phyur phrag bzhi dang / bye
ba phrag drug gi bar du gnas par bshad do/ / / /

'phags yul bal po'i rgyal rabs bzhugs/ na mo arya mai tri ye/ byams dang thugs rjes srid gsum 'gro ba yi/ /mgon gyur sa bcu'i dbang phyug rab btud nas/ /de yi sprul pa bstan
pa rgyas mdzad cing / /li yul chags 'jig khrims gnyis gnas tshul bshad/ /li yul bal por grags pa 'dis/ sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa dang / bstan 'dzin gyi gang zag rgyal blon
ji ltar byon na/ ston pa shAkya thub pa 'gro ba'i don la sangs rgyas nas/ bzhugs pa'i pho grangs nyi shu rtsa gcig yod pa'i/ rting ma de li yul 'di yin pas/ gzhan las
kyang yon tan lhag par che/ sngon sangs rgyas 'od srung 'jig rten du byon dus/ li yul 'di la tsan dan gyi yul zer dam chos shin du dar ro/ /'od srung mya ngan las 'das nas/
de'i sku gdung bzhugs pa'i mchod rten go ma sa la ghan dha phyi bstan du bzhengs shing / de'i nang na 'od srung gi sku gdungs yang ril po gcig tu bzhugs par byed la/
da lta ni 'phags pa shing kun gyi mchod rten zhes grags par byed do/ /drang srong rnams nam mkha' la 'phags nas yul gzhan du 'byon/ de rting bstan pa nub pas li yul mtshor
gyur to/ /de nas yun ring po zhig nas sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa rgya gar du byon/ 'gro don mdzad nas mya ngan las 'da' bar nye ba na/ yul khams so so srung ma so so la
gtad pa'i tshe/ li yul yang / rnam sras dang / yang dag gshed la

sogs pa la gtad nas ston pa nyid rang yang / 'khor mang po dang bcas nas nam mkha' la lding nas li yul mtshor gyur pa der byon/ da lta yang chu bo shel chab gong ma'i 'gram/
ghung tir gyi mchod rten gyi thad/ steng gi nam mkha' la padma'i gdan la bzhugs nas/ byin gyis brlabs 'od zer bskyed nas phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas byang sems rnams kyi 'od
zer ston pa'i dbu la thims/ dge'o zhes pa'i sgra byung ngo / /de nas phyir bstan pa 'byung ba'i rnam 'phrul dang lung bstan mang du mdzad cing / sha ri'i bu'i gseg shang
gi rtsa ba dang / rnam thos kyi bu'i mdung thung gis mang pa ba ra na/ pa ra ba ta zhes pas/ ri rnag gi kha dog 'dra bar/ mtsho 'di dbrol la gying sham gtsang po la pho
zhig zhes bka' bstsal pa bzhin byas pas/ ston pa nyid kyang glang mgo ri'i steng/ sku gzugs chen po bzhugs pa'i g.yon logs kyi lha khang na/ da ltar mchod rten chung ngu
gcig yod par dgung zhag bdun bar la bzhugs/ kun dga' bos sngar gyi rgyu rkyen de rnams ci lags zhus pas/ mtsho dbral ba las chu skam nas nga mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'og
tu 'dir li yul bya ba 'byung ste/ 'u than gyi mkhar grong lnga ldan zhes pa'i chen po gcig dang / de srung ba'i rA dza gra ma'i dus sangs rgyas kyi sku gzugs tsan dan gyi
nang du/ sku'i grib ma rang la nub pa zhig rgya gar nas byon/theg pa chen po la spyod pa'i dge slong pho mo gnas pa'i gtsug lag khang sum brgya drug cu rtsa gsum rgyal blon
dad pa can gyi bzhengs pa nas/ sku gdung la mchod pa'i byang sems dge slong pho mo dang / khyim pa skye bo'i tshul du gnas pa phyed ma'i lnga brgya rtag tu gnas so/ /gzhan
yang phyir mi ldog pa'i byang sems/ theg pa

chen po la spyod pa phal cher gnas ste/ 'di ni dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing khud pa yin no gsungs/ srung ma rnams la bka' bgos te gtad do/ /der mtsho pho ba dang / 'od
srung kyi mchod rten phyi rten chen mo dang / ri glang ru mkhar dge ba'i shul rnams mngon par gyur to/ /de nas/ sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas lo nyis brgya lnga bcu
rtsa bzhi lon pa'i dus su/ rgya gar gyi rgyal po chos rgyal mya ngan med yin dharma a sho kas/ sdig chen chos byed pa slar bshags sngom byas/ 'dzam bu'i gling du gtsug lag
khang dang / mchod rten brgyad khri bzhi stong bzhengs par dam bcas pa'i tshe/ mtsho bskams li yul stong par 'dug pas/ der 'ongs da lta 'u than gyi sku mkhar yod sar nub
gcig bzhugs pas/ rgyal po'i btsun mo dam pa la btsun mo de skyed mos tshal du khrus phyed dus/ rnam sras nam mkha' la gshegs pa yar mar gnyis kas gzigs/ sems chags pa
las byung ba'i ba'i bur byed do khye'u gcig btsas pas/ mtshan mkhan na re/ 'di ni mtshan bzang dbang thang che bas yab sku ma 'phos pa la rgyal srid byed par mchis so zer
bas/ rgyal po khros nas bu 'di ni nga la mi dgos kyi bor gcig zer ba ltar bor bas/ bu chung rang gi bsod nams las/ sa las nu ma gcig byung ba nus pas gsos skyed che bar
byung ngo / /de'i skabs su rgya nag gi rgyal po/ ce'u wang zhes pa'i byang sems kyis sprul pa/ bu stong la dbang sgyur/ dgu brgya dgu bcu rtsa dgu yod pa cig byung ba/ de'i
bsam pa la/ nga la bu gcig byung na sangs rgyas kyi zhabs kyi bcags pa'i li yul zhes bya ba bzang po gcig yod 'dug pa de 'dzin du 'jug snyam nas/ rnam sras la gsol ba
btabs pas/ sa la nu blangs nas 'di ni nga'i bu yin

pas khyod la sbyin par bya'o zer nas byin/ ming yang rgyal po sa las nur btags/ de cher skyes pa dang li yul 'tshol ba la rgya rjes brdzangs/ dmag stong phrag bcu dang bcas
te nub phyogs su phyin/ li yul me dkar du slebs pa'i dus su/ rgya gar du rgyal po dharma ko kas/ blon po yakSha bya ba la nyes phab nas/ de spun pha khu nye 'khor dang bcas
pa bdun brgya tsam spyugs/ shar phyogs su yul 'tshol ba la yong / 'u than gyi shel chab gong ma na yod pa dang / sa la nu'i 'khor gnyis/ ba sbrum ma bros pa 'tshol du
'ong ba dang 'phrad/ rgyu mtshan bsnyad pas/ nged gnyis sngar nas rgyal blon gyi rgyud du 'dug pa/ da'ang rje 'bangs byed par rigs la/ 'u than gyi gzhong 'dir yul sar bzung
bar bya'o zer nas/ ko nya'i 'og yul hang mu dze bya bar mjal/ rgyal blon byed par bshams pas/ sngan ma yul bgos la ma 'chams/ rnam sras dang dpal lha mos sdum byas te/
'u than shel chu gong ma man chad/ rdol me skar dang / skam sha yan chad sa la nur 'khor rgya nag pa la phye/ shel chu gong ma yan chad/ ko shel man chad yakSha'i 'khor
rgya gar pa la phye/ shel chu'i dbus ni rgyal bu rang rgya dkar nag gi blon 'bangs/ stod rim 'dres ma dang bcas pas bzung te/ yul btab mkhar rtsig rgya dkar nag 'phrad pa'i
dbu ni yin te/ skad ni gnyis ka mthun/ li skad thog ma 'jam dpal/ dge slong bai ro tsa nar sprul nas/ byis pa la bslab pas 'phags pa'i gsungs las chad pa/ yi ge dang
chos lugs ni rgya gar ba dang shas cher mthun la/ 'jig rten pa'i lugs ni rgya nag pa dang shas cher mthun no/ /sangs rgyas 'das nas rgyal po sa la nu lo bcu dgu pas li rje

byas pa yan la lo nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa bzhi song zhing / rgyal po sa la nu dang / blon po yakSha ni li'i rgyal blon gyi thog ma'o/ /de nas sa la nu'i bu/ rgyal po ji dza
ya sam bha wa byung ba/ rgyal sar zhugs nas lo lnga song ba dang / li yul du chos kyi thog ma byung ste/ de yang byams pa rgyal po dza ya dang / 'jam dpal dang 'phags pa
bai ro tsa nar sprul nas/ sngon la phyugs rdzi byas pa la/ skad dang yi ge bslabs/ de nas dam chos dbu brnyes rim par byung ngo / /rgyal po des tsar ma'i gtsug lag khang
bzhengs/ de'i nang na klu rgyal hu lor gyis kha che nas nam mkha' la spyan drangs pa'i mchod rten byin rlabs can yang bzhugs la/ li yul du gtsug lag khang dang / mchod
rten gyi thog ma'o/ /de nas rgyal rabs bdun gyi bar la/ gtsug lag khang mang du brtsigs so/ /byams pa rgyal po bi dza ya birya zhes par sprul nas/ bstan pa'i bya ba rgya
cher byas shing / ghung tir gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ mchod rten gong ma sa la ghandha'i bsngags pa brjod pas/ rgyal po dad de/ glang mgo ri'i steng du/ gyi'u shan gyi
gtsug lag khang bzhengs so/ /de nas rgyal rabs gnyis kyi bar la gtsug lag khang mang po brtsigs/ de rting rgyal po bi dza ya dzas/ ma zha'i mchod rten dang gtsug lag khang
bzhengs so/ /rgyal po de la sras gsum byung ba'i che ba 'don 'gros/ bar pa dar ma nan tir gnyis/ rgya gar du chos slob pa la byon/ chung ba bi dza ya dar mas rgyal srid
bzung / dpa' rtsal che zhing gsod pa la skye na pas sdig che/ phu bo dar ma nan tir gyis dgra bcom pa thob nas/ thabs kyi bdud btul/ sdig bshags byed du bcug te/ dro ldir
gyi gshongs na/ sngon thub pa chen pos rgyal

bu zla 'od du gyur tshe bram ze la dbu byin pa'i sa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhabs kyi bcags pa'i ghe'u to shan dang / bhod bha long kyi tshal du gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten
chen po re bzhengs so/ /gcen che ba 'don 'gros rgya gar nas phebs/ sku mched mjal bar/ 'ja' mo ka ko rong nga'i lha khang bzhengs shing / nor gtsang mas sang tir gyi
gtsug lag khang bzhengs so/ /de nas bi dza ya dar ma'i bu/ rgyal po bi dza ya seng has som nya'i gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten bzhengs/ de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya
kirtis pun nyo'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs nas/ ding sang bar du chu'i 'jigs pa klus bsrungs pa yod do/ /de'i bu ji dza ya sam tra las/ dgra bcom pa dznyA na yakSha'i bka'
bzhin du/ dar ma tir gyis gtsug lag khang dang / ghung shan gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs so/ /de'i bu bi dza ya seng has/ byams pa'i zhal mthong / gzha' gser ma'i gtsug lag
khang bzhengs so/ /de'i bu/ rgyal po ji dza ya pha la 'chang rgyal po rabs drug gi bar la/ gtsug lag khang gzhan ma brtsigs so/ /de nas rgyal po bi dza ya sa tra las/
sangs rgyas kyi sku gzugs bcu dgu khyer nas li yul du nam mkha' la byon byung ba bzhugs pa'i gtsang khang dang / bkra shis bsil ba'i tshal du mchod rten dang / dgra bcom
pa mu gu sdes/ a pa ya dhengs kyi bka' bzhin du/ gzha' sam ma'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs so/ /de'i bu rgyal po ji dza ya sha ta man chad/ rgyal rabs bzhi'i bar la gtsug lag
khang gsar pa ma brtsigs so/ /de nas rgyal po bi dza ya karti la/ klu'i rgyal pos bskul nas/ la bha ya nya'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa 'di ni bod rgyal pos li yul la mnga'
mdzad/ de'i blon pos

mgar stong btsan li yul du yong dus bzhengs so/ /rgyal po de dang sras bi dza ya gra ma bhad gnyis rgya yul la byon pa'i ring la/ li'i blon po a ma cha ge meg bya bas/ lo bcu
gnyis rgyal tshab byas/ de'i dus la nang sde'i mchod rten dang / gtsug lag khang bzhengs so/ /de nas rgyal po bi dza ya bhad/ li'i yul du slebs nas/ gyer zhig gre rma
bya ba'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs so/ /de'i 'og tu rgya'i ser thi shis/ bang mkhar du/ byams pa mi tri'i gtsug lag khang / rgya'i blon po ka thi shis/ khe gwan rtse'i gtsug
lag khang dang / sngon 'phags pa bai ro tsa nas/tsar ma'i tshal du phyugs rdzi la skad bslabs pas/ pu to nya'i mchod rten chen mo bzhengs/ rting la de zhig pa dang / rgyal
po bi ya ho han dang / rgya'i dge slong ba la shis/ sa der gtsug lag khang gcig bzhengs so/ /gzhan yang rgyal po na rim gyis btsun mos bzhengs pa dang / btsun mo'i slad
du gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa ni/ nu bo nya zhes bya ba'i gtsug lag khang dang / mo zo 'jo'i dang / ze ro 'jo'i dang / so yan sdo'i dang / 'go mo 'ja'i dang / bka' gro
mdzo'i dang / ho ron mdzo'i dang / so lon mdzo'i dang / yar lon no'i dang / kho bon no no'i dang / gu rai ma'i dang / a ko no'i dang / kus tsi or stong nag gi'i dang / ci
tu no'i dang / khye'o no'i dang / na mo bho thong gi dang / na 'ong yo nu'i gtsug lag khang bya ba sogs mang du bzhengs so/ /spyir 'u than na gtsug lag khang chen por brtsi
ba/ sku mkhar gyi phyi nang na/ drug cu rtsa brgyad/ 'bring dgu bcu rtsa lnga/ chung ngu brgya bzhi bcu zhe brgyad/ dgos tshos kyi lha khang chung ngu na dang / yon
bdag med pa'i lha khang dang / mchod rten chen po gsum stong drug brgya brgyad cu rtsa brgyad

bzhugs so/ /'u than na dge 'dun dgos tsho yan byin no/ /byi ba lo la brtsigs pas khri tsho gcig tsam bzhugs so/ /mdo lo dang me skar phyogs na/ gtsug lag khang chen po bzhi/
chung ngu na brgya lhag tsam dang / dge 'dun brgya nyi shu tsam bzhugs/ kam shang dang / pho nya dang / berga Da dang / o ku yan chad/ byi li man chad sku mkhar gyi nang
na gtsug lag khang chen po nyi shu rtsa gsum/ 'bring po nyi shu rtsa gcig chung ngu nyi shu rtsa gsum tsam dang / dgos tshos kyi lha khang mchod rten chung ngu la sogs/
brgyad brgya sum cu rtsa dgu tsam bzhugs/ dge 'dun sde gnyis ni/ las rkyen dang dgos tsho man chad na/ bzhi brgya sum cu rtsa brgyad bzhugs so/ /gyim kang man chad keM shang
dang / dur brgya yan sku mkhar gyi nang tshar ma yan na gtsug lag khang chen po bco lnga tsam dang / lha khang chung ngu dang mchod rten mang du bzhugs/ dge 'dun sde
