gnyis ni/ las rkyen dang / dgos mchod yin la/ spyir dgu brgya drug cu rtsa gsum tsam/ rgyal po sa la nu'i tsha bo/ rgyal po bi dza ya sam bha ba'i dus su/ rgya yul du chos
byung ba'i thog ma yin pa de nas rtsis lo bshol bor nas/ khyi lo ston zla tha chung yan la/ lo grangs ni stong dang nyis brgya lnga bcu tsam song 'dug go/ dang po rgyal
po sa nus rje byas nas/ bzang btsan bzang la btang / li rjer bskos pa yan la/ li'i rgyal rabs lnga bcu rtsa drug dang / phyag tshab gcig byung gda'o/ /li yul du rgyal rabs
bdun pa/ rgyal po ji dza ya kirti zhes pa'i ring la/ saM ka pa gra ha ma'i gtsug lag khang dang / nye ba'i lung pa/ saM ka na nyir bya ba na/ saM gha ba pa na zhes pa'i
dgra bcom pa gcig bzhugs te/ de'i slob ma ban de

zhig gis/ 'dul ba tsandra gar bha dang / 'dul ba dar ma sangs rgyas kyi lung bstan pa mthong nas/ dgra bcom pa la zhus pas/ thub pa mya ngan las 'das nas/ lo nyis stong gi
bar la/ li yul 'dir chos kyi gzugs brnyan dang / ring bsrel gnas par 'gyur te/ de nas nub par 'gyur zhing / li yul dang / shu lig a san gsum ga rgya dang / gdong dmar/ po
byi/ gru gu/ hor la sogs pas 'joms par byed do/ /de'i rjes la byang chub sems dpa' gcig gdong dmar gyi rgyal por skye ba blangs nas/ bod khams su dam chos 'byung zhing /
gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten brtsigs/ dge 'dun gyi sde 'dzugs/ rgyal blon rim gyi chos la sbyor/ yul khams gzhan gyi mkhan po dang / gsung rab mang po gdan 'dren/ li
yul 'di'ang bod kyi rgyal po de'i mnga' ris su dbang byed pa 'gyur ro/ /de nas gdong dmar du rgyal rabs bdun gyi bar la/ dam pa'i chos la spyod par 'gyur/ de'i tshe li
yul 'dir chos nub pa la nye ba'i tshe skabs su/ de'i rgyal po gzhon pa gcig chos la gnag pas/ li yul gyi dge 'dun bskrad pas tsar ma dang / 'bong dang / me skar/ ko nya'i
gtsug lag khang rnams su rim bzhin du bud nas/ gdong dmar gyi yul la kha bltas/ g.yag sgal can gyi lam sna byas pa ltar phyin/ bod yul mtshal gyi bya bar slebs/ de'i rgan
pas gdong dmar rgyal po la bsnyad pa dang / btsun mo byang sems sprul pa/ rgya'i kong jo zhig yod pa des/ li'i dge 'dun rnams gdan drangs/ sbyin bdag byas/ da dge 'dun
e yod byas pas/ de'i mkhan po na re/ an be dang / shu lig kha che rnams na mang po yod zer ba ltar/ de rnams kyang gdan drangs/ gtsug lag khang du bzhugs su bcug lo gsum
bzhir zhabs tog legs par

bsgrubs/ de dus kong jo la 'brum nad byung nas 'das/ gzhan yang mi mang rab shi bod blon rnams gros 'chams par/ lho bal gyi dge 'dun mkhan po rnams bos pas lan zer/ de rnams
kyi ban de bos pa rnams thams cad nub phyogs su bskrad/ de rnams ghan dha ra chen por chas nas 'gro ba la/ lam du klu'i rgyal po e la pa tras sbrul du sprul nas/ mtsho
la zam pa byas te bsgral bas sbrul shi dga' ldan du skyes mtsho yang bskams so/ /de'i dus bod yul na/ dge 'dun dang ring bsrel/ gsung rab/ mchod pa'i yo byad gcig kyang ma
lus pa bkal song ngo / /der 'dzam bu gling gi dge 'dun thams cad/ ghan dha ra chen por slebs/ de'i rgyal pos lo gnyis kyis bar la 'tsho ba sbyangs/ ci bde la so sor bzhag
go/ de'i mtshams su rgyal po de 'das/ de la bu gnyis yod pa'i chos la dad pa de/ ban des bskul nas ban des rgyal po byas pa/ blon 'bangs byin pos ban de'i rgyal po bsad/
dge 'dun byin po 'khyam du bcug pa / ke'u shA gyi'i rgyal pos spyan drangs te/ yul der 'dzam bu gling gi dge 'dun ril 'dus par gyur to/ /zhes gsungs so/ /sangs rgyas zhabs
bcags yul mchog lung bstan nas/ rgyal po sa nu blon po yakSha gnyis/ /las kyi bdas nas yul khams gsar du bzung / /sa nu tsha bo bi dza saM bha bas/ /byon ring byams
dang 'jam dbyangs sprul pa yis/ /li yul dam chos dar ba'i dbu brnyes nas/ /chos rgyal mang pos mchod rten gtsug lag khang / /brgya stong dpag med bzhengs pas bstan pa dar/
/dgra bcom pho mo lo paN mang du byon/ /sangs rgyas gshegs nas nyis brgya lnga bcu'i skor/ /chos byung the ba'i nyis stong lo yi bar/ /yul der thub bstan dri med byung
bar bshad/ /de nas da lta yan chod lta spyod

rnams/ /phyi nang 'dres ma shas cher phyi rol snang / /rgyal bas bsngags pa'i 'phags yul bal po yis/ /rgyal rabs bris pa'i rnam dkar dge ba des/ /slar yang 'phags pa'i yul
der chos dar zhing / /'gro kun byams pa mgon po'i sa thob shog/ //

blo ldan rgya nag gi rgyal rabs bzhugs so/ / na mo arya manydzu shrI ye/ blo gros mkhyen brtse'i 'od kyi 'gro kun gyis/ /blo ngan ma rig mthug po rab bsal nas/ /blo gsal spobs
pa'i snang ba mchog stsol ba'i/ /blo ldan 'jam dbyangs zhabs la gus btud nas/ /de yi zhing mchog ri bo rtse lnga zhes/ /de lta'i 'khor yug rgya nag thang gi yul/ /de
nyid bzung 'dzin rgyal rgyud byung tshul rnams/ /de'ang 'dir mdor bsdus don gsal 'bri bar bya/ rgya nag po'i yig tshang la/ ce hu wang zhes pa'i rgyal rabs bzhi pa/shing
pho rta lo la rgyal sar bton nas/ lo nyi shu rtsa gcig lon pa'i dus su/ shing pho stag lo zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad la/ rgya gar du bcom ldan 'das rgyal ba shAkya thub
pa rgyal bu don grub tu sprul nas sku 'khrungs/ de'i 'od dang cho 'phrul rnams rgya nag yul du'ang mthong bas/ rtsis byas dus/ sangs rgyas 'byon par shes shing / de'i bstan
pa rgya nag tu'ang 'ong bar 'dug zer/ rgyal bu don grub dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu par rab tu byung / sum cu so lnga la sangs rgyas/ de nas lo bdun 'das pa nas/ yum la
chos 'chad pa'i don la lha yul du byon/ zla ba gsum bzhugs/ de'i shul du rgyal po u Ta ya nas mo'u 'gal gyi bu la bskul nas/ lha'i yul du sangs rgyas kyi sku tshad/ tsan
dan go shirSha las bzhengs te mi yul du gdan drangs/ bcom ldan 'das lha las babs nas rgya

gar du phebs pa'i tshe/ tsan dan gyi sku de bzhengs nas dbu btud te spyi bor phyag bzhag nas ston pa mya ngan las 'das rting / la stong lon pa'i tshe/ sku 'dis rgya nag gi
yul du sems can gyi don byed par 'gyur ro/ /zhes lung bstan/ de nas lo sum cu so brgyad song ba'i dgung lo brgyad cu la mya ngan las 'das so/ / de nas chu mo phag la se chen
rgyal po rgyal sar phebs nas/ lo ngo phyed dang gsum 'gro dus brtsis pa yan la lo sum stong bzhi brgya bcu gsum song / tsan dan jo bo bzhengs nas lo sum stong bzhi brgya
lnga bcu rtsa lnga 'gro zer ba/ rgya'i tsan dan jo bo'i lo rgyus la yod par snang / chu mo phag nas tshal pa'i chos 'byung / me pho khyi lo la brtsis pa yan la/ lo brgya
dang bzhi bcu zhe bzhi 'gro bar 'dug de nas deng sang shing pho stag srog rme brgyad dkar dbus na yod pa'i gong dkar ba la skyes nas/ dbus gtsang bde dog chen mo langs
pa'i lo 'di yan la lo brgyad cu gya dgu song 'dug kun dril bas ston pa sa pho 'brug la 'khrungs nas/ da lan shing pho stag lo 'di yan la/ lo grangs sum stong lnga brgya
gya lnga song 'dug rgya nag tu ce'u la/ rgyal po sum cu so drug byung / lo brgyar srid bzung / de nas chin hri hwang gi rgyal po gnyis byung / de nas han ka'o dzung zhes
pa nas bzung ste/ rgyal rabs bcu bzhi byung / de nas blon po gcig gi ngo log byas nas/ lo bco brgyad rgyal sa bzung / phyis han gyi rgyud pa/ sle'u gong bus/ blon po ang
mang bsad nas/ des rgyal srid bzung ba la/ bu lnga byung ba'i chung ba la bu han min ti rgyal po byung / de dus paNDi ta dzu ha lam bya ba bden pa mthong ba gnyis kyi/ rgya
gar nas/ rta dkar po gcig la theg pa chung ngu'i

chos bkal nas/ rgya nag ho nan du pa'e ma si lha khang bzhengs/ chos bsgyur/ de phyin chad nas rgya nag tu/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar ba yin no/ /paNDi ta de gnyis kyi dgra
bcom pa thob nas/ rdzu 'phrul gyi gcig nam mkha' la 'phur nas/ rgya mtsho'i gling ka'u li dkar po'i rgyal khams zhes par song nas mya ngan las 'das/ gcig ni lha khang
de'i 'og tu 'gog pa'i ting nge 'dzin la zhugs nas/ byams mgon byon dus mjal nas mya ngan las 'da'o zer/ han gyi rgyal rabs nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa/ han hen ti'i rgyal po'i
blon po tsha'o tsha'o zer bas rgyal sa phrogs pa mi rgyud lngar rgyal po byas/ yang de'i blon po si ma zhes pas/ rgyal sa phrogs nas bzung / de sting he'u tsing gi rgyud
pa la/ tung cin zhi cin gnyis byung ba'i/ zhi cin gyi rgyal po'i dus su/ rgya gar paNDi ta rgas po gcig byung nas/ rgya gar dang ljang yul gyi bar rgyal khams chung ngu zhig
na/ sngon sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa sum cu rtsa gsum du byon dus bzhengs pa'i lha/ sangs rgyas dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i sku tshad jo bo shAkya mu ne dang / sangs rgyas
kyi ring bsrel dang / ku m'a ra zhes pa'i paNDi ta mkhas pa gcig rnams yod pa/ der rgyal khams chung bas/ 'gro don mi 'phel bar 'dug rgyal po khyed la stobs 'dug pas/ dmag
thongs la de rnams blangs na/ sems can mang po la phan par 'dug zer bas/ rgyal po de la blon po zhing gi phying sang zhig dang / chu mi dbyen gyi mi dpon zhig yod pa
las/ mi dpon la dmag khri tsho bzhi bcu thams pa bskur nas btang bas/ jo bo dang ring bsrel ngo bo dang / paNDi ta de 'das 'dug pa'i tshab la ku mA ra chung ba rnams gdan
drangs/ lam du paN chung des/ mkhas pa'i rnam

'phrul rim par ston no/ /bka' chems bka' khol ma nas/ rgya gar gyi rgyal po dharma pha la'i rting la/ mu stegs pa'i dmag gis shrI na lendra bcom/ bstan pa bsnubs pa'i dus su/
rgya nag rgyal po de ba rA dza la/ dmag grogs sbran pas/ de'i lam thon/ skyes kyi nor dngos bzang ba skur gyi/ de la brten nas/ phyi pa thul cig zer/ za 'og gi gos srubs
med pa'i ri mo can/ mtshon dang zong gi mi phig pa/ thugs kar dpal be'u yod pa zhig gi 'go byas pa'i/ skyes bzang po thengs gnyis bskur bas/ mu stegs thul/ lha chos dar
bar byung ba'i skyes lan la/ sangs rgyas dgung lo brgyad pa'i sku tshab dang / mdo za ma togastug po bkod pa/ chu klung gi mdo/ 'dul ba ko sha dge slong bzhi sde gcig dang
bcas pa dgos zer byung bas/ khong drin che bar yod zer nas bskur bas/ rgya nag tu phebs par byed do/ /mi dpon dmag dang bcas pas/ rgya yul du 'khor dus/ zhi cin rgyal
po sku gshegs/ rgyud chad nas/ sngar gyi ching sang des rgyal po byed kyin 'dug zer ba thos pas/ dmag dpon des rang gi dmag khri tsho bzhi po bsdus nas/ si chon dang / ci'u
mkhar nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i rgyal po byas so/ /dus phyis dmag dpon de'i rgyud pa'i lag nas/ ching sang rgyal pos jo bo ring bsrel paNDi ta rnams/ kiM shang hur gdan drangs/
bkur sti chen po byas/ paNDi ta de la btsun mo bcu yod pas/ dge 'dun rnams ma mos pas zhal du khab gsol nas dag snang sbyangs/ paNDi ta de'i slob ma ce'u hwa shang zhes
pa mkhas pa zhig byung ba de la'ang / paNDi ta zer/ de la rgyal po'i btsun mo che ba 'grogs pa la bstan nas/ ske bcad pa'i khrims phog mgo bo bregs pas khrag 'o mar byung
/ rang gi

lag pas/ mgo rang gi blangs pa ske thog tu sbyar nas/ gtsug lag khang du phyin/ 'khor mang po la las rgyu 'bras kyi chos bstan nas/ mgo bo rang gi pang du lhung nas/ tshe'i
dus byas so/ /ching sang gwa'i rgyal rgyud chad nas su'i dbyang di zer ba'i rgyal po pha bu gnyis byung / des mnga' 'og nas/ thang ka'u cung dzung zhes pa tha'e yang tha'i
hu'i gle'u shu si'i gle'u shu byed cing yod pa des/ ngo log nas/ rgyal sa phrogs te/ de ni thang gi rgyal po'i thog ma yin no/ /de la bu gsum yod pa'i/ 'bring po thang
tha'i dzung rgyal po'i dpung thang zam tshang zhes pa'i/ lo tsA ba slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi slob ma zhig gis/ rgya gar nas chos mang po bsgyur/ de yan la rgya la lo tsA
ba nyis brgya byung / de dus zon klu shrI zhes pa'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po zhig yod pa/ de ri mthon po'i zur nas g.yang la lhung ba/ lha bu zhig gis bar snang nas bzung
ste/ ma bsnad pa la/ de su yin dris pas/ bdag rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi bu gnyis pa yin/ nged spun gnyis kyi gsung rab yan lag bcu gnyis bsrung bar dam bcas pas/ bdag
'dul ba'i sde snod srung ba yin zer zhing / zon klu shrIs dang / thang zam tsang dang / ku mA ra chung ba rnams ci 'dra yin dris pa la/ lan btab pa yod/ thang tha'i dzung
gi sras mo/ su'i lan kong jo/ bod skad du/ mtsho nang gi padma zhes pa de/ bod du 'ong dus/ jo bo shAkya mu ne yang byon pa yin/ de nas da lta me pho khyi lo 'di yan la/
lo bdun brgya 'gro zhes pa rgya'i deb ther rnying pa las/ dzaM bha la sogs shrI mgon gi mthong ba/ lha sa'i gtsug lag khang na yi ger 'dug pa mthong nas bris pa yin no/
/thang shu thu hwan zhes rgya'i deb ther las thang ka'u dzung rgyal pos/ sa pho stag

la rgyal sa bzung / lo dgu rgyal srid bskyangs/ bdun cu la 'das/ de'i bu thang tha'i dzung gis shing pho rta la/ bod kyi rgyal po dang grogs po byas/ skyes skur res byas/ rgya
bod 'brel ba'i sngon ma yin no/ /thang gi bu mo slong ba la/ bod rgyal srong btsan sgam pos/ gser gyi khrab bskur btang bas ma byin pa la/ bod dmag 'bum phrag gnyis khyer
nas/ thu yus hun bcom te bzung / dmag rnams phyir ldog de'i rting yun ring po nas/ bod kyi blon po mgar stong btsan la gser stong tsho lnga dang / rin po che'i rigs
mang po bskur nas/ bu mo slong ba la btang bas/ tha'i dzung gi sras mo/ wun shing kong jo lcags mo bya la byin nas/ pA'i hwa nas skyel mi dang / bsu mi 'dzoms bod yul du
slebs/ kong jos rgyal po la zhus nas/ bod na sngar yig tshang med pa la/ yig tshang bcas blon po mgar la thang gi rgyal po mnyes nas/ tsha mo kong jo zhig dang / g.yi'u g.yu
tha'i jung kun zhes pa'i ming byin/ bod la rgya'i las ka byin pa'i sngon ma yin no/ /tha'i dzung gis rgya gar du/ ma ga ta bcom/ de thos nas/ bod rgyal pos ma ga ta bcom
zer ro/ /thang tha'i dzung gi me pho byi lo nas/ lo nyer gsum rgyal sa bzung / lnga bcu nga gnyis pa sa mo bya lo zla ba bzhi pa la 'das zer/ de'i bu dgu pa cha'i ko'u
dzung gyol sar bton/ bod rgyal srong btsan sgam po la/ las ka sngar rting gnyis byin pas/ dang po/ hU ma du da wi si'i ha'i thun dbang / zhes pa dang / rting ma tshung
dbang bya ba yin/ bod yul du sngar med pa'i dar gyi 'bu dang / 'bras chang dang / shel bzo ba sogs/ bzo rigs pa mang po btang / der rting

bod rgyal mang srong gi dus su/ rgya bod gnyis/ re 'ga' mthun/ re 'ga' dmag 'khrug rtsod pa mang du byung / rgya'i blon po/ dpya zhin gus la dmag khri tsho bcu skur nas/ lha
sa'i bar du slebs pa/ bod kyi blon po/ mgar gyi bu che ba'i dmag dpon byas/ rgya dmag thams cad pham par byas/ chi ko'u dzung gi sa mo bya nas lo sum cu so bzhi srid bzung
/ lnga bcu nga drug chu mo lug la 'das/ sngar tha'i dzung gi btsun mo'i 'khor na yod pa zhig tha'i dzung 'das nas ban mor yod pa la babs nas/ ko'u dzung gi btsun mo byas
pa la/ bu dzu dzung dang / wi dzung dang / bu mo tha'i phing dang / gsum yod pa las/ rgyal pos bu che ba la rgyal sa skos zer ba'i kha chems yod kyang ma nyan par/ mo
rang gis rgyal mo byas/ rus wu yin pas/ wu dzi than zhes bya'o/ /rgyal mo des dmag khyer nas/ bod la song ba'i rgyal khams mang po phrogs/ de dus bod rgyal 'dus srong mang
po rje gzhon rin la blon po mgar gyi bu spun tsha bo dang bcas pa nas dbang ches/ phyis rgyal pos skyon yong bar go nas/ mgar gyi bu che ba lceb nas shi nu bos gcen po'i
bu tsha bo mang po rje dmag dang bcas pa khyer/ rgya'i rgyal mo la ngo bltas pas/ kun de khun dbang zhes pa byin nas blon por bskos/ tsha bo mang po rje la g.yon phyogs
dpa' bo/ dza'u ling ti tsang kun ngan gu'i gung zhes pa'i ming byin/ kho gnyis la phyis nyes pa byas kyang / skyon med pa'i rtags la lcags kyi yi ge byin pa'o/ /rgyal mo
wu ji than gyis shing pho spre'u lo nas lo nyi shu rtsa gcig rgyal sa byas/ brgyad cu pa shing pho 'brug la 'das so/ /gtam rgyud gzhan la/ rgyal mo 'di la bu bong sna can
gcig skyes nas ngo tsha nas bsod du btang bas/ bod kyi blon po che ba gcig yod pa des phag tu nyar ra byas/ phyis mo rgas dus/ thang gi

rgyud med pas/ mos ming po wu san zhes pa la/ rgyal sar bsko rtsis kyi mi mang po tshogs pa la/ wu san bskos pa e 'thad/ skad ring bton pas/ su mi 'thad zer ba bsod pas/ rgyal
mos 'ja' sa byas pa las/ bod blon des wu san la nga bskos pa mi 'thad gyis shig byas/ skad byung dus kho bos de skad byas pa dang / bod blon des ral gri brgyab nas bsad/
de ci yin byas pas/ rgyal mo rang gi lung yin byas pas/ bya sa ma rnyed/ de nas mya ngan du gyur pa la/ blon po des bong sna can khyer nas yong nas rgyal sar bskos pa/
rgyal po bong sna can du grags pa de yin cing / bong sna sgrib phyir du gser gyi 'bag gcig sgron pas rgyal po gser zhal bya ba yang de nas byung bar byed do/ /ma bu 'di
gnyis kyi dur da lta khan rje'u yi byang phyogs na yod pa de yin zer/ rgyal mo 'di la bod rnams rgya'i 'a dzi rgan mo zer bar 'dug gtam rgyud 'di'i lugs la/ shing mo sbrul
la/ rgyal po rang bu dzu dzung rgyal sar bton/ bod kyi rgyal pos bu mo slong du byung ba la/ nu bo ji dzung dbang gi bu mo/ kim shing kong jo byon/ rdzongs par gser srang
khri tsho mang po dang / bzo rigs sna tshogs/ rol mo'i sgra'i rnam grangs du ma dang / mi nyag gi yul thams cad dang bcas pa byin no/ /dzu dzung rgyal pos lo drug srid
bskyangs/ lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa lcags pho byi ba la 'das/ lcags mo phag la kong jo'i pha/ wu dzung rgyal sar bskos/ lo bcu gnyis kyi bar la srid bskyangs/ lnga bcu rtsa
lnga ba chu pho?bo byi ba la 'das/ chu mo glang la dzi dzung gi bu gsum pa han dzung rgyal sar bskos/ de phan chad la thang gi rgyal khams bzung nas lo brgya dang bcu drug
song / han dzung gi lo bzhi bcu rgyal sar bsdad/ rgyal khams bde zhing 'jam par byung / bdun cu rtsa gsum pa lcags mo

bya la 'das/ me pho spre'u lo la han dzung gi bu gsum pa/ dzu dzung rgyal sar bton/de'i lo bod dmag 'ongs nas/ sman rtse'i wi ji'u la sogs mang du blangs nas bzung / phyis
ci'u mkhar nyi shu rtsa bzhi bod la shor/ dzu dzung gi rgyal srid lo bdun bzung / lnga bcu rtsa gcig chu pho stag la 'das/ lo de la de'i bu che ba tha'i dzung rgyal po rgyal
sar bskos/ chu mo yos la bod dmag byung nas/ tha'i dzung shel chur bros pa'i shul du/ rgyal po'i blon po ka'u his bod la ngo bltas/ bod dmag ki ma byang hur 'ong / thang
gi rgyal po ga'u dbang zhes pa bskos/ rgya'i lo ming spos/ 'ja' sa 'grems du bcug phyi'i rgyal po ga'u dbang bsad bod dmag rnams bton nas/ tha'i dzung gi rgyal sa lo
bdun bzung / lnga bcu lo pa me mo lug la 'das/ de'i bu che ba ding dzung / lcags pho spre'u yi lo la rgyal sar bton/ ding dzung bsam pa che bas/ lo mang po rgya bod 'khrug
pa ma byung / de dus rgya bod kyi tshigs/ mi nyag yul nas ha la shAn du byas/ bod kyi rgyal khams kyi mtshams ni/ nub tu lan ju/ wi ji'u/ wan je'u/ he'i ji'u/ shar du shing
kun/ lhor je'u dang / gyang nam gyi bar/ byang ni byang du te'i tu nas/ lho nub kyi bar dang / rma chu'i byang phyogs phan chad bod kyi sa char byas/ rgya'i sa mtha'
ni/ ke je'u/ phyogs than jing ha/ lu ju la shing hu/ hung ce'u/ thang ku/ si chon la tha'i tu ha/ tshun chad thang gi sa char byas/ sa mtshams kyi bar/ sug bcu dang / tsabye'u
dang / ha la shan/ tha tha ling rnams stong par bzhag nas/ gnyis kas mi 'dzin par byas/ phyis rgya bod 'khrug pa mang du byung zhing / me mo glang la bod kyi rgyal
po mu ne btsan po 'das/ de dzung gis rgyal sa lo nyi shu rtsa lnga bzung / drug cu rtsa bzhi pa shing mo bya la 'das/ de'i bu che ba/ shun dzung / lo de la rgyal sar

bskos/ rgyal po lo gcig byas/ bzhi cu rtsa drug pa me pho khyi la 'das/ de'i bu che ba hun dzung / lo de la rgyal sar bskos/ byi ba lo la 'das/ de'i bu mu dzung glang lo la
bskos de shed du/ lha sa'i thang du bod kyi blon po tshogs/ ban chen pos mna' tshig bton/ bden pa bdar/ thams cad gtsigs dang mna' chad byas so/ /mung dzung me pho rta la
blon pos bkrongs/ de'i bu gnyis pa bu dzung me mo lug la bskos/ sa mo lug yan chod la lo nyis brgya dang brgyad song / bu dzung gi lo bcu gnyis srid bzung / sum cu pa shing
pho 'brug la 'das/ lo de la bu dzung gi bu lnga pa wu dzung bskos/ lo drug srid bskyangs/ sum cu so bzhi shing mo glang la 'das/ me pho stag la bu dzung gi bu bcu gsum
pa/ zon dzung bskos/ de nas bod kyi sa cha phal che ba rgyas blangs/ dang po thang gi rgyal khams kiM jang hu nas bod kyi bar la sa le bar stong tsho dgu dang / dgu brgya
yod/ phyis zon dzung nas bzung ste/ bod la mkhar mig gsum brgya shor/ yang thang gi thams cad thob/ zon dzung gi lo bcu bzhi srid bzung lnga bcu pa me mo yos la 'das/
sa pho 'brug la de'i bu che ba ghing dzung bskos/ de yan chad bod dang 'brel che'o/ /de ltar thang gis rgyal po ka'u dzung nas/ 'di yan chad la lo nyis brgya dang sum cu
so dgu song / ghing dzung ga rgyal srid lo bcu bzhi byas/ chu pho 'brug la 'das/ shing pho rta la de'i bu lnga pa/ hying dzung bskos/ lo bco lnga srid bzung / sa pho spre'u
la 'das/ lo de la de'i bu bdun pa je'u dzung bskos/ lo bcu bzhi srid bzung / chu mo phag la 'das/ shing pho byi ba la de'i bu dgu pa nga'i ding bskos/ lo bzhi srid bzung
/ me yos la 'das/ de nas thang gi rgyal rabs chad/ de yan la rgyal po nyi shu byung ngo / /rgyal khams gyi bdag po lo brgya dang / brgyad cu rtsa

brgyad byas/ des rjes su myang zhes pa la rgyal sa 'phos pa yin no/ /rgya bod kyi lo rgyus 'di/ tha'i dzung gi dus kyi yig tshang pa 'ba' su khyi bya bas brtsams/ phyis na
han se'u tshas btus te bsdebs/ rgya'i lo tsA ba ha gyang jus/ shing mo bya la/ shing kun du bsgyur/ bla ma rin chen grags gu shrIs/ shing mo glang la bod yig gis par du btab/
'di la lo'i dbang thang nor pa 'ga' re snang ngo / /thu yus hun/ hor ser yin/ wu then/ o thon yin/ zhib par rgya'i yig tshang thang shu thu hphan/ mtshan nyid la sogs
par blta'o/ /de yang thang gi rgyal po'i dus su/ hang ma'i zer ba/ se'u tshe gcig gi ngo log nas/ rgyal po byas/ ju wun zer bas/ blon po byas/ rting la dzu wun gyis/ thang
la ngo ltas nas/ chu mi dbyen gyi dmag dpon byas/ de'i rting sor ngo log nas/ rgyal sa phrogs pas/ myang rgyal po zhes bya ba'i rgyud byung / de la sogs pa rus mi gcig
pa'i mi rabs tshan pa lnga la/ rgyal po bco lnga byung / lo lnga bcu thams pa rgyal sa bzung / de'i rjes la ce'u tha'i dzung zhes pa'i rgyal po la/ spen lang gi sa char
rgyal po brgyad byung / brgyad pa/ shwang hang pha'u gnyis kyi lag nas/ chi twa tA'i gle'u zhes pa'i spen lang sogs rgyal khams kyi phyed phrogs/ rgyal khams de la tA'i
gle'u zer/ shwang hang gi bu khang dbang zhes pa/ sman tsha'i yul du song nas/ khri'i yul gyi rgyal khams phyed po bzung nas/ hor gyi/ nam tha'i zer/ rkyen khang hang je'ur
gtad/ rgyal khams de la srungs zer/ de nas sman rtser lha btsun yan la rgyal rabs brgyad byung / chi twan ta'i gle'u rgyal po brgyad kyi rjes su blon po che ba ne'u rje
zhes pa las rgyal sa blangs/ de la bu a'e tan khan zer ba brgyud pa dgu byung / rgyal khams la ta'i gam zer/ de'i rgyal po dgu pa la/ hung dbang zhes

pa'i lag nas/ hor jing gir rgyal pos/ rgyal sa blangs par byed cing / hor gyi rgyal khams la ta'i dben zer bas/ ta'i dben thong ji'i deb ther bya ba/ rgyal khams kyi khrims
kyi bya ba phra rags kyi bkod pa'i deb ther de nang du gsal ba'o/ / zhes dzam bha lha twan shrIs mgon gyis smras pa rnams bris pa'o/ / / /

dpa' bo mi nyag gi rgyal rabs bzhugs so/ / dpa' bo mi nyag gi rgyal rab ni/ sngon dang po/ gha thag la sogs mi nyag gi yul thams cad/ rgya'i rgyal po'i 'og na yod pa la/ byang
ngos dang gha'i bar na smon ri zhes pa'i ri'i gzhi bdag go'u zhes pa yod pa/ nyin gcig gi tshe byang ngos kyi mkhar nang na/ bud med gcig gi sar rta pa dkar po bdun byung
pas/ dang po nyid dang 'grogs pa las bu gcig skyes/ de'i dus su sngon med pa'i skar ma gcig shar bas/ rgya'i rtsis pa rnams kyi 'khor 'di'i nang rgyal srid 'phrog pa'i
mi gcig skyes 'dug byas pas/ rgyal pos da dung rtsis gyis la bu tsha de tshol zer bas/ rgan mos bu chung sa kyong zhig tu sbas/ pang leb kyi kha bcad/ de'i steng du chu
phor gang bzhag pas/ rtsis pa rnams na re/ mtsho chen po'i 'ogashing gi sa gzhi'i 'og na 'dug zer nas/ 'tshol ma thub pa dang / mkhar nang na lo gnyis 'gro ba'i bu tsha
thams cad sod ces lung bsgrags nas/ bu tsha kun bsad pa'i dus su/ rgan mos kyang bu shi ba ltar byas/ sgam nang du bcugangu zhing khyer nas chu'i dkyil gyi rtsa mthug po'i
dkyil du skyur bzhag pas/ nyin re bzhin bya rgod zhig 'ong nas bu tsha de mi 'khyags par byas/ res rgan mo gzhan zhig la/ ba bzho ma zhig yod pa de nyin re bzhin bu chung
de'i rtsa ru phyin nas 'o ma ster ba la/ nyin zhig ba bdag rgan mo des/ ba'i rjes la ltar phyin

pas/ de bzhin byed pa mthong ste/ bu tsha de khyad par can zhig yin pa 'dug bsam blangs nas/ bu dod byas/ rus pa ngo nus zhes pa/ bod skad du ba la 'o ma nu zer/ byis pa de'i
lo bdun lon nas/ na mnyam kyi byis pa drug btsal te/ byang ngos kyi sa gangs ri'i gseb tu bros nas/ ngo log brtsams/ ri de la shing 'thu ba'i skyes bu thams cad bzung
nas/ dmag mi bcol/ bu tsha des byang ngos kyi mkhar nang du shes rab che ba'i mi la/ ngo log brtsam thabs 'bri ru phyin pas/rgya'i rgan mo gcig na re/ zla ba 'di'i tshes
bco lnga'i nyin/ khyed rang dmag khyer la shog rta lcag dang / rta'i sbang mang po chu la skyur/ de nas rgya'i rgyal khams dam kha khyed la yong ba'i thabs ngas byed zer/
rgya'i rgan mo des lcags ri'i steng du/ brang brdung ngu zhing phyin pas/ rgyal pos ci yin 'drir btang bas/ lha'i dbang po'i lung gis mi nyag rgyal po gcig bskos yod/ de
la ngo ma bltas na rgya'i ming yang med pa byed zer/ sang nyin dmag bsam gyis mi khyab pa yong bar yod zer/ de ci yin byas pas/ khyed rang rnams sang snga mor rma chu la
ltos dang / rta sbang dang / rta lcag lhung bas chu mdog 'gyur ba yod zer/ sangs lta dus de bzhin du byung / da ci 'thad dris pas/ rgan mo na re/ ngo bltas na 'thad zer
nas rgyal po dpon g.yog gsum gyi/ dam kha skyel du phyin pas/ mi nyag rgyal po rta pa bdun dang 'phrad/ dam kha blangs rgyal po bsad/ der rting rim gyi rgyal po'i blon po
drag pa rnams kyang bsad/ rgyal sa blangs pas/ rgya'i yul du grags pa la rgan mo gcig gi kha'i nyes pas/ zur gsum sgo drug yod pa'i rgyal mkhar shor/ /zhes pa byung ngo
/ /mi nyag rgyal po'i thog ma de'ang / pha'i ming nas gras

te/ ga dzu rgyal po zhes par btags te/ de nas rgyal rabs drug nas/ mi nyag rgyal rgod byung / de'i dus su si no wa/ bod skad du sems nag po'i ra zhes pa la skyes pa'i mi'i
rgyal po'i blon po byas nas/ rgyal po gsod par 'gyur zhes pa la/rgyal rgod kyi tshor nas/ ri de la yod pa'i mi thams cad bsad na e 'thad ces/tha'i hu rgyal po la zhus pas
khong chos la dkar bas ma nyan/ de nas rgyal pos/ byang ngos su sdod ma nus par/ gha ru 'phos kyang phyis ri de la skyes pa'i mi zhig yod pa ma tshor ba la blon po thob
nas/ des mi nyag rgyal rgod bsad/ de'i rjes su rgyud chad nas/ tho 'dzin zhes pa'i rgyal po gzhan gcig byung ba/ de'i lag nas hor jing gir rgyal pos/ rgyal sa phrogs te/
mi nyag tho dzi rgyal po srog me yin/ jing gir rgyal po srog chu yin pa'i don gyi/ ji tsam 'thab kyang ma thub pa yin/ mi nyag rgyal rgod kyi skye ba/ hor rgyal po go dan
yin/ khong byang ngos su slebs pa dang / sngar mi nyag rgyal rgod bsad pa'i sa cha der lha khang bzhengs zhing / gsod mi tshang ma brlag par byas so/ /ge go dan e yin stag
gan rgyal po la/ ngan byed mi/ phyis gin thi mu yang sri gnon yi gzhan du skyes pa yin na no/ /zhes pa mi nyag btsan che shes rab ye shes kyi bkod pa/ yi ger bris bkod
pa'o/ /'di la rgya'i rgyal po ci'u tha'i dzung spun gnyis kyis rgyal sa bzung ba'i rjes la se'u rgyal po byung zhes pa dang / se'u rgyal po nas mi nyag rgyal po bcu gnyis
byung / lo ni brgya dang drug cu rgyal srid bzung / /de nas hor la rgyal sa shor ba yin/ /zhes pa yang gtam rgyud 'ga' re na snang ngo / /mi nyag rgyal rabs bris pa'i dge
ba yis/ /mi yi 'gro ba 'khor ba'i g.yul ngo las/ /mi 'jigs dpa' bo thob cing 'gro kun gyis/ /mi 'gyur rdo rje'i go 'phang myur thob shog///

chos rgyal bod kyi rgyal rabs bzhugs so/ /na mo lo ke shwa ra ya/ thugs rjes 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal chen po rnams/ /thugs rje'i spyan gyi ras su ma shor 'bar/ /thugs rje dang
ldan rgyun du gzigs pa yis/ /thugs rje'i dbang phyug khyed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de dag zhing mchog bod yul gangs chen 'dir/ /de yi sprul pas mi yi 'gro ba spel/ /de rnams
mgon du shAkya'i rgyal rgyud byon/ /de dang de yi rgyu mtshan 'di ltar ro/ /de'ang bod kyi rgyal rgyud nyid kyang / rje mang bkur rgyal po las rgyud pa sel ma zhugs par
'dod de/ de ni shAkya chen po dang shAkya li tsa bi/ shAkya ri brag pa rnams las/ ri brag pa ni/ 'phags rgyal gyi yul gnas te/ rgyal pa rtsib gyi mu khyud mtha' yas zhes
pa la/ bu rgyal po gtum po rab snang de ni/ bcom ldan 'das dang zhag dus mnyam du 'khrungs par byed la/ de'i bu rgyud rgyal po skyabs seng / de'i bu bod kyi rjer gyur pa
ni/ sngon gyi yig tshang rnams na 'di ltar snang ste/ dang por bod yul 'dir mi mi med/ mi ma yin du mas gang ba la/ srid pa cha'i sa yang 'dug cing / bod khams pa rnams/
dbra/ 'bru ldong gsum/ /sga dang bzhi/ nu bo dba'as dha gnyis dang drug la bod mi bu gdung drug zer ba 'dug na'ang / thog ma rang ni bod kyi mi'u rigs bzhi po yin par sems
so/ /de rnams bod mi snga shos yin/ khams rigs dbye ba mi'u rigs bzhi bya ba yod

pa yin/ ye sang dkar po gnam kyi 'ju thag can dang gcig ye mon nag po khro chu'i pha bong 'dra ba dang gnyis/ spyang phrug ye shes lha'i sgron me dang gsum/ mon rdzu nag po
khyi'i rnga ljang can dang bzhi'o/ /mi de rnams mang du 'phel nas bod la dbang byas te/ de dus gdong dmar can gyi yul zhes par grags shing / ma sang spun dgu rgyal phran
nyi shu rtsa lnga/ rgyal phran bcu gnyis/ rgyal phran sil ma bzhi bcus rim par dbang byas skad/ mkhan rjes dbang mdzad/ de nas dmu rje btsan pas bdud po ma TaM ru tra/ srin
po yakSha de ba/ klu rgyal gang ba rnams kyi rim par dbang byas so/ /de'i skabs su 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa de/ bcom ldan
'das snang ba mtha' yas dang / bstan pa'i bdag po rgyal ba shAkya thub pa'i bkas bskul zhing / ri bo po ta la'i rtse nas byang la zhal gzigs te/ kha ba can gyi sems can rnams
'dren par dgongs te/ nyin mtshan dus drug tu gzigs pas/ kha ba can 'di ni 'dzam bu gling du/ yul gru chen po lnga'am dgu yod pa'i nang nas/ ngan shos su'ang 'dug cing
/ sangs rgyas kyis zhabs kyi ma bcags/ gsung gi 'od zer gyis ma khyab/ bstan pa'ang med/ gdul byar ma gyur pa mun pa mun nag lta bur 'dug pa la/ stod khams gsum ni gangs
dang g.ya'i ra ba/ rdzing 'dra ba na/ sha dgo ri dwags kyis dbang byed/ bar khams brag dang spang gi bskor ba/ yur ba 'dra ba na/ spre'u dang brag srin mos dbang byed/
smad khams gsum nags kyi rdzing 'dra ba na/ glang po che dang / 'dab chags la sogs pas dbang byed/ mi'i 'gro ba med par 'dul ba'i skabs ma rnyed pa dang / kha ba can gyi
rgyal khams

chos kyi snod du ma gyur pa/ de rnams 'dul ba la/ thog mar mi ru bsgyur ba'i/ sprul pa btang dgos pa 'dug snyam nas dgongs pa na/ spre'u yi gyad ha nu mantha zhes pa de 'phags
pa'i sku drung na byung ba la/ khyod kyis kha ba can du sgom nus sam gsungs pas/ nus zer ba la/ dge bsnyen gyi sdom khrims lnga phog mi sdug pa sgom pa'i chos bslab nas
btang bas/ spre'u des kha ba can gyi yul gyis dbus/ brag chen gyi rtse la sgom pa'i drung du/ brag srin mo gcig nyin re bzhin byung nas/ mi tshangs par spyod par 'dod
pa'i rnam 'gyur sna tshogs dang / de'i phyir du srog 'dor ba'i rnam 'gyur gyis tshul ston gyin 'dug pas/ spre'u snying rjes ma bzod de/ 'phags pa'i drung du phyin nas/ rgyu
mtshan zhus pas/ 'phags pa dang sgrol mas gnang ba byin te/ spre'u dang brag srin mos 'dod pa spyad pa las/ zla ba dgu ngo bcu nas pa ma mi 'dra ba spu dang mjug ma med
pa gcig skyes pa de ni/ sha dmar po dang / khrag dron mo la rab tu dga' ba zhig go/ de nags tshogs can du spre'u'i khyur bskyal bas/ spre'u mo dang 'grogs nas lo gcig la
de 'dra ba'i phrug gu bzhi brgyar 'phel lo/ /de rnams kyang pha rigs shas che ba ni/ dad pa dang shes rab dang / snying rje dang brtson 'grus che ba/ chos dang dge las
la mos pa/ blo gros rgya chen po dang ldan pas na/ byang chub sems dpa' blo chen gyi rigs zhes bya'o/ /ma'i rigs shas che ba ni sha khrag la dga' ba| tshong khe sogs sems
pa/ bdag 'dzin dang chags pa che ba/ skad che ba/ ngo mi rtag pa/ gzhan gyi skyon 'don pa la dga' ba/ mos gus dang dad pa chung ba/bya byed mang ba/ mig mi la mi chags pa/
gdong dmar sha zan gyi rigs sha stag

byung ngo / /rigs rgyud de rnams 'phel ba'i ched du/ 'phags pas 'bras bu sna lnga dang / gser la sogs pa rin po che sna tshogs kha ba can gyi phyogs la gtor/ byin gyis brlabs/
de la longs spyad pas/ sprel phrug mir gyur pa de rnams je mang la song bas/ 'bru la mi 'cham par/ tsho bzhir bgos pas/ se dang dmu ldong dang / stong dang / bzhi la
mi'u rus bzhi zer/ la lar dbra/ 'bru/ zhang zhung / stong sum pa/ ldong mi nyag rnams bgrang pa na/ mi rje lhas mdzad pa ni gong bzhin/ rgya gar du rgyal po skyabs seng gi
bu lnga'i bar pa/ mig bya ltar mas nas 'geb pa/ g.yu'i smin ma yod pa/ sor mo dra bas 'brel ba/ dung so 'khor ma yod pa zhig skyes pas rgyal po na re/ ltas ngan du 'dug
pas sod cig gsung pa la/ blon po rnams kyi mtshon gyi gsod ma nus par/ zangs gyi ga'u kha sbyor du bcug gzer gyi bsdams nas/ chu bo gang gA la skur ro/ /de grong khyer yangs
pa can gyi zhing pa rgan rgon gyi rnyed nas/ nags gseb tu gsos pas/ bya dang ri dwags gcan gzan rnams kyi yang zas skom bskyal/ rtse grogs byas/ ljon shing dang me tog
kyang de la 'dud par byed da do/ /der rgyal bu na re/ nga la 'khor ngan pa 'di lta bu gang yin/ nga'i pha ma su yin zer ba la/ sngar gyi rgyu mtshan bsnyad nas/ khyod
phas ltas ngan du byas nas chur bor ba/ nged kyi rnyed pa sogs kyi gtam bsnyad pas/ yid skyo nas gangs gseb bros pas/ lha ri gyang mtho'i mkhar du byung / de nas rim gyi
'phyugs nas/ /kha ba can gyi rgyal khams gyi dbus/ yul yar mo sna bzhi dang / lha yar la sham po mthong nas/ der byon/ lha ri gong po ri rtser phebs/ dmu'i skas la babs te/
btsan thang sgo bzhir byon

pas/ ya gam lha sras dang / thog lha bon po la sogs shes pa can gyi bu tsha bcu gnyis/ phyugs skyong gin yod pa dang mjal/ de rnams kyi khyed su yin byas pas/btsan po zer/
gang nas 'ong byas pas/ mdzub mo gnam la sgreng/ de'i skad ma go yang / 'di ni ngo mtshar can gcig 'dug pas/ nges par gnam nas byon pa'i btsan po gcig yin par 'dug 'o cag
gis jo bo bya'o zer nas shing gi khri la bzhag gnya' bar khur nas khyim du phyin pas/ ming yang gnya' khri btsan por btags so/ /der phyugs rdzi rnams kyi rje'i bzhugs sa
la/ pho brang yum bu bla mkhar brtsigs te/ pho brang snga shos yin/ 'di la rgya gar nas byon pa'i lugs mi 'dra ba 'ga' snang zhing / bon po rnams/ gnam nas rmu thag dang
/ rkyang thag la byon no zer na'ang / gnya' khri btsan por thams cad mthun no/ /bod kyi rgyal po la snga ba de yin te/ 'di ni chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa'i shes bya rab
gsal na/ thub pa mya ngan las 'das rting / lo stong lhag song pa na byon par bzhed do/ /des sum pa'i bon po a yang rgyal ba btul lo/ /de'i sras mu khri btsan po/ de nas
bu rgyud rim pa bzhin/ ding khri btsan po/ so khri btsan po/ dwa khri btsan po/ gdags khri btsan po/ srib khri btsan po dang bdun la| gnam gyi khri bdun zer/ de yan chad
'od gsal gyi lha dag yod pas/ sras kyi chibs kha thub pa dang / yab 'od kyi nam mkha' la byon pas/ lha lus ro med 'ja' ltar yal ces so/ /srib khris sras gri gum btsan po
'khrungs dus/ a phyi gdags kyi lha mo dkar mo la/ mtshan ci gsol bris pas/ a phyi rgas nas/ dbang po mi gsal bar brda don ma go ba la brten nas/ ming gri gum

btsan por btags so/ /de la sras/ sha khri/ bya khri/ nya khri gsum 'khrungs ste/ yab de mu stegs kyi ston pa dig skad pa dang / shing sgrod pa dang / srog gzan pa bya ba rnams/
mchod gnas su rim par bkur ba'i skyon gyis/ rgyal po'i thugs gdon gyi bskyod nas/ rang gi blon po long ngam rta rdzi bya ba la/ khyod kyi nga'i 'thab zla bya dgos zer
ba la/ zhu ba phul kyang ma nyan par/ nyang ro rtsib kyi thal la tshal du rje 'bangs 'thab pas/ long ngam thabs rten 'brel la mkhas pas/ rgyal po rang gi bod kyi ral gri
la snga ba/ dgu zi glang po sna bya ba/ de klad la skor bas/ lha'i dmu thag chad/ lha nyams pas 'bangs kyi bkrongs/ spur de zangs kyi ga'ur bcug nas/ lci mda' zam kha nas/
nyang chu skya mo la bskyur btang bas/ rgyang mkhar pa tsha ru dgung zhag bdun dang / tshong 'dus mgur mo'i thad du gung zhag bcu gsum chags kyang / 'dzin mkhan med pas
kong chu rlag tu khyer bas/ klu srin byed mo rje rigs mo'i bran mo/ klu srin bye ma lag ring / chu la nya bshor du phyin pas/ ga'u rnyed nas/ rje mo la phul bas bang mdzod
du sbas so/ /de la stod kyi steng zer ro/ /rgyal bu gsum pos yab mes kyi bang mdzod na/ lha glang ru dkar bya ba'i/ glang 'phur shes gcig yod pa de la bzhon nas kong
yul la bros so/ /de rnams kyi ma la long ngam kyis rta rdzi bcol/ lha gcig la chu ma bcol lo/ /ma des rta 'tsho ru phyin pas/ gnyid du song ba'i rmi lam du/ mi dkar po gcig
dang bshos pa rmis/ gnyid sad pa dang sngas kha nas g.yag dkar po gcig langs song ngo / /zla ba brgyad song ba na/ khrag gi gong po lag mgo tsam gcig skyes/

de bor ni ma nus/ gso ba la ni kha mig med/ 'gul gyin 'dug pas 'brong rwa zhig gi nang du bcug pas/ rkang rnams kyi ngar ma blo'i drod la btsos pas/ ci zhig tsam na/ bu khye'u
zhig byung ba de'i ming / 'jang gi bu ru las skyes kyis ngar gsos por btags/ de lo bcu gnyis lon pa dang / pha dang pho bo gang na yod 'dri ba la/ sngar gyi rgyu mtshan
bshad pas/ spur dang / pho bo spun zla 'tshol du phyin/ spur rnyed kyang slong bas ni mi ster/ rkus pas ni ma thob/ nyos rin ci dgos byas pas/ mi'i bu mo bya lo ma bya
mig yod pa/ lo bcu drug lon pa zhig 'dod zer nas/ btsal pas/ g.ye'i gangs dbar yul gong nas/ pha mtshar la re then/ ma skyid la rung zhum gyis bu mo dge'u yu me bya ba/
de 'dra zhig 'dug na nyo bar byas nas/ pha na re gser mo rang tsam gcig 'dod zer/ ma na re spur de la mtshal gyi thig brgyad cu rgyag chug zer ba/ khas blangs/ bu mo khyer/
spur blus so/ /kong yul sen mo phug tu bang so brtsigs na'ang / der ma bzhugs/ bang so rtsig pa'i sngun ma yin no/ /de nas gcen sha khri kong po dang / gcung nya khri
dwags po'i rje mdzad nas/ gdan ma 'drongs/ kong rje dkar po dang / nyang btsun rgyal po bya bar grags so/ /da lta'ang de gnyis na rgyal rgyud mang skad do/ /spu bo brag thog
gi rje mdzad pa'i 'bring po/ bya khri gdan drangs nas rgyal sar bcug spu de gung rgyal du mtshan gsol lo/ /spu rgyal bod kyi yul bya ba de nas grags so/ /de nas spu rje
yar klungs su gdan drangs pas/ bon po spa ra'i bu/ kye rgyal sma bo ches/ gri btul nas/ lo bcu gsum song ba'i spur zangs de kha phyes pas/ skad nga ra ra zer bas/ yul
de'i ming ni nga ra thang du btags/ de

nas spur de 'phyongs rgyas grang mo grang chu kha'i zom la sbas pas/ gnam nas gser gyi thi gu gcig byung nas/ de la thim pas/ gnam la gser thig tu mtshan gsol/ de nas ru las
skyes kyi nyang ro bsham po mkhar gyis ri rtse la/ bya rgod kyi gseb tu zhugs nas/ lo ngam pho mo dang / phrug gu thams cad bsad/ bsham po mkhar gyi rtse phab/ sku mkhar
'phying nga stag rtse'i rmang rdo byas/ she'u yug thams cad snangs su bcad/ der rje spu de gung rgyal snyes [mnyes]nas/ ru las skyes la/ khu khu lha bu smon bzang bya ba'i
ming btags/ yab gri gum btsan po'i ring la/ zhang zhung dang / bru sha'i bon pos/ gshin gyi 'dur bon byung ngo / /sa zin du bya bar mga' ra spun dgus brdungs pas/ bod
ral dgu zi dang / dgu rogs zer ba 'di yang de dus nas dar ba'o/ /sras spu de gung rgyal gyi ring la/ sku mkhar 'phyings pa stag rtse brtsigs/ sgrung dang ldeb byung / gnam
bon gshen po bya ba byung ngo / /blon po ru las skyes dang / de'i bu lha bu mgo dkar gyi blon po byas pa'i ring la/ 'brong mthun du sdeb/ chu yur bar bcug spang zhing
du rmos/ sol bas rdo bzhus nas/ gser dngul bcos/ snol rnam lde/ snol bo lde/ lde stsol rnams/ lde snol bo/ lde rgyal po/ lde sprin btsan rnams la/ bar gyi sde brgyad ces
zer ro/ /lde brgyad bang so chu bo'i gzhung la btab/ lde sprin btsan gyi sras/ rgyal po to re long btsan/ thon mi 'bring po rgyal dang / snubs smon do re/ 'dar gyi bu stong
'dar chen rnams kyi blon po byas so/ /'di yan gyi rgyal po rnams kyis lha klu'i bu mo dang bshos te/ btsun mo bsten dgongs pa la ma 'tshal zer nas/ sa la ro ma byung skad
do/ /de rting 'bangs dang gnyen bsres pa

ste/ rgyal po to re long btsan nas/ bu rgyud rim pa bzhin/ rje khri btsan nam/ blon po snubs gnya' to re gtsugs lo dang / rtabs khri bzung mong kheng gis byas/ rje khri dgra
dpung btsan/ blon po mgar khri sgra ji thun dang / thon mi klu dbang bstad pos byas/ rje khri thog rje thog btsan/ blon mgar btsan gnya' ldom bu dang / snubs skyes thog
rje lo btsan gyi byas so/ /de yan mi rje lhas mdzad nas gdung rabs nyi shu rtsa bdun gyi bar la/ chab srid/ sgrung dang / ldebs/ bon dang gsum gyi bskyangs zer ro/ khri
thog rje thog btsan dang / ru yong bza' stong rgya mtsho'i sras/ lha tho tho re snyan btsan ni/ bod rgyal gnya' khri btsan po byon nas/ lo dgu brgya drug cu rtsa drug song
ba'i me mo yos lo la 'khrungs so/ /de rnams la btsan lnga zer ro/ /rje de'i blon po khri thog rje btsan dang / sbrang khri bzung lan pas byas so/ /rgyal po de'i sku ring
la rgya gar nas/ paNDi ta mkhan po si li byin byon kyang / bod na yi ge dang lo tsA shes pa gzhan med pas/ rgyal po'i phyag tu mchod pa'i rten la/ rags sku'i rigs lnga
cha gcig bzhag nas/ khong rgya nag la byon no/ /der rting rgyal po lo brgyad cu bzhes pa/ sa pho spre'u'i lo la/ pho brang yum bu bla mkhar gyi rtser/ nam mkha' nas zangs
kyi ga'u'i nang du/ dpa' skong phyag rgya ba dang / mdo za ma tog bkod pa/ gser gyi mchod rten 'khru gang pa/ tsan dan ma Ni'i gzungs rnams byon te/ da nas gdung rabs lnga
nas 'di'i don shes par 'gyur ro/ /zhes sgra grags so/ /de chos yin par ma go na'ang / ngo mtshar can zhig go snyam nas/ pho brang gi rtser bzhugs/gser skyems dang g.yu
sngon sogs kyis mchod pas/ rgol po dgung lo brgyad cu

pa la se'u skyes/ skra dkar rnams por gyur/ gnyer ma med par gzhon sha chags zhing / lo brgya dang nyi shu thub/ rten de la gnyan po gsang ba zhes par mtshan gsol/ nga'i rgyud
'dzin rnams kyis 'di la mchod pa phul la/ gsol ba thob cig 'dod pa'i don rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes gsungs so/ /rgyal po nyid 'phags pa kun tu bzang po'i sprul
par grags shing 'di'i ring la/ bod du dam pa'i chos kyi dbu brnyes par byed da do/ /btsan lnga po'i bang so yul du btab/ yul gyi ming ni 'phying lung so ra thang / btsan
lnga'i chad pa sa phung sbra 'drar yod/ yul med che gru bzhi yi mi shes skad/ rje de'i sras/ khri snyan bzung btsan/ blon po sbas snang gzher zla btsan dang / mgar khri 'bring
gis byas/ khri snyan chad pa don mkhar mda' ru brtsigs/ de yang yul med sa phung brdal ba 'dra/ de'i sras 'bro snyan lde ru/ blon po gnyag thang pa yang rje dang /
snubs khri dar res thong pos byas/ de'i sras stag ri gnyan gzigs dang / yab sras gnyis la/ bar gyi steng zhes zer/ de'i lo rgyus/ 'bro gnyan lde ru khab tu/ mchims za klu
rgyal ngan bu zhes pa'i skyon gyis/ khong rang la klu nad tsi tsi dzA la byung nas/ yab yum gnyis blon po gnyag thang pa yang rje dang gsum ga gson dur la bzhugs dgos byung
/ sras gcig yod pa dmus long du gyur/ ming dmus long dkon pa bkra zer/ zhal chems la bsam pa bzang po gser dang 'dra ba ste/ /bzang po'i gros ni bdud rtsi yin pas nyon/
/ngan pa rnams ni me dang 'dra bas spongs/ / mi chos rtog pa yin pas rnam rtog skyur/ khyed kyis gnyan po gsang ba mchod/ /'a zha'i sman pa bos la mig phye/ /mig ma byung
na/ sum pa'i yul na bon po

gcig gis chung ma/ rgyal mo rgya lcam bya ba dang / nga nub gcig 'grogs pa la/ bu sum ring po bya ba yod pa de bos la gcen chol/ rgyal sar chug gsungs so/ /'gro gnyan lde ru'i
bang so zhang mdar brtsigs/ de nas rmu long dkon pa bkras/ gnyan po gsang ba rgyas par mchod/ 'a zha'i sman pa bos nas pho brang yum bu'i rtser spyan phyes pas/ skyid
shod stag mo'i ri la/ gnyan rtswa za ba mthong / mchan yang stag ri gnyan gzigs su gsol nas/ rgyal sar bcugade'i blon po de ni mon khri do ri snang btsan dang / sna nam
mang gnya'/ sbrang khri gzung min rnams kyis byas/ yab sras de gnyis kyi bar du zhag nyi shu rtsa gcig bzhugs skad do/ /gnyan gzigs bang so don mkhar mda' ru brtsigs/ gral
ni khri gnyan gong dngos ni g.yon na yod/ de yang yul med sa phung brdal ba 'dra/ de'i sras gnam ri srong btsan/ blon po sbas snang bsher dang / che spongs nag ser/ nyang
rtseng dgu snon ban sngags gsum rnams kyi byas/ rgyal po 'di'i ring la/ rgya nag nas rtsis dang / sman dpyad byung na'ang cher ma dar/ rgya dang gru gu btul/ nyang sbal
snon gsum mnga' 'og tu bcug sku mkhar khri brtsigs 'bum gtugs bya ba/ ba dmar mo'i 'o mas sbrus pa'i 'jim pas brtsigs so/ /rgyal po des dmus te long ba khrid nas brag gsum
ding ma mtsho'i 'gram nas rnyed pa'i rta cang shes la chibs/ sbrang dga' bo dang / dmu spun rgyang ring po bya ba'i gyad mi gnyis kyis khrid nas/ phung g.yag thal kha
ru ring bya ba 'brong na le bong zan bsad nas yong / sha dras sga la btags pa sa la lhung pas/ lan tshwa rnyed de/ tshwa la drug cu sde byed pa byung / de gong bod na lan
tshwa'i ming med do/ /

'di yi chad pa don mkhar mda' ru brtsigs/ de nas phul skyes brtsigs pa sogs mkhar yod/ gral ni khri gnyan bzung btsan g.yon na yod/ rgyal po gnam ri srong btsan la/ yum tshe
spong bza' 'bri ma thod dkar gyi sras khri srong btsan ni/ me glang lo la/ pho brang byams pa mi 'gyur gyi gling du/ mes pho tho tho ri snyan btsan nas lo brgya dang dgu
bcu go gcig song ba'i dus/ sku 'khrungs nas/ lo bcu gsum nas yab 'das/ lo de nyid la rgyal por mnga' gsol/ chab srid lo drug cu re bzhi bzung / 'di ni 'phags pa spyan ras
gzigs dngos kha ba can du byon na nas/ gdul bya smin par mdzad pa'i phyir/ dam pa'i chos kyi srol gtod pa'i tshul gyis/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa bzung ste/ lha mo dri ma med
pa'i mdo dang / dam pa dang po'i rgyud las lung bstan pa bzhin yin la/ bod kyi rgyal po lo bcu bzhi pa gcig gis/ rgyal srid chos bzhin du skyong gin 'dug ces pa'i snyan
grags kyis/ 'dzam bu gling khyab ste/ phyogs bzhi'i rgyal pos/ nor khyad par can gyi skyes dang / yi ge bskur byung ba/ bod kyi rgyal po la/ skyes lan bskur rgyu'i nor yod
kyang / kha 'phrin ma gtogs yi ge med pas/ bod la yi ge zhig ci nas kyang dgos pa 'dug dgongs nas/ thon mi a nu'i bu/ saM bho Ta mi chung bya ba blo gsal bas/ gser bskur
nas rgya gar du yi ge dang chos slob tu btang bas/ mkhas pa li byin na re/ ngas yi ge bris rigs mi 'dra ba nyi shu shes pas/ rgyal po'i 'gram du rdo ring la yi ge bris
yod pa bstan nas/ slob ma khyod gang 'dod zer ba la/ bod kyi yi ge'i lugs 'di bslabs/ /lo tsA yang mkhas par shes/ slob dpon dang paNDi ta/ shI la nan ta

bya bas/ mdo dkon mchog sprin dang / tog gzungs/ snying rje pad dkar la sogs spyan drangs 'ongs pas/ rgyal po thugs rab tu dgyes?dges so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba dang / yig mkhan
la snga ba de yin no/ /rgya gar na yi ge thams cad/ dbyangs yig dang gsal byed sum cu rtsa bzhi la/ mi tshud pa gang yang med na'ang bod sgra ngan pas de bzhin ma go rgya
gar ba gcig la e ka zer/ 'jig rten la lo ka chos la ngharma/ zhus la kri ta zer la/ smras pa zer dgos pa sogs bod skad du ma khug par/ thon mi thugs mug nas/ gzim khang
gi sgo bsdams/ chum gzims nas gnyid log sad pa dang / gam na rgan po gu ba lta bu zhig 'dug rgan po gang nas yong / gar 'gro/ ngas sgo bsdams nas yod pa ji ltar byas nas
yong / ci byed byas pas/ chos kyi don la 'gro 'ong med/ /yang dag don la ci bya med/ /nam mkha' dag la lam byas pas/ /sgo cha dam pas mi thub pa zer/ der the tshom skyes/
yang bskyar nas bris pas/ ngas za hor nas yong / 'a zha'i yul du 'gro zer/ thag ci tsam yod/ ci cha zer/ rgyags ji tsam yod/ ja yod zer nas rgan po mi snang bar gyur te/
de ni 'jam dbyangs gyi sprul pa'o/ /de nas bsam pas/ ca cha ja dang gsum/ zha za 'a dang drug byung ba/ de rnams bcug yi ge lnga bcu po/ ka mad sur cur bsdus nas/ bod
kyi sgra skad dang mthun pa'i yi ge 'bru sdeb tu btub pa byung ba dang / bod kyi rgyal po'i zhal nas/ da nga'i yab mes kyi gnyan po gsang ba 'di'i nang na/ ci 'dug ltos dang
zer klog pas/ mdo za ma tog dang / sngang skong phyag rgya ba/ tsandra ma Ni'i gzungs/ mu dra'i phyag rgya rnams bzhugs 'dug pa la mos nas/ rgyal pos kyang lo bzhir

mtshams bcad/ yi ge dang chos bslabs so/ /mdo dkon mchog sprin la sogs pa thon mis spyan drangs pa rnams bod du bsgyur/ chos sgyur ba'i thog ma yin no/ /chab 'og thams cad
la chos dang yi ge rgyas par spel cing / bod yig ga thog ma/ rgyal pos jo bo gtso 'khor gsum po'i bstod pa/ 'di brtsams nas lha sa zla ba'i brag la bskos nas phud du phul
yod do/ /lha skyon gyi ma gos sku mdog dkar/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi dbu rgyan can/ /thugs rje'i spyan gyis 'gro la gzigs/ /spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thugs rje
dang ni shes rab gnyis/ mnyam par sbyor ba'i thugs mnga' zhing / /phyag gnyis thugs kar thal mo sbyar/ /dpal ldan mnyam sbyar la phyag 'tshal/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi snying
po'i gtso/ /gsang sngags rgyal po bgrang 'phreng ni/ /mu tig ltar dkar g.yas na 'dzin/ /rigs sngags 'chang la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'khor ba'i skyon gyi ma gos pa'i/ /padma
shel gyi 'od pas gsal/ /padma dkar po g.yon na 'dzin/ /phyag na padma la phyag 'tshal/ /chos dbyings rnam dag dri ma med/ /zla ba'i 'od ltar rgyas pa'i yum/ /gzugs kyi
lha mo yid 'ong ma/ /yi ge drug ma phyag 'tshal lo/ /mtha' yas yon tan gser mdog can/ /yid bzhin nor bu chen po ltar/ / sems can re ba skong mdzad pa'i/ /nor bu 'dzin pa
phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes pa'o/ /de dus rgyal po lo bzhir sgor ma byon pa des/ blon po rnams na re/ rgyal pos ci yang mi shes/ bod bde ba nged rnams kyis byas pa yin zer ba/
rgyal pos gsan nas glen par brtsi na/ bod mi thul ba dgongs nas rgyal po gcig pu gnas pas kun bde ba yin te/ sngon yang khrims med pas/ shes pa can bcu

gnyis mthar 'khyams 'dug da ngas dge ba bcu la dpe blang ba'i chos khrims bca'o gsungs/ bsad pa la stong nyis khri chig stong / rkus pa la brgyad cu 'jal/ byi byas pa la yan
lag gcod pa/ rdzun byas pas lce 'breg par byas/ yang mi chos gtsang ma bcu drug gi khrims kyi gzhi bzung bar byas te/ dkon mchog la dad pa dang / skyo ngal med par sgrub
pa dang don dam par sangs rgyas kyi chos btsal zhing sgrub pa dang / gtsug lag dang chos la blo sbyangs pa dang / pha ma la drin lan gsab pa la slob pa dang / yon tan can
gyi rigs kyi rgan pa la bkur sti bya ba dang / sha nye dang mdza' bshes la gzhung drang por srong zhing / khong sems chung zhing dang du blang ba dang / ma brtags shing
ma bcol ba'i las la rtogs 'dod med pa dang / yul mi khyim mtshes la phan gdags pa dang / gzhi drang por bsrang zhing khong sems chung ba dang / las dang spyod pa thams
cad ya rabs kyi rjes su bsnyegs shing / phyi mig ring du lta ba dang / zas dang nor la tshod zin pa dang / drin chen gyi mi'i lan mi bcag bzang lan brlan pa dang / bu lon
dus la 'jal zhing bre srang la g.yo mi bya ba dang / thams cad la snyoms par bya shing 'gran sems mi bya ba dang / gros kyi nang du bud med kyi kha la mi nyan pa dang /
rang tshod zin par bya ba dang / sems can gang la brdung ba'i sems mi 'chang ba dang / byams snying rjes skyong ba dang / bcu drug go / bod kyi khrims dang / chos rnams skyid
shod sho ma ra na bar gtan la phab pa'o/ /der blon 'bangs rnams dga' nas/ rgyal po 'di ni shin tu sgam po gcig 'dug go zer nas/ srong btsan sgam por mtshan gsol lo/
/gzhan yang skye bo tha mal pa

rnams/ blo kha chos la drangs zhing dad pa'i phyir/ thog mar sgrung dang / lde'u dang /bon rnams bas bstan/ rgyal pos mdzad pa'i sgrung rgyud/ lde'u yi bkod pa ra sa 'phrul
snang gis blo 'bur nang na bris nas bkod yod do/ /de dus blon po mang nyang po rje zhang snang la sogs pa mdzangs pa mi drug gis/ tshig drug drug sum cu so drug la sogs
pas/ gtan tshigs gtan la phab/ bod ru bzhi stong sder 'byed/ sku srung phyogs bzhir bskos/ mi la yig tshang skur/ mdo ba'i rta la cho ris bris/ phu chu rdzing du skyil/ gzhung
chu yur du drangs/ ri khyim klungs su brtsigs/ thang zhing du slog zhing lhur bcad/ chur gru btsugs/ bre srang gtan la phab/ mtha'i rgyal phran rnams dang / lho mon/
rtswa mi shing mi la sogs pa thams cad mnga' 'og tu bsdus/ chab srid rnams bde zhing skyid par gyur te/ chos lugs la phal cher zhugs so/ /der rgyal po'i dgongs pa la/ nga'i
khrims rnams kyang btsan par byung / da chos kyi 'dul du btub par 'dug pas chos bya'o/ /chos byed pa la yi dam gyi lha dgos pas/ ci la bya snyam na/ tshes brgyad kyi
srod la sprin gseb nas lha'i bu mo na re/ rgya gar lho phyogs mthar thug pa rgya mtsho'i 'gram/ bye ma'i gseb/ sing ga'i gling / kha sar pa Ni sku rgyab/ glang po che nyal
ba'i 'og gis/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i sdong po'i khog na zhal bcu gcig pa'i sku rang byon gcig yod pa/ spyan drangs na kha ba can du don chen po byed par 'gyur
ro/ /zhes zer nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de la rgyal po thugs rab tu dgyes te/ rang gi smin mtshams nas 'od zer skyes pa'i sna la/ dge slong shI la a ka ra bya bar sprul
nas/ skyod de spyan 'dren pa la btang ngo / /de nas

dge slong des rgya mtsho'i 'gram na sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig gi rang la rtsa ba zug gser thub kyi ring la lo 'dab rgyas/ 'od srung gi dus me tog shar/ shAkya thub pa'i dus
na 'bras bu smin/ de'i steng la rtsa ba rul nas 'gyel ba bye mas non nas/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i khog nas/ dal pos mchod cig ces pa'i sgra dang bcas bcu gcig zhal
sor bcu gnyis pa/ phyag bcu pa/ ma nu ka'i mdog lta bu/ lta bas chog mi shes pa zhig byon pa de dang / tsan dan gyi tshal pa zhig bye ma'i gling nas/ 'jag ma'i phon zhig
po ta la'i 'dam nas me tog myu gu'i sdong po tshal pa zhig grong khyer ke ru'i mchod rten 'khor lo'i nang nas/ sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig dang / 'od srung / shAkya thub
pa rnams kyi/ sku gdung ring bsrel de la bzhugs pas byang chub shing gi mchod sdong gsum/ gnas chen brgyad kyi bye ma/ chu bo nai ra dza na'i 'gram du sangs rgyas kyi lhung
bzed na sa/ chu bo ba'i shul gyi bye ma/ rin po che sna gnyis rnams dge slong gi bsnams byon te/ mchod rdzas khyad par can bcu po de/ bod kyi rgyal po la phul bas/ thugs
rab tu dgyes shing ngo mtshar bar gyur to/ /dge slong de yang rgyal po la g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ de'i smin mtshams su nub bo/ /de nas mchod g.yog la mtshan
ldan ma bcu drug bskos te/ dus drug tu mchod pa phul cing / rgyal po rang lha'i drung nas 'ben gang mi 'da' sar bzhugs so/ /de nas yang rgyal po'i thugs la/ de bzhin rten
khyed par can de 'dra gdan 'dren rgyu gar yod dgongs nas/ yi dam gyi lha de la gsol ba btab pas/ lha'i thugs ka nas 'od zer gsum 'phros pa bal yul gyi phar mtha'i lung pa
gcig gi tsan dan gyi

nags gseb na/ tsan dan ha ri'i sdong po gcig la phog 'dug pa/ yang rgyal pos sprul pa bkyes nas/ dge slong shI la a ka ra spyan 'dren du btang bas/ nyin mo tsan dan gyi sdong
po la/ mchan mo spyan ras gzigs kyi sku rang byung gsum gong 'og brtsegs mar bzhugs pa/ steng ma na re/ nga rgya bal gyi mtshams su zhog cig sa de na snga dro re la tshong
dpon re sbos grir 'chi ba yod pa de chad do gsungs jo bo 'ja' ma li'o/ /bar ma na re nga bal yul yam bu ya 'gal du zhog cig de na mi mang po rims nad kyi 'chi ba yod
pa de chad do gsungs pa de jo bo u khang ngo / /smad ma na re/ nga mang yul skyid grong du zhog cig/zla ba re la grong dpon re mdze nad kyi 'chi ba yod pa de chad do gsungs/
de ni 'phags pa wa ti yin no/ /lha gsum po de ltar bzhugs pa'i rgyu mtshan/ rgyal po la zhus pas/ 'dir ma phebs kyang sems can gyi don chen po byas 'dug gsungs nas/
shin tu dgyes par gyur to/ /der rgyal po'i thugs la yi dam gyi lha dngos dang mjal phyin/ sems can gyi don la tshegs med/ bod 'bangs kyi 'gro don phyogs gang nas 'grub brtag
dgongs nas gzigs pas/ mes po tho tho ris byang chub sems dpa'i sprul pa des zhabs kyi bcags pa'i skyid smad lha sa dmar po ri'i phyogs der/ theg pa chen po'i chos spel
du btub par dgongs nas/ mchod gnas rnams shing rta la spyan drangs/ rgyal blon rnams byon/ sbra stod tshal du zhag mal mdzad/ sang gro btab sar rgyal po dang blon po tshos
chu khar khrus mdzad/ chab gsol dus dbus kyis gye rer yi ge drug ma 'byon par lung bstan to/ /dmarapo ri rtser phebs yab mes kyi bzhugs shul du pho brang btab

nas bzhugs/ de nas ngas sems can gyi don byed par dam bcas pa yin pas/de dag 'dul ba'i thabs gang legs dgongs nas/ lha la gsol ba btab pas/ de'i thugs ka nas 'od zer skar mda'
lta bu gnyis/ shar nub du song bas/ rgya nag dang / bal yul du thims pas/ khro gnyer can dang / sgrol ma'i sprul pa spyan drongs zer ba'i sgra byung nas/ sngon la blon
po mgar dang / thon mi mi chung gnyis gyi 'go byas/ rta pa brgya la gser gyi dong rtse brgya dang / gser gyi bang ba bdun/ glang po che gser gyi dra ba lha'i rin po che'i
brgyan pa zhigagaser phye bre phyed/ yi ge bcu pa'i gser dngul zangs gsum gyi sgrom bu dang bcas pa bskur nas/ ston zla ra ba'i tshes brgyad/ skar ma nab so'i nyi ma rtse
shar la/ bal po'i lha gcig slong ba la brdzangs so/ /der khong rnams kyi/ nub phyogs bal po'i pho brang yam mkhar du slebs/ rgyal po 'od zer go cha dang mjal/ rgyu mtshan
zhus pas/ bal bza' khri btsun skal rdzongs bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ yi dam mi bskyod rdo rje/ byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo/ tsan dan sgrol ma'i sku rang byung gcig dang
bcas pa gnang ba/ gdan drangs nas pho brang dmar po rir phebs so/ /de nas bal bzas rgyal po thugs mi skyo zhing / pha rol gyi dmag gi mi tshugs par bya ba'i phyir/ rin po
che mang po sbyar/ gnod sbyin pho mo mang po bran du bkol nas/ dmar po ri'i khongs su bcug pa'i so phag gi lcags ri/ gyang rim sum cu rtsa gnyis dang mnyam pa/ srin yul
lang ka pu ri'i grong khyer dang 'dra ba/ mkhar dgu brgya dgu bcu rtsa dgu'i rtse mo nyag stong du tshang ba/ mkhar re re la mdung ba dan dmar po can bzhi re btsugs pa/ phyogs
re

re na sgo dpe bzhi srung mi yod pa/ rtse mkhar la bya ra ba mi lnga re rgyun du yod pa/ de'i lho ngos lcags ri'i nang na/ pho brang sog po mkhar bya ba dgu thog dang / rgyal
po'i rtse mkhar mnyam pa/ de gnyis lcags thag gis sbrel nas/ dngul zam la rgyu ba/ mkhar dang lcags ri rnams la mda' yab dang / sgo chung dang / rnga yab dang / pha gu
dang / kha bad dang / rta babs rin po che'i dril bu er kha/ mu tig gi dra ba dra phyed rnams kyi brgyan pa/ pha rol gyi dpung gis mi tshugs pa zhig bzhengs so/ /der rting
yang blon po mgar dang / thon mis 'go byas/ rta pa brgya la gser gyi dong rtse brgya/ gser phye bre phyed/ rin po che'i gos gcig rnams bskur nas/ shar rgya nag po'i lha
gcig slong ba la brdzangs so/ khong rnams kyi rgya'i bkra shis khri sgor slebs/ thang tha'i dzung rgyal por zhus pas/ de'i sras rgya mo kong jo rdzongs ba bsam gyis mi khyab
pa/ yi dam gyi lha shAkya thub pa/ gab rtse drug cu skor/ bzo sna bco brgyad/ sman dpyad chen mo/ 'bru sna tshang / g.yog pho mo mang po dang bcas pa gnang bod du phebs/
lha sa'i mthil bye ma'i gling nags gseb/ chu mig gi 'gram du/ lha'i shing rta byings nas/ gyad lha dga' klu dgas btegs kyang ma thegs pa/ jo bo de khar bzhugs pa yin/
sa dgra mnan pa la dgongs pa'o/ /sku srung la gyad gnyis bzhag gos dar gyi bla yol gyi spyad do/ /der kong jo rgyal po dang mjal/ yab yum gsum blon 'bangs dang bcas pa dga'
mgur spyod do/ /de nas rgyal po'i thugs la/ lha rten gsung rab 'di rnams bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag khang zhig bzhengs dgos dgongs nas/ kong jo la rtsis byas pas/ yul de na
bkra shis pa'i rtags brgyad la sogs pa'i dge

du ma tshang 'dug kyang / lar bod yul kha ba can 'di srin mo gan rkyal du nyal ba dang 'dra/ 'o thang gi mtsho 'di srin mo'i snying khrag tu 'dug pa 'di gnon dgos/ de la'ang
/ dang po ru bzhi'i lha khang brtsig dgos zer nas/ dpung mgo g.yas pa la ka tshal/ g.yon pa la khra 'brug brla g.yas pa la gtsang 'gram/ g.yon pa la grom pa rgyang brtsigs
so/ /yang srin mo'i yan lag bzhi gnon pa'i phyir/ mtha' 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang bzhi ni/ gru mo g.yas pa la kong po bu chu/ g.yon pa la lho brag mkho mthing / dpus mo
g.yas pa la ka brag g.yon pa la pra dum rtse ba brtsigs/ srin mo'i nying lag bzhi gnon pa'i phyir yang 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang bzhi ni/ lag mthil g.yas pa la/ byang mtshal
gyi rlung gnon/ g.yon pa la khams su klong thang sgron ma/ rkang 'go g.yas pa la byams sprin/ g.yon pa la mon bum thang skyer chu rnams bzhengs/ der rting ra sa'i rmang
gting yang zhig nas rtsig tu ma btub pa la rgyal pos/ tsan dan gyi lha la gsol ba btab pas/ sngon la lho phyogs su pho brang brtsigs la/ der mchod pa'i rten ngo mtshar
can rnams spyan drongs shig de nas rim gyi 'dod pa 'grub par 'gyur ro zer ba byung nas/ bal bza' la bka' bsgos nas/ lho phyogs ngos su pho brang brtsigs/ mchod pa'i rten
rnams spyan drangs/ rgyal po yang phebs nas/ sngon la lha khang bzhengs/ der rting yi dam gyi lha zhig kyang bzhengs par dgongs te/ bal po'i lha bzo ba la bka' gnang ste/
lha'i rgyu khyad par can dang / lag cha rnams rgyal po'i spyan sngar bsags/ sang nyin nas lha bzhengs brtsis la/ de nub pho brang gi mthong khung na mar/ sangs rgyas byang
chub sems dpa' thams

cad 'od zer dkar dmar shar ste byon/ lha'i rgyu la thims song bas/ rgyal po'i dgongs pa la/ nga'i yi dam 'di la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang
byin rlabs mnyam pa zhig yong ba 'dug pa shin tu legs/ de yang bod kha ba can pa'i lha skal thugs rje chen po rigs lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi nang nas/ gang bzhengs na drags
dgongs pa la/ sang nam lang tsa na/ dbu'i sngas kha na rgyal po rang dang sku bong mnyam pa'i/ bcu gcig zhal zhig rang byon du 'dug pas/ shin tu legs na'ang / tsan dan gyi
sku rang byon 'di dang / mchod sdong 'di gsum lha'i khong snying du bzhugs pa zhig byed dgos bsam pa yin te/ gsungs pa dang lha sku rang gi phyag gnyis gyi rang gi sham
thabs pus gong du brdzes te/ zhabs g.yas pa'i mthil nas 'od zer 'phros/ tsan dan gyi sku dang mchod sdong gsum po spyan drangs/ thugs kar bzhugs pa'i sku shin du spram/
a mi dhe wa yang g.yon gyi phyogs su yo/ zhabs sngar shul du byon kyang / sham thabs pus gong du lus te/ chags pas rgyal po shin tu ngo mtshar cing dgyes par gyur to/ /der
rting rgyal pos yi dam la gsol ba btab pas/ zhal dbus ma nas 'od zer byung / lho nub la wa ba tshal du dug gi sdong po la phogade 'thor bas 'dre srin gyi bdud dpung bshig
'od zer phrag pa la phog pas/ kha sar pa Ni dang / rta mgrin/ a mi de wa rnams kyi sku dod 'dug pa bzhin 'bur du brkos yod cing / brag lha can gdong zhes par grags so/
/'od zer de nub phyogs brag lha klu phug gi ma mo'i nyal sa phrogs/ rgyal pos sprul pa bkye nas/ phyag stong spyan stong gi bzo mdzad/ bal po'i lha bzo bas lo ke shwa ri
dang /

kha sar pa Ni/ dbyangs can ma 'od zer can ma rta mgrin bdud rtsi 'khyil ba rnams bzhengs ste/ gtso 'khor dgu bzhugs so/ /de nas jo mo ru yong bza' rgyal mo btsun gyi/ ma mo'i
nyal sar/ bcom ldan 'das rnam snang kun du 'od kyi zhal brag la 'bur du dod par bzhengs/ pho brang gi lho nub btsan gyi rgyug srang yod sar/ mchod rten ke ru brtsigs/
klu'i pho brang steng gi gser gyi lha shAkya mu nes mnan zin/ rgyal pos phyogs bzhi dang / sa dgra brgyad mnan/ bkra shis pa'i rtags brgyad po gsal bar byas pa ni/ gnam la
'khor lo rtsibs brgyad sa la padma 'dab brgyad kyi bar na/ han dkar stag mo'i ri la gdugs yod/ ra ka'i brag la nya yod/ rdzong tsan gyi brag la bum pa yod/ grib se sgrom
na dung yod/ yugs ma'i zur na rin po che dpal be'u yod/ bshun gyi ri la rgyal mtshan yod/ der rting yon tan thams cad thon pas/ ra sa'i lha khang rtsig tu btub par mkhyen
nas bod kha ba can du legs so cog 'phel cing / nyes so cog sgrib pa'i phyir du/ rgyal pos sprul pa lnga stong bkyes nas lha khang bzhengs/ btsun mo dam pa bal bza' khri
btsun gyis ra sa 'phrul snang / rgya bza' kong jos rgya stag ra mo che/ zhang zhung bza' li tig sman gyis/ khram bu lkog ma/ ru yong bza' rgyal mo btsun gyis/ brag lha
klu phug mong bza' khri lcam gyis/ yer ba'i lha khang rnams bzhengs so/ /ra sa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs nas lo gsum lon tsa na/ bod 'bangs byin pos nam zla dus bzhi'i/ rtsis
ma shes shan ma phye ba la/ rgyal pos dgongs pa la ngas chos 'jig rten gyi khrims 'chos/bod 'bangs dge la skul thub pa byung na'ang / 'jig rten pa'i rnam rtog gi dra
ba

sel thabs/ rgya dkar nag gi rtsis kyang rgyas par spel nas/ rgyal khams la phan gdags dgos snyam pa 'khrungs te/ bod phrug blo gsal ba/ 'bre gnya' brtan bya ba dang / lang
tsho ldong legs/ bya gag stong kun/ 'dar mi stag kha dang bzhi po la cha rkyen mang du bskur nas/ rgya nag la rtsis slob tu btang / rgya'i rtsis pa khri ma hA ya na la sogs
la/ lo gcig zla ba bdun gyi bar du gtugs/ gson gshin gyi rtsis phal che ba shes par byas nas/ yar slebs pas/ rtsis la mkhas pa mi bzhir grags pa byung cing / khyad par
bya gag stong khun nas/ pha tshe bu rabs su rje'i bla rtsis byas pa'i rigs rgyud ni/ da lta ga rings pa tshang yin par byed do/ /de nas bod rgyal po blon po bcu drug dang
bcas nas/ rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar byon nas/ rgya'i so kha 'bul ba dang / kong jo'i lan dus kyi khas blang chad btsan par bya ba'i phyir/ lha khang mang po bzhengs/ lo
bcu gsum gyi ring la/rgya bod du lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs tshar ba'i rting ma la/ rab sgang du yongs rdzogs lha khang bya ba bzhengs so/ /bka' khol mar chos rgyal
'di'i ring la/ rgya gar nas slob dpon ku mA ra dang / bram ze shang ka ra/ bal po'i slob dpon shi la manydzu/ rgya nag gi slob dpon ha shang ma hA ya na la sogs pa spyan
drangs/ sde snod gsum dang / rgyud kyi cha lag mang rab bsgyur cing / rgyal po rang gi zhal nas/ thugs rje chen po'i chos skor ma bu brgya rtsa brgyad gsung / lha sa'i
byang chub gling gi rta mgrin zhabs 'og na gter du sbas yod bya ba dang / zhang zhung gi yul nas/ bon po'i grub thob zhang zhung lha ldem bya ba bos nas/ bod mi a ho rnams
bsags/ bya ba bon slob tu bcug nas/ nad pa'i rim 'gro sogs la

bon yang dar bar mdzad do/ /zer ba 'dug mdor na bod 'bangs rnams lung gi chos la yid ches par bya ba'i phyir/ khro bo dkyil du nad pa dang / sman pa dang / mo ma rnams dang
/ bon bos shwa ba nam mkha' la 'gro shes pa sprul nas/ nad brtag pa dang / de la khrom rnams ngo mtshar skyes pas/ da ltar gyi nad pa 'di 'dra rnams las/ ches na ba'i ngan
song gsum dang / 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal brjod pas yid ma ches/ spre'u'i gyad ha nu man tha'i sgrung bshad nas bod kyi rigs rgyud dang / las kyi 'bras bu sangs rgyas kyi
gsungs pa mdo sde dang sbyar bas yid ches/ bslab pa gsum la 'god pa'i phyir/ bon byas nad pa gso las phan che ba'i bslab pa gsum gyi yon tan sangs rgyas kyi rgya gar du
mdzad pa bcu gnyis mdzad pa'i dod por/ rgyal pos ra sa'i gtsug lag khang dang / mdzad pa bcu gnyis bstan pa'i lo rgyus yod cing / khro bo sme brtsegs kyi rgyab na mchod
rten brgyad po bya ba yod do/ / de lta bu'i chos rgyal chen po 'di ni/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen po dngos yin par grags zhing / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i srol legs po gtod
nas/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa gnyis bzhes pa sa pho khyi lo shar ba'i stod la/ spyi dgos su zhal gdams mang du gsungs zhing / der rting rgyal po dang / bal bza' khri btsun/
rgya bza' kong jo yab yum gsum gar 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang byang mar/ rang byon bcu gcig zhal gyi thugs khar thims so/ /rgyas par bka' chems bka' khol mar blta
bar bya'o/ /'ga' re rgyal po 'phan yul zal mo sgang du grongs zer ba 'dug ste/ blon po sna chen po dang se ru gung ston la sogs/

gros la dbang ba rnams kyi bod 'bangs byin po spro ba bsring ba'i phyir du re zhig zal mo sgang du snyung ba skad dang / sku gshegs pa'i tshul byas par byed do/ /rgya bza'
kong jo lcags mo glang lo la rgya nag nas byon/ bod yul du lo lnga bcu rtsa brgyad bzhugs par byed do/ /srong btsan bang so 'phyongs rgyas mda' ru btab/ /che chung tshad
ni dpag chen mda' rgyang gang / /nang na lha khang lnga yang byas so so skad/ /bang so nang rgyan can du grags pa yin/ /bang so gru bzhir brtsigs pa de nas byung / /ming
la smug ri smug po legs so skad/ /rje de dang / mon bza' khri lcam gyi sras/ gung srong gung btsan/ blon po ni/ mang po rje zhang snang dang / snubs btsan do res byas/ chab
srid lo lnga bzung / dgung lo bco brgyad pa la 'das nas/ slar yang yab kyi rgyal srid bzung ba phyed mar bgrang skad/ gung srong bang so don mkhar mda' ru brtsigs/ /gral
ni gnam ri srong btsan g.yon na yod/ / ming ni gung sri gung chen legs so skad/ /rje de dang / sha bza' kong jo mo rje'i sras/ mang srong mang btsan lo bcu gsum nas/ mes
po 'das/ lo bco lnga'i bar la srid bzung / blon po mgar stong btsan yul zung dang / 'chi mas 'das gnyer gyi byas/ lo nyi shu rtsa bdun pa la gtsang gi bang snang du 'das
so/ /mang srong bang so srong btsan g.yon na yod/ ming sdong shar sral po bya ba lags/ rje de dang 'gros khri se khri ma lod kyi sras/ 'dus srong mang po rje rlung nam
'phrul gyi rgyal po ni/ chu mo bya lo ba ste/ ma 'khrungs gong tsam du yab 'das/ 'khrungs 'phral nas dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu'i bar la srid bzung / 'di'i ring la bod du
rol mo'i rnam grangs mang po 'byung ba'i snga ltas la/ rtsal po che mi bdun byung ba

ni/ ar po ldong btsan gyis seng ge dkar mo'i gnya' ba nas bzung byung skad/ mon khri bzang gi stag dar ma gnyis lcags thag gi sprel nas ngar sgras lung pa bkang ste khrid byung
skad/ lho don dam yang dag 'phags kyis/ seng ldeng gi gdung chen po bcu gsum gyi steng du/ gong dza la lcags dos gcig rgyab nas khur byung skad/ lcog ro zangs dkar gyis/
lha sa'i rdo ring rked la btsugs nas yo ga yo gin khur byung skad/ rngog rings nag pos bal yul nas glang po che'i phrug gu zhig gson por / khur byung skad/ mgos shag
byung gis/ sha ba yu mo'i blud bu tshwas rgyangs nas klad la dbyug gin byung skad/ smon rgyal mtshan rnam grags kyis/ mig mthong gsum de mda' rgyang gang res sleb cing /
gtsang po la phar mchongs tshur mchongs byed kyin sleb byung skad do/ /rgyal po 'di snyung ba'i dus gcig bya yid du 'ong ba gcig gis sngar ma mthong ba'i shing gi yal 'dab
nyung shas zhig pho brang gi rtser khyer byung ba/ ci yin brtag pas/ rje'i zhal skyems la phan par byung ba la brten nas/ blon 'bangs blo kha nye shos rnams kyis/ phyogs
bcur btsal bas sngar bod na med pa'i ja shing rnyed/ de 'thung ba'i snod la/ bod dkar byang skya dar tshe bya ba bzos pa lags/ bzang ngan gyi dbye ba drug te/ bzang shos
sham tshe la/ bya kha na shing khyer gyi ri mo yod/ de 'og lab tshe la/ mtsho nang nya dang bcas pa yod/ de 'og shang tshe la/ spang ri sha ba dang bcas pa'i ri mo yod/
theg tshe/ deb tshe/ rdo tshe gsum ni phal dkar ste/ ri mo med pa'am/ me tog la sogs sna tshogs yod/ ja dang dkar yol gyi sngon ma de nas byung bar byed do/ /rgyal po 'di'i
ring la bod ma yin pa'i 'jang yul la

sogs rgyal khams mang po 'og tu bcug mnga' thang che bar byung / dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu pa la 'jang yul du 'das/ spur gnyer lcog gru khung khri zhes bya bas byas so/ /'phrul
rgyal bang so mang srong g.yon na yod/ ming ni seng ges brtsigs pa can no skad/ /bang so 'di nyid lcags ris bskor nas yod/ /de ni hor gyi mi sdes bcigs so skad/ /der
rje dang mchims bza' btsan la me tog gi sras/ khri lde gtsug brtan mes ag tshom du grags pa de/ lcags pho 'brug lo pho brang ldan dkar du 'khrungs/ de'i lo gzhug la yab
'das/ srid bzung blon po sba skyes bzang stong btsan dang / mchims rgyal gzugs/ skyi sho ting 'gro chu bzang hor mang gsum gi byas/ de yang mes srong btsan gyi lung bstan/
zhal chems su bzhag pa de nga yin snyam du dgongs nas/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba dang / sangs rgyas zhi ba spyan drangs/ theg chen gyi mdo lnga dang / de bzhugs pa'i
brag dmar mgrin bzang / brag dmar ka chu/ lha sa 'khar braga'aphying bu nam ral/ ma sa gong dang / lha khang lnga bzhengs/ rgya nag ke shang nas mdo gser 'od dam pa dang
/ mdo las rnam 'byed bsgyur/ bi ji tsan pa shi las/ sman dpyad bsgyur/ 'di'i ring la pho brang 'phying nga stag rtse nas g.yu rdog chen po gcig rnyed do/ /des btsun mo
'jang bza' khri btsun khab tu bzhes pa la| sras shin tu mtshar ba gcig btsas pa las/ 'jang tsha lha dbon du btags/ de'i khab tu 'os pa bod na med pas/ rgya nag rgya rje
wing 'jung zher gyi sras mo/ kim shing kong jo blangs/ kong jo ma slebs pa la/ gnyags khri bzang 'don gyi bu mo ma blangs pa la ko long byas nas/ 'jang tsha gnyags kyis

bkrongs so/ / ljang tsha lha dbon bang so yab kyi mdun/ zlam por brtsigs nas yod skad do/ / der yab dang / kong jo 'dus pa'i sras/ khri srong lde btsan ni/ mes srong btsan
sgam po 'khrungs rting / lo brgya dang bdun cu don bzhi song ba'i lcags pho rta lo la/ brag dmar du sku bltams/ yab ni dgung lo drug cu rtsa gsum pa la ya 'brag sbal tshan
khar 'das so/ /ag tshom bang so mu ra ri la brtsigs/ gral ni 'phrul gyi rgyal po'i g.yon na yod/ ming ni lha ri gtsug nam bya ba lags/ khri srong lde btsan dgung lo bcu
gsum pa la/ yab 'das te/ rgyal srid lo bzhi bcu rtsa gsur bzung / 'di ni 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sprul par grags zhing / 'dis dam pa'i chos dar zhing rgyas par mdzad pa'i
tshul ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ khyad par de'i dgung lo 'ga' zhig gi bar la/ sdig blon ma shang khron pa skyes kyis gros ston nas/ sngar phan rgyal rgyud sku tshe thung
ba la sogs pa rnams chos khrims byas pas lan pa yin/ da bar chad zlog thabs la bod kyi lugs bzhin sus ma byas pa la 'chad pa byed zer nas/ lha shAkya mu ne bye thebs su
bcug pa dang / mang yul du skyel ba dang / dkon gnyer ha shang rgan po rgya nag la bskrod pa dang / 'bangs gum pa la dge rtsa mi gtong ba la sogs pa'i khrims bu chung bcas/
bstan pa la gnod pa'i bya ba mang po byas 'dug pa thams cad rgyal bu rgyal sar ston 'phral nas bkag ma zhang khron pa skyes gson dur du bcug jo bo mang yul nas gdan drangs/
dam chos dar bar byas pa dang / bsam yas kyi lha khang bzhengs par 'dod nas/ bod 'bangs rnams shed gcog par bya ba'i phyir/ khyed rnams kyi ngas 'dod pa'i las/

gdam ga bzhi yod pas 'di rnams gang rung zhig byed dam/ lha khang zhig bzhengs gsung pas/ lha khang bdams nas/ rgyal pos dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gcig lon nas stag gi lo la sba
ye shes dbang po 'am/ dba'as gsal snang la sogs rnams za hor gyi yul nas/ mkhan po bo dhi sa twa spyan 'dren pa la btang / phebs nas/ bsam yas gtsug lag khang gi rmangs
bting bas/ bod kyi lha srin rnams phrag dog che bar byung nas/ dba'as mang po rje dang / seng gho lha lung gnyis/ u rgyan gyi slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ bal yul yang le
shod kyi brag phug nas spyan 'dren du btang / dam chen gyis bskul nas/ slob dpon mang yul nas tshur 'byon pa dang mjal/ bsus nas rgyal po yon mchod mjal sar/ slob dpon
gyis nga che nga gnyan gyi mgur gsungs pa/ klu rgyal mal gro pa la klu gter bcug lha srin thams cad dam la btags nas lha khang bzhengs pas/ nyin mo las mtshan mo mgyogs par
brtsigs/ zur phud dbu mtshal klu yis shing phul/ der rgya gar o tan ta pu ri'i gtsug lag khang la dpe blangs nas bsam yas dbu rtse rigs gsum ri rab kyi tshul du byas/
khor sa phyi nang rim pa bdun du byas/ gling chen po bzhi/ gling phran bgyod/ nyi zla gnyis rnam sa kyi lha khang thams cad/ mdo rgyud sde snod gsum dang mthun par/ phyi
lcags ri zur mangs 'khor gdugs dang bcas pa rgyal pos bka' gnang nas bzhengs/ btsun mo dam pa dkar rgyal mtsho me tog sgron gyis/ khams gsum zangs khang gling / 'bro bza'
byang chub sgron gyis dge rgyas bye ma gling / pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun gyis/ bu tshal gser khang gling / yum gyim shang kong jos/ dam pa'i

shing khang rtse dgu bzhengs/ blon po chen po shud bu dpal seng dang / rgyal tsha lha stsang / stag sgra klu gong / mchims rdo rje spre chung rnams kyis mchod rten chen po
bzhi bzhengs/ de rnams shing pho stag lo spyir zla ra ba'i tshes bdun/ skar ma rgyal la 'gram bting nas/ la drug la thams cad 'byongs te/ sa mo lug la mkhan po bo dhi sa
twa dang / slob dpon padmas rab gnas mnga' gsol mdzad dus byang chub sems bskyed gling gi lha gtso bo rnam snang nam mkha' la 'phags pa la sogs/ ngo mtshar ba'i rnam 'phrul
mang du byung bas/ rgyal po thugs rab tu mnyes shing / blon 'bangs thams cad ngo mtshar dad mos tshugs par gyur te/ dpal gyi bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyi grub pa'i gtsug
lag khang zhes par mtshan gsol/ rgyal pos rje'i dga' glu bcu gsum bya ba dang / blon po chen po rnams gyi skyid pa'i dpal dgu la sogs pa mi res bkra shis pa'i glu re blangs/
brag dmar mtsho mo'i mgur/ me tog pad sdong rang 'khrungs lo bcu gsum gyi bar la skyid kyi bro mo che brdungs/ dga' ston rgya chen po byas/ de nas lha khang rnams kyi
dkon gnyer byed mkhan dgos pa byung nas/ des rken byas yon mchod bka' bgros te/ sba gsal snang dang / dba'as khri bzher/ ba gor bai ro tsa na/ ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs/
'khon klu yi dbang po srung ba/ rma a tsarya rin chen mchog gtsang legs grub rnams la/ btsun pa byar rung mi rung nyams sad pas/ khyad par du 'phags pa byung bas/
bod kyi btsun pa la snga ba sad mi mi bdun du grags pa byung / de rnams la ska ba dpal brtsegs la sogs/ lo tsA ba brgya rtsa brgyad slob tu bcug de rnams la cog ro klu'i
rgyal

mtshan dang / zhang ban de ye shes sde la sogs/ lo tsA ba stong rtsa brgyad slob tu bcug nas/ mtshan nyid kyi chos dar bar byas shing / lug lo la dge 'dun de rnams mkhan po'i
chos lugs bzhin yod par smra ba'i sde tshugs/ rgya gar nas dbu ma'i dge slong bcu gnyis gdan drangs nas/ dbu ma bye brag tu smra ba'i sde btsugs/ dam chos dar zhing rgyas
par byas la/ lo gcig gi bar la chos mang po bsgyur te/ mkhan po'i zhal nas bod du mu stegs mi 'byung gis/ bstan pa 'di la gnyis su gyes nas rtsod par 'gyur te mthar rtsod
pa phyogs gcig zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes lung bstan/ der rting mkhan po bo dhi sa twa'i dbu la chibs pa'i 'phra phog nas mya ngan las 'das/ spur bsam yas has po ri'i rtse
la mchod rten brtsigs nas bzhugs so/ /slob dpon padma 'byung gnas kyi spyir bod yul du mi lo lnga bcu rtsa bzhi bzhugs te/ lha klu gdug pa can thams cad dam la btags/
sa gzhi gnas gangs brag mang po gnas chen du byin gyis brlabs/ chos gter nor gter bsam gyis mi khyab pa sbas/ gsang sngags la yang lo tsA ba sad mi mi drug bya ba byung
te/ gnubs nam mkha'i snying po/ 'dre rgyal ba blo gros/ ru gong birya rtsa/ gru gu u pe sha dpal rlangs kyi seng ge lang gro dkon mchog seng ge rnams kyi blon po la gsang
sngags kyi chos skor ma lus pa zhus cing / sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms/ lce ku ku ra tsa la sogs pa'i/ lo tsA byas nas gsang sngags kyi rgyud sde mang po gsungs pa rnams
bsgyur to/ /gzhan yang gnyags ku mA ra dang / so zur snubs gsum/ mkhan po rdo rje rin chen la sogs/ dkyil 'khor bco brgyad du grags pa'i slob ma grub

thob mang du spel/ gsang sngags kyi bstan pa dar bar mdzad nas/ lho nub rnga yab gling la gshegs te/ lha sras mu ne [tig]btsan pos thog drangs bod kyi blon 'bangs mang pos
mang yul gung thang gi la khar skyel ma byas/ la thog tu padma bka' chems su grags pa'i zhal gdams gsung nas/ nyi ma'i 'od zer lachibs te/ zangs mdog dpal ri'i gzhal yas
khang du byon/ da lta srin po'i kha gnon mdzad cing / 'chi med tshe'i rig 'dzin brnyes pa'o/ / yang bod kyi dge slong mi lnga/ tshe 'di la sangs rgyas pa'i chos 'tshol du
rgya gar la btang / bai ro tsa nas chos lon no/ /yang tshe gcig la 'tshang rgya ba'i chos 'dod gsung na sa/ rgyal po indra bo dhi'i mchod gnas/ mkhas pa bi ma la mi ta gdan
'dren pa la/ ka cog gnyis dang / rma rin chen mchog btang / kha che'i yul du mjal/ bsus nas yon mchod mjal dus rgyal blon rnams la/ slob dpon 'di phyi pa gcig yin pa
'dra snyam pa'i log lta byung ba la/ lha rnam snang dang / rgyal po la phyag 'tshal grabs byas pas/ log lta sel dad mos che bar byung cing / gdams pa mang du zhus so/ /yang
rgya nag ha shang 'dul ba la/ paNDi ta ka ma la shI la gdan drangs nas/ rtsod du bcug pas ha shang pham nas/ rgya nag la bros sar lham ya gcig lus pas/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus
phyi mor/ bod du nga'i lta ba 'dzin pa 'ga' re yong ba 'dug zer ro/ /slob dpon ka ma la shI las sgom rim gsum brtsams nas rgyal po la phul/ gang zag las dag pa rnams ni/
ka ma la shI la'i chos lugs dang / lta ba la zhugs pa'o/ /yang sing gha la'i blo dpon dha na shI la sogs/ paNDi ta mkhas pa mang po gdan drangs nas/

rang rang gi yul skad dang mthun pa'i bstan bcos gsung tshad thams cad/ mkhas pa bai ro tsa na/ ka cog zhang gsum la sogs/ rgya bod kyi lo tsA ba rnams kyi rim par bsgyur/
mdo rgyud man ngag 'chad nyan sgom sgrub kyi bstan pa nyi mo ltar gsal bar mdzad cing / yang ya rabs kyi skye bo pho mo brgya bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis dus gcig la rab tu byung
te/ shar du dga' ldan lha phug lhor stag tshang seng ge phug nub tu brag dmar po thon/ byang du arya pa lo'i phug dang bzhir sgom grwa chen po yang btsugs/ mkhas grub chen
po bzhi'i rtse gcig gi sgrub pa mdzad cing bskyangs so/ /yang jo mo 'bro bza' byang chub sgron gyi sku tshe'i smad la g.yas ru smad kyi lha khang dang rgyal bu mu tig
btsan pos/ shangs su mtshal gyi lha khang / jo mo dkar rgyal mtsho me tog sgron gyis/ sku tshe'i smad la dpal chu bo ri'i lha khang bzhengs/ mchims bza' lha mo btsan dang
/ mkhar chen bza' mtsho rgyal gnyis kyi sgrub pa mdzad pas/ lha khang phyag rjes med do/ /sba ye shes dbang po la sogs chos blon rnams kyi yang lha khang mang du bzhengs
so/ /chos rgyal de'i ring la gso byed sman gyi rig pa yang dar bar mdzad la/ de yang bod du sman dpyad bsgyur ba'i dus gsum byung ni/ dang po chos rgyal srong btsan sgam
po'i ring la/ gso ba rig pa'i dbu brnyes/ lha sras khri srong lde btsan gyi ring la/ srol gtod/ lha bla ma byang chub 'od kyi ring la sman dar zhing rgyas par mdzad zer
la/ chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan gyi bka' gnang / lo tsA ba bai ro tsa nas phyogs thams cad kyi sman pa spyan drangs nas/ rgya gar shanti gar bha la sogs kyis bod du bsgyur
nas/ spyir sman pa la mkhas par grags pa dgu bcu rtsa

gnyis byung / de'i nang nas dar byed kun tu grags pa'i sman pa bzhi bcu rtsa lnga/khyad par rgyal po'i bla sman du bskos pa dgu ni/ stod na bi ji che rdzi 'ug pa gsum/ bar
na mi nyag brang ti g.yu thog gsum smad na gnya' dang 'thab zhi stod dang gsum/ /zhes bya ba'i drang srong sprul pa mkhas btsun ldan pa'i sman pa rim par byung ste/ rgyal
po'i lung gis/ nga ni kun gyi lha yin la/ /'di dag nga yi rje yin pas/ /kun gyi lha rjer mtshan gsol la/ /mchod cing bkur sti'i gnas su bstan/ /gsungs pa'i 'phrin gyi dril
bsgrags so/ /rje de'i blon po ni/ mgos khri bzang yab lhag dbas rgyal to re/ khri gsum rjes stag sna/ gnyags stag btsan ldong gzigs la sogs pas/ mdzangs kyi las thabs
byas/ zhang rje rgyal gzigs dang / stag sgra klu gong gis phyi dgra btul/ rgya'i bkra shis khri sgo phab pa la sogs kyi lo rgyus phyis rdo ring la yod do/ khri gsum rje stag
snas/ rgya dang gru gu 'jang gsum gyi mol 'dum byas/ rgya bod mtshams su bod kyi dpa' bo mi dgu'i 'go byas/ skye 'dus kyi dmag dpung so kha srung ba la bzhag pas/ bka'
