ma log zer ba'i bod 'brog gi sde mang po chags pas/ mtha' dmag bod du mi 'jug pa sogs/ sprul pa'i chos rgyal chen po 'di ni/ rgyu mtshan du ma'i sgo nas/ bod la bka' drin
shin du che'o/ /'di'i dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa drug bzhes pa/ shing mo glang gi lo la zur mkhar du sku gshegs so/ /khri srong lde btsan bang so mu ra ri la yod/ /ming ni
'khrul ri gtsug snang bya ba yin/ /bang so phyi rgya can zhes bya bar grags/ /'di'i rtsa na rdo ring yi ge bris pa zhig kyang yod/ rje de dang / tshe yong bza' dkar rgyal
me tog sgron gyi

sras bzhi la/ gcen mu khri btsan po sku gzhon nu la gshegs nas bang so med do/ /de 'og mu ne btsan po chu pho stag la brag dmar du 'khrungs/ lo gcig zla dgu rgyal sa bzung/
yab kyi dus mchod la/ tshul 'jug gis zla ba la bsam yas su mdo sde mchod pa dang / cho 'phrul zla ba la 'dul ba'i mchod pa btsugs// bod 'bangs byin po'i dbul phyug theng
gsum snyoms kyang / rang rang gi sbyin shugs yin par dgongs/ mngon pa'i mchod pa 'dzugs rtsis la sogs/ khrims gnyis dar bar mdzad pa'i dgongs pa yod na'ang / dgung lo nyi
shu rtsa dgu pa la dug gis bkrongs so/ /'khrul chen mu ne btsan po'i bang so ni/ /ag tshom bang so'i mdun ngos g.yas na yod/ /ming ni lha ri ldem bu bya ba yin/ / de'i
'og mu tig[rug]btsan pos/ zhang rgya tsha lha snang bsad pas/ de tshang gi g.yo thabs kyi bkrongs so/ /mu tig [rug]btsan po'i bang so don mkhar mda' na yod/ /ming ni skya
rengs ldem pa lags so skad/ /gcung po khri lde srong btsan/ shing pho 'brug la brag dmar du 'khrungs/ lo bzhi pa la btsan po 'das nas/ khong la rgyal srid bskos pa'i nyams
sad pa'i phyir/ khri steng du bzhugs/ dbu la nor bu'i gtsug rgyan gsol bas/ ljid ma theg par mjing pa yon tsam byung na'ang / bkra shis pa'i rtags mang du byung bas/ sad
na legs mjing yon zhes pa'i mtshan chags/ rgyal srid lo sum cu rtsa gnyis bzung / blon po sa mang rje ldang ldong dang / sgra rgyal mtshon skong gi byas/paNDi ta bi ma
la mi tra dang / ka ma la shI la/ dznyA na se na/ bal po hUM ka ra rnams spyan drangs/ lo tsA ba 'khon klu'i dbang po srung ba la sogs pa rnams kyi sngar

skad sna tshogs kyi bsgyur ba'i chos thams cad/ rgya gar bstan pa'i 'byung khungs yin pas/ rgya gar gyi skad zhe gcig tu bsgyur/ bod skad gsar bcad kyi gtan la phab/ snga so'i
yab mes rim pas lha khang mang du bzhengs 'dug gi ngas ni 'dzam bu'i gling du che tshad thub pa'i lha khang zhig bzhengs par 'dod pas/ nyi ma tsam dang zla ba tsam dang
/ skar chen gyi tshad tsam bzhengs pas/ sa dmigs tshol cig gsungs pa la blon 'bangs byings po'i blo la ma chud de/ chu dang brag gi bkag nas de 'dra shong sa bod yul na
ni mi bdog zer ba rim par zhus pas/ 'o na skar ma chung shos kyi tshad rgyang grags yin zer ba de tsam zhig bzhengs so gsungs nas/ skar chung rdo rje dbyings gyi lha khang
bzhengs/ rab byung thams cad kyi 'tsho ba sbyar/ lha sa dang bsam yas la sogs su bshad grwa bcu gnyis/ yer pa dang mchims phu la sogs su sgom grwa bcu gnyis btsugs/ stangs
'bul 'bul drug sems phyogs gnyis su byas nas dam chos dar zhing rgyas par mdzad/ lha sa'i khyam phra bzos/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa bzhi pa me mo bya lo la sbrags kyi
phur 'das so/ /rgyal chen bang so 'phrul rgyal mdo na yod/ /yum gyi chab gang skong pas nang gi mthong / /ming ni rgyal chen 'phrul rigs lags so skad/ /de'i mdun na yi ge
yig tshang bris pa'i rdo ring zhig kyang yod do/ /	rje de dang 'bro bza' mang po rje'i sras lnga la/ gtsang ma/ dar ma/ ral pa can/ lhun rje/ lhun grub rnams las/ gtsang
ma chos la dga' ches/ dar ma sdig la dga' ches pas rgyal sar ma bskos/ lhun rje lhun grub gnyis gzhon nu la 'das pas bang so med do/ /

bar pa ral pa can ni mes khri srong lde btsan 'khrungs nas/ lo bdun cu don drug song ba'i/ me pho khyi lo la 'u shang rdor sku 'khrungs lo bcu gnyis pa'i dus blon po rnams
gros byas nas/ rgyal sar bskos srid lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i bar la bzung / blan po bran kha dpal yon dang / 'bro khri bzung rams shags/ 'dre khri rje stag snang gsum gyi byas/
rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / su landra bo de pra dznya dhe ba/ shinting gar bha rnams spyan drangs/ lo tsA ba ban de ye shes sde la sogs pa mang pos dag
ther legs par mdzad/ sngar ma bsgyur ba rnams kyang bsgyur/ 'u shang rdor dpal dpe med bkra shis dge 'phel gyi gtsug lag khang rgya phibs dgu brtsegs khyung nam mkha' lding
ba 'dra ba bzhengs/ yab mes kyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs par dam bcas nas/ ma 'byongs pa rnams gsos/ rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar lha khang dang / sha chu sdong btsan gyi
mtsho dkyil du/ lcags kyi sdong po'i steng du/ sangs rgyas stong gi lha khang dang / glang yul du/ ring po gsum par/ sle'u 'phrul gyi kre'i dang 'og tu/ ka brag dkon mchog
'byung gnas/ 'o du byams chen lha khang / nyang ro rtsig sna gsar du lha khang khrab sgo can rnams bzhengs/ btsun mo cog ro bza' dpal gyi ngang tshul las/ btsan thang
g.yu'i lha khang dang / nya bza' mchog lha mos/ smon 'gro stag mtshal gyi lha khang bzhengs/ gcen dar mas 'dre'i lha khang dang / de'i gcen mo btsan po 'phan gyi/ yar klungs
su dpag bsam ljon shing dang / phug po che'i lha khang dang / mkhas btsun sngags pa dang / btsun chen rnams kyi/ brag lha mgon po dang / yer pa yang g.yan dang / nyang
ting 'dzin bzhi'i lha khang dang / bran ka dpal

yon gyi g.yas mtshal dang / dam yul me long thang / ka ba dpal brtsegs kyis ka ba yul sna/ tshe spongs stag bzang rab mdos/ stong lung lhag ma/ tshe spongs lha bzang klu dpal
gyis/ bo dong bya rgod shong kyi lha khang rnams bzhengs so/ /lar ni 'di yan la bod kyi rgyal blon rnams kyi rgya bod du/ gtsug lag khang stong rtsa brgyad bzhengs par
'dod do/ /chos rgyal de ni sngon sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan par byed cing / phyag na rdo rje'i sprul par grags/ 'phrin las kyi gtso bo dam chos la spyod/ dkon mchog mchod/
tshogs gnyis kyi nor gsog rgyal khrims chos bzhin du skyong / rab tu byung ba re re la/ 'bangs mi khyim bdun bdun phul/ 'tsho ba sbyar bkur sti dang phud dud bgyis/ bstan
pa'i gshed dang / mnga' thang skyed yab mes kyi ring la chab 'og tu ma chud pa'i/ shar phyogs rgya nag po dbang du 'dus/ spo lon shan dar dkar gyis yol ba bkrams pa
'dra ba la gtugs/ nub phyogs stag gzig gi so mtshams/ stag sha dung gi sgo mo 'dra ba dang / byang phyogs hor gyi so mtshams/ bye ma rkang ring nya yi rgyab 'dra ba dang
/ lho phyogs mon lta la wa ta'i shel gyi dum bu 'dra ba/ de rnams la gtugs shing 'dzam bu gling gi sum gnyis dbang du 'dus par byed do/ /bod rgyal po'i mnga' thang che shos
la byung bar gda'o/ /de'i dus tsa na khyim ni bag gro/ mi ni khong dal/ phyugs ni lo dang zla ba na sdud/ mi nyal nyi ma klong / 'bri yan sna med/ rta yan sgrog med/ sgo
la khyi med/ rje byams 'bangs gus/ grogs gzhung bzang / gnyen sha tsha/ pho ni dpa'/ mo ni mdzangs la chas bzang / bod 'bangs byings po bde skyid la longs spyod/ sangs
rgyas kyi bstan pa ches dar

zhing rgyas par mdzad pa na/ sku drin shin tu che'o/ /'di yan chod la skyid pa'i gdung rabs phyed dang bcu dang / shin tu skyid pa'i gdung rabs phyed dang lnga zer ro/ /phyed
po ni chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po dang / mes ag tshom gyi sras gzhon nu la 'das nas/ rgyal srid bskyar ya re bzung ba la zer ro/ /	der rting nag po'i phyogs dar tu
nye ba dang / bod spyi mthun gyi bsod nams 'gribs pas/ rje la btsun mo/ cog ro bza' dpal gyi ngang tshul ma dang / mchims bza' skar rgyal/ sna nam bza' mang mo khong legs/
nyang bza' mchog gi lha mo/ tshe spong bza' mthor rgyal ma dang lnga yod kyang srid ma zin/ rgyal po'ang ha cang chos la dad ches pas/ sba stag sna la sogs sdig blon rnams
kyi ban chen po bkums/ lha sras gtsang ma gro mor spyugs/ btsun mo dam pa dang / bran kha dpal yon nyes med la skyon phab/ rgyal po nyid kyang dgung la so drug pa shing
mo bya la/ cog ro legs sgra dang / lha gdong gtsang gi mang gro zhang gi lha khang gi rdo skas la tsud [bzhud]pa'i tshe/ ral gris btsabs nas bkrongs so/ /khu chen ral
pa can gyi bang so ni/ don mkhar mda'i g.yon gyi phyogs na yod/ ming ni khri steng rmang ri legs so skad/ de'i rtsa na rdo ring yi ge med pa zhig kyang yod/ da de ltar na
rgyal po la sras med/ lha khang la mnga' gsol ba med/ rdo ring la yi ge med zer/ de yan chad la mu ne btsan po the ba'i/ rgyal sar bzhugs pa bzhi cu rtsa gnyis byung ngo
/ /rje 'bangs skyid pa'i nyi ma 'de ba'i dus yin no/ /gcen po glang dar ma chu mo lug lo ba yin/ so dgu lon pa'i dus na khri ral bkrongs nas/ khong pas rgyal srid bzung
/ lo

gnyis rgyal po tshul bzhin bzung / chu mo phag gi lo gzhug nas thugs la gdon gsol ba dang / blon po rgyal to re/ stag sna can la sogs sdig la dga' ba rnams kyi bsgyur nas/
sngar nu bo la rgyal srid bskos pa'i snying gnad byas/ bod du sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsnubs/ lo phyed dang bzhir sdig rgyal kho na byas/ lo zhe bzhi pa me pho stag lo'i
dus/ yer pa'i lha ri snying po na/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje gab nas rtse gcig tu sgrub pa la yod pa/ lha mo nag mos bskul nas/ lha sa'i rdo ring rtsa ru/ lha lung dpal
gyi rdo rje rgyal po bkrongs nas bros so/ /de dus rgyal po na re/ nga yang na sgrol ba lo gsum gyi phyis/ yang na lo gsum gyi sngas zer/ sdig rgyal de'i rkyen gyis/ chu mo
phag nas me pho rta'i bar lo drug cu rtsa brgyad tsam/ bod du dam chos snub 'dug dar ma'i bang so 'khrul dang rgyal chen bar na yod/ de'i ming ni bang rim 'khor lo can
zer ste/ rtsig 'phro la lus so skad/ glang dar ma la smad kyi steng zer ro/ /'di man chad smad sil bur song / dar ma grongs rting btsun mo che bas bu chung gcig btsal nas
mdang mo rang la skyes pa'i bu yin byas pas/ yum ka brtan du chug zer nas/ yum brtan byung / des dbu ru bzung / chun ma la lto bor gyi sras gcig yod pa/ mar me'i 'od la
srung bas 'od srung byung / des g.yon ru bzung / dbu g.yor 'khrug pa byas/ rgyal rigs gcig la phyogs rigs gnyis su gyes/ blon po khu theg sbrangs shang srid dang / rngog
pas sum sgra rje yab dang / rdog rgyal lto ro gel pa rnams kyi byas/ rgyal blon de rnams bsod nams chung bas/ sa mo glang la khengs log byung / me mo bya la bang so rnams
bshig rje 'bangs bye/ rgyal khrims zhig

chos khrims nyams/ phyi'i so kha shor/ bod nang 'khrugs/ glang dar mas bstan pa bsnubs pa'i 'go tshugs nas/ dbus gtsang gi mi drug gam bcu'i mdo smad du rab tu byung nas/ bsam
yas su/ bod rgyal tsha la na yab sras kyi spyan sngar slebs pa yan/ lo drug cu rtsa brgyad kyi bar la/ spyir bod dang / sgos dbus gtsang ru bzhir/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan
pa'i sgra mi grags pa byung te/ sdom pa 'bogs lan gyi bka' chad/ gtsug lag khang rnams wa khyi'i tshang bcas/ tsher phung skyes/ bshas ra lud khang byas/ lder bzo la sprang
po'i sba zom bkal/ mi dge ba'i las thabs sna tshogs byung bas/ glang dar ma yab sras ni bod khams rnams la bka' drin shin tu chung ngo / /yum brtan dgung lo sum cu
so drug la 'das te/ bang so med do/ /'od srung ni shing lo lug gi lo la pho brang yum bur btsas pa ste/ sum cu rtsa dgu la/ yar lung 'phan mdar 'das so/ /'od srung bang so
'phrul gyi rgyab na yod/ /ming ni skye'u lha bstan lags so skad/ de phyin chad bang so brtsigs pa yang nub bo/ /bstan pa phyis dar gyi byung tshul ni/ glang dar mas bstan
pa bsnubs pa'i tshe/ dpal chu bo ri nas 'jad pa gtsang rab gsal dang / bo dong pa g.yo dge 'byung / stod lung pa dmar shAkya mu ne gsum gyis/ 'dul ba'i po ti dre'u rgyab
khal gcig bkal nas/ mnga' ris la bros gar log la phyin/ lo tsA ba med pas 'gro don ma byung ba hor yul bskor nas/ mdo smad an chung rnam rdzong / dan tig shel gyi lha
khang du slebs/ de phyogs rnams sdig rgyal dang thag 'gyangs shing / snying rus che bas chos kyi brda mtshon tsam yang 'dug pa dang /

bon rgan dmu zu gsal bzang bya ba'i tsha bu/ dmu zu rab gsal 'bar bya ba/ lo bco lnga pa gcig khongs rnams la dad nas/ gtsang gi mkhan po gsol g.yos slob dpon byas te/ dge
tshul zhus pa'i ming / dge ba rab gsal du btags so/ /'di'i skabs su lha sar/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rjes sdig rgyal bsad nas bros pa'ang / mdo smad du khong rnams 'dzoms pa'i
dge ba rab gsal bsnyen rdzogs byed pa la/ sngar gyi mkhan slob dang / dmar gyi gsang ston byas/ lha lung dpal rdor gyi rgyal po bsad pas kha skong mi rung zer/ rgya'i
ha shang ke wang dang / gyi wan bya ba btsal nas/ de rnams kyi drung du bsnyen rdzogs byas/ ming dgongs pa rab gsal du grags zhing / des bstan pa'i me ro smad nas bslang
zhes zer ro/ /der rting lo lnga nas/ bla chen dgongs pa rab gsal gyis mkhan po mdzad/ spang gong ye shes g.yung drung dang / par rin gsal/ 'al rdo rje dbang phyug snubs
rakshi ta/ jo bo ye shes seng ge cog ro shes rab byang chub rnams/ dge tshul sgrub tu bcug pa/ mkhan slob cha ma tshang bas/ bla chen gyi slob ma la snga ba khams kyi zog
po mi drug bya bar grags pa byung / bla chen gyi bka' rtags kyi phyag rgya bzhi bya ba yang de rnams la byas par byed de/ bzhi ni zhwa theb kyi mu thum dang / bla gos kyi
mtha' mtshams dang / tor bu/ ka pa la'i nang rnams sngon por mdzad pa/ bla chen dang po bon po'i rgyud par song bas/ thugs zhen gyi brda mtshon yin zer bar 'dug de rnams
kyi rgyu mtshan/ bsam yas nas yum brtan gyi rgyal rgyud/ mnga' bdag tsha la na yab sras kyi gsan nas/ dbus gtsang gi mi drug mdo smad du chos 'tshol ba la btang ba ni/

dbus nas klu mes shes rab tshul khrims/ 'bring ye shes yon tan/ gtsang nas tshong btsun shes rab seng ge lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug dang bzhi pos/ bla chen dngos la sdom pa
blangs/ rba btsun blo gros dbang phyug dang / rakshi tshul khrims 'byung gnas/ sum pa ye shes 'byung gnas gsum pos/ grum snubs gnyis la sdom pa blangs te/ de rnams la rba
rag gnyis po gcig tu dril bas/ mi drug zer ro/ /yang dbus pa gsum dang / gtsang pa gsum/ gtsang min dbus min gcig dang / mi bdun zer ba yang 'dug yang dbus gtsang gi mi
bcur byed pa yang yod pa ni/ klu me shes rab tshul khrims/ 'bring ye shes yon tan/ klan shes rab 'bar/ rba blo gros dbang phyug rakshi tshul khrims 'byung gnas rnams la
dbus pa mi lnga dang / lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug tshong btsun shes rab seng ge u pa lte dkar/ 'o brgyad spun gnyis rnams la/ gtsang pa mi lnga zer ba 'dug pa / rim pa
bzhin/ phyin pas mang du song pa yin nam snyam/ gang ltar yang khong rnams kyi sdom pa blangs chos mang du zhus nas/ yar yong dus bla chen gyi zhal nas/ klu mes btsun pas
mkhan po gyis/ lo ston mthu che bas bstan pa srungs shig tshong dge blo rno bas ston pa gyis/ 'bring kha bkod mkhas pas gzhi zung / thams cad kyi bstan pa dar ba'i khur
khur gsungs nas/ brdzangs pa bzhin khong rnams yar slebs nas/ rgyal po dang mjal/ bya dga' dang bkur sti chen po byas nas/ thog mar thams cad 'dzoms nas/ myang smad rgyan
gong gi lha khang bzhengs/ de rting dbus gtsang gi char/ rang rang so so nas khas len byas pa'i gtsug lag khang mang du bzhengs/ dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ dam pa'i chos

dar zhing rgyas par mdzad pas na/ bstan pa phyi dar la/ a mes bla chen dgongs pa rab gsal dang / slob ma dbus gtsang gi mi rnams/ sbyin bdag mnga' bdag tsha la na yab sras
dang bcas pa thog ma sku drin shin tu che ba lags/ rgyal po glang dar ma'i sras gnyis la gdung rgyud ji ltar byung na/ gcen yum brtan dang / pa tshab bza' bkra shis mtsho'i
sras/ khri lde mgon gnyen/ de'i sras khri lde rig pa mgon dang / nyi ma mgon dang / gcung de'i sras la/ nyi 'od dpal mgon de'i rgyud/ klung shod 'phan yul mdo khams na
mang ngo / /gcen po'i sras khri lde so dang / rdo rje 'bar lde so'i rgyud/ bug pa can dang / thang lha brag pa rnams so/ /rdo rje 'bar ba'i sras khri dbang phyug btsan/
de'i sras tsha la na ye shes rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras mnga' bdag khri pa yab sras/ 'di gnyis kyi dbus gtsang gi mi rnams mdo smad nas chos 'tshol ba la rim par brdzangs pa
dang / dge 'dun gyi sde/ lha khang bzhengs pa/ bsam yas chos mkho sgrub pa la sogs/ bod dbus gtsang gi bstan pa'i me ro gso ba'i bdag rkyen brjid khur che bar mdzad do/
khri pa'i sras a tsa ra dang / dge slong bla ma bo dhi rA dza rnams so/ /a tsa ra'i rgyud 'khrong po pa/ gtsang rgyab pa/ glags pa lam pa/ grib pa/ snye thang pa/ khum pa
btsad po la sogs pa'o/ /bla ma la rgyud med/ dge slong gi spel bzhi pa/ bo dhi rA dza'i rgyud/ lha btsun sngon mo/ gnyug rum pa/ lha 'bri sgang pa la sogs pa byung / da
lta 'on mdo chab thang btsad po rnams so/ /de rnams yum brtan gyi rgyud yin no/ khri lde 'od srung dang / cog ro bza' rgyal mo legs kyi sras/ mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan
shing mo bya la yar klungs 'phang mdar

'khrungs/ yab mes kyi mdzad spyod ngan pa bor nas/ myang smad sgrol bu'i sman lung la sogs gtsug lag khang brgyad bzhengs/ blon po spyang rgan a po dang / 'bro gtsug dgra lha
ldong gis byas/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa la/ gnyags stag rtse bas yar klungs shor por bkrongs so/ /'di pa dang yum brtan gyi sras/ khri lde mgon gnyan dang / tsha bo rig pa
mgon gyi ring la/ sa mo glang la khengs log dang / bang so bshig pa/ sku mkhar rtse nas 'bebs pa la sogs byung bar byed/ de'i btsun mo tshe spong bza' dkar rgyal g.yo rur
bzhag pa'i sras skyid lde nyi ma mgon/ chun ma dba' bza' 'phen rgyal/ dbu rur bzhag pa'i sras khri bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal lo/ /de gnyis kyi srid phal che ba yum brtan
tshang gis khyer bas/ sku mched gnyis rim pas mnga' ris stod phyogs la bros ste nyi ma mgon la/ sras dpal gyi mgon dang / bkra shis mgon/ lde gtsug mgon rnams byung ba
la/ stod kyi mgon gsum zer ro/ /yab skyid lde nyi ma mgon gyi sngon ma byon nas/ stod yul rnams mnga' 'og tu bsdus pas/ phyi ma la mnga' ris zer cing / sras che bas mar yul
dang / nub ral la mnga' byas/ bar pas zhang zhung dang spyi cog gnyis/ snyi gong ru thog gnyis/ pu rangs pa dang ya tshe gnyis/ drug la mnga' byed/ chung bas gar zha dang
/ zangs dkar la mnga' byed du bcug de nas mnga' ris skor gsum du grags so/ /bkra shis mgon sku mkhar nyi zangs su bzhugs so/ /sras 'khor re srong nge gnyis/ 'khor re'i
sras na ga rA dzadang / de ba rA dza'o/ /yab 'khor re'i sku tshe smad la yab mes kyi yig tshang gzigs pas thugs skyo nas/ gong ma'i phyag srol bzhin/ sangs rgyas

kyi bstan pa dar bar bzhed pa la/ rab tu byung ba'i mkhan po med par rten gyi drung du bslab nos te/ mtshan yang lha bla ma ye shes 'od ces bya ba ni/ 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud
nas lung bstan pa ltar ro/ /des mtho lding gser gyi lha khang bzhengs/ sras gnyis kyang rab tu byung te/ zhi ba 'od dang byang chub 'od/ yab sras de gnyis kyi ya rabs kyi
khye'u blo rno ba nyi shu rtsa gcig rab tu byung nas/ /kha cher chos 'tshol ba la btang bas/ gzhan bcu dgu tshad pas shi/ mdo sde las lung bstan pa'i g.yas ru gzhung pa/
lhung bzor rin chen bzang po la/ dge slong bya'i gdong pa can du grags pa de lo chen dang / yar 'brog mtsho'i 'gram pa/ ri nang pa legs pa'i shes rab kyi lo chung du gyur
pa de gnyis kyis lo tsA dang chos mkhas pa lobs nas tshur slebs/ lha bla ma la da lta rgya gar shar nub kun na/ jo bo di paM ka ra shrI dznya na las lhag pa mi 'dug zhus
pas/ cis kyang gdan 'drongs pa zhig byed gsungs nas/ gtsang stag tshal bas lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng dang nag tsho gnyis/ 'khor mang po dang bcas nas thebs su btang /lha
bla ma rang gi kyang rgyal srid gcung la gtad nas/ paNDi ta spyan 'dren pa'i cha rkyen gyi gser 'tshol ba la/ rgya gar mtha' 'khob la byon pas mu stegs rgyal pos btson
du bzung / de blu ba'i rtsis kyi bod 'bangs byin po la/ sras gnyis pos gser bsdus pas/ sku lus dang mnyam pa'i gser 'dus na'ang / dbu tsam zhig ma byung ba la rnyed nas
lha bla ma mu stegs pas bkrongs/ zhal chems la khyed rnams kyi byed lugs de ka yin te/ nga blus kyang nga rgas pas/ sems can la phan mi thogs/ gser rnyed pa rnams kyis jo
bo dang / paNDi ta mkhas pa

rnams gdan drongs/ mtho lding du mchod pa chen po shoms/ yab mes kyi bzhengs pa'i lha sa dang / bsam yas la sogs pa la zhig gsos gyis/ mdor na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar
ba'i thabs rtsol gyis shig gsungs nas bzhag 'dug de'i skabs su gcung srong nge'i sras/ lha ldes paNDi ta smr-i ti dang / phra la ring mo spyan drangs nas chos bsgyur rtsis
la/ lo tsA ba bal por pho log byung nas shi chos bsgyur mkhan ni med/ sngar shes pa rnams nyams su len mkhan ni yod de lo tsA med pas paNDi ta gnyis po bod du lo 'ga' yang
'khyams so/ /de'i tshe bal po rme ru rtse bya ba/ bod du yong chos bshad na'ang lo tsA ba med pas/ ma go bar phar log de mtshams lo mang rab kyi bar la lo paN gyi 'byon
zhud chad do/ /de rting lha btsun byang chub 'od kyi btang ba'i/ rgya brtson seng dang / nag tshos/ jo bo rje spyan 'drongs nas bal por phebs dus/ rgya brtson seng la
mu stegs pa'i ngan sngags byung nas 'das/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ bod spyi mthun la rgya brtson seng mi 'chi ba'i bsod nams yang mi 'dug da lo tsA mkhas pa med pas nga phyin kyang
bod la phan mi thogs/ phyir log 'gro gsungs pa la/ nag tshos/ lo tsA ba chen po rin chen bzang po la sogs pa yod pas/ zhu ba nan skyed pas/ mtho lding du yon mchod zhal
mjal/ chos mang po bsgyur/ mnga' ris dbus gtsang gi sa char lo mang po bzhugs/ rten rab gnas med pa la rab gnas/ yon bsngo ba med pa la bsngo ba/ gshin dge ba med pa la
dge rtsa gtong ba la sogs/ dge ba dkar phyogs 'phel ba'i srol mang po btod/ dam pa'i chos dar zhing rgyas par mdzad pas na/ jo bo yon mchod slob dpon de rnams/ bod la bka'

drin shin du che'o/ /de'i dngos slob khu rngog 'brom gsum la sogs/ bka' gdams pa'i rgyud 'dzin sde dgon dar rgyas che bar byung ngo / /jo bo rje'i gsung / lo chen rin chen
bzang po rnams kyis bsgyur ba yan gyi/ sngags mtshan nyid thams cad la snga 'gyur zhes grags so/ /jo bo de nyid ni dgung lo bdun cu rtsa gsum pa/ shing pho rta lo'i zla ba'i
tshes bco brgyad la snye thang nas dga' ldan du zhi bar gshegs so/ /	gcung srong nge'i sras/ lha lde dang gnam la 'od chen/ u pa dang gsum byung te/ yab sras de bas kho
char gyi lha khang bzhengs/ paNDi ta punye shrI spyan drangs so/ /lha lde'i sras 'od ldes rgyal srid bskyangs/ lha btsun byang chub 'od dang / gcung 'od zer go cha gsum
mo/ /yab sras 'di pas paNDi ta shraM dha ka ra warma/ dharma pA la/ padmA ka ra rnams spyan drangs/ de rnams kyis gsungs pa lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer/ 'gos khug
pa lhas btsas la sogs kyis bsgyur ba man nas/ gsang sngags gsar 'gyur zhes pa'i 'go tshugs/ gcen po 'od ldes/ dznyA na shrI spyan drangs/ 'od lde'i sras mnga' bdag rtse
lde'i ring la/ rgya gar na mkhan po zhi ba bzang po/ mkhas pa dznyA na shrI/ 'chi med sa ra hi ta/ paNDi ta gha ya dha ra/ btsun mo can/ paNDi ta pu nye shrI/ su siddhi/
paNDi ta su ma ti kirti/ paNDi ta gzhon nu 'bum pa/ gser gyi go cha/ bal po bha laNTa/ kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI rnams spyan drangs/ de rnams kyi rngog lo tsA ba blo
ldan shes rab/ gzu dga' rdor/gzhon nu mchog chos seng / khyung po grags seng / gu ru rin chen grags/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ zangs dkar 'phags
pa shes

rab/ gnyan chung dar ma grags/ cog ro chos mchog mar pa do pa/ lho brag mar pa lo tsA/ pa tshab nyi ma grags/ rma ban chos 'bar/ rwa lo/ cal lo/ sa lo kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
khro lo byams pa dpal la sogs pa/ rgya bod gyi lo tsA ba mkhas pa mang pos/ sngags mtshan nyid/ bka' bstan bcos dpag tu med pa bsgyur/ bstan pa ches cher gsal bar mdzad
pas/ bka' drin shin tu nas kyang che'o/ khyad par gyis kyang mnga' bdag rtse lde'i sku tshe'i smad la/ khro lo byams pa'i dpal rgya gar nas paNDi ta spyan 'dren du btang
bas/ kha che'i paN chen shAkya shrI zhes pa de nyid/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa lnga bzhes na'ang / yi dam kyi lung bstan byung bas/ me pho rta lo la gdan drongs/ bod yul du
lo bcu gnyis bzhugs/ sa khro lcal gsum la sogs slob ma mkhas pa mang du spel/ gtsang so ba tshul khrims mdzes dang / rdor byang rnam gnyis la sogs pa'i slob ma bskos nas/
bstan pa'i srol btsugs/ bod kyi spyi mchod tshogs pa sde bzhir grags pa'i/ bstan pa'i rgyun chu bo'i gzhung ltar gsal ba 'di nyid mdzad cing / dgu bcu rtsa bdun pa la
rgya gar la bzhud/ go dgu bzhes pa me yos la chos dbyings su gshegs par gda'o/ /mnga' bdag rtse lde'i sras/ bha lde/ de nas rim pa bzhin/ lde bha lde/ na ga lde pa rnams
byon/ 'di yan chod la gu ge spu rangs/ mar yul la sogs pa'i btsan po rnams chad par 'dod cing / dpal 'khor btsan man chad 'di la/ sngon rabs kyi yig tshang dang mi mthun
pa 'ga' re snang ngo / /na ga lde'i sras btsan phyug lde ya rtser byon/ de'i sras bkra shis lde/ de'i sras bkra btsan lde/ de'i sras grags pa ldes/ gser phye bre bcu bdun
la/

'jam dbyangs kyi sku bzhengs/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi la mchod rten bzhengs/ dngul dkar lnga brgya la phag dkar dang lhan skyes bzhengs/ dngul dkar stong phrag bcu gnyis kyi byams
pa bzhengs/ gsungs rab mang po bzhengs so/ /de'i sras a sogs ldes/ rdo rje gdan du chos rgyal mya ngan med kyis phul ba'i grong bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis sog po las nyos nas/
rdo rje gdan du phul/ rin dngul dkar bcu gnyis re/ lo re bzhin sog po la gdab pa byas so/ /de'i sras 'dze dar smal dang / a nan smal la/ pho bos/ kyai rdor lha dgu dngul
dkar lugs su bzhengs/ nu bos rdo rje gdan gsos/ gser gyi bka' 'gyur bzhengs/ de'i sras re'u smal gyis rgya gar nas rgyal khams mang du blang / dngul dkar bzhi bcu la sman
lha mched brgyad bzhengs/ lha sar jo bo'i dbu thog tu gser thog phub/ de'i sras sangga smal yin/ ji dar smal gyi sras/ ar 'ji smal gyis gser dkar bcu gcig la sgrol ma'i
sku bzhengs/ rgyal sa ma thob gong du sa skyar lha btsun byas/ de'i sras yar rtser skyes pa sri ti smal dang / dpal ldan grags pas sa skya'i chos khri chen mo dang / lha
sa'i bcu gcig zhal gyi steng du gser thog byas so/ /de rnams gcen skyid lde nyi ma mgon gyi rgyud pa yin no/ /	gcung po khri bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal gyi sras/ dpal lde
'od lde skyid de rnams la smad kyi lde gsum zer/ yab sras 'di pa mnga' ris gung thang man la chags te/ dpal lde'i rgyud sngon po'i tshon po la thug pa ni/ khab gung thang
pa/klu rgyal gling pa/ sla lung / gtsang skor ba rnams te/ las stod yan chod rnams so/ /gcung skyid lde 'jad rta nag na yod pa rnams so/ /gcig ni rgyud btsan po

rgyal ba 'od la thug pa ste/ gtsang grom pa rgyang myang stod na yod pa rnams so/ /'od lde'i rgyud gtsang g.yas ru na yod de/ skyid mkhar btsad po la thug cing / shar tsong
kha'i rgyal po gcen mnga' 'od chen la sogs pa/ mdo smad kyi rgyal rgyud rnams kyang yin no/ /mnga' bdag khri chung gi ring la/ yar klungs su byon te/ de'i rgyud dbus kyi
btsad po 'od srung pa rnams yin pa/ de'i sras 'od skyid 'bar/ de'i sras bdun gyi che ba/ zhang rje tsha khri lde 'bar/ gtsang pa tsha drugakhri lde 'bar la sras drug gi
g.yu thog pa'i rgyud sna mo ba/ 'phying nga pa/ don mkhar pa/ thang 'khor ba rnams yin no/ /bye chung lha sgom gdung chad/ gung lde 'od 'bar/ spe skyar gdung chad/ zla ba'i
rgyud/ rta bshags pa dang / gra sna ba yin no/ khri thog thag ma ru sper gdung chad/ chung ba/ bzhengs spyan 'bar gyi rgyud/ mon mkhar ba/ zhang mda' ba/ spun bdun thang
pa rnams so/ /lha ston dkar mo'i rgyud bye chung ba rnams yin no/ /gtsang pa tsha drug la/ 'od btsan/ lha btsan/ gung btsan gsum gyi rgyud/ bying ba'i btsad po rnams yin
no/ /lhun po'i rgyud bya ra na yod/ da ri'i rgyud khram drug pa dang / chu mig gog po ba rnams te/ 'od srung gi rgyud yin no/ /	bod kyi rgyal rabs byung tshul 'di la/
yar klungs jo bo dang / byang ji ston pa/ tshal pa kun dga' rdo rje la sogs kyis bsgrigs pa'i yig tshang rnams nas/ legs par btus te/ bsdebs pa yin cing / yar rtse'i rgyal
rabs ni gser thog pa rin rdor la zhib par dris nas bris pa yin zer bar 'dugamado rgyud mkhas mang phal cher bzhed mthun par/ /rgyal ba'i bstan pa lnga stong

gnas pa la/ /thub dbang sa pho 'brug la 'khrungs pa nas/ /lo grangs chig stong lnga brgya sum cu drug /'das pa'i chu bo khyi la bod rgyal gyi/ /snga ba gnya' khri btsan po
rgyal sar byon/ /de nas dgu brgya drug cu rtsa gcig la/ khyi lo tho ri snyan btsan byon pa nas/ /brgya dang go bdun song ba'i me mo glang / /srong btsan sgam po 'khrungs
nas chig brgya dang / /don bzhi lcags rta lo la brag dmar du/ khri srong lde btsan 'khrungs rting don drug pa'i/ /me pho khyi la mnga' bdag khri ral 'khrungs/ /so drug lcags
bya'i bar la rgyal srid bzung / /de yan rgyal rabs bzhi bcu zhe gnyis byon/ /de rting chu mo phag nas lcags rta'i bar/ /drug cu rtsa brgyad dar mas bstan pa bsnubs/ /bod
khams dbus gtsang dam chos sgra mi grags/ /de nas bstan pa phyi dar me stag lo/ /paN chen byon pa yan la nyis brgya dang / /dgu bcu go bdun me stag de lo nas/ /deng sang
shing stag brgyad dkar dbus gnas yan/ /nyis brgya nyi shu rtsa brgyad sngar 'das kun/ /	dril bas sum stong lnga brgya gya lnga song / /ma 'ongs bstan pa'i lhag ma chig
stong dang / /bzhi brgya bco lnga yod pa brtsi ba la/ /rtags tsam 'dzin pa lnga brgya the zhes lo/ /'di don go ba'i skyes bu shes ldan kun/ /bstan pa rin chen sgron me
gsal dus 'dir/ /rnam grol thar pa'i lam la 'jug pa rigs/ /chos rgyal rgyal rabs 'di bris dge ba yis/ /thub bstan bstan pa'i sgor zhugs 'phags tshogs kyi/ /bstan 'dzin 'dzin
ma'i ngos kun khyab gyur nas/ /'gro kun kun mkhyen rgyal po myur thob shog///

bod kyi blon chen mdzangs pa mi bdun gyi byung tshul bzhugs so/ / oM swa ti/ bod du chos rgyal mes dbon rim pa yi/ /mnga' thang chab srid rigs mthun bsod nams las/ /sprul pa'i
blon chen mdzangs la mang ba byon/ khyad par bod 'bangs byin la drin che ba'i/ /mdzangs pa mi bdun bya ba 'di ltar ro/ /thog mar gri gum btsan po'i sras gsum gyi/ /bar
pa spu te gung rgyal sku ring la/ /gcig tu mdzangs pa chen po mdzangs kyi bu/ /ru las skyes kyi ngar gsos bya ba yin/ /de yis thabs dang las ka ci byas na/ /ba glang 'bri
gnag ra lug khrims su bstsal/ /rtswa la chun po byas nas dbyar rtsi dgun du bascal/ /spang thang zhing du slog nas ri yi ngo rnams bzung / /de yi gong na bod na rtsi thog
lo thog med/ khri snyan bzung btsan rgyal po'i sku ring la/ /gnyis su mdzangs pa blon chen khu yi bu/ /lha bu mgo dkar zhes pa de nyid byung / /de yis thabs dang las
ka ci byas na/ /'brog gi don dang zhing gi mthun du 'debs/ /mtsho la gtar kha byas nas yur ba dkyus su bcug /phu chu rdzing du bskyil nas mtshan chu nyin du drangs/ /de'i
gong na zhing rnams char mar 'debs/ /stag ri gnyan gzigs rgyal po'i sku ring la/ /gsum du mdzangs zhing mkhas pa mong gi bu/ khri do ri yi gnang tshab bya ba byung / /de
yis thabs dang las ka ci byas na/ /rdo la

sol bas bzhu nas gser dngul zangs lcags bton/ shing la bug pa phug nas shol dang gnya' shing bcos/ /mdzo glang dor du sdeb nas thang la thams cad btab/ /de'i gong na bod na
rgal dang rin chen med/ /chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po'i sku ring la/ /bzhi ru mdzangs pa thon mi sam bho Ta/ 'jam dbyangs sprul pa skye dgu'i sgron me des/ /'gro ba'i
don la dka' ba dpag med kyis/ / ka kha sum cu bod kyi gug skyed bcas/ /'dogs dang 'brel sbyar tshag dang shad kyi bcad/ /tshig gi dbye nas skabs don smra ba brtsams/ /de
gang bod na klog dang yi ge med/ khri lde gtsug brtan rgyal po'i sku ring la/ /lnga ru mdzangs pa khri bzang yab don byung / /de yi thabs dang las ka ci byas na/ /bre dang
srang gi 'du 'god gtsigs su bzung / /bre dang khyor gyi za ma zung du 'dzin/ /dga' gnyis tshong byed mthun gnyis las la yod/ /de gong bod na bre srang nyo tshong med/ /chos
kyi rgyal po khri srong lde btsan ring / drug tu mdzangs pa khri bzang yab lhag byon/ /de'i thabs dang las ka ci byas na/ /ra khyim thams cad klung gi bde la phab/ /zhing
mtha'i sgang la so nam khang khyim bcas/ /thang ma zhing du slog nas chu rnams gzhung du bcug /de'i gong na ri la mkhar khyim 'dzin/ khri srong lde btsan 'phrul rgyal
sku ring la/ /bdun du mdzangs pa chen po gnyer gyi bu/ /stag tshab ldong gzigs bya ba de nyid byon/ /de'i thabs dang las ka ci byas na/ /phyogs bzhi'i srung mas sku'i
rim gro byed/ /rgod kyi stong sdes so kha'i dgra la rgol/ / nang gi khod snyoms khrims kyi gsos stong bcad/ /de'i gong na bod na gsos stong med/ /mdzangs pa mi bdun byung
tshul de ltar lags/ / / /

chen po hor gyi rgyal rabs cha lag tshang ba bzhugs so/ /na mo badzra pa ni ye/ mthu stobs gnam lcags rdo rjes bdud dpung dang / /gzir byed sdigs mdzub drag pos dgra bgegs
tshogs/ /bskal ba rgya mtsho'i pha mthar sprod mdzad pa/ khro rgyal nam mkha'i mdangs ldan zhabs la 'dud/ /de yi sprul pa byang phyogs hor yul dang / /srid bzung skabs su
rgya nag bal bod du'ang / /bstan pa skyong dang rgol ba bzlog pa sogs/ /byas byung lo rgyus don gsal 'di ltar ro/ /chen po hor gyi rgyal rabs snga ba/ dang por gnam gyi
bu bhor ta che/ de'i bu bhar ta che gan/ de'i bu tham chag de'i bu chi seng mer gan/ de slob dpon padma'i sprul pa yin zer/ de'i bu rgyud la rim pa bzhin/ a 'u dzam po de
wo la/ ye kha no bdun no/ /sems za'o che'i ga chu/ tho bu me gen/ de 'das pa'i rjes la/ nag mo a nan khro las/ nyi ma dang zla ba'i zer las skyes pa'i bo thon char mun khan/
yang de'i bu rgyud rim pa bzhin/ ga'i chi/ be khir/ ma nan tho don/ ga'i thu gan/ ba'i shing / khor dog shing / dum bi na'i khan/ ga bu la khan/ bar than ba dur/ ye
su ga ba dur/ 'di yan la/ hor gyi rgyal rabs bcu dgu hor yul du byung ngo / /ye su kha dur rgyal po dang / btsun mo hu lun gyi sras/ tha'i dzung jing gir rgyal po/ shing
pho rta lo la sku 'khrungs te/ sku mched bdun yod/ khong gi dgung lo sum cu so gsum lon pa sa pho stag lo la/ mi nyag rgyal rgod kyi rjes la/ tho dzi zhes pa'i rgyal po gcig
gis/ sung gi rgyal

po byed pa'i lag nas dpung shed mong gis rgyal sa phrogs/ hor gyis rgya nag gi rgyal sa lo nyi shu rtsa gsum bzung te/ dgung lo drug cu re drug pa me pho stag gi lo/ ston zla
dang po'i tshes bcu gnyis la/ mi nyag gi sa char gnam du gshegs so/ /gnam mam/ bya tshe ring gis byin pa'i nor bu'i tham kha yang rgyal po de'i ring la byung ba yin zer/
de'i bu rdzong chi dang / cha ga ta'i/ tho la no yon la sogs pa dgu yod do/ /rgyal po rang yod dus/ sras che ba gnyis pos/ rgyal sa la mi rtsod pa'i yi ge bcug nas/ g.yas
ru g.yon ru'i rgan pa la bskos/ nu bo che ba o ko ta yis/ rgyal sa lo drug mdzad/ 'jo chi la bu brgyad dang / ca ga ta la bu dgu yod/ o ko ta'i sras che ba go yug rgyal
pos rgyal sa zla ba bdun mdzad/ de'i nu bo go dan la sogs pa bdun yod/ go yug la bu gsum yod/ tho lo no yon gyi sngar yi ge ma shor bas rgyal sa la rtsod pa yod cing /
de dang btsun mo za yin e ka ze rog ta'i bu che bas/ mo gol gan gyi rgyal sa lo dgu mdzad/ sras gnyis pa e chen go dan/ gsum pa go pe la shi dzung se chen gan/ shing mo
phag lo la 'khrungs/ rgyal sa lo sum cu so lnga mdzad/ bzhi ba a ri bho ga lnga pa hu la hu/ 'di lhag pa'i rgyal po yin zer nas/ rgyal khams 'tshol ba la/ stod du btang bas/
stod hor du grags pa 'di byung ba yin no/ /se chen dang dpon mo cha bu'i sras bzhi'i che ba rdo rje/ gnyis pa 'jing gim/ gsum pa mangga la/ bzhi pa na mo gan/ btsun mo
zhwa gon ma'i sras brgyad kyi che ba hur dkar che/ a rog ce/a la che/ go lug thi mur/ e san bho kha/ tho gan/ go go chu/ rdo lo/ thams cad bsdoms pas se chen gyi bu bcu
gnyis byung / se chen rang gi dgung lo sum cu so bzhi pa lcags pho spre'u'i lo nas bzung ste/ rgyal sa lo sum cu so lnga mdzad/

brgyad cu tham pa'i thog shing pho rta lo gnam du gshegs/ se chen gyi sras che ba rdo rje la sras med/ rgyal po jing gam dang de'i btsun mo go go cen gyi sras che ba ka ma
la/ dharma pha la lkugs pa/ o ja dur ti mur dang / gsum yod pa'i/ o ja du 'dis dben cing lo gnyis dang / ta'i ti lo bcu gcig te/ rgyal sa lo bcu gsum mdzad do/ /de'i bu ti
shu myur du 'das/ dharma pha la dang btsun mo tha hong tha'i ghi'i sras che ba/ hi shan gyis lo lnga rgyal sa mdzad de/ ming go lug rgyal po yang zer ro/ /sras gnyis pa
a yu par pa ta'i sras rgyal srid lo dgu bzung / ming bu yan du rgyal po yang zer ro/ /ka ma la'i sras ye sun the mur gyis rgyal sa lo lnga bzung / bu yan du'i sras sa ti'i
pha la g.ying dzung gi gan rgyal pos rgyal sa lo gsum mdzad/ go dan rgyal po'ang zer ro/ /go dan la sras/ ji big thi mur la sogs pa gsum yod/ ye sun thi mur gyi sras/
ra khyi phag gis zhag bzhi bcu rgyal sa gzung / mangga la'i sras a nan ta/ de'i sras u rug thi mur bsad/ de la bu gnyis yod/ go lug rgyal po'i sras che ba/ ku sha las/ khri
thog tu lo gcig zhugs te/ go thug rgyal po'ang zer ro/ /gnyis pa thog thi mur gyis rgyal sa lo lnga mdzad/ dzwa yan du rgyal po'ang zer/ ku sha la'i sras gnyis kyi chung
ba rin chen dpal rgyal po/ thog mar rgyal sar bton pa/ zla ba gcig song ba dang gnam du gshegs/ de'i skabs su rtsis pa rnams bsags nas rtsis byas pas/ de'i gcen po tho
gon thi mur/ bya lo zla ba drug pa shar nas/ rgyal sar bton na se chen dang mnyam pa gcig yong zer ba byung ba la/ mi dpon rnams na re/ de tsam rgyal sa stong par 'jog pa/
rgyal khams kyi khag sus thig zer ba la/ el thi mur tha shi na re/ khyed lam khyim thi sa rnams kyi da dung legs par

rtsis/ de ltar bden na gong ma sku tshe ring ba las lhag pa med/ de bar la rgyal khams kyi khag ngas 'khur zer nas/ zla ba drug rgyal sa stong / khrims kyi bya ba rnams/ el
thi mur gyis byas/ de rting chu mo bya lo zla ba drug pa'i tshes brgyad la/ pho brang chen po shang rdor/ tho gon thi mur rgyal sar bton nas/ ci shun lo gcig dang / en thun
lo gnyis/ ci dben lo drug ci bying lo nyi shu rtsa bdun te/ dril bas lo sum cu so drug rgyal sar bzhugs shing / khri thog tu phebs nas lo nyi shu rtsa drug lon pa'i skabs
su/ sa pho khyi lo la ti shri kun rgyal zhi bar gshegs/ sog po'i mi dpon ngo log nas/ pho brang shang rdo mes bsregs/ bde bar gshegs pa'i tshems chen dang / rdo'i lhung
bzed nam mkha' la byon ces gleng / de rting lo bcu lon pa'i/ sa pho spre'u hor zla brgyad pa'i nyer dgu'i srod la gong ma chen mo yab sras/ pho brang ta'i du nas hor
yul du gshegs dgos pa byung shing / rgyal sa rgya twa ming rgyal pos bzung ba yin zer ro/ /de yang snga sor pho brang shang rdor sog pos me la bsregs dus/ sman tshe'i rgyal
pos/ hor rgyal po la gus btud byas pas ma lo bar/ yul nas phud sa skyar yong / chos byas pas mi 'dus pa chen po byung 'dug de'i skabs su hor gyi rtsis pa na re/ nub phyogs
kyi ban de ngo log nas/ rgyal sa 'phrog par 'dug zer ba byung nas ltar btang bas/ sman tshe lha btsun 'khor mang pos bskor ba mthong / de hor rgyal po la zhus pas/ gsod
zer ba'i lung byung nas/ bod du phyin pas kho na re/ nga ngo log byed rtsis min pa la gsod na skye ba phyi ma hor gyi rgyal sa 'phrog par gyur cig zer ba'i smod bor bas/
rgya twa ming rgyal por skyes nas rgyal sa phrogs pa yin zer ro/ /sman tshe lha btsun der bsad dus/ khrag yang 'o mar byung zhes

grags so/ /se chen rgyal po'i btsun mo chung ba'i sras/ a rog che nyi ma nub phyogs la gshegs su bcug nas/ rgya bod mtshams su bzhugs/ dbus gtsang du yang byon/ ngo log yang
mang po mnan/ de'i sras thi mur bho khas kyang / gdan sa chen po'i zhabs tog dang / khrims la phan pa'i bya ba bzang po mang po byas/ de'i sras lab de yab kyi go sar bskos
nas/ dbus gtsang du ma byon/ ma chung ba'i sras chos dpal la/ ri rtsing dbang gi ming byin dbus gtsang du byon/ rgyal gyi rtsib ri'i zhol du/ stod hor gyi dmag dpung
btul/ 'bri khung sgom pa khrims la bsgral/ de'i bu rgyud padma twa/ pra dznyA dbang la sogs ga chu na yod pa rnams yin cing / phyi skor dbus gtsang du phebs pa'i rgyal po
hong tha'i ji dzong thing chen po yab sras pa rnams kyang yin no/ /hor gyi rgyal po rgya nag tu byon pa'i thog ma/ thi dzung jing gar rgyal pos sa pho stag la rgya nag rgyal
sa thob nas/ rting ma tho gon thi mur rgyal pos/ sa pho spre'u'i lo la rgyal sa shor ba yan la/ lo brgya dang lnga bcu nga gcig song zhing / hor gyi rgyal rabs rkyang
grangs bco lnga byung 'dugachos rje sa paN dgung lo drug cu re gsum bzhes pa/ shing pho 'brug lo la/ hor gyi gser yig pa la snga ba/ rdor tha ches sa skya nas/ gdan drangs
nas byon/ lam bar la lo gsum song / dgung lo drug cu re drug ba me mo lug la byang ngos sprul pa sder hor rgyal po go dan dang mjal nas/ hor gyi rgyal sa shor ba yan
la/ hor dang sa skya ba yon mchod lo brgya dang bcu drug mdzad do/ /hor tho gon mur rgyal po'i lag nas/ rgya'i twa ming rgyal pos sa pho spre'u'i lo la rgya nag rgyal sa
blangs nas/ da lo shing pho stag gi lo/ srog sme brgyad dkar dbus na yod pa 'di yan la lo drug cu re bdun song 'dug go/

bod dbus gtsang du thog mar hor jing gir rgyal pos/ rgya nag rgyal sa lon nas rgyal khams byings po mnan/ bu rnams la sa bgos byas pa'i dus dang / gzhan yang hor rgyal po na
rim gyi bar la/ lha sde mi sde phye gsal dang sa tshigs/ dud bgrang lugs ci rigs su byung 'dug na'ang / 'dir hor tho gon thi mur rgyal pos/ khri thog phebs nas/ dho shu
ta a nu gan bya ba dang / gab phyag twa'i phing chang mngags nas/ dbus gtsang dpon chen gzhon dbang skyar ma'i dus/ sa tshigs dud grangs/ hor dud bcas pa ni 'di ltar snang
ngo / khang pa ka ba drug gi khyon cig zhing hor son khal bcu gnyis kyi sa/ mi bza' mi bu tsha bran khol pho mo dang bcas pa drug phyugs sgal rmos bzhon gsum/ ra lug mgo
chen gnyis rnams la mgo swe nyi shu rtsa bzhi yod par 'dug pa/ de 'dra zhig la hor dud tshang ma gcig zer bar 'dug cing / hor dud lnga bcu la rta mgo gcig de gnyis la
brgya skor gcig de bcu la stong skor gcig de bcu la khri skor gcig zer zhing / khri skor lugs can tshang ma la/ lha sde stong skor bzhi dang / mi sde stong skor drug dgos
pa yin pa 'dug khri skor bcu la klu gcig de bcu la zhing gcig zer ro/ /'di bzhin rtsis pa'i zhing bcu gcig hor se chen rgyal po'i dus mnga' 'og tu chug pa yin pa 'dug cing
/ zhing gi ming ni ta'i tu'i mkhar nang na cong zhing / phyi so na ho nam zhing / zhim za zhing / gam zu zhing / si chon zhing / hu nam zhing / gyang si zhing / byang
ci zhing / gu ru zhing / le'o yang zhing / bod chol kha gsum gyis/ zhing gtsang ma ma long na yang / bla ma'i bzhugs gnas dang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar ba'i sa phyogs
yin pas zhing gcig tu bgrangs pas/ bcu gcig yin zer ro/ /las gnas bskos pa'i rim

pa ni/ bcu dpon/ lnga bcu dpon/ brgyadapon/ stong dpon/ khri dpon/ klu'i da ra kha che/ klu gsum la dbang na/ klu gun min dban hu zhes pa'i ming dang / shel kyi tham kha ster
ba yin pa 'dug pa/ bod du dpon chen shAkya bzang po la gnang 'dug gzhan yang dpon chen phal che ba la/ dhing zwam lu son wi si du dbyen sha zer ba'i ming dang / dngul
dam gling drug ma stag mgo dang bcas pa ster bar 'dugadapon chen zhes pa ni bla ma'i nye gnas la/ bod kyis che ming btags par 'dug cing / chol kha zhes pa hor rgyal pos bla
ma la dbang yon phul ba'i mdo stod smad dbus gtsang dang bcas pa la ming btags par 'dug rgya hor gyi yul zhing dang / khri stong la sogs pa ma gtogs/ chol kha'i ming ni
brjod bya med zer ro/ /zhing du long nas zhing gi mi dpon chen po zer/ rgyal rgyud bu dang mag pa la bkod pa yin par 'dug cing / dbang gi ming dang / gser gyi dam kha gser
sgor/ dngul sgor ster ba yin par 'dug de yang bu che 'bring chung gsum la dpags pa'i ming rab 'bring tha las tshan rim pa gsum du bskos pa yin 'dug rgyal khams 'jags
dgos pa'i don la/ rgyal po yab sras la/ ngo srung med pa'i snyan skul zhu ba dang / rgyal rgyud mi dpon rnams kyis gsug pa zos pa dang / bya ba nor pa byas pa na/ 'chos pa
dang / skyon 'dzin pa'i khrims ra tha'i sa gsum yod pa'i/ sku'i tha'i khrims ra/ tA tu na yod/ si tha'i kiM cha hU na yod/ gnam tha'i hang byi'u na yod/ tha'i sa gsum gyi
'og na glen hang zi nyi shu rtsa bzhi yod pa/ mtshan la'ang son hang bzhin ming / tsa he tsa ho de rnams kyang khrims kyi dgag bzhi yin/ de bzhi skor la khrims ra drug
bzhi nyi shu rtsa bzhi yod pa'o/ /mi chen hor gyi rgyal rabs 'di bris pas/ /dge chen rnam dkar 'bras bu 'di yi mthus/ /sa chen 'di la gnas pa'i 'gro ba kun/ /bde chen thar
pa'i gling du myur bgrod shog /dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig///

dbus gtsang khri skor gyi dud grangs dang / 'ja' mo 'dzin lugs bzhugs so/ /hor se chen rgyal po'i lung gis/ mi chen das man la bka' bstsal pa/ das man khyod nyon gcig bod 'di
mi thu mo rang yin par/ sngon bod kyi rgyal po yod pa'i dus/ thang tha'i dzung rgyal po'i ring la/ ri bo rtse lnga'i bar bod dmag mang po yong / hu thing hus sar bka'
ma log zer ba'i mtshan chen po sdod pa byas 'dug da lta bod la rgyal po med/ jing gir rgyal po'i sku bsod la/ /rgyal khams chen po dbang du bsdus/ /sa skya bla ma'ang rang
re'i bla mchod du khugs pa 'di yin/ bla ma 'phags pa khu dbon 'di pa/ yul gzhan gyi rgyal po yin na/ khong shes rab ches bas rang res mi thub/ da lta bod byings rang re'i
'og tu chud pa 'di yin/ das sman khyod spyod pa bzang po yod pas/ sa skyar thengs gcig song shig /bod byings po se chen go pe li'i 'og tu chud nas/ mi chen das sman yang
sa skya na sleb yod pa 'dug zer ba'i gtam snyan po thos pa yin gsungs/ das sman gyis zhus pa rgyal po khyed kyi lung bzhin 'gro bar byed/ de ltar na'ang bod bya ba mi
thu mo yin 'dug pa dang / khong rang gi rgyal khrims kyang zhig rgya hor gyi khrims ni ji bzhin ma chags/ so kha rnams kyang ma tshugs par yod 'dug pas/ yar phyir gyi mthun
rkyen sbyor ba dang / bya ba chen po 'grub pa ji

ltar yong min zer/ yang rgyal po'i lung gis/ rang re tshang la bod byings po 'og tu chug yod pa 'dug zer ba'i gtam snyan po des chog chas kha cha rkyen gang dgos ma thung gan
pas skur/ sa skya man la 'ja' mo che chung du 'os/ sa 'jam rtsub/ mi snge dar rgud/ rgya 'jam la dpe ltos la tshugs shog bla ma 'phags pa yar la byon dus 'byon lam bde
dgos pa yin/ yang don gcig la/ khyod swan jing dben du bskos pa la/ bod kyi gnas lugs rnams zhib par go na/ gnam sa'i bya ba chen po dang / mi mang po la phan pa yin pas
song shog gsungs nas/ bla ma'i bka' shog dang / rgyal po'i 'ja' sa dgos pa rnams gnang / das sman 'khor mang po dang bcas pas yar phyir chas/ bod kyi ban skya rgan 'go drag
rigs spyi sgos la/ gnang sbyin cha rkyen bzang po dang bcas pa/ gan mdzod che chung nas skur te yar yong / thog mar bod du bstan pa phyi dar kyi chos byung sa yin pas/
mdo smad kyi dan tig shel gyi lha khang dang / mdo stod gtso mdo bsam 'grub/ gtsang dpal ldan sa skya rnams su rim par mi mang po bsags/ gang la gang 'os kyi gnang sbyin
sprad/ bka' lung bsgrags shing rgya bod kyi so mtshams nas/ sa skya man la 'jam chen nyi shu rtsa gsum btsugs/ so sor phye nas mdo smad sa 'jam pas 'ja' mo bdun/ mdo stod
la 'ja' mo dgu/ dbus gtsang la 'ja' mo bcu gcig de'i nang nas kyang dbus pas 'ja' mo 'dzin dgos pa la/ sog shag rtsi bar/ sha pho/ rkang / dgon sar/ byam gya ba dang bdun/
gtsang pas 'dzin dgos pa la/ stag tshong 'dus/ dar lung / grom pa sa skya rang dang bzhi btsugs/ khri skor so sos 'jam skyor 'dab pa'i bkod pa

byas/ bod byings po la rgyal po yon mchod kyi bka' lung 'phrod/ sa skya 'khor/ bod spyi sgos kyi gnas lugs thams cad khong du chud nas/ rgyal po'i drung du slebs/ rgyu mtshan
rnams zhus pas go chod 'dug gsungs/ gsol ras dang / gnang sbyin bzang po sbyin/ swan jing dben gyi/ khrims dar rtsa ba'i dpon chen du bskos/ bod kyi 'ja' mo rnams gsar
btsugs yin pas 'jags par byed pa'i mi gcig bsko dgos pa yod zhus pas/ mi chen i ji lag zer ba la/ bod 'jam shes pa'i 'ja' sa dang / thong ji las bka' gnang nas yar la btang
/de nas bzung / hor sa skya ba yon mchod du ji tsam sbrel kyi bar la/ bod 'jam nyi shu rtsa bdun po de bde mor 'jags pas/ bla ma dpon chen/ hor gyi gser yig pa rnams
la/ 'byon lam bde zhing bod 'bangs byings po skyid par byung skad/ 'di ni se chen rgyal pos sa skyar gser yig pa mngags pa'i sngon ma yin cing / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa
dang / sa skya ba la shin tu dad pa'i mi dpon bzang po gcig byung 'dug pas/ rnam thar zur tsam bris pa yin/ thong dzi i thi ji lag gis bod 'jam thog tu ma slebs gong hor
rgyal po 'jang yul la dmag thog tu byon dus/ mdo smad kyi 'ja' mo gnyis/ rgya 'jams kyi zhor la/ mar la bsdus pas/ rim shugs rgyab pas/ mdo stod ga re/ go dpe'i 'ja' mo gnyis
dbus gtsang pa la stag skor nas gal/ khrums zhig nas lo shas nan ltar sbyong ba la/ thong ji sleb nas/ ga re go sa'i 'ja' mo gnyis po sngar bzhin mdo stod pa rang la
khel bas/ theng dzi i ji lag de yang dbus gtsang la drin che bar byung bar gda'o/ /hor se chen rgyal po'i dus/ bod khams byings po la mi brtsi dud

grangs byung ba'i dus/ mdo smad nas yar rtsis par 'dug pas/ ga chu rab kha nas/ nang so la gtogs pa'i gzhis dang / gyang gi rtsa dang / bla ba 'khar dang /de'i 'og na dem khang
gzhis bya ba yod pas/ de rnams bla ma 'phags pa la/ sa phud du lung gi phul nas/ gan 'jam la sogs dang / rgya bod kyi khral dud gang yang mi 'khri ba/ gtsang mar yod
pa la/ hor son lnga brgya'i sa yin zer bar 'dug hor dang sa skya ba yon mchod du 'brel nas/ 'go ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pas/ rgya nag ta'i tu'i pho brang du thengs
gsum byon/ gong ma se chen rgyal po yab yum sras bcas la/ sa skya ba'i khyad chos/ rgyud gsum gyi dbang mo che tshar gsum bskur ba'i dbang yon snga ma la/ dbus gtsang gi
khri skor bcu gsum phul ba ni/ mnga' ris rdzong kha'i 'og gi glo dol rdzong gsum khri skor gcig la stod lho byang / chu zhal rnams re re bgrangs pa khri skor bzhi/ sbra
ber khyung gsum khri gcig /yar 'brog tshal pa khri skor gnyis/ /rgya 'bri g.ya' phag khri skor bzhi/ /zur nas bsdus pa'i gcig byung ba/ /bya yul hor dud stong phrag gcig
/'brug pa hor dud dgu brgyar byed/ /stong dang dgu brgya phyed khyer du/ khri skor gcig gi bya ba bsgrubs/ /de rnams dril bas bcu gsum tshang / /dbang yon bar ma la/ bod
chol kha gsum phul ba ni/ mnga' ris gung thang nas/ sog la skya bo yan dam pa chos kyi chol kha/ sog la skya bo nas rma chu khug pa yan/ mgo nag mi'i chol kha/ rma chu khug
pa man/ rgya mchod rten dkar po yan/ dud 'gro rta'i chol kha dang gsum yod de/ mi rta chos gsum gyi 'bul ba'i lugs su byas nas/ phul ba yin par 'dug cing / chol kha re
la dpon chen re

re rgyal po yon mchod bka' gros su bstun nas bsko bar mdzad 'dugadabang yon rting ma la bla ma'i bka' bzhin/ rgya'i yur ma chen mo phul nas/ rgya mi khri khrag mang po srog
thar du bcug de dus bla ma 'phags pas bsngo ba smon lam 'di ltar mdzad do/ /nam mkha'i khams ni khrag gi mdog ltar dmar/ /rkang leb ro yis phyi yi rgya mtsho gang / /'di
'dra bcad pa'i dge ba gang de yis/ /mkhyen rab dbang phyug thugs dgongs rdzogs phyir dang / /phan bde'i bstan pa rab tu dar phyir dang / /mi dbang sku tshe shin tu brtan
phyir bsngo/ /zhes gsungs shing / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang 'gro ba sems can gyi don la phan pa rgya chen po mdzad par gda'o/ /gong ma se chen rgyal po dang / bla ma
'phags pa gnyis thugs so bsod 'bel gtam gleng ba'i skabs na/ rgyal pos bla ma la/ dang por jing gir rgyal pos rgyal khams byings po bsdus pa'i skabs na/ nged kyi rgyal khams
chos pa dang / 'jags su 'jug pa'i dus su yang / shed mong legs par gdabs pas/ hor kyi dmag mi rnams la/ da lta zas nor gyi stobs zhan pas/ shed mong snon pa'i thabs
dang chos phyogs ji ltar byas na 'thad gsungs pas/ bla ma'i zhal ta/ khyed rang la yod pa'i mdzod kyi cha rkyen dang / dmag mi res pa'i grangs longs la/ lo 'ga'i bar la gzhi
bcas kyis lto gos 'tsho ba'i gnang sbyin byed par 'os gsung ba byung nas de bzhin byas pas/ dmag mi la rtsa ba'i hor dmag khri tsho lnga bcu dang / res pa yang tshan
che bar byung ba la/ gnang sbyin byed pa'i cha rkyen ma ldang byung pas/ yang rgyal po'i gsungs nas/ da lta cha rkyen gyi ma lcog byung bas/ hor yul gyi lho phyogs na/ /

sman tshe zhes bya ba'i rgyal po dang / de'i 'og na mi sde phyug po yod par 'dugade rang gi dmag gis blangs nas/ bu rta'i shed mong bcos na e 'thad gsungs pas/ bla ma'i zhal
nas/ da lta khyed la don chen po 'di sgrub pa'i mi mi snang bas ma rings/ nged kyis brtag pa byed gsungs/ de'i phyi lo rgyal po'i gcung po e chen hu la hus/ gong ma la
gdab nor lo gsar skyel ba la khong gi mi dpon ba yan zer bas 'go byas/ 'u lag lnga brgya tsam dang bcas pa yong ba'i lam du/ u lug non yon bya ba/ ri dwags la yong / nam
la byed pa dang 'phrad/ shes rab che ba dang / gzugs bzang ba'i mi dpon de gnyis/ rta thog tu dri ba gtam lab byas pas/ gcig la gcig mgu ba yan rgyal po dang mjal 'phrad
byas rting / rgyal rgyud mi dpon rnams kyi rtsar/ hor yul na/ u lug zer ba'i mi dpon bzang po gcig 'dug de rgyal po'i rtsa ru sdod 'os pa gcig 'dug ces lab pas/ gtam de gong
mas gsan nas u lug 'bod mkhan thugs la gtags nas/ nang blon chen por gyur te/ 'dis kyang ba yan la phan gtags pa'i/ gtam rting la yod/ der ba yan rgyal po dang mjal/
pho brang du ston mo chen po byed pa la/ bla ma dam pa gdan drangs pa'i dus na/ ba yan mjal ba'i spyod pa dang 'gro lugs/ zhu ba'i gtam brjod mkhas pa yon tan che bar 'dug
pa bla mas mkhyen nas/ rgyal po la mi bzang po kho pa la 'dug gsung / rgyal pos dgongs nas ba yan gyi tshab tu/ gong ma'i res dpon gcig dang / gser yig pa byin po de la/
gnang sbyin bzang po byas/ lo lan bskur nas btang / ba yan sdod gsungs nas bsdad yod pa'i skabs su/ khong pa yan dang / u lug

gnyis gcig las gcig bzang ba'i blon chen gnyis yod pa'i skabs der/ yang rgyal pos bla ma la/ da ba yan 'di sman tshe'i phyogs su btang na gsungs pa la/ de 'pher ba 'dug nged
kyis don 'grub pa'i thabs dang rten 'brel byed gsungs nas/ bal po e ner dga' sprul pa'i lha bzo ba lta bu la zhal ta mdzad/ 'ju tshur lha khang dang / chos skyong ma hA
ka la 'khor bcas kyi sku bzhengs/ rab gnas bla ma rang gis mdzad/ mgon po'i zhal sman tshe phyogs la gzigs su bcug lob dpon dam pa kun dga' der/ chos skyong sgrub pa mdzad
pa la bskos/ ba yan la ching sang gyi ming dam kha byin nas/ grogs la rgya'i rigs kyi byang bi thang chu'i phing chad zer ba'i mkhas pa zhig kyang btang zhing / ching
sang gi 'go byas hor dmag byings po brdzangs nas/ sman tshe'i rgyal khams longs la shog gsungs pa'i lung byung dus/ ba yan ching sang gis nged sman tsher slebs nas dmag po
che'i bya ba 'dra mi 'dra the tshom byung dus/ zhu ba gtong dgos te/ nged kyi gser yig pa gong ma'i drung du 'gro ba dang / de sgug pa'i bar du dmag gi 'gro 'dug ji ltar
byed zhus pas/ kho bden par 'dug nga'i lung yin gyis la khyod rang gi thag chod la/ bya ba rnams bsgrigs su chug gsungs pa'i lung thob nas phyin pas/ ching sang dmag legs
nas/ sman tshe rgyal po'i pho brang yang thob nas/ rgyal khams blangs pas/ thad ka thad kar mi dpon gyi bsko bzhag byas/ sman tshe rgyal po'i mu tig gi gos gcig dang dam
ga rgyal ba'i rtags byed zer nas ching sang gis bzung / gzhan cha rkyen byings po rgyal po la gdab tu btang ba'i dus su/ sman tshe'i sa phyogs rgyus yod pa'i skye bo 'ga'
res/ mkhar

mig gi sa cha mi sde bzang sar las ka zhus/ 'ja' sa khyer song bas/ ba yan gyi 'grims du ma bcug cha gcig par nga dang po lung thob yod pa dang / mi dpon bskos tshar ba rnams
brtan du ma bcug na/ mi sde khrums zhig gis dogs byas nas bya ba 'jags rting / rgyal po'i drung du 'ong nas mjal ba'i tshe/ ching sang res dang mjal 'phrad grub ma thag
kho rang gi khang par ma yong bar/ res khang du bsdad pa'i bar la/ rgyal pos kho la nga rgyal chen po yod dgongs pa gcig byung nas/ zu gur che gcig ba yan gyi rtsar btang
nas/ khyod ba yan tshan pa'i mi yin pa gan pa la/ sras ming dang las ka chen po byin nas btang ba yin/ sman tshe'i rgyal khams len pa la brtson 'grus bya ba phing chang
gis byas/ ming khyod kyis blangs nas nga rgyal ma che gsungs pa zhig bskur nas btang / zu gur che song rting / rgyal po la the tshom byung nas slog mi btang ba la ma zin/
khos ching sang la/ lung bskyal pas/ ching sang na re/ khyod kyi rgyal po'i lung nged la 'phrod/nga'i zhu ba rgyal po la e thengs bris pas/ thengs zer ba dang / ching
sang gis/ nga'i don la rgyal po khyed thugs bde bar mdzod/ 'tshams pa'i mi 'tsham par bzhag na/ 'tsham par ka 'gro/ ming dang las ka byin pa ches na rgyal po'i rang dbang
yin/ sman tshe'i rgyal khams len pa la/ brtson 'grus dang bya ba phing chang gis byas nas ming ba yan gyis blangs gsungs pa ste/ de'i rgyu mtshan sman tshe ba rnams kyi
lab ste 'ong / rgyal po khyed la don grub pas mi chog gam/ zhus nas btang bas/ gtam de rgyal por zhus pas/ nga'i gtam de mgyogs drags/ khos de zer du byung dogs gsungs lo/
/de rting rgyal pos sman tsher 'ja' sa

byin btang ba'i mi/ ching sang gis mi 'grim du ma bcug pa de rnams kyis/ ba yan gyis sman tshe'i rgyal po'i cha rkyen la rang nor byas/ gan mdzod pa la ma gdabs/ 'ja' sa bskos
pa'i mi 'grim du ma bcug par/ kho rang gis mi rnams las ka la bskos zer nas/ gtug gsher byung ba la ba yan rang la dris gsungs/ ba yan bzung nas phyi rol na bzhag yod
pa'i dus su/ u lug no yon gyis go nas nang du byung na/ rgyal po'i drung du 'gro ba ching sang gas mthong nas/ u lug an ta khyod kyis ma go ba ci yod byas pas/ ngas go zer
nas gong ma la ba yan ching sang / mi ngan pas gtug gsher byas/ khong bzung nas gyam bcos 'dug ba yan mi gcig rang res gsod kyang sla/ rtswa gcig gcod pa dang khyad ci
yod de/ sman tshe'i rgyal khams pa rnams kyis rgyal po khyed la/ 'phya smod mi yong ngam zhus pas/ de bden kho thongs gsungs nas/ las ka phab rang gi khang par bsdad yod
pa'i dus re zhig na/ ba yan gyi dmag po che hor yul la 'degs par 'dug zer nas 'ur chen po byung nas/ blon po rnams skrag ste rgyal po la ci drag zhus pas/ khyed rnams gros
gyis gsungs pa la/ khong rnams kyi gros byed rgyu ma rnyed par rgyal po la bskyar nas zhus pas/ khyed rnams kyis bya thabs ma rnyed pa na/ thabs kyis ba yan la gros dris
gsungs nas phyin pas/ ching sang na re nga go ma chod par las ka phab nas bsdad pa'i mis ci shes/khyed rang rnams shes mod zer ba byung nas/ de bzhin rgyal po la zhus
pas/ gong ma rang gi rtsar ba yan bos nas gros dris pas/ rang re'i hor dmag rnams kyi steng du/ mi bzang po bskos te/ dmag gis 'thab na thub yong mod zhus pas/

ba yan ching sang rang 'gro dgos gsung / dmag dpon la bskos nas/ khong 'gro ba'i skyel thung byas par/ ba yan ching sang ci zer lta ba'i khad nyan pa la btang / ching sang
rta bzhon 'gro khar sdod pa'i blon po skyel thung pa rnams la/ khyed mi mngags pa la/ 'di 'dra ba'i mi mngags pa zer ba gsum byas nas/ song zer ba thos nas rgyal po la zhus
pas/ gtam de ma bzang ba yin pas log shog zer ba'i mi btang / zim dem 'ja' mor slebs pa phyir bos nas/ sang snga mor sleb pa dang / rgyal pos ba yan khyod kyi kha sang
/ je gon mthing nas rta bzhon 'gro khar ci lab gsungs pas/ cang ma smras zer/ rgyal po rang gisakhyed mi 'di 'dra mngags pa zer lab 'dug pa khyod kyis smras pa min nam gsungs
pas/ de ni bden zer/ ci'i don la byas pas/ ching sang gi zhus pa/ ngas sman tshe'i rgyal po khyed la rgyal khams gtad pa de/ nyi ma shar nas nub kyi bar la rgyal khams
pa rnams kyis shes pa yin/ de'i rting la nga nyes med pa dmangs su phab nas bzhag pa de'ang nyi ma shar nas nub kyi bar du thos yod/ 'di lta bu'i skyon chen gyi mi gtong
ba byang phyogs hor gyi yul na/ rgyal po khyed kyi rgyud pa mi che la mang ba rnams yod/ mi nga skyon phog pa'i mi khong rnams kyi steng du bskos nas btang tsa na/ khong
rnams kyang rgyal po khyed la yid chad byed/ dmag po che'i bya ba ci 'dra yong ngam bsams nas lab pa yin zhus pas/ rgyal po na re khyod bden/ ba yan las bden pa med/
da lta rang 'ja' sa bris/ ba yan gyi sman tshe rgyal khams blangs pa dang / shed mong gi 'dab pa rnams 'ja' sa'i stod du bris/ mi ngan pas rdzun zhus byas pa bar der bris/
ba yan bden pa yin pas

ming dang / shed mong bsnan pa rnams gting la bris la/ rgyal rgyud bu mo mag pa dmag mi/ mi dpon mi sde rnams kyis/ ba yan gang zer gyis ngag la nyon zer ba'i 'ja' sa sgrog
mi sngon la thongs la/ de'i rjes la ba yan ching sang 'grim gsungs/ de bzhin byas pas ba yan gyis dmag dpung thul/ hor yul rgyal khams bde bar byas nas tshur 'khor ba dang
/ rgyal pos kyang ba yan la gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i thugs 'dogs bzang po mdzad/ rgyal rgyud blon po'i tshogs rnams kyis kyang / legs par bkur ba'i blon po rin po che yin
par 'dugagal ching gi 'ja' sa la snga ba 'di yin zer ro/ /bla ma 'phags pa la rgyal pos chos zhus pa lta ci smos te/ 'jig rten bya ba chen po rnams kyang bka' gros byed
pa'i gtan tshigs gcig 'di yin no/ /bla mas kyang chos dang mthun pa'i 'jig rten gyi bya ba legs pa rnams kyang / rgyal po la ston pa yin zer/ sman tshe rgyal pos 'go byas
ngo ltas pa rnams yong ba'i dus su/ ji ju'i mgon khang bstan pas/ rang re'i yul du dmag sna la byon pa'i mi nag 'khor bcas de pa yang 'di na 'dug ces zer lo/ /yon mchod
gnyis bka' sgros nas ba yan ching sang sman tsher btang nas rgyalal khams blangs pa'i don la 'gro mgon 'phags pas khyed rang lus ma bskyod par/ sman tshe'i rgyal rab mang
po'i bar du/ khong rang 'jags zin gyi rgyal khams rang res lon pa 'dzam gling gcig tu 'dres 'drar gyur/ khyed rang 'khor los sgyur rgyal dag dang mtshungs/ zhes pa'i bstod
pa mdzad pa'ang 'dug mdor na 'gro mgo na chos kyi rgyal pos byin rlabs nas/ hor dang rgya nag po'i 'byor ba chen pos/ sa skyas 'go byas bod yul 'dir

bstan pa'i mthil yod pa/ yon mchod 'di gnyis kyi bka' drin yin pa gda'/yi ge'i ngo bo cong zhu zhing gi khrims ra na 'dug pa/ bca' tshe blangs 'dug pa de ngo bshus sbag po
ching sang gis dpon chen dbang phyug brtson 'grus la byin nas/ yu gur gyi yi ge ngo bo ta'i dben mthong ji deb ther hor gyi ma yig dang lhan cig tu yodapa/ yar lung pas khyer
'dug na'ang / don 'di rnams blo la yod pas skabs don bris pa yin yang bsod nams can se chen rgyal po'i dus su/ mi chen sam gha bya ba de/ rus pa bka' ma log yin pa'i
mi gzhon zhig hor skad rgya skad yu gur skad bod skad la sogs/ skad rigs sna tshogs shes pa'i lo tsA ba zhig dang po bla ma 'phags pas mdo smad rgya bod kyi mtshams su byon
dus mjal nas shed mong 'dab pa/ ja zhus pas lo tsA ba la bcug zu gu chen po'ang byed gin yod pa'i dus su/ khong shes rab che/ skad rigs mkhas pa'i don la/ bla ma mnyes
nas rgyal po'i drung du yang yang mngags pas/ gong mas kyang shes rab dang yon tan la dgongs nas/ bla ma la bslangs/ las ka rim par bskos pas/ go chod po byung / son jing
dben gyi mi dpon bskos pa'i dus su/ khong gi me tog ra ba'i bde chen gyi rtsar/ bla ma la chos zhus pa'i sgos kyi mtshams khang zhig byas pa la/ tha'i sas skyon bzung
nas/ saM gha btson du khyer ba'i dus su/ ka le hu na sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi sangs rgyas kyi sku bzhugs pa spyan drangs nas/ 'dzam bu gling 'dir rol mo dang
/ ltad mo yod pa la rgyal po'ang byon nas skor ba dang / gzigs mo mdzad pa'i sar/ bla ma gdan 'dren du btang bas/ bla ma'i gsung nas/ nged kyi bod yul na bu btson du khyer
ba'i pha

de/ sprang la 'gro ba la'ang ngo tsha byed/ nga'i saM gha nga la chos zhu ba la dmigs pa'i khang chung zhig byas pa la/ tha'i sas skyon du bzung nas btson du khyer 'dug na/nga
mi yong gsungs pas gong ma la zhus pas/ bla ma phebs pa'i gzim khang la dmigs pa yin na kho la skyon ma bzung bar thongs/ bla ma la byon gyis gsung pa'i lung byung byung
bas/ saM gha nyes pa las grol/ yon mchod zhal mjal/ slar yang son bying dben du bskos pa'i skabs su/ bla ma sa skyar byon/ dpon chen kun dga' bzang pos dam nyams byas
pa'i rgyu rkyen gyis/ gong du zhu ba btang bas/ sa skya ba dang sgos su 'brel che bas zhabs tog 'grub par dgongs nas/ mi chen sam ghas 'go byas khri dmag stobs che ba 'grim
gsungs pa/ lung byung gis sam ghas bod dbus gtsang sa rong dog dmag po che shong sa med/ rtsa ba'i hor dmag khri tsho bdun gyi steng du/ bod stod smad dang bcas pa'i
dmag 'bum phrag gcig lhag yong / des 'chun pas de bzhin gyi bka' gnang dgos zhus pa/ de ltar yin chug gsungs nas/ khri dmag bteg 'u yug me tog gling du slebs pa dang / sa
khad yangs pas lha shangs la dmag lam byed rtsis yod pa/ chab li grong pa slob dpon blo gros bzang pos dmag sgar du ja zhal la byon pas/ dmag lam lang 'gro nang la skyog
thub/ hor dmag gi kha 'bebs thum 'jug la/ snga sor lang 'gro mkhar dmar gyi mkhar phab/ babs blangs/ de rting dpal rnams bya rog tshang gi mkhar la sgyogs skor rgyag drag
po byas nas/ kun dga' bzang po khrims la bsgral/ dmag po che'i bya ba mthil phyin pa byas/ bla ma dang dgon pa phra mo la mos pa dang dad gus che ba'i stobs kyis/ sa skyar

byon/ lcog chung brang khang shar 'di khong gis bzhengs nas/ sgo yig g.yang tshe yang rgya lugs su yod cing bla ma'i drung du cis kyang yong ba'i dgongs pa mdzad par gda'/
de rting khrims dmag byings po phyir ldog spom 'bor sgang nas nyi ma mgon dang / dar dges 'go byas dmag rags bsdus brgya drug cu slob dpon dharma pha la'i sku srung la sa
skya nye 'khor du bzhag hor dmag stong tsho bdun gyi nang nas/ bdun brgya stod hor gyi so kha srung ba la ba la bzhag gnam dgon gsar du/ u dmar chag gi 'go byas hor dmag
grangs chen bzhi brgya bzhag rdor thas 'go byas sba rag gi dmag se ri rong la bzhag u phur gyi dmag lcags tshe gri gu dang / yar 'brog tu dung reng gi kha gnon la btang
nas bzhag hor ban du man gi dmag gdan sa spyi'i zhabs tog la 'dam/ na dmar/ na rong la sogs byang gi rtswa kha la bzhag pas/ saM gha de drin che/ de man la byang gi 'ja'
mo sogs/ swAg shag rtsi dmar/ sha pho/ skong / dgon gsar/ gya ba rnams kyi 'jams chen/ bod dbus gtsang gi khri skor rnams kyis 'dzin mkhan lo khor mar gtong dgos pas/ bka'
tshegs sbyong spyod shin tu che ba zhig yod pa 'dug cing / bod dmag rnams kyis byang ma thub par bros nas/ 'jam brang so ma zin pas/ hor bod kyi gser yig 'grul pa la sa
rim gyi o ge kha'i 'u lag rang rang la babs pa'i don la thams cad kyis zhus pa bzhin/ mi chen sang ghas phur dang sba rag la sogs pa'i dmag mi/ byang khar yod pa rnams 'ja'
mo'i za 'khri 'then pa la/ tha dad du bzhag nas/ dbus pa khri skor rnams kyi/ dud rta mgo'i steng nas rta khal pa/ bzhon ma/ bshas lug 'jams rgyags kyi nas/

cha ther sbra/ sga gdan/ khal g.yag thab chas/ gdan chas/ sman rin/ dud mi dang bcas pa hor la ster ba'i khrims bcas nas/ dbus pa byang du sdod mi dgos pa/ hor dmag rnams la
bod rdzas kyi 'jams skyor 'di rnams lo lo bzhin yong ba 'grul ba rnams la 'ja' mo/ 'u lag rnams ma stong pa byung nas/kun la phan pa 'di yang sam gha'i drin/ khong gis
bod 'khor nas/ cong zhu zhing gi ching sang la bskos pa'i dus su/ sngar mkhar ba'i dor tshe 'grim pa cha 'or gyur pas/ gan pa'i zhabs tog dang / rgyal khams la phan par byung
bas/ gtam snyan thob/ dang po mi dpon rnams kyi gsug zos pa'i don la nyes pa phog pa'i mi dpon mang po byung / khrims kyang yang por song ba/ sam gha ching sang gis
sngon rgya nag po'i dus kyi srol rnying pa zhig btsal nas/ khrims ra che chung gi mi dpon rnams la/ bza' rgyu dang / gon rgyu'i hun rtsen/ bud med la sogs pa la yang / za
'bras dmar po dang bcas pa byin nas/ gsug pa mi za ba'i khrims su bcas pas/ khrims dam por song / mi sde'ang skyid/ da lta'i bar la mi dpon rnams la hun rtsen 'jags pa yang
/ saM gha'i drin dran par byed/ gzhan yang bstan pa dang bod la phan pa dang / 'bul ba gtong ba la sogs pa'ang khong gi bla ma'i zhabs tog la dmigs nas zhus pas/ phan
pa mang po byung gda'o/ /yang don zhig la saM gha ching saM shes rab che/ longs spyod dang ldan pas hor mang po'i mig tu ma shong bar/ khong gi gan pa shas cha rkyen ma
phangs byas pas res pa she mong la bsnan zer ba'i don la ching sang gis/ gzhan ma'i cha rkyen gsug mar zas zer ba la bsnyad byas nas/ gong ma phyi lam du dos pa

rnams kyis zhus/ gtug gsher byas pas lung gis res pas ji ltar byed 'chos nged shes mod/ saM gha la don ci yod/ gsug pa byas na gzhan gyi gtug mod/ kho la cha rkyen 'dug zer
nas nyes pa 'tshal ga nas nyan gsungs nas zhu ba ma bzhes kyang / dos dpon rnams kyis res pa rnams skul nas/ bskyar gin zhus pas de gong nas snon thabs mdzad/ saM gha la
u lug dang / khyed gnyis 'phrod par gyis gsungs byung nas/ saM ghas u lug gung gral la bzhag ston mo bzang po byin nas saM gha rang gi zhwa gos ske rags phul/ an ta byed
byas pas/ zhwa gos ske rags khyer na mi 'dod/ ston mo gong ma'i gsol ras yin pas zos yod/ zer nas/ bzhud skad/ rting du yang res pa rnams kyis res dpon rnams dang / u lug
no yon bskul nas/ saM gha la sngar bzhin skyon bzung nas zhus pa'i mthar/ kho'i cha rkyen la bsnyad nas nyes pa len gar nyan/ rgyal khams kyi cha rkyen rnams nga rang gi
yin/ de yin na nga rang gis dri ba byed gsungs nas/ saM gha la sngar gtsigs che/ phang byed pa'i dus su/ rgyal po rang gi mkhyen pas/ nyes pa gsangs zin rnams phyis rtol
ba la/ sam gha khyod shang mdo nas/ ta'i tur mngags dus 'ur rdo 'grims pa'i lam du/ shing sdong po'i rtsa bar nged bsil grib la sdod pa'i khri thog tu khyod kyis bsdad
pa dang / ta'i tu nas nged la skur ba'i se thog gi sgam/ hung la bshig nas zas phud khyod kyis zas pa'i nyes pa med dam/ yang nged lus rngul che bas gos dri ma can bkrus
te/ bskyar nas btsem dus/ dog mor 'gro yin 'dug pas/ de'i don la/ rgya'i 'thag mkhan gyis gos srubs med pa btags pa ston pa gnyis yod pa khyod la gsum 'dug

zer/ nga las lhag pa byed pa khyod kyi nyes pa min nam gsungs te/ dri ba gsum po mdzad rting la/ ding sang rgyal khams kyi bya ba pher ba'i mi ji 'dra yod gsungs pas/ mi gcig
gda'/ gzhan mi gda' zhus pa dang / gcig yod pa su yin gsungs/ ching sang kho rang gi sna la mdzub mo btsugs byung / de pho nya la bskul nas btang bas/ rjes na phar ching
sang ci zer lta mi btang bas/ khong sgrol ba'i sar slebs tsa na khyed rnams kyis/ mtshon rno ba dang / lag yang ba dang myur ba'i thabs kyis byas yod 'dug pa la/ sgrol
mkhan gyis khyod kyis bzlas pa'i khar mi 'gro/ ji ltar byed nged shes pa yin mod zer zhus pas/ rgyal po na re/ nga'i saM gha 'gro khar sems sdug tu bcug 'dug mi ngan de
rnams la rgyug pa brgya dang bdun re rgyob gsungs pa'i lung byung zer/ dus de tsa na bla ma 'phags pa bzhugs na/ thugs rje la bstan nas tshe thar 'gro zer gleng bar gda'/
'di 'das kyang phyag rjes can gyi blon po bzang por 'dug pas gnas lugs bris pa yin no/ // //

khri skor bcu gsum gyi dud kyi grangs dang 'ja' mo 'dzin lugs yod/ swa sti/ lhar bcas 'gro ba'i mun sel phyir/ /sangs rgyas shAkya thub 'khrungs nas/ /lo grangs sum stong nyis
brgya dang / /dgu bcu 'das dus hor yul du/ /bsod nams chen po'i chu gter las/ /rgyal po jing gir gan zhes pa/ /sa 'dzin rin chen 'khrungs par 'gyur/ /mi dbang de nas
rgyal rabs lngar/ /stobs kyi 'khor lo bsgyur mdzad pa/ /se chen gan zhes grags pa des/ /'jam dbyangs rnam 'phrul sa skya pa/ /chos rgyal 'phags pa spyan drangs nas/ /bcu
phrag lo ni song ba'i dus/ /sa pho 'brug lo shar ba dang / /gong nas mngags pa'i gser yig pa/ /a kon ming gling gnyis yong nas/ /mi sde sa cha dang bcas pa/ /chen po hor
gyis ming btags pa'i/ /rtsa ba'i dud drangs rtsis pa na/ /stod kyi mnga' ris skor gsum dang / /lha sde gzhung pa la sogs kyi/ khri stong gseb tu mi the bas/ /bod 'brog gang
yod zur bzhag nas/ /dbus gtsang khri skor so so yi/ /dud grangs bcas pa 'di ltar ro/ /la stod lho pa'i dud kyi grangs/ /stong dang dgu cu rtsa dgu yin/ /la stod byang
pa nyis stong dang / /nyi brgya lnga cu tham par bar brtsi/ /chu mig khri skor hor dud grangs/ /sum stong nyer gsum yod pa'i bar/ /zha lu khri skor sum stong dang / /brgyad
brgya dgu bcu rtsa

gnyis yod/ /byang 'brog khri skor rting la 'byung / /yar 'brog khri skor khyad chos la / /leb ni bcu drug zer ba de/ /hor dud phyed dang brgyad brgya'o/ /dbus phyogs rtsa dud
'khyer lugs ni/ /'bri gung bod 'brog gnyis po la/ /sum stong brgyad brgya sum cu yod/ /tshal pa sur stong bdun brgya yin/ /phag mo gru pa nyis stong dang / /bzhi brgya
sum cu rtsa brgyad yod/ /g.ya' bzang pa la sum stong dbang / /rgya ma ba dang bya yul ba/ /lnga stong dgu brgya phyed 'khyer yin/ /stag lung pa la lnga brgya dang / /de
steng lha 'brug la sogs pas/ kha 'thor stong dang bzhi brgya yod/ /tshul 'di hor dang sa skya pa/ /yon mchod 'brel nas dbus gtsang du/ /sa brtsis byas pa'i thog mar 'dug
/mnga' ris man nas zha lu yan/ /o kon mi ling zhes byas brtsis/ /de min 'bri khung yan gyi sa/ /si tu a skyid dag gis brtsis/ /de phyir sa skya'i dpon chen ni/ /zam glu gun
mi dban hu'i sa/ /ming thob shAkya bzang po de'i/ /deb ther shog ril can bzhin yin/ khri skor de pas dbus gtsang gi/ 'ja' mo 'dzin lugs 'di ltar snang / /lho byang mnga'
ris dang bcas pas/ /dpal ldan sa skya'i 'jams chen dang / /gyam ring zhabs kha mar la thang / /ma phang me tog si tu yi/ /'jams chung rnams dang bcas pa 'dzin/ /dar lung
'ja' mo chu mig pas/ /tshong 'dus 'jams chen zha lu pas/ /steng du bya rog tshang pa'i dud/ /lnga bcu rtsa bdun brgyab nas 'dzin/ /stag 'jam yar 'brog khri skor te/ /
bya rog chang ga rta 'go ni/ / nyi shu rtsa brgyad de dang ni/ /shangs kyi chu phyogs sta mgo'i grangs/ /bcu gcig rgyab nas 'dzin pa yin/ /yas sribs 'jams chung yar 'brog
pas/ /'dzin no de

rnams gtsang phyogs yin/ /dbus pas 'ja' mo 'dzin lugs ni/ /go dper 'jams chen 'bri khung pa'i/ /ga ra 'ja' mo bya yul ba'i/ /steng du tshal pa'i ri rtse dud/ /phyed dang bzhi
brgya bsnan pas 'dzin/ /brtsi bar 'ja' mo phag gru'i khar/ /sa stag hor dud lnga brgya dang / /lha sa'i drug brgya brgyab nas 'dzin/ /sha pho 'jams su gru gu sgang / kha
rag 'brug pa 'ol kha ba/ /grwa ma thang pa bsdus nas 'dzin/ /kong 'jams g.ya' bzang pa yis 'dzin/ /chu lug 'di dag sngon dus yin/ /de rting lo grangs nyi shu'i tshe/ /me
mo phag la khrims ra nas/ /dho shu a nu mkhan gnyis mngags/ /dbus gtsang sa rtsis zhib par byas/ /dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig/ //

dpal ldan sa skya 'khon gyi gdung rabs bzhugs so/ /bla ma dang mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgyal ba kun gyi mkhyen rab mtha' yas pa/ /gcig tu bsdus
nas sna mang gdul bya la/ /sna tshogs sprul pa'i thabs kyis don mdzad pa'i/ /'khon ston rim par byon pa'i zhabs la 'dud/ /dri med gdung rgyud rim par byon pa dang / /de'i
mdzad pa ngo mtshar mtha' yas pas/ /thub bstan gsal dang 'gro kun smin grol tshul/ /rnam thar ngo mchar phreng ba bdag gis spel/ /bdag cag gi ston pa thub pa'i rgyal
tshab dam pa/ 'khon gyi gdung rgyud rin po de nyid/ thog mar 'od gsal gyi lha las babs par bzhed de/ dang po sa gtsang gnas mtho ba/ la stod mnga' ris kyi sa char gnam nas/
lha mched gsum byon pa'i che ba gnam lha spyi ring / bar pa gnam lha g.yu ring / chung ba gnam lha dbu se bya ba byon/ de rnams la mi'i rje zhus pas/ chung ba de mi yul
du bzhugs nas/ mi'i rje mdzad/de la sras bzhi byung ba/ sa ji li spun bzhir grags so/ /de dag gis ldong rus chen bco brgyad dang 'thab/ de'i grogs la gnam lha g.yu ring
gis byon nas/ ldong rus chen bco brgyad po btul nas/ bran du byas skad do/ /'o na gdung rgyun 'di gang nas 'ded na/ gnam lha g.yu ring gis dmu'i bu mo/ dmu bza' ldem bu
khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras bdun byung ba la/ ma sang spun bdun du grags so/ /

de'i gcen po drug yab dang bdun/ dmu thag dang dpyang thag la lha yul du byon/ chung ba des thog lha 'od chen gyi bu mo/ thog can 'ur ma khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras thog rtsa
dpa' bo stag byung ngo / /des klu'i bu mo klu mo lcam gra ma khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras klu tsha ta pho 'od chen byung / de dang mon za mtsho rgyal bshos pa'i sras gcig byung
ba/ de g.ya' dang spang gi mtshams su skyes pas/ ming g.ya' spang skyes su btags so/ /de rting srin po skya rengs khrag med bya ba la/ chung ma g.ya' 'brum si le ma
zer ba'i shin tu mtshar ba zhig yod pas/ skya rengs khrag med bsad/ g.ya' 'brum si le ma phrogs nas/ khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras gcig byung ba de srin po dang 'khon pa'i bar
du skyes pa la/ de'i ming 'khon bar skyes bya bar btags te/ de nas gdung rus 'khon zhes bya bar grags so/ /des btsan bza' lcam bu mon khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras gcig 'khrungs
te/ de nyid ni mthu dang rdzu 'phrul che ba/ blo dang rig par ldan pa/ gzugs dang / longs spyod rgyas pa/ mthong ba tsam gyis yid 'phrog pa/ shin tu ngo mtshar ba zhig
byung bas/ 'di 'dra mi yul du 'byon pa dkon zer nas/ dkon pa rje khung stag tu btags so/ khye'u de yab kyis yul gang bzang brtag tu btang bas/ snyan tshe dar gyi ya chang
la yul gyi dge brgyad tshang bar gzigs nas/ 'khon gyi yul la snga ba de yin no/ /de'i dus su bod na sprul pa'i rgyal po khri srong lde btsan bzhugs pas/ dkon pa rje
'di blo che zhing / 'jig rten gyi bya ba la mkhas pa'i don gyis bod rgyal po'i nang rje yun ring du byas/ dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs pa byung bas/ ming la 'khon dpal 'byor
cher grags te/

de nas 'khon la mi chos kyi sgo nas/ snyan grags che bar byung ngo / /de nyid kyis rlangs khams pa lo tsA ba'i lcam mo rlangs bza' sne chung khab tu bzhes pa la sras 'khon
klu'i dbang po bsrung ba dang / gcung rdo rje rin chen byung / chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan gyi sku ring la/ za hor gyi mkhan po bho dhi satwa spyan drangs/ de'i dngos
slob bod kyi btsun pa la snga ba sad mi mi bdun du grags pa byung bas/ rgan gsum ni/ dbas ratna rakShi ta/ rin chen bsrung ba/ bha dznyAnte rakShi ta/ ye shes dbang po bsrung
ba/ rta dbyangs sprul par byed/ ratna ne nTe rakShi ta rin chen sprul par byed/ bar pa gcig rlangs khams lo tsA bas te/ su ga ta/ warma rakShi ta/ bde bar bshegs pa
bsrung ba zhes pa'o/ /gzhon gsum ni ba gor bai ro tsa na rakShi ta/ rnam par snang mdzad bsrung ba dang / 'khon na gendra rakShi ta/ klu'i dbang pos bsrung ba/ gtsang de
bendra rakShi ta/ lha'i dbang po bsrung ba bya ba de rnams byon te/ 'khon klu'i dbang po de nyid ni/ lo tsA ba gzhon gsum gyi nang nas/ thugs rab shin tu che zhing dba'
ye shes dbang po dang / rang gi zhang po'i thad du slob gnyer gsan sbyong mdzad pas/ sngags mtshan nyid kyi yon tan phun sum tshogs pa mnga' zhing / slob dpon padma la'ang
rdo rje phur pa dang / yang dag la sogs mang du zhus nas/ yer pa'i brag la sgrub pa mdzad/ grub pa brnyes so/ /de nas 'khon la lha chos kyi ngos nas grags pa shin tu che
ba byung ngo / /de'i gcung po rdo rje rin chen pas kyang / slob dpon padma dang rang gi gcen la dbang dang gdam ngag mang tu nod de mkhas par grags shing / slob dpon padma'i
dngos slob/ dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo brgyad du grags pa'i gseb tu gtogs

so/ /sngags rnying ma'i 'go yang 'di tsam nas tshugs pa yin/ de gong du spyir bod dang / sgos su 'khon la sngags pa dang rab byung gi tha snyad ma byung bar 'dug go /'khon
rdo rje rin chen pas 'bro dgra 'dul gyi bu mo 'bro g.yang lon skyid de khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras 'bro tsha spun bdun byung te/ 'bro snyan rtse ba'i gson gshid kyi ltad mo/
nyi ma gsum btud byas dus/ khong spun bdun posanyi ma re la rta lus chas 'dra 'dra ba 'ba' zhig spos nas/ rta rgyug rtsal 'gran pas khrom thog chod pa byung / 'bro'i bsam
pa la khong la mtho mtshams par go nas/ dmag bsags 'khrug pa byed zer ba la/ gcig par zhang po yin/ gnyis par 'grogs yun ring po song bas 'khrug pa mi byed/ rgyal khams
yangs po la 'jigs med gsungs nas/ 'bro tsha spun bdun gyi che ba/ mar yul du byon/ de 'og rnams rim pa bzhin gung thang / gad/ gnyal lo ro/ myang shab/ grom pa g.ya' lung
rnams su gyes so/ /tha chung gi yab yul du bzhugs/ 'bro dang 'khrug pa yang sprad/ de las gyes pa snyan tshe reng na/ ma khrigs sde gsum du grags pa yod do/ /tha ltag
grom par byon pa de'i mtshan shes rab yon tan/ de la sras gnyis byung ba'i che ba tshul khrims rgyal po/ chung ba khab so stag thog tu byon/ der yang 'khon ci rigs pa 'phel
te/ de nas g.yas ru byang du gyes pa'i 'khon tsho'i sde pa mang du yod do/ /'khon tshul khrims rgyal po la sras gsum byung ba'i che ba gtsug tor shes rab la sras bdun
byung ba/ khu bo chung ba dang bcas pa 'khon g.ya' lung na yod/ sras bdun po'i lnga pa 'khon dge skyabs/ des shab tu byon/ de la sras gnyis byung ba'i che ba 'khon dge mthong
/ chung ba las

shab stod kyi 'khon mi rnams gyes pa yin skad/ dge mthong gi sras 'khon ston bal po/ des tsha mo rong glang gi brag la/ yang phur gyi sgrub pa mdzad pas/ grub pa brnyes shing
bstan ma bcu gnyis bran du 'khol ba'i nus mthu can cig byung ngo / /de'i sras shAkya blo gros kyis/ bya ru lung dang / shab stod smad du yang yun ring du bzhugs zhing
sku tshe'i smad la yab mes kyi yul/ g.ya' lung mkhar thabs su byon/ de la sras gnyis kyi che ba/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims ni/ yab mes kyi chos lugs la rgyud sbyangs
shing / rdo rje phur pa'i grub pa brnyes nas/ mthu dang rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan zhing / gzhon nu la gzhu ston gzhon nu brtson 'grus kyi drung du/ go
mi dge bsnyen mdzad shin tu btsun zhing / tshangs par spyod pas mdzes la mkhas pa dang / bzang po'i grags pa cher thob pa zhig byung ngo / /'di go mi dge bsnyen yin pas
sras 'phel ba med/ de man chad 'khon rim par byon pa rnams/ pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs/ phyi mtshan nyid kyi chos rnams dang / rdo rje theg pa la gsang ba sde drug sngags
snga 'gyur lnga/ phra mo nyi shu rtsa gcig la sogs pa/ gsang sngags snga 'gyur gyi chos rnams la shin du mkhas zhing / yang phur la thugs dam gyi mthil mdzad cing / grub
pa ci rigs pa brnyes la/ chos skyong dkar mo nyi zla lcam sring la byed cing / nus pa thon pa sha stag byon no/ /'khon rog gi gcung po ni/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po zhes
bya ba/ de nyid ni shing pho khyi lo la sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nyid nas yab dang / gcen la dbang dang gdams ngag zhus ste/ yab mes kyi chos lugs la shin tu mkhas pa byas
shing / gsang sngags phyi 'gyur la spro ba yod

pa'i skabs su/ 'bro'i lung ston chen po zhig byung ba'i tshe/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal pos kyang byon/ ltad mo de dang / rtsed mo mang du 'dug pa'i nang nas/ sngags pa 'ga'
zhig gis/ dbang phyug ma nyi shu rtsa brgyad kyi mgo brnyan rnams gyon nas phyag mtshan so sor khyer/ ma mo ral pa can dang / lcam dral 'cham gyin 'dug pas/ de kha ltad mo
yang che/ khrom thog kyang des bcad song bas/ phyir log nas gcen la 'di lta bu gda' zhus pas/ gcen na re/ de gsang sngags 'chol ba bya ba'i dus byung ba yin/ phyin chad
rnying ma la grub thob mtshan nyid pa mi yong / rang re la yod pa kun rang dbang che bas/ a po rgan pa'i dpe cha lha rten/ gsang sngags kyi lag cha kun gter du sba'o/ /nga
ni na so rgas 'dugakhyed gzhon pa yin pas gsang sngags gsar 'gyur bya ba bzang po yod pa 'dug cing / de'ang mang mkhar na/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba mkhas par yod 'dug pas/ de
la slob tu rgyug gsungs nas/ dpe rnying thams cad gter du sbas so/ /der chos skyong gis cho 'phrul byung nas/ phur pa'i chos 'khor ci rigs pa dang / gtor ma'i cho ga seng
ldeng gi phur pa bco lnga pa cha gnyis dang / dkar mo nyi zla nyid kyis 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims rang la zhal dngos su bstan nas/ mdzad pa'i gtor chog rnams/ bton
nas gcung la gnang / gdung rgyud pa rnams da lta'ang dus gtor ma chag pa mdzad dgos so/ /de na bla la dkon mchog rgyal po mang mkhar mug gu lung du 'brog mi'i spyan sngar
