ma thon par/ g.ya' lung dur khrod du/ 'khyin lo tsA ba la brtag gnyis gsan/ de tshar la khad pa dang bla ma 'khyin sku gshegs pa'i zhal chems la/ chos 'phro de 'brog
mi

la zhus shig gsungs nas/ khong gi drung du phyin pas mnyes tshor chen po byas/ yul nas tshong 'phrul byas pa'i rta bcu bdun khal dang bcas pa/ rtsa rin la jo mo'i nor 'phreng
bzang po zhig khur yod pa/ de rnams phul nas gsung ngag rin po che zhus pas/ rim gyis gnang zhing / gzhan yang gsar 'gyur gyi chos phal che ba gsan sbyong rgya chen po
mdzad pas/ chos kyi mnga' bdag chen por gyur to/ /de nas zhang yul 'jag gshongs su/ yab dang gcen gyi sku 'bum bzhengs/ de'i nang du phur pa byin rlabs can cig kyang gzhug
phur pa cha gcig gar gshegs sar thugs dam la bsnams/ phyis sa skya na yod zer ro/ /g.ya' lung chu skyar du bzhugs/ bra bo lung par dgon chung zhig btab nas lo 'ga' bzhugs/
sa skya gog por grags so/ /de'i tshe dpon slob 'ga' zung gis skyo sangs la byon ri rtse nas gzigs pas/ 'dir dgon pa zhig btab na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang / 'gro
ba mang po la phan thogs pa zhig yong ba 'dug dgongs pa byung te/ jo bo gdong nag pa la zhus pas gnang / sa de'i sgos kyi bdag po zhang zhung gu ra ba ban de grong bzhi/
lha mo gong bdun bya ba 'dug pa la/ sa cha 'dir nged dgon chung zhig byed pa la/ khyed rnams la 'gal med na rin yang 'jal byas pas/ rin ye mi 'tshal dgon pa mdzad par zhu
zer ba la/ 'on kyang phyis tshun chad 'di 'thad pa yin gsungs nas/ rgod ma dkar mo gcig mo gos gcig nor bu'i phreng ba gcig khrab gcig rnams kyi 'go byas rin bcal/ mon
'brog nas/ bal 'brog yan gyi sa de bla mas bdag par byas skad/ bla ma de nyid dgung lo bzhi bcu bzhes pa'i dus su/ thub pa sa pho 'brug

la bltams nas/ me mo phag la myang ngan las 'das rting / lo sum stong nyis brgya dang bdun song ba'i chu mo glang lo la/ dpal ldan sa skya'i gdan sa'i 'gram bting / bla brang
shar gyi cha 'di la/ bla brang gi mthil mdzad/ lcags ri rtsa brgyad du bya ba zhig yod do/ /bla ma de nyid kyi gdan sa lo sum cu bzung zhing / bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen
po mdzad nas/ dgung lo drug cu re dgu pa chu pho rta lo dbyug pa zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi la zhi bar gshegs so/ /gdan sa chen po 'gram bting ba'i/ chu mo glang lo de nas
da lan shing pho stag gi lo/ srog sme brgyad dkar dbus na yod pa 'di yan la/ lo sum brgya drug cu re gcig song 'dug go /bla ma dkon mchog rgyal po de nyid dgung lo nga
dgu bzhes pa'i dus/chu pho spre'u'i lo la/ jo mo chung shos gu ra ba'i sring mo zhang mo la sras shig 'khrungs pa ni sa chen kun dga' snying po zhes bya'o/ /de'i mdzad pa
rnam thar rgya che ba ni/ rnam thar chen mor blta'o/ /de'ang sras 'di 'khrungs pa yum gyis re zhig gsangs nas yod pa la/ chen ma rdo rje phyug mos tshor nas/ 'o skol gyi
gdung rgyud 'di 'chad du phangs pa la/ zhang mo la sras shig yod par gda' ba nan tar legs/ nga la gsang mi 'tshal/ da nga la nor mi dgos/ bu'i a ma la dgos pa yin zer nas/
sa skya mdun gyi mchod zhing ma gtogs/ gzhan thams cad yum sras la gtad/ gzhon nu nyid nas rig pa'i gnas mtha' dag la sbyangs shing / thog mar yab la dgyes pa rdo rje'i
dbang zhus/ de dag gi thugs la mnga' ba'i chos thams cad zhus/ dgung lo bcu gnyis lon pa dang yab bde bar gshegs te/ rtsis byas pas gshegs rdzongs byed pa dang / phyi
rten 'gram

'ding ba/ gdan sa bsko ba rnams nyi ma gcig la grub na rjes su phun sum tshogs pa 'byung zer nas/ yum na re/ nyid rang gi yab kyi slob dpon yang lo tsA ba yin/ lo tsA ba dang
'brel ba'i chos 'di nan tar rdzun chung gsungs nas mnyes pa gcig yod/ khyed chung bas 'u cag ga gdan sa mi zin/ gdan sa 'di ba ri lo tsA ba la gtad pa drag zer/ ba ri
ba g.yu mkhar mo na yod pa gdan drangs nas gdan sa gtod pa dang / gshegs rdzongs chos 'khor byed/ phyi rten 'gram 'ding ba rnams nyi ma gcig la tshar bar mdzad/ zhing mo
che ma gtogs gzhan thams cad bla ma ba ri ba la gtad/ ba ri ba'i zhal nas khyed jo sras kyi bu bya ba/ slob gnyer byed dgos pa yin/ de la shes rab dgos pa yin/ de'i lha 'phags
pa 'jam dpal/ a ra pa tsa na dhi sgrubs gsungs nas/ sgrub pas zla ba drug na 'jam dpal dngos su zhal gzigs/ sgrub khang 'jam dpal brag khung du grags pa bla brang shar
gyi dkyil na yod do/ /de ltar yi dam gyi lhas mngon sum du byin gyis brlabs pas/ shes bya phal che ba thugs su chud yod kyang / gang zag rnams kyi bsam blo dang bstun
pa'i phyir/ gzhon nu nyid nas slob gnyer la thugs gtad de/ sngun la rong ngur mig du drang ti dar ma snying po la / mngon pa slob tu byon/ bla ma ba ri bas gdan sa lo brgyad
mdzad pa'i ring la/ dbus gtsang mnga' ris man kyi sa cha na bzhugs pa'i/ bla ma lo paN bzang tshad kyi zhabs la gtugs nas/ thos pa gsan sbyong mthar phyin pa mdzad cing
/ ba ri lo tsA ba'i thugs la yod tshad kyi yon tan bum pa gang byos gnang te/ lo brgyad thims nas gdan sa bla ma sa chen la gtad/ ba ri ba bar phug tu zhi

bar gshegs so/ /de nas bgres po rnams gros byas nas/ da pha chos shig brtsad bcad pa drag pa 'dug zer/ 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar gyi drung du byon pas/ dbang bskur zhus
pas/ sta gon gyi nub mo srid pa'i rgya mtsho yin zer ba'i chu chen po dmar me re ba zhig la zam pa gsum 'dug pa'i 'gram na/ nga sgrol bar zhu zer ba'i mi mang po 'dug
pa/ zam pa phyi ma la mi gsum/ bar pa la mi bdun/ nye ba de la mi mang po zhig sgrol ba rmis/ cung snyel nas nyi ma gcig la snyel ba gso ba snyam byed tsa na/ mnal sad/ nang
par rmi lam 'di 'dra byung zhus pas/ bla ma'i zhal nas khyod kyi mkhos khas mi gsum las gang na sgrol gsungs/ zhal kur yang mdzad/ de nas bla ma de nyid kyis dbang bskur/
rgyud lung man ngag thugs la mnga' tshad rdzogs par gnang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis rjes su bzung nas/ chos thams cad tshar re gsan pa dang thugs su chud pa byung skad
do/ /bla ma sgyi chu ba zhi bar gshegs dus/ zhal chems la/ kun dga' snying po khyod rab tu byung la 'khon tsho'i sde 'di skyongs gsungs pa/ bzhag pa yang 'dug pa bzhin/
rab tu byung dgongs pa la/ bla ma gnam kha'u ba'i zhal nas/bla ma mnyam po'i nang nas khong gshin po las/ nga gson po'i ngag la nyon/ khyod rab tu ma byung na sems can la
pan che bar 'dug gsung nas ma gnang / rab tu ma byung kyang 'khon tsho'i dpon mdzad/ yang gung thang na la rtse gnas sar du/bla ma mal lo tsA ba la chos zhus/ bla mas mgon
po'i rjes gnang sgrub thabs las tshogs tshang ma gnang / de'i rten du bse 'bag nag po 'gro shes dang / dar nag la gri khrag gis rtsa sngags bris pa/ lcags kyi rdo rje
rtse dgu pa gcig dang

bcas te/ chos skyong la mi lab pa bzhin du/ da nga na so rgas pa la khyod mi dgos/ khyod rang 'khon sa skya ba'i rjes la song zhig gsungs nas brdzangs pa/ de phyin chad sa
skya pa'i chos skyong gur mgon la byed pa byung ba yin no/ /bla ma zhang ston chos 'bar la gsung ngag ri po che zhus/ bla ma gnam kha'u pa la chos skyong zhal bzhi pa'i sgrub
thabs cha lag tshang ma zhus/ de nas sa skya pa'i chos skyong che chung du grags pa byung ngo / /bla ma sa chen 'di nyid kyis gdan sa lo zhe brgyad bzung ba'i dgung
lo drug cu rtsa bdun pa sa pho stag gi lo/ tha skar zla ba'i dkar phyogs tshes bcu bzhi'i dus su/ g.yas ru skya bo'i kha gdangs su zhi bar gshegs so/ /de'i dus su kun gyi
mthun snang grub par/ bde ba can dang / po ta la dang / u rgyan dang / byang phyogs gser mdog can rnams su gshegs pa'i sku'i bkod pa bzhi bstan par grags so/ /bla ma de
nyid kyi jo mo chung ba/ jo lcam phur ma la/ thog mar sras kun dga' 'bar 'khrungs/ gzhon nu la rgya gar du byon/ ma ga dhar/ rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas par gyur nas/ bod
la 'byon khar tshad pa'i snyung gzhis dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa la ma ga dhar zhi bar gshegs so/ /jo mo che ba tsha mo rong pa/ ma gcig 'od sgron ma'i sras che ba/
slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ yab dgung lo nga bzhi pa'i dus su chu pho khyi lo la sku 'khrungs te/ sku bltams pa tsam gyis pha rol tu phyin pa'i blo gros dang
ldan pa zhig go/ dgung lo zhe gcig pa chu pho stag gi lo smal po zla ba'i tshestshe bcu gcig la zhi bar gshegs so/ /bar pa rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan ni/ yab dgung lo
nga drug pa'i dus/ me mo yos lo smal po zla ba'i tshes brgyad la sku

'khrungs te/ bzod pa thob pa'i rgyal ba yin cing / dbu rtse rnying ma bzhengs/ rgyas par rnam thar chen mor blta'o/ /gdan sa lo zhe lnga mdzad/ dgung lo bdun cu pa me pho byi
lo khra zla ba'i tshes bcu gnyis pa bde ba can du gshegs so/ /gcung po chung ba dpal chen 'od po ci yab dgung lo nga dgu pa/ lcags pho rta lo smin drug zla ba'i nyi shu
lnga la 'khrungs te/ nga bzhi bzhes pa chu mo phag lo zla ba lnga pa'i nyi shu gcig la bde ba can du gshegs so/ /bla ma de'i jo mo ma gcig gar phu ma nyi ri lcam la/ sras
che ba chos rje sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po de nyid yab dgung lo so gsum bzhes pa'i dus chu pho rta lo khra zla ba'i nyi shu drug la sku 'khrungs
te/ gzhon nu nyid nas yab mes kyi chos lugs/ ma lus par mkhyen cing / dgung lo nyi shu rtsa lnga lon pa'i me pho stag lo la/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ 'khor paN chung
mang po dang bcas pa bod du byon dus/ myang smad rgyan gong gi gtsug lag khang du/ paN chen gyis mkhan po mdzad/spyi bo lhas pas slob dpon mdzad/ zhu 'phreng bas gsang
ste ston pa mdzad nas/ rgya bod kyi dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i dbus su rab tu byung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs pa yang de ltar ro/ /bla brang shar/ shar pa shes rab 'byung
gnas la gnang / bzhi thog bla brang btab/ kha che paN chen la sogs pa mkhas grub mang po bsten/ rig pa'i gnas lnga la phul du phyin nas/ skyid grong du 'phrog byed dga'
bo la sogs/ mu stegs kyi ston pa drug btul/ 'khor bcas rab tu byung nas/ nang pa'i bstan pa la btsud/ chos kyi mnga' bdag chen por gyur/ dgung lo drug cu re gsum bzhes
pa shing pho 'brug lo la/ hor gyi rgyal po e chen go

dan gyis gdan 'dren la rdo tha che bya ba mngags byung dus/ bla mas dgongs pa gtad/ rten 'brel rtags pas/ dang por khu bo rje btsun chen po'i gsungs nas/ khyod la dus nam zhig
shar phyogs nas gdan 'dren 'di lta bu zhig yong /de'i dus the tshom med par song zhig bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don la phan par yod do gsungs pa'i lung bstan gnang ba thugs
kyis zin te/ sa skyar chos dpon la bla ma 'u yug pa bsod nams seng ge dang / shar pa sher 'byung / gdan sa'i brjid 'khur ba la bzhag nang gnyer ba grom pa shAkya bzang
po bskos nas/ bla ma'i phyag phyir dbon chen 'phags pa dang / phyag na gnyis kyang sku gzhon nu la khrid nas byon/ lam la lo gsum 'gor/ byang ngos su rta'i lo gzhug la
phebs/ rgyal pos go yug rgyal sar bton pa'i mjal 'phrad 'khor ba dang / lug lo la yon mchod mjal nas gnam mchod pa'i rgan pa thob/ rgyal po'i bla ma dang sangs rgyas kyi
bstan pa phyogs kun tu dar zhing rgyas pa mdzad/ hor sa skya pa 'brel ba'i snga ma yin no/ /bla ma 'dis gdan sa lo so lnga mdzad/ dgung lo bdun bcu pa lcags mo phag lo/
smal zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi la/ ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te/ byang ngos sprul pa sde'i/ lha khang du bde bar gshegs so/ /de na sku 'bum mchod pa'i rgyun dang
bcas pa yang bzhugs so/ /bla ma de'i gcung slob dpon chen po zangs tsha bsod rgyal ni/ yab dgung lo zhe lnga pa'i dus shing pho 'brug lo la sku 'khrungs/ khong rang gi mda'
rgyang la tshad mdzad pa'i dan gyi lcags ri btab rgyal sgo bcug lnga bcu rtsa drug pa sa mo phag lo la stod kyi pa ri ru sku gshegs so/ /des jo mo lnga khab tu

bzhes pa la/ rigs kyi sras pho bzhi dang / sras mo bzhi 'khrungs pa'i thog mar/ ma cig kun skyid la sras gnyis kyi che ba/ bla ma 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po ba/ yab dgung lo nga gnyis pa'i dus/ shing mo lug lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes drug la sku 'khrungs/ 'di nyid ni dang po nyid nas sbyangs pa dang / skyes stobs kyi shes
rab dpag tu med pa mnga' bas/ gzhon nu nyid nas slob gnyer gsan sbyong mdzad pas/ gang la'ang mthong ba tsam gyis mkhyen pa kho na byung / thams cad kyis 'di lta bu khyad
'phags zer/ mtshan yang 'phaT pa zhes su grags pa yin la/ dgung lo bcu pa'i dus su/ chos rje sa paN gyi phyag phyir byang ngos la byon pa'i lam du zul phur chos rjes mkhan
po dang / zul phu mkhan chen chos kyi byang chub pas/ slob dpon mdzad nas rab tu byung / byang ngos sprul pa sder/ /khu dbon pa phebs dus/ se chen rgyal po'i lung gis
byang ngos na/ sa skya bla ma bya ba khyad 'phags sleb yod 'dug pa/ nged kyi bla mchod byed dgos gsungs pa byung nas/ chos rje pa sku nas bgres pas ma byon/ bla ma 'phags
pas rgya nag tu byon/ se chen rgyal po dang mjal bas shin tu mnyes te/ hor gyi rta pa brgya skor gcig byang ngos la phyin nas sa skya pa dang yon mchod du 'brel/ bla ma'i
brtag pa mdzad rin dang / byang ngos su chos rje pa bde bar gshegs pa'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs sgrub pa la sogs pa rgya hor gyi yul du/ lo mang bar bzhugs/ dgung lo nyer
gcig pa shing mo yos lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin/ rgya yul gyi he tse hu dang nye ba'i sar/ phywa pa chos kyi seng ges thog drangs pa'i mkhan slob gsang ston dad
dge la sogs pa bzang la mang ba'i dbus su

bsnyen par rdzogs par mdzad/ de nas pho brang ta'i tur byon nas/ se chen rgyal po yab yum sras bcas la/ rgyud gsum gyi dbang mo che bskur/ ti shri'i mtshan gsol/ dbus gtsang
gi khri skor bcu gsum dang / dbang yon bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ hor sa skya pa yon mchod du 'brel/ bod yul go pe le'i mnga' 'og tu tshud pa'i snyan grags brjod pa dang
/ 'ja' mo 'dzugs pa la mi chen das sman bya ba sa skya man la mngags/ se chen gyis gser yig pa bod la btang ba'i sngon ma de yin/ de'i phyi lo me pho 'brug la bla ma dbus
gtsang du phebs/ lo de la dpon chen shAkya bzang pos/ lha khang chen mo'i 'gram gzhi bting / de nas da lta shing pho stag lo srog sme brgyad dkar dbus na yod pa 'di yan
la/ lo brgya dang brgyad cu gya gcig song 'dug sa skya'i 'gram 'ding ba dang lha khang gi bar na lo brgya dang brgyad cu yod par 'dug de rting yang bla ma 'di gong du
byon/ rgyal po yab yum sras bcas la dbang bskur ba'i dbang yon bar ma la bod chol kha gsum po phul/ gsum pa la rgya'i yur ma chen mo phul nas bcad/ bsngo bas rgyas btab zer
ba 'dug cing / che ba'i yon tan mtha' yas mnga' bas/ bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don rgya chen po mdzad tshul rgyas pa rnam thar chen mo na gsal lo/ /bla ma 'dis gdan sa lo
so drug mdzad/ dgung lo zhe drug lcags pho 'brug lo smal zla ba'i tshes nyer gnyis kyi snga gro nyi ma me bzhi 'phrad pa'i tshe/ dkon mchog la mchod pa shoms gsungs/ skyil
mo krung mdzad/ rdo rje dril bu thugs kar snol nas/ rtse gcig tu bzhugs pa'i ngang la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te/ dpal ldan sa skya'i lha khang bla brang
du bde bar gshegs so/ /

de'i gcung po slob dpon phyag na rdo rje ni/ yab dgung lo drug cu pa'i dus/ sa mo phag la sku 'khrungs shing / dgung lo drug pa'i dus byang ngos la chos rje pa'i phyag phyir
byon/ sa skya pa rnams kyi dbon po mched gnyis sku na phra bas 'byon mi thub 'jog par zhu zhus pas/ chos rje'i gsung nas/ sgo nga bya'i drod la skye ba yin gsungs nas khrid/
bzhag na phyis mi mjal bar mkhyen pa yin 'dugasku na phra mo de nas phas kyi rgol ba tshar gcod cing / 'gro ba sbyor sgrol thub pa'i ngo mtshar can cig byung zhing
/ chos rje pa dang / gcen la dbang dang gdams pa mang du zhus/ rgyal po go dan gyi hor chas su bcug cing / dpon mo buddha me ga dun gnang / se chen rgyal po dang mjal nas/
pa'e len dbang gi ming dang / gser tham thong ji g.yas g.yon gyi khrims ra dang bcas pa gnang / bod spyi'i steng du bskos/ spyir bod dang sgos sa skya pa la dbang gi lung
las ka gnang ba'i snga ma 'di yin no/ /de nyid dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu pa/ me mo yos lo zla ba bdun pa'i tshes gnyis la dpe khang gzims khang du bde bar gshegs so/ /ma
gcig jo mo 'gro la sras lcam sring gnyis byung ba'i gcen slob dpon chen po rin chen rgyal mtshan ni/ yab dgung lo so gcig pa'i dus sa pho khyi lo la sku 'khrungs/ rgyud
lung man ngag thams cad mkhyen nas/ se chen rgyal po'i bla mchod mdzad/ bla ma 'phags pa bod la byon shul du me tog ra bar gdan sa lta bu mdzad/ pho brang nye bar dge 'dun
gyi sde shing kun bde chen btsugs/ bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don la brtson pa'i ngang nas/ dgung lo zhe gnyis bzhes pa me mo yos lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bcu la shing
kun du sku gshegs so/ /de'i lcam mo/ slob

dpon ma cig me tog bya ba sku 'khrungs so/ /yang gung thang btsad po'i sras mo lha cig mdzes ma la/ slob dpon ma bsod nams 'bum pa dang / nyi ma 'bum 'khrungs te/ che bas rab
byung mdzad/ jo mo gling btab btsun ma'i sde btsugs so/ /lha cig mdzes ma'i nye gnas ma jo mo rdo rje gdan la/ slob dpon ye shes 'byung gnas 'khrungs pa yab dgung lo so
gcig pa'i dus sa pho khyi la/ slob dpon rin chen dang dus mnyam du 'khrungs te/ bla ma shar pa chen po sku mched pa la slob gnyer mdzad/ yon tan du ma dang ldan zhing /
mkhan po shar lag zugs par grags/ phyis rgyal po hu dkar che'i bla mchod mdzad/ ljang yul du byon/ dgung lo so bdun pa shing pho khyi lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu la
mdo khams su bde bar gshegs so/ /yang jo lcam hor mo la/ slob dpon ma rin chen 'byung gnas 'khrungs so/ /de rnams zangs tsha bsod rgyal gyi sras/ lcam sring brgyad yin
no/ /slob dpon phyag na la jo mo zha lu ma nam mkha' 'bum bya ba yod pa la/ phyag na rang bde bar gshegs nas/ zla ba drug song ba dang sa pho 'brug lo zla ba dang po la sras
bdag nyid chen po dharma pha la rakShi ta sku 'khrungs te/ 'phags pas zhal lta mdzad/ de'i bar chad bsrung ba'i phyir du shing khang bla brang bzhengs/ de'i zhabs tog
la zha lu bas/ zha lu khang gsar bzhengs nas phul ba lags so/ khu bos thugs gtsigs shin tu che bar mdzad cing / 'phags pa'i yon tan bum pa gang byo gnang / mdzad pa 'phrin
las thams cad khu dbon dbyer mi phyed zhes kun la grags shing / dgung lo bcu gsum pa la 'phags pa bde bar gshegs nas/ de'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs rgya chen po bsgrubs
shing / slob

gnyer gyi 'phro rnams shar pa ye rin la gtugs/ bcu bzhi pa la gong du byon rten dge bsnyen yin yang / bla ma'i gdan sa lta bur mdzad/ se chen rgyal po la zhus nas/ bla ma 'phags
pa'i sku gdung ring srel bzhugs pa'i shel gyi mchod rten chen po dang / de bzhugs pa'i me tog ra ba'i sde chen po bzhengs/ rting la/rgyal po ji big thi mur gyi sras
mo/ dpal ldan sa skyar gnang / lo lnga bzhugs bla mchod la bskos nas/ yar byon mdo khams su phebs shing / 'di'i gdan sa lo bdun mdzad/ dgung lo nyi shu pa me mo phag lo
smal zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te/ mdo khams te maNDal du zhi bar gshegs so/ /'di'i jo mo stag 'bum la sras dharma bha dra 'khrungs
gzhon nu la sku gshegs so/ /bla ma ye shes 'byung gnas/ dgung lo nyer lnga pa chu pho khyi lo la lung nag gnyer pa dpal rin gyi gzhi pa chos rin skyid la bla ma'i sras
gcig 'khrungs pa ni/ bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal ba de/ skyes stobs kyi thugs rab phun sum tshogs pa mnga' yang / sku gzhon nu'i dus su slob gnyer la sogs pa mdzad rgyu
cher ma byung / sman tshe'i yul la sogs su yun ring po 'byon dgos pa byung bas/ dharma pha la rakShi ta sku gshegs nas/ lo bco brgyad kyi bar la rgyud dri ma med pa dang
/ 'phrin las dbyer med pa 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan pas gdan sa mdzad/ 'chad nyan sgom sgrub gzhan phan bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po mdzad/ ces grags so/ /phyis
khang gsar ti shri sangs rgyas dpal bas/ bla ma'i dbu 'don gong du zhu ba legs pa la brten nas/ o ja du rgyal pos bla ma bdag nyid chen po gdung rgyud du mnga' gsol/
nga'i bla ma'i

gdung 'chad du phangs pas dbus gtsang du byon la/ gdung rgyud 'phel ba gyis gsungs pa'i lung gnang bas/ thog mar ma cig hor mo la sras slob dpon bsod nams bzang po/ lcags mo
yos lo la sku 'khrungs pa/ sku gzhon dus byang ngos su gu'i gung mdzad/ de rting gong ma a yu par pa ta ge gan rgyal pos/ pa'e len dbang gi mtshan dang / sras mo dpon mo
buddha gan gnang / yar byon mdo khams su sku gshegs so/ /'di la lcam mo gcig kyang byung ngo / /bla ma bdag nyid chen pos dbus gtsang du phebs nas rgyal po'i lung bzhin/
jo mo lnga khab tu bzhes shing / gdung rus gcig pa'i gdan sa 'dzin mkhan gzhan med pa'i don gyis/ yab mes kyi chos lugs rnams la'ang gsan sbyongs mdzad/ bla ma 'phags pa
dang dharma pha la'i phyi rten bzhugs sa'i gser thog g.yu thog dang /lha khang chen mo'i thigs khang du/ dkyil 'khor mi gcig pa drug brgya nyi shu rtsa dgu 'bri ba/ shing
mo lug lo la phyi'i lcags ri chen mo gcod pa la sogs pa'i zhal bkod mdzad cing / bstan pa dang rgyal khams gdan sa'i phyis su mdzad pa'i 'phrin las rgya chen po mdzad/
gdan sa'i dpal 'byor yang 'di'i ring las che ba ma byung zer ba 'dug ces grags so/ /bla ma 'di'i lha khang bla brang du lo bco lnga bzhugs/ bu yan du rgyal pos/ gu shri
gnang / bzhi thog tu bzhugs/ gdan sa lo zhe lnga nas/ re gsum gyi bar du lo bcu dgu mdzad/ re gsum pa shing pho byi lo la/ bzhi thog gzim khang du zhi bar gshegs/ bla ma
'di nyid la sras yongs su grags pa dgu gzhon nu la gshegs pa bzhi/ sras mo gnyis rnams byon pa gong du smos pa'i bsod nams bzang po lcam sring gnyis/ bod du

yar 'brog dpon chen gyis jo mor phul ba'i ma cig mang mkhar ma kun dga' 'bum la/ bla ma dam pa kun dga' blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa ni/ yab dgung lo so brgyad pa
sa mo phag lor 'khrungs te/ rnam thar ni bla ma 'phags pa dang tshul mtshungs shing / gong du byon pas siddhi pha la ing khyung ge gan rgyal po'i ti shri mdzad/ bstan pa'i
mnga' bdag chen por gyur te/ dgung lo rtsa dgu pa me mo yos lo zla ba gnyis par/ me tog ra ba'i sde chen por zhi bar gshegs so/ /yang ma cig nam mkha' rgyal mo la sras
che ba mkhas btsun chen po nam mkha' legs pa'i blo gros dpal bzang po pa ni/ yab dgung lo zhe bzhi pa shing mo sbrul lo la 'khrungs te/ mkhyen rab phun sum tshogs pa mnga'
zhing / khyad par chos skyong che chung la nus pa thon par grags so/ /gong nas ku sha la go lug rgyal pos/ kon ting gu shri mtshan dang shel dam gnang / gdan sa lo bcu
dgu mdzad/ dgung lo so dgu pa chu mo lug lo zla ba dgu pa'i tshes brgyad la bzhi thog gzim khang du zhi bar gshegs so/ /sras bar pa gcig gzhon nu la sku gshegs so/ /chung
ba slob dpon nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ yab sku gshegs pa'i lo shing pho byi ba la sku 'khrungs te/ sku gzhon nu la go thub rgyal po'i bla mchod mdzad/ dgung
lo nyi shu pa la pho brang dang nye bar bde bar gshegs so/ /yang ma cig kun dga' nam mkha'i rgyan la sras che ba slob dpon chen po/ kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ yab mes kyi chos lugs thugs su chud nas gong du byon/ ja yan du rgyal po'i ti shri mdzad/ bstan pa'i mnga' bdag chen por gyur te/ me tog ra ba'i
sder zhi

bar gshegs so/ /sras bar pa bla ma dam pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ yab dgung lo zhe dgu pa lcags pho byi lo la 'khrungs/ nyer gnyis pa la gong du byon/ ye sun
the mur rgyal po'i dus su/ chang gu'i gung mdzad/ ja yan du rgyal po'i sku tshe'i smad dang / rin chen rgyal po tho gan thi mur rgyal po'i sku tshe'i stod la/ rgyal po
rim pa gsum gyi ti shri dang / bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po mdzad de/ dgung lo lnga bcu pa phag lo la me tog ra ba'i sde chen por zhi bar gshegs so/ /gcung chung ba gcig
gzhon nu la sku gshegs so/ /yang ma cig re mda' ma lha cig nyi ma rin chen la/ sras snga ma gcig gzhon nu la sku gshegs so/ /de 'og slob dpon ma kun dga' 'bum/ chung ba
dbang kun dga' legs pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ yab dgung lo zhe bdun pa sa pho spre lo la 'khrungs te/ gong ma tho gan thi mur rgyal pos/ pa'e len dbang gi mtshan
dang / gser dam bod chol kha gsum la shes su bcug pa'i lung bzang po dang / sngar dbang bsod nams bzang po'i jo mo yin pa'i dbon mo' bha gan dang bcas pa gnang / dgung lo
nyer dgu pa me pho byi ba'i lo la srad bu'i sa char sku gshegs so/ /yang ma cig zha lu ma gzhon nu 'bum la sras bzhi'i che ba/ ta dben kun dga' nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po pa/ gzhon nu nas mkhyen rab tshad med pa mnga' bas/ gong du siddhi pha la i khyung ge gan rgyal po'i bla mchod mdzad/ ta dben gu shri mtshan dang / shel dam gnang
/ 'gro don rgya che bar mdzad/ chu pho khyi lo la pho brang ta'i tur/ bde bar gshegs so/ /de'i gcung che ba 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ yab dgung

lo zhe dgu pa'i dus lcags pho khyi lo la sku 'khrungs/ 'di ni 'jam dbyangs dngos yin par kun la grags pas/ rgyas par rnam thar chen mor blta'o/ /dgung lo so lnga pa shing pho
spre'u'i lo zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu gcig la rin chen sgang gong ma'i gzims khang du zhi bar gshegs so/ /gcung bar pa bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po pa/ yab dgung lo nga gcig pa chu pho byi ba'i lo la 'khrungs te/ 'di ni rdo rje 'chang dngos yin par the tshom mi za'o/ /gu shri mtshan thogs shing / tho gan thi mur
rgyal po'i bla ma la gdan 'dren rim par byung na'ang / chos kho na don du gnyer nas ma byon/ dgung lo drug cu re bzhi pa shing mo yos lo zla ba drug pa'i nyer lnga la ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te/ dpal bsam yas lhun gyi grub pa'i bla brang bkra shis sgang gi gzims khang du bde bar gshegs so/ /gcung chung shos gcig gzhon nu la sku
gshegs so/ /de rnams kyi bla ma bdag nyid chen po'i sras lcam sring bco lnga'i rnam thar zur tsam bstan zin to/ /bla ma bdag nyid chen po'i sras 'di la rgyud pa ji ltar
'khrungs/ bla brang gang dang gang gi zhal bdag mdzad pa ni/ gong du dbang bsod nams bzang po'i jo mo bungha gan la/ sras slob dpon chen po ratna shri shing pho byi lo
la 'khrungs te/ dgung lo nyer lnga pa sa pho byi ba lo la sku gshegs so/ /ti shri kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa bsnyen rdzogs ma mdzad pa'i gong du ma cig byang pa mo la/ slob
dpon chen po chos skyong rgyal mtshan bzang po ba chu pho sprel lo la 'khrungs shing / kun spangs pa'i lcam mo la/ slob dpon chen po blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal

bzang po pa yang / chu pho sprel lo de kha la sku 'khrungs te/ tho gan thi mur rgyal pos ta dben gu shri'i mtshan dang / shel dam lung bzang po dang / bcas pa gnang / sku mched
'di gnyis kyis lha khang bla brang du bzhugs so/ /bla ma mkhas btsun chen po'i ma cig dbon mo dge 'dun 'bum la/ sras slob dpon chen po kun dga' rin chen pa/ sa mo yos
lo la 'khrungs te/ tho gan thi mur rgyal po'i tho ling shin tu hu ta dben gu shri'i mtshan dang / shel dam gnang / bzhi thog bla brang gi gdan sa mdzad/ dgung lo drug cu
re gcig pa sa mo yos lor gtsang chu mig ring mor bde bar gshegs so/ /kun dga' legs pa'i jo mo/ gung thang khab pa'i lha gcig kun skyong rgyal mo la/ slob dpon ma bsod nams
'bum 'khrungs shing / ti shri grags pa'i 'od zer gyi lcam mo/ /ma cig dge 'dun 'bum la sras che ba bla ma chen po bsod nams blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ yab
dgung lo nyer lnga pa chu pho spre'u'i lo la 'khrungs te/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gsum bzhes dus/ khong rang gi dpon skya slob dpon rin bzang gis do dam byas rdzong gi rtsa
ba dag blon chen kun dga' bzang po'i tsha bo/ dpon don grub rgyal mtshan bya ba la sa cha nyos nas/ stag tshang rdzong gi 'gram shing pho rta lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes
lnga nas bting / rdzong bla ma chen po sku mched pa la phul ba yin/ dgung lo sum cu pa glang lo la tho gan thi mur rgyal pos gser yig pa dharma kirti dben shri dang / i
bu dben shri sngon rting du mngags/ ti shri mtshan bod nas gsel/ gcung po la dbang gi las ka gnang / gong du gdan drangs/ rgyal po'i bla ma ma mdzad/ dgung lo so gcig pa
chu pho stag lo zla ba bcu pa la me tog ra

bar bde bar gshegs so/ /bar pa gcig gzhon nu la sku gshegs/ gcung chung ba slob dpon chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ me pho byi lo la yab gshegs nas/ zla ba
drug song pa dang 'khrungs/ tho gan thi mur rgyal pos/ pa'e lan dbang gi mtshan dang / khrims ra nyi ma nub phyogs la shes su chugs gsungs pa'i lung bzang po dang bcas pa
gnang / dgung lo zhe gcig pa me pho 'brug lo'i zla ba dang po'i nyer gnyis la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te stag tshang rdzong gi gzims khang rnying par zhi bar
gshegs so/ /'di pa sku mched kyis dus mchod bla brang 'dzin skyong mdzad do/ /'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan pas bsnyen rdzogs ma mdzad gong du/ ma gcig zha lu ma la
sras bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal 'khrungs zhing / 'di pa'ang yab sras khu dbon pas rin chen sgang bla brang 'dzin skyong mdzad de/ phyis chos rje bla ma dam pas
bla brang dus mchod pa la sbyar ro/ /yang bla ma sku mched de rnams kyi sras rgyud ji ltar 'khrungs na/ lha khang pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa bsnyen rdzogs ma mdzad gong
du/ ta dben byang pa'i jo mo'i sras che ba/ chos rje kun dga' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ sa mo glang lo la 'khrungs te/ mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan
phun sum tshogs pa mnga' zhing / dgung lo nga bzhi pa chu pho 'brug lo la rgya nag ye dbang rgyal pos mngags pa'i gser yig ser yig pa/ ta'i ta bzhin dang / a nu dri hor pa
rnams kyis gdan drangs nas/ rnam thos pho brang dang / rgya nag gi ri bo rtse lngar byon/ rgyal po'i ti shri mdzad/ shel gyi dam kha dang / lung bzang po gnang / ci gyo
ta'i ching ha wa pa si than/ shang shen/

ki kang ti/ kong sha kong mi'ing / ba wo/ bod skad du 'phrin las sna tshogs rgyas pa/ dam chos mchog tu rgyas pa/ yang dag pa'i ye shes/ snying rje rgya chen kun la rgyas par
phan pa/ zhing bsrungs shing bstan pa bshad pa/ yang dag par rig pa theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ nub kyi phyogs dge ba/ rdo rje kun khyab 'od zer chen po'i sangs rgyas
zhes pa'i mtshan yang de rnams gsal lo/ /lha khang chen mo lag tu len pa la sogs/ gdan sa'i phyag phyir 'gyur ba'i thugs khur chen po bsnams/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i me
ro bslangs pa lta bur gyur pas na sku drin shin du che zhing / rgya nag tu lo ngo gsum bzhugs/ shing pho rta lo la bod du phebs nas/ bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don rgya chen
po mdzad de/ dgung lo don bdun pa shing mo sbrul lo zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu la lha khang chen mo'i yang rtser bde bar gshegs so/ /de'i gcung po bla ma chen po bsod nams
bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor de nyid kyis kyang bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don rgya chen po yun ring du mdzad de/ sa pho byi ba lo la dpal ldan
lha rtse rdzong gi gzims khang du bde bar gshegs so/ /lcam mo gcig kyang 'khrungs so/ /yang dpon chen dbang phyug dpal gyi jo mo dpal mo skyid dpal la/ drung chos rgyal
ba'i sras/ bla ma rdo rje rin chen pa dang / bla ma dharma dpa'o/ /bzhi thog kun rin pa'i jo mo gnyis thog dbon mo la sras gcig 'khrungs pa/ gzhon nu la sku gshegs/ mnyam
med dbon mo la/ sras che ba blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal la| rgya tA ming rgyal pos ta'i gu shri gnang / gdan sa mdzad/ gcung grags pa blo gros pa gtsang chu mig ring mo
na bzhugs so/ /yang dbang grags pa rgyal

mtshan pa'i jo mo byang pa ma gcig lha mo rin chen la/ sras che ba ta dben kun legs pa/ yab dgung lo nyer gnyis pa me mo bya lo la sku 'khrungs/ tho gan thi mur rgyal pos/
ta dben gu shri'i mtshan dang / lung bzang po gnang / dgung lo nyer brgyad pa shing pho byi ba lo la rta nag ri khud du bde bar gshegs so/ /de'i gcung po dbang rnam sras
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ yab dgung lo nyer lnga pa lcags pho byi ba'i lo zla ba dang po la sku 'khrungs te/ tho gan thi mur rgyal pos/ khong rang gi sras che ba dang
mnyam pa'i las ka ri rtsing dbang gi mtshan/ gser dam dbang hu hu ye byang She zi ma/ rnams g.yas g.yon gyi khrims ra brgyad/ khrims gyi tha'i sa/ pha ming gcig pa'i hu
shri nyi ma nub phyogs la shes su bcug pa'i lung bzang po dang bcas pa gnang nas/ khrims ra gnyis kyi mdzad 'phrin rgyas par mdzad/ dgung lo zhe dgu pa sa pho byi ba lo
hor zla bzhi pa'i nyer bzhi la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te/ smon mkhar rtse gdong gzims khang du bde bar gshegs so/ /yang rtse gdong pa ma gcig sras 'dren la
dbang gi sras mo/ slob dpon chen po chos kyi bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ sa mo phag lo la 'khrungs te/ gzhon nu nas yab mes kyi chos lugs phyi nang gi yon tan
mtha' dag thugs su chud te/ byang sems chen por grags pa de nyid dgung lo bdun cu pa/ sa pho spre'u'i lo hor zla gsum pa'i tshes brgyad la/g.yas ru srin po ri'i gzims khang
rnam rgyal sgang du bde bar gshegs so/ /'di dang yab yum gcig pa'i lcam mo/ /slob dpon ma bkra shis 'bum byung / yang thong ja'i dbon mo la dbang gi sras mo/ slob dpon
ma byang sems bsod

nams rgyal mo ba byung / yang bla chen kun rgyal gyi jo mo snye mo sku zhang pa'i sras mo/ma cig nam mkha' rgyal mo la sras/ slob dpon chen po nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa sku
mched gnyis byung / shab dge sding na bzhugs/ lcam mo gcig kyang yod do/ /de rting lha rtse ba bdag chen bsod nams bkra shis pa'i sras/ nyi shar dpon mo rnam rgyal la 'khrungs
pa/ slob dpon chen po bkra shis rgyal mtshan pa theg chen chos rje'i gdan sa mdzad pa de/ lha khang chen mo na bzhugs so/ /yang bzhi theg slob dpon rgyal mtshan pa'i
sras gcig yang gdan sar bsko rgyu yod do/ /yang ta'i dben kun dga' legs pa hu shri dbon mo la sras slob dpon ma kun dga' 'bum 'khrungs so/ /dbang rnam sras pa la sras
po gnyis dang / sras mo lnga yod pa'i/ ma gcig nyi ma 'bum la slob dpon chen po kun dga' blo gros pa 'khrungs te/ chu pho byi ba lo la bla brang rin chen sgang du bde bar
gshegs so/ /yar 'brog pa ma gcig bsod nams 'bum la/ sras po slob dpon chen po nam mkha' legs pa'i blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa/ yab dgung lo bzhi bcu pa/ sa mo
yos lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bco lnga la 'khrungs te/ dgung lo bcu drug pa shing pho rta lo la theg chen chos rje'i sku drin las/ rgya nag ye dbang rgyal pos/ hu kyang ho
dbang gi mtshan dang / gser dam bod la shes su bcug pa'i lung bzang po dang bcas pa gnang nas khrims mdzad/ 'phrin las rgyas par bzhugs so/ /de'i lcam mo che ba slob dpon
ma nam mkha' 'bum dang / 'dzom pa rgyal mo/ /kun dga' 'bum/ lha mo rin chen/ nam mkha' rgyal mo dang / lnga 'khrungs so/ /mdor na dang po gnam lha mched gsum nas da lta
yan/

gdung rabs rkyang pa nyi shu rtsa lnga song zhing / so sor gyes pa'i rnam grangs kyang dgu bcu go bdun/ lcam mo nyi shu rtsa gcig tsam byon par bzhed do/ /tshe rabs kun tu
dpal ldan bla ma la/ /mi phyed dad pa'i shugs kyis kun blangs nas/ /bla ma rgyud pa'i rnam thar thor bu tsam/ /bris pas dge ba'i bstan pa 'phel ba dang / /rgyud 'dzin sku
che dpal 'byor rab rgyas nas/ /gdul bya rnam mkhyen sa la myur 'khod shog///

sa skya'i bu chen shar nab gung gsum dang / /khang gsar chen mo ba'i byon tshul bzhugs so/ /chos rje khu dbon gyi slob ma/ shar nub gung gsum khang gsar pa dang bzhir grags
pa'i shar pa'i gdung rus ni/ zhang zhung sngags rnying ma ba/ jo 'bum zhes pa'i sras gsum gyi gcen po pa/ bla ma shar pa ye 'byung chos rje pa la rab tu byung / des dpon
chen shAkya bzang po la/ bla brang shar nyos nas bzung / dgung lo drug cu rtsa bzhi thub/ gnyis pa slob dpon rdo rje 'od zer bas shar gyi gdan sa lo bdun mdzad/ dgung lo
re gnyis thub/ gsum pa slob dpon 'od zer 'phen rten dge bsnyen yin/ khong sku mched kyi lcam mo'i sras bla ma ye shes rgyal mtshan/ chos rje pa dang shar pa ye 'byung gi
slob ma yin/ gong ma se chen mangga la'i bla mchod byas/ bla ma rdo rdze 'od zer gshegs rting gdan sa lo bcu dgu mdzad/ dgung lo re drug thub/ shar pa chen po rab tu ma
byung bar kyi sras/ phyug mo rdze btsun skyabs ma la sras gsum byung / 'gro mgon'gon 'phags pa'i slob ma yin/ gcen po dus 'khor pa ye rin/ bla ma 'phags pa shing kun nas
gdan 'dren pa la sa skya pa spyis brdzangs/ phyi'i se chen rgyal po'i ti shri mdzad/ dgung lo zhe bdun pa la rtse lngar gshegs/ bar pa bla ma kun dga' seng ge sa pho spre
lo la gong du byon/ gong ma dang rgyal bu A nan ta'i bla mchod

mdzad/ dbus gtsang du phebs nas gdan sa lo dgu mdzad/ dgung lo re brgyad bzhugs/ gcung 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan sa pho rta la 'khrungs/ me mo phag lo nas se chen
gyi lung gis sa skya bzhi thog gi bla chos lo bco brgyad bshad/ nyi ma re la chos dung lan lnga lnga 'bud pa byung / phyis gong du o ja du rgyal po'i ti shri mdzad/ dgung
lo zhe dgu la gong du sku gshegs/ lung dang rtogs pa'i yon tan phun tshogs mnga'/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i mnga' thang bla ma de dus che ba lags/ bla ma shar pa kun seng dang
/ ma cig mkha' 'gro 'bum gyi sras che ba slob dpon chen po seng ge dpal dgung lo sum cu pa la rgya yul du gshegs so/ /bar pa kun dga' bsod nams pas gdan sa lo so bzhi
bzung / re gnyis pa me pho khyi lo la sku gshegs/ gcung po slob dpon chen po kun dga' rin chen dang / ma gcig nam mkha' rgyan gyi sras che ba/ slob dpon rin chen rgyal mtshan
pas gdan sa mdzad/ rta lo'i lo lnga bcu bzhes/ bar pa slob dpon kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ gcung po slob dpon nyi ma gzhon nu la sku gshegs/ nub pa'i thog ma slob dpon
'u yug pa bsod nams seng ge chos rje pa la thug de la slob dpon zangs tshas nyi thog phog de'i gcung po gcig gi sras bla ma kun smon yang chos rje pa la thug de'i gcung po
kun dga' mdzes sku mched gnyis/ phyis dpon chen kun dga' bzang po'i phyogs su chad nas bla ma 'phags pa'i thugs dang ma mthun par/ se chen gyi lung gis spyugs nas/ gcen
po sman tshe'i yul du 'das/ de'i dbon po yon tan dpal gyi/ dbon po sangs rgyas dpal gyis gdan sa mdzad do/ /

gung pa ni chos rje pa'i slob ma/ skyo ston dri med/ de nas dbon rgyud med par slob mas gdan sa bzung ba la/ bla ma dar yas/ gung pa dpal rgyal/ gung pa sher rgyal/ gung pa
bkra shis bzang po/ gung pa blo bzang / de 'das nas yang dge bshes bkra shis pa'i bskyar nas byas so/ /yang khang gsar chen mo ba'i brgyud pa ni/ dang por sum pa grags kyis
sras/ bla ma grags pa 'od zer ba de/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer dang / ye pa'i btsun pa yin/ phyis bla ma 'phags pa'i dkon gnyer gyi rgan pa thob/ slob dpon dharma pha la'i
phyag phyir gong la phyin/ bla ma dus 'khor ba'i rjes la se chen gyi ti shri mdzad/ dgung lo nga brgyad pa la gong du sku gshegs so/ /de'i gcung po sras bla ma sangs
rgyas dpal gyis khang gsar bla brang bzung / gong du o ja du rgyal po dang / go lug rgyal po/ bu yan du rgyal po gsum gyi ring la ti shri mdzad/ dgung lo zhe brgyad pa la
gong du sku gshegs/ 'dis bla ma bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal yul sman tshe'i yul nas/ hor rgyal po dang mjal ba'i mthun rkyen mdzad pas/ sa skya pa'i gdung rgyud kyi
zhabs tog byed pa che bar byed do/ /de'i sras bla ma grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bas/ gu shri'i las ka mdzad nas/ rting la dbus kyi re tsha yon tan khang du/ khang gsar pa
rang gi nye gnas/ nam mkha'i g.yog gis khrims med byas pas nyes blangs nas sa skyar byon/ phyag rdzas thams cad dbus gtsang mnga' ris kyi dge 'dun la gser zho'i 'gyed byas/
bla ma bdag nyid chen po la gser gar bu'i lha chen dang / khyad nor mang po phul/ khong rang khang gsar chen mo nas mar gseb kyi spu bton pa bzhin du/ kun spangs mdzad
pa'i ngang la/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa drug pa la rta nag gi brag ske rags can du grongs so/ /phung po lhag med la

'gro rgyu yin na na 'ang / nye gnas kyi dgung zhag bdun nas spur la reg pas lhag ma dum bu gcig lus zer ro/ khang gsar pa'i pha spun ring po'i rgyud/ slob dpon chen po nyi
ma rgyal mtshan pa gong du gu shri mdzad nas grongs/ de'i sras slob dpon chen po bde legs rgyal mtshan pa'o/ sngon tshe sa skya bla mas bod khams bskyangs pa'i dus/ /bzang
ldan slob mas chos bzhin byas pa'i mthus/ /mthun rkyen bla ma'i gdan sa rgyal sa'i ti shri thob/ /thob pa de 'dra phyin chad 'byung ba e srid ang / /bu gcig ma bzhin 'gro
la brtse ba'i sa paN gyis/ /bu chen slob ma'i byon tshul 'di bris pas/ /bu ram shing pa'i rgyud kyi bstan pa 'phel byed pas/ /bu slob 'phags pa'i dge 'dun phyogs bcur
dar bar shog/ //

dbus gtsang dpon chen dang / sa skya nang chen rim pa'i byon tshul bzhugs/ oM swa sti/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung rgyud dri ma med pa 'di dang / hor rgyal po yon mchod du
'brel nas gtsug lag gnyis ka'i sgo nas/ bod khams bskyang ba'i phyir/ zhar la byung ba dbus gtsang dpon chen gyi rim pa ni/ thog mar dpon chen la snga ba shAkya bzang po
de la/ chos rje sa paN dgung lo re gsum pa sa pho 'brug la/ hor rgyal po e chen go dan gyi gdan 'dren byung nas/ byang phyogs sprul pa sder phebs dus/ bla ma 'u yug pa dang
/ shar pa sher 'byung ma gtogs/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad kyang phyag 'tshal du bcug sa skya dang gzhi ba'i rgan pa la bskos nas bzhag bla ma 'phags pa'i dus su/
se chen gyi lung gi zon glu gun min dben hu'i ming dang shel dam gnang nas/ dbus gtsang gi dpon chen bskos/ khang gsar chen mo btab/ me pho 'brug lo la/ bla ma 'phags pa
gong nas phebs pa'i bsu ba la dpon chen pas kyang byon dpon slob noms gye re lha khang du bzhugs pa'i nub mo/ bla ma'i zhal nas mi khong la nye gnas go chod byung bas/ lha
khang 'di lta bu bzhengs thub 'dug te gsungs pa dpon chen pa sku rgyab na yod pas gsan nas/ bla ma dam pa mnyes na 'di tsam rgya mthongs su tshud pa'i lha khang zhig bzhengs
pa lags zhus pas/ nan ltar

legs gsungs/ de 'phral la thig tshad byas par yar khyer nas/ 'dam sog yan dbus gtsang gi khri stong / mi sde rnams la bka' shog bkram/ mi lag bskul nas/ de kha'i lo la lha
khang chen mo'i 'gram bting / lcags ri nang ma lcog spe 'bur lcog chung dang bcas pa brtsigs pa'i dus su/ shing cha rnams drangs nas lha khang chen mo'i 'og thog ci rigs
phub tshar ba'i mtshams dpon chen ngang la sa skyar sku gshegs so/ /'di sa skya pa la yus po che'i mi gsum gyi rgan pa blon po drin chen du 'dug pa/ khong gi dbon po bsod
dbang 'das rting dus mchod kyang mi gnang pas/ dpon chen dbang brtson gyis lha sa gro khud phul byung / ba mo gzhung rnams la gzhis chung re yod pa rtsad na sa/ dus mchod
la btsugs yod pas/ dpon chen dang nang so su 'dzin gyis 'di bzhin gyi do dam byed dgos/ dpon chen shAkya bzang po'i rjes la/ nang gnyer kun dga' bzang pos dpon chen tshang
ma lo drug byas/ de'i bar la lha khang gi lcags ri lcags chung 'og thog thigs khang zhabs su phyug par byas/ gser 'phru chen mo btsugs/ chos rje sa paN gyi nang bstan
byang chub chen po'i gser sku dang / lha khang gi khyams la ri mo thams cad bzhengs/ rin chen sgang bla brang dang / dbu rtse byang lha khang bla brang dang bcas pa 'debs
pa'i do dam byas/ kun dga' bzang pos las kha btad nas/ bya rog tshang du lo drug bcu'i bar la/ dpon chen zhang btsun dang / phyug po sgang dkar ba byang rin gsum po/ bla
mas zhal ltas rim gyis bskos/ kun dga' bzang po la bla ma ma mnyes nas/ se chen gyi lung gi saM gha ching sang gis mgo byas rtsa ba'i hor dmag 'bum phrag gcig btang / dmag

lam stag tshang phu la zhugs/ khang dmar gyis sa mkhar la mtshon kha bslangs te steng bya rog tshang la skor rgyag byas/ lcags pho 'brug lo la dpon chen khrims la bsgral/ de
nas yun ring ma song bar bla ma 'phags pa yang zhi bar gshegs pas gong du zhu ba la nye gnas gzhon nu dbang phyug btang / se chen gyi lung gis byang rin la dpon chen bskos/
son wi sa'i dngul dam gling drug ma dang / shel gyi dam la yang gnang / rting la byang rin shang sdong po thang gis sgar thog tu kun dga' bzang po'i g.yog byang pa ye
shes bzang pos bsad zer/ de nas dpon chen kun gzhon/ dpon chen gzhon dbang / de'i ring la phye bsal chen po dang / khrims gyi zhib cha phal cher byung ba/ de nas don chen
byang rdor/ de nas dpon chen ag len/ de'i ring la lha chen mo'i spen bad bkal/ rgya mthongs ka brgyad btsugs/ thigs khang logs la bla ma bdag nyid chen po'i bka' bka'
bzhin/ phyi nang gi dkyil 'khor mi gcig pa drug brgya sum cu rtsa dgu bzhengs/ shing mo lug lo la phyis lcags ri chen mo dang / dbon po ra'i lcags ri gtod pa/ bla ma 'phags
pa dang / dharma pha la'i phyi bstan bzhugs sa'i gser thog g.yu thog 'gel ba/ jo mo gling 'debs pa/ 'bri gung la dmag 'khyer ba sogs/ gdan sa chen po'i :chags/[phyag ]/
phyi dang / zhabs tog byas pa shin tu che bar byed/ dgas por dmag 'khyer jus legs len pa'i dus/ sa mtshams na brag la ag len gyi ming bris pa bzhag 'dug zer/ bzhon dbang
dang / byang rdor/ ag len gsum gyi ring la/ sa 'bri 'thab/ ag len gyi dpon chen ngang la rgya yul du byon/ a yu par pa rdar/ bu yan du rgyal bu dang mjal/ mi rabs kyi

bar la yar 'brog khri skor 'jags pa'i lung bzang po thob/ de nas yang dpon chen gzhan dbang la bskyar nas bskos/ che gsal la sogs pa 'di'i skabs su byung bar yang byed/ de
nas dpon chen legs pa dpal/ dpon chen seng ge dpal/ dpon chen 'od zer seng ge 'di'i swan jing dben gyi dam kha yang bzung / de nas dpon chen kun rin/ dpon chen don yod dpal/
dpon chen yon btsun/ yang dpon chen 'od zer seng ges bskyar nas byas/ de nas dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po/ dpon chen dbang phyug dpal/ dpon chen bsod nams dpal/ dpon chen
nam mkha' bstan pa'i tshab la/ yang dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po khyon gyis bskos bskyar nas byas/ de nas dpon chen dbang brtson/ de nas dpon chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/
de nas dpon chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ dpon chen dpal 'bum/ dpon chen grags dbang / rting ma ming gi dpon chen la/ a mo gha pa rnams byung ngo / /sa skya nang chen gyi
rim pa ni/ thog mar nang chen kun dga' bzang po/ de'i tsha bo dpon gzhon nu dpal/ dpon kun gzhon/ dpon don grub dpal/ dpon blo/ zha lu dpon shes/ ston pa rin chen dpal/
dpon grub bzang / nye gnas dkon mchog bzang po/ nye gnas 'jam rgyal/ yang ston pa rin chen dpal/ lung gis bskos/ ston pa ring mo/ jo btsun kun shes/ nye gnas kun dga' 'phel/
dpon yon btsun grags pa dar/ lung gi bskos/ si tu'i dam kha byung / yang gsar bskos byas/ rin bsam du dban shA lung gis bskos/ nye gnas nam mkha' rgyal mtshan lung gis
bskos/ dpon kun rin nye gnas 'bum skyabs/ nam mkha' dpal du dben

sha nye gnas bzang po dpal/ dpon po chos rgyal/ dpon seng ge rgyal mtshan/ shes rab 'od zer du dben shA/ dpon po dkon mchog rin chen/ nang pa 'phags pa dpal bzang po/ nang
pa kun dga' 'bum/ nang chen kun dga' 'phags/ nang chen rab mthor 'phags rnams so/ /dpon chen nang chen rim pa'i byung tshul 'di/ /mi chen blo chen bya las 'dzin pa rnams/
/brtse chen khur chen 'khur cing chab srid kyi/ /sa chen bde chen thob pa'i rgyur gyur cig///

/khri skor mchog gyur zha lu ba'i byung tshul dang / myang yul chags lugs bzhugs so/ /oM swa ti/ 'gro ba'i bla ma dpal ldan sa skya pa/ /'jam dbyangs rnam 'phrul rim pa'i sku
drin las/ /dbus gtsang 'di yang khri stong dbang bsgyur ba'i/ /sde dpon stobs ldan che gnyan mang byung ba/ /de'i nang nas rigs bzang sku nye shing / khri skor bcu gsum
dag gi mchog gyur pa/ /zha lu sku zhang byon tshul 'di ltar grags/ de'ang 'di ltar thos te/ sngon rgyal po khri lde 'od srung dang / btsun mo lcog ro bza' dkar rgyal mo
legs la/ sras mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan/ de'i btsun mo tshe spong bza' dkar rgyal la/ sras skyid sde nyi ma mgon dang / bal bza' phan rgyal la/ khri bkra shis brtsegs
pa dpal btsan chung btsan 'dis/ sngon ma stod phyogs su byon/ gu ge spu hreng ya tshe rnams kyi/ mnga' bdag mdzad pa la sras dpal gyi mgon dang / bkra shis nyi ma mgon/ lde
gtsug mgon rnams byung ba la/ stod kyi mgon gsum zer ro/ /de'i rgyud stod kyi rgyal rgyud rnams yin no/ /gcung po khri bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal/ /rting la stod phyogs
su spyugs/ mnga' ris gung thang man la chags/ sras dpal lde dang 'od lde/ skyid lde rnams byung ba la/ smad kyi lde gsum zer/ gcung skyid lde de/ 'jad rta nag ngos su phog
pa la/ sras drug byung ba'i lnga pa'i rgyud 'gro

rtsod dang / mus mdzad la sogs byang phyogs la yod/ sras gcig gtsang grom pa dang / shab sran/ myang stod smad du byon pas/ myang yul du sras gsum pa'i che ba / khyung btsad/
bar pa bre btsad/ chung ba la lce btsad zer/ khong mched gsum gyi myang stod smad la yul bgos/ sa ris byas pa ni/ phu ha'o gangs bzang nas/ mda' bcug pa gcung pa yu ba
gdong yan la/ bod 'brog cha snyoms pa'i yul sde chen po gsum du phye te/ phu byang shar ri nang spang mkhar la gtad/ mda' lho nub gangs ye sham bu la gtad pa/ bseg 'gros
su yod pa la/ yul sde chen po gcig tu byas te/ gcen khyung btsad kyi sa mtsham gtsang khang brag kha yan yin/ 'di'i sa khong na phu na/ 'brog sde chen po gsum yod pa ni/
gam ru rgyang ru nying ru gsum/ bar na tshong 'dus chen po gcig yod pa ni/ sal ma tshong 'dus bya ba yod de/ phyis bkag nas gnas snying du 'phos pa'o/ /sa khong de rnams
na mi rigs mi 'dra ba gnyis yod pa ni/ drag?brag shos rnams shes rab che dge ba la brtson pa kho na yod do/ /phal shos rnams sdig shas che/ nya dang ri dwags rngon pa'o/
/zong sna mi 'dra ba gsum yod pa ni/ zha mo snam phrug phad phyar yang yod/ de skor phu'i 'brog sde ches/ mda' zhing sa khyon chung bas cha ma snyoms pas/ sha se khog tu
nyo tshong byed par byung ngo / /bar pa lde btsad kyi dbang rigs/ gtsang gad brag kha man/ sna bo brag rdog yan la/ yul sde chen po gcig tu byed pa'i/ de'ang phu swa ma
sA'u/ byang shar dang / mda' gab bya dkar/ lho nub la bstan pa/ bseg 'gros su yod pa/ phu'i 'brog sde gsum ni/ rgyang mkhar/ skyid mkhar/ mag ngag rnams so/ /bar gyi tshong
'dus gcig ni/ 'od gsum ti du dgu'i tshong

'dus bya'o/ /mi rigs mi 'dra ba gnyis ni/ brag shos rnams shin tu phyugazhan pa rnams dbul zhing 'phongs/ zong sna mi 'dra ba gsum ni/ rnga ma phyings pa/ sle khra yod do/
/phu'i 'brog sde dang / mda'i zhing pa rnams cha snyoms pas/ sha phyed tshong byed pa byung ngo / /chung ba lce btsad gyi dbang rigs/ sna bo brag rdog man bcug pa yu ba gdong
yan la/ yul sde chen po gcig tu byed/ de'ang phu byang shar 'khor stod la kha dang / mda' lho nub chu sgo gzhung la bstan pa/ bseg 'gros su yod pa/ de'i phu na 'brog
sde gsum ni/ sgrol lcags ra gsum mo/ /bar gyi tshong 'dus ni/ gtsang tshong 'dus mgur mo'o/ /mi rigs mi 'dra ba gnyis ni/ brag shos rnams mdzangs shas che/ zhan shos rnams
khram shas che'o/ /zong sna mi 'dra ba gsum ni/ gtsang ther/ dor skyegs/ star zon rnams yod do/ /phu'i 'brog sde chung/ mda'i zhing sa khyon ches cha ma snyoms pas/ sha
gzugs tshong byed pa 'byung ngo / /de ltar yul bgos byas pas/ gzhan gang dang gang cha snyoms par byung na'ang / gam ru'i g.yam pa legs po de la gang yang yong / mi 'dzad
pa'i gter dang 'dra bas/ phyug pa dang g.yam pas rgyal lo/ /zer byung zhing / da lta khyung g.yam du grags so/ /dus phyi rting btsad po mched gsum la/ dar gud byung te/
yul sde gsum ga gcung po lce btsad kyis bzung / de gong myang stod gzhung phal che ba zhing la thag ma dang / chu mig la brten pa las med pa la/ lce btsad/ shes rab dang
'byor stobs che bas sa rgya 'di la bde chod pa'i thabs dgos pa 'dug zer nas/ myang stod kyi byang rgyud du/ rtsa rnams kyi rgyal rkas dang / lho rgyud du spang yul bzhengs
kyi 'od rka bya ba dang / myang smad byang du

pa tshab rka mo che dang / lho rgyud pa snam rka mo che rnams bzos/ rka bo che re re'i 'og na son khal khri khrag re re yod par byed cing / rka chen rnams ma 'jags bar la bsrung
mi sdod pa'i mkhar gnyis bzhengs pa ni/ stod du rgyal grogs rtse mkhar dang / smad du pa snam rtse mkhar gnyis/ lce btsad kyi bzhengs pas na lce mkhar du chags pa yin
la/ de lta bu'i rka chen bzhi dang mkhar gnyis ni/ da lta'i bar du yod cing / sa 'dul la bed spyod shin tu che bar byung bas/ lce btsad kyi byas pa lag rjes shin tu che
bar gda' cing / zha lu ba'i dpon rgyud 'dis rtsa ba lce btsad kyi rgyud pa yin pas/ de nas gdung rabs mang rabs 'ong pas/ bod du bstan pa phyi dar gyis thog ma/ dbus gtsang
gi mi bcu pos mdo smad nas chos zhus pas/ lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug gi myang smad rgyan gong gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ de'i dngos slob/ mgo dmag g.yu 'khrungs gi
bu chen/ lce btsun sher 'byung gi zha lu wa mo'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ chos sde btab rgya gar du byon/ sdom pa bskyar nas blangs/ zab chos mang du zhus so/ /der rting
zha lu ba mnga' thang 'byor stobs je che la song tshul ni/ khri skor gzhan rnams las lhag pa'i/ che khyad rnam pa lnga bya ba yod de/ de yang / gdung rus btsad po yin pas
che/ las ka bka' bzhi'i byas pas che/ dam chos rgya gar ma yin pas che/ de rnams ni gong du smos pa ltar gdung rgyud sku zhang yin pas che/ sbyin bdag rgyal po yin pas
che/ bya ba ni thog mar sku zhang ye shes kun dga'i lcam mo/ /ma cig mkha' 'gro 'gro 'bum/ 'go mgon phyag na'i khab tu byon pa nas bzung ste/ chos rje bla ma sku mched/ bla
chen kun rgyal ba yab sras la sogs/

ding sang yan/ gdung rgyud khu dbon pas sku zhang na rim gyi bar la/ sku nye 'brel ba nas/ sde bdag gzhan rnams las ches lhag par/ sa skya pa dang 'brel che'o/ /'gro 'gon phyag
na yab yum pa'i sras/ bla ma dharma pha la rakShi ta gong du byon/ hor o ja du rgyal po dang mjal dus/ bod dbus gtsang na nged kyi zhang po zha lu khri dpon bya ba yod
pa la/ lung las kha bzang po gnang dgos zhus pas/ bla ma'i zhang po yin na nged kyi yang zhang po yin du chug la/ khri skor dpon po stong dpon byings pos phud du khur
ba gyis shig mi rabs kyi bar la khri skor 'jags su chug gsungs pa'i lung gtsang ma gnang ba dang / gong ma yon mchod kyi sku rim la dmigs nas/ gser dngul las grub pa'i rten
gsum gtsug lag khang dang bcas pa bzhengs pa gyis gsungs nas/ gser bre chen brgya dang / dngul bre chen lnga brgyas mgo byas pa'i gnang sbyin bzang po bskur/ de'i cha
rkyen gyis zha lu gser khang du grags pa'i lha khang dbu rtse che chung ngo mtshar can mang du thugs rje chen pos bzhengs/ tshong 'dus 'phrul pe bzhengs/ de'i rting sku zhang
kun dga' don grub pa dang / sku zhang grags pa rin chen pa'i ring la/ rang byon 'phags pa spyan drangs/ zha lu gnas nang dang / ri phug yang dgon btab/ chos dpon la/
chos rje bu ston kha che gdan drangs/ de pa yab sras la sogs mkhas grub mang po'i zhabs tog bdag rkyen mdzad pas/ da lta'i bar du/ thub bstan nyin mo ltar gsal ba 'di lags
so/ /sku zhang byon tshul myang yul chags tshul 'di bris pas sku chen gyis mchog bstan 'dzin yon mchod rnams sku tshe ring zhing / 'gro kun rgyal ba'i sku gsum myur du
thob pa'i rgyur gyur cig dge legs 'phel gyur cig/ //

lha dbang sprul pa dpal ldan shar dga'i byung tshul yod/ 'gro kun dga' mdzad dpal ldan sa skya pas/ /mkhyen brtse'i thugs rje'i nam mkha' yangs pa las/ /shar ri'i rtse nas
'od stong 'bar ba bzhin/ /shar phyogs ldan ma las skyes shar dga' ba/ /rigs bzang khungs btsun lha dbang rnams 'phrul ltar/ /'ga' zhig pas rgol dpung 'joms dmag dpon rin
chen dang / /ding sang bstan pa'i srog shing chos rgyal chen po'ang byon/ /des na bde bas thub bstan gsal byed dang / /mdzad pa'i rnam thar rgyal mtshan grangs mang yang
/ /ngo mchar 'phrin las rags pa zur tsam bris/ /de yang dpal ldan shar dga' par grags 'di pa'i byon tshul ni/ rigs mtho ba/ sga ldan tre ho gsum gyi yul khams la dbang bsgyur
ba'i/ jo bo'i rigs su gyur cing rus bzang ba/ bod mi'u drug gi nang nas/ dmu tsha lha'i gdung rgyud kyi nang tshan ldan ma'i bu rgyud ste/ dang po khri srong lde btsan
gyis dus su/ ldan ma rtse mang zer ba'i/ sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po dang / ldan ma byang khri/ byang dmar la sogs/ ma sangs kyis sprul pa'ang mang du byon par 'dug
cho 'brang btsun pa ni/ ldan stod sga'i yul du/ sga a snyan dam pa zer ba'i/ 'byor ldan dkar phyogs la mos pa byung 'dug pas/ de sga ldan tre bo'i sa phyogs su/ lha khang
rgya phibs khyung mgo can brgya rtsa brgyad/ lha khang de'i nang du rten ngo mtshar can dang /

bka' 'gyur ro cog cha tshang ma re re bzhengs pa'i drung du dkar me 'khor yugamachod pa rnams lnga'i rgyun ma bcad pa'i dge rgyun btsugs pa lags so/ /bstan pa dar rgyas 'phel
ba'i bya ba chen mo mdzad 'dug de'i dbon sras kyis rgyud pa/ ldan ma dbon po bzang po rgyan mtshan man/ yab sras 'khor bcas kyis dbus gtsang dag pa zhing khams/ khyad
par dpal ldan sa skya bla ma'i/ spyan sngar byon par bzhed nas/ yar btegs byon pas/ mi shi ba lha ru song ba'i ldan ma dbang rgyal zhes par grags pa/ lha btsan bzang po gcig
yod pa des/ rmi lam du lung rim par bstan pa bzhin/ gtsang g.yas ru'i ru lag bcung pa yu ba gdong / bzhi dga' gser sdings rnams su rim pas phyugs/ gser sngings su gzhi
phab/ sras po de gzhon nu nas klog yig sogs yon tan dang ldan pas/ grong pa rnams kyang / dpon yig bzang po dpal 'dis/ rang re thams cad la phan thogs par byung zer cing
/ gnas po phyug po chen po zhig yod pa'ang / bu chung la zhe mgu nas/ nga'i bu mo dang bza' mi gyis shig zer nan gyis bskul bas/ bu mo lha mo sman dang / yab yum du 'brel/
lo 'ga' song ba dang / pha rgan sku gshegs/ der rting bu mo la rmi ltas bzang po byung nas/ bya lo la sras po zhig 'khrungs pa/ mtshan dpal ldan dar zhes par btags so/
/yang lha'i lung bstan la/ 'di nas shar lho phyogs kyis la rgyab ba'i pha rol der song zhig der nga'i 'dug gnas kyang 'chos la/ rten tshugs bya ba thams cad kyang yar 'phel
du 'byung ngo zer ba byung nas/ yab yum sras kyis yar byon/ thar pa dgon sar/ lcam [dpyal ] ston chos 'phags kyi drung du/ sras pho la

dge bsnyen zhus/ bla ma'i mtshan las dras nas/ 'phags pa dpal bzang po zer ba'i mtshan btags/ 'phags pa'i ming can mi rabs bdun gyi bar la/ bstan jus mnga' thang yar 'phel
du 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes pa'i bka' gnang / de nas lar rgan la byon ste/ bod mkhar sngon mo lung du bzhugs pa'i nub mo/ lha byon nas 'dir mkhar gzhis phob/ nga'i lha rten
tshugs zer ba byung nas bzhugs pas/ lha yul sngon mo lung du grags pa byung ngo / /de'i skabs su/ yul pa rnams/ sa skyar 'dab skor 'bul du 'gro dus yig ris dgos pas grogs
ldan la/ dpon yig bzang po dpal ba'i kyang / thengs 'ga' byon pas/ sa skya nas nang chen gyis yig mkhan la bskongs/ de nas yun ring ma 'gyangs par/ bla ma bdag nyid chen
po bzang po dpal ba'i drung du/ yig tshang pa'i mthil bzhugs thob/ thugs rjes bzung nas mnga' thang yar 'phel du byung zhing / ma cig lha mo sman la/ /sras po 'phags
pa'i rin chen dang / ma sangs dar po dang / sngon mo lung du 'khrungs so/ /sras che ba la klog yig mkhas par bslabs/ gzhon nu nyid nas sa skya/ bla ma'i drung du skyabs/
ma sangs kyi sprul par song nas gzhan las 'khrungs bskyed che zhing / bya ba'i rnam dbye shin tu mkhas pa zhig byung bas/ khams pa dge 'dun rgyal mtshan rnams/ dung reng
gi kha non dang sngags pa'i zla la/ yi ge shes pa zhig kyang dgos pa byung bas/ khong pa btang / khams pa mi bdun pos thog drangs rgan pa gong gsum bar dgar byas pa'i/ shar
dga' bar grags pa de nas byung / khams pa rang bzhugs rin la'ang / dung reng gi kha non rab tu byung zhing / khong pa bon nag 'od chen du sku

gshegs/ zhal chems bzhag pa bzhin/ dpon yig 'phags pa dpal ba/ dpon tshab tu khur/ mdun ma rtse gcig tu bsgril pa'i chad 'gag bsdams/ dpal ldan shar dga' ba'i bstan pa'i mgo
sngon ma de nyid nas tshugs par byed do/ /gsum de mtshams dbus gtsang khri skor dmag gis dung reng la 'gag sgugamathar 'ded byed par bshams pa/ shar dung rnams ring ldan
zur la 'chur/ khos pha rol nas gur sha'i ri phug la 'chur dus/ gong gsum gyis sgar pas mthar 'ded rtsis la/ dung reng depon don grub dar gyi lam bskrad nas/ dpon 'phags
pa dpal khyod bsam pa che na/ nged rnams la chas kha sbyin nas thongs/ zla ba rting ma la/ ngo lta sleb pa byed zer bas/ de'i phugs khebs che bar 'dug bsam nas/ gtsang mar
btang bas sa skya nas nyes pa la thug pa khad tsam byung nas/ bzang chad byas lugs zhus pas/ zla dus la don grub dar gyis shar dung gis mi sna drag btus thams cad khrid/
mi khyod kyis bzang po byas phyin/ nga yang bzang po byed pa yin zer nas/ mi nor thams cad ngo bltas/ drag pa rnams las 'dzin la bcug gzhis chags nas/ dung reng gis mi
rgyud/ myang stod na da lta'ang yod do/ /der rting phag ri rin chen sgang dang / lho spa gro ban 'phreng ba'i/ blon po grags pa 'od zer 'jam grengs skug gzhan slu rgod thams
cad kha drangs nas lho dung thams cad btul/ nag che ba rnams kyi mgo lag rin chen sgang gi mgon khang / them 'og na yod/ der rting bla ma'i bka' bzhin/ phag ri rnam
rgyal gyi rdzong brtsigs/ lho dung gis sa chad thams cad 'og tu bcugalas sgo che chung rnams btsugs/ rdzong dpon sngon ma la gcung po 'phags rin pa

bskos/ de ltar shar dung / lho dung / rim par thul bas dpon jus dang / rang don grub pa shin tu che bar byung / de ltar sa skya nang chen gyis go sar yang lo 'ga' bzhugs shing
/ mi rtsag pa sag shi dar ra kha che/ ti shri kun rgyal bas phyag phyir gong du brdzangs/ hor rgyal po tho gan thi mur la zhus nas si tu'i mtshan dang / tham rtags 'ja'
sa blangs/ sham po rtse dgu'i ldan la/ lha khang dang bde yangs chen mo bzhengs/ chos sde btab rdzong rtse chen zer bar ming btags/ rgyal mkhar gyis ri bsrung ba'i/ rtse
khang dang / lcang ra/ brgya grong gis sa mkhar brtsigs/ der rting phag mo gru pa si tu byang rgyal ba dang / thugs nye 'brel zab po yod pas/ sne gdong du byon zer ba
byung ba la/ thugs bkal nas byon pas/ si tu pa grongs pa dang thug bros pa rnams kyis/ bra phyi tshong 'dus su bzang btson la skong dus su phyag phyi ba/ dge slong shAka
bzang dang / a po bkra hor/ yar klungs dge bsnyen la sogs/ dpon zhen can rnams kyi sems khur byas pas/ gtsang mar thon/ yar byon/ gnas rnying du bzhugs/ rtse chen lcang ra/
rgya grong nang na phag rin pa sku mched bzhugs pa la/ sne gdong nas nag po tshul bzang dang / pag shi dkon mchog skyabs/ mda' phog nas 'das pas/ dmag dpung bros thabs
la phyir log dgos byung nas/ shar dga' ba'i bstan jus kyi gzhi gcig de nas tshugs par byed do/ /ta'i si tu 'phags pa dpal bzang po'i sras che ba/ nang chen kun dga' 'phags
pas yong / rgyal mkhar rtse rdzong dang / 'dug chung gi sa mkhar bzhengs/ stag rtse rdzong phag mo gru pa'i lag nas blangs/ sa skya nang chen gyis khog par zhugs nas/
sde srid chen

po'i bstan jus yar 'phel gyis mdzad 'phrin rgya che bar mdzad/ gcung po ta'i si tu bsod nams dpal bas/ rdzong rtse chen bzung / phyi nang du/ dgra zun gyi blang dor/ sde gzar
ci rigs pa dgos pa byung na'ang / ma sangs kyi sprul pa/ thabs la mkhas pa'i skyes bu dpa' mdzangs 'joms 'dug pas/ mthar thug dgra gnyen blang dor ma nor pa'i 'dul sbyongs/
sa skya pa'i zhabs tog spyi jus su che ba dang / ma las bu dga' ba'i rdzong bzhi/ shab seng ge rtse/ sde chen rtse/ 'jad/ bo dong la sogs pa'i mnga' zhabs gsar 'phel
rim par chod cing / rgya'i ta'i ming rgyal pos/ tu si'i mtshan/ dngul dam lung bzang po dang bcas pa gnang nas/ dpal ldan sa skya pas thog drangs/ gtsang srid spyi dgos
kyis bstan pa'i srog shing lta bur bzhugs pa 'di lags so/ /de'i sras che ba dpon po rgya mtsho pa/ sku na gzhon rab la sku gshegs/ gcung po dbon po rin chen 'phags pa la/
ta'i ming rgyal pos/ su si'i las ka gnang zhing / sde srid 'dzin skyong gis phra rags thams cad yab las mi zhan pa byung ba'i/ snyan grags yar 'phel du bzhugs so/ /'phags
pa rin po che'i sras che ba/ rtse chen chos rje pa mdo rgyud kyis dgongs pa rnams thugs su chud ste/rnal 'byor gyis dbang phyug chen po de nyid kyis 'gro ba'i 'dren pa
la sku brtan par bzhugs so/ /de'i gcung po rgyal chen pa/ yang dpon po shAkya dpal ba dang / chen po dbang rgyal bas/ sa skya nang chen bzung / nang ltar gyis mthun sbyor
mdzad pa dang / mi mthun phyogs rnams kyis spyi thogs su/ ri bo ltar brjid pa zhig byon par gda'o/ /yang ma sangs dar po'i sras/ a chen bzang po

dpal ba yin cing / de'i sras dpon rin chen rgyan mtshan dpal ba dang / nor bu 'phags pa yin no/ /nang chen kun dga' 'phags pa'i sras/ mched gsum gyi che ba/ rab brtan kun bzang
'phags pa myang stod rgya grong du/ ma gcig bzang mo dpal ba la/ sa mo sbrul lo 'byung ba lnga ldan gyi thog tu sku 'khrungs 'di nyid ni nges par byang chub sems dpa'i
sprul pa ste/ rnam par dkar ba'i mdzad 'phrin rgya che lugs ni brjod par mi nus kyis/ ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar rags pa tsam zhig khrims gnyis kyi sgo nas bstan par bya
ba ni/ dang por sku gzhon nu'i dus su zhi dul dang ldan pa sogs/ chos mthun gyis yon tan du mas mdzes shing / dgung lo bcu gsum bcu bzhi nas/ sems dpa' pa chen po chos
kyi rin chen gyi zhabs rdul spyi bor blangs/ rjes su bzung / nyi shu ba la yab mes khu dbon pas thugs dgongs rdzogs phyir sgrub mchod chen mo'i gzhi btsugs/ nyi shu rtsa
bzhi pa la yab dang yum gyis sku drin bsab pa'i phyir/ sgrub mchod yun ring dang gzhi rten bzang po btsugs/ nyi shu rtsa lnga pa la mkhyen rab kyis mnga' bdag dge legs dpal
bas thog drangs/ lung rigs smra ba brgya phrag bzhi lhag 'du ba'i lcang ra chos kyis gzhi bting / nyi shu rtsa drug pa la/ myang chu la zam chen bkag che dang bcas pa
bzhengs/ sum cu pa la gos sku chen mo ston pa'i sku khru brgyad cu pa dang / der rting gser 'phan chen mo'i dbus na/ byams pa'i sku khru bzhi bcu pa dang / gzhan yang gos
dar la khru bdun cu re yod pa'i 'phan brgyad rnams bzhengs/ rdo rje gdan gyis mkhan po/ ma hA so ma sogs rgya gar gyi paNDi ta du ma spyan drangs/ bdag rkyen bzang po mdzad/
der rting yang bstan

pa'i bdag po de nyid kyis thugs la/ sems can gyis bde skyid sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa la rag las/ bstan pa'i gsal byed/ lung rtogs thos bsam la rag las 'dug pas/ bstan pa dar
zhing yun ring du gnas par bya ba'i phyir dang / dge 'dun 'du ba'i gtsug lag khang dang bcas pa zhig kyang bzhengs dgos dgongs pa byung nas/ thub pa mya ngan las 'das
nas lo sum stong lnga brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum song ba'i/ sa pho khyi lo la mnga' bdag dpal khri btsan gyi pho brang rgya gar rtse'i nye 'khor la sogs su/ chos grwa chen
mo dpal 'khor bde chen/gtsug lag khang dang bcas pa'i 'gram bting / lung rigs smra ba brgya phrag bcu dang / rim gnyis zab mo la brtson pa brgya phrag lnga tsam/ rtse gcig
sgrub pa la brtson pa brgya phrag la sogs/ dge 'dun 'du ba'i sde btsugs dge ba bcu'i khrims bcas/ gtsang khang ka chen bgyod/ rnam par sgo gsum/ khyams ka ba bzhi cu zhe
brgyad kyis/ yongs su ka ba lnga bcu khyon/ gse 'phru khru nyi shu lnga pa/ rten gyi gtso bor rdo rje gdan gyi mahA bo dhi'i sku tshad dang mnyam pa'i byang chub chen po'i
sku'i thog drangs/ steng 'og gi lha khang thams cad nas gser sku/ lder sku gzhal yas khang blos bslangs la sogs bris legs pa ngo mtshar can gyis yongs su gang bar bzhugs
cing / rten gtso'i spyan snga na/ gser kong / dngul kong / maNDal chen mos thog drangs/ lha khang spyir dgos kun na/ mar me 'khor yug dang / mchod pa'i rgyun phun sum
tshogs pa btsugs/ dgung lo so bdun pa la lcags ri chen mo/ lcog nyi shu sgo chen brgyad/ phyi ljon shing gis ra bas bskor ba dang bcas pa bzhengs/ so dgu pa la sku 'bum
chen po bkra shis sgo mang kyi

'gram bting nas/ yun ma 'gyangs par zhabs su chug de rting byams chen gyis gos sku khru brgyad cu pa zhig bzhengs/ rin po che'i bka' 'gyur/ bstan 'gyur bzhengs shing bskor
ba dang / gzung sngags mang po'i bzlas brjod rgyun pa btsugs/ phu ru sgrub pa po brgya rtsa brgyad bzhugs pa'i/ ri khrod dga' ldan gyis 'gram bting / 'di ltar bshad grwa
sgom grwa 'dzugs pa/ rten lha khang bzhengs pa/bod 'brog dge rgyun la sbyor ba/ mnga' zhabs la khral 'chag ster ba sogs/ dkar phyogs kyi mdzad 'phrin kho na gtso bor 'don
cing / phun sum tshogs pa chen po bco brgyad dang / nye ba'i phun tshogs bco brgyad dang ldan pas/ sems can thams cad bde ba'i lam la bkod do/ /mi dbang de'i rnam thar thugs
rgyud la/ /'khrungs pa'i dge las byed dang byed 'gyur dang / /'gro la phan bde'i sgrub pa 'di ltas na/ /byams mgon sprul pa yin par kun gyi bsngags/ /zhes pa rnams chos
khrims dar bar mdzad pa'i rnam thar zur tsam bkod pa'o/ /rgyal khrims bde bas bskyangs tshul ni/ gzhon nu nyid nas rtsa ba'i dpon yang / 'khon gyis gdung rgyud rin chen
rnams kyi zhabs la gtugs/ yab khu bo bgres rim rnams gtsug tu khur/ bting 'jags thon/ rgya ta ming rgyal pos ta'i si tu'i mtshan dang / dngul dam lung gnang sbyin dang
bcas pa gnang / stag tshang rdzong pa dang / dpon blon sngar las kyang nye bar 'brel nas/ mi dbang nam mkha' la sogs pa'i thugs sras su gyur cing / lte rtse rdzong gis gnyer
las bzung nas/ zhabs tog tshul bzhin du bsgrubs/ bzhi thog gdung rgyud pas/ sku phra mo nas/ mnga' zhabs byin dge ba la bskul cing / kun gyis chos rgyal chen

mor mtshan gsol/ dpung mi lag tu zas nor gdangs nas/ ngal dub dang phangs pa med pa'i phan cha mdzad pa'i/ srid rtogs yar 'phel du gyur/ mi mthun phyogs pa'i thad du dpa' dpung
'joms pa'i nga rgyal gyis/ yar mar gang du su dang thug kyang / jus kyis rgyal kha lon cing / nor bu khyung rtse dang / g.yul rgyal stag rtse/ stod du ldan dkar rdzong
/ smad du yar 'brog stag lung / lho brag skor la sogs/ rdzong bzhi'i/ mnga' zhabs gsar du chod pa mang zhing / khri skor brtan lhing gtso bor ston pas/ chen po dgra la
byams byas nas/ /tha mar dgra bo dbang du sdud/ /mang pos bkur bas kun bskyangs pas/ /kun gyis rgyal po dbang bskur ro/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ srid mi gcig pa rnams kyang
srid la mthun par byed do/ /'dir sde srid 'dzin pa'i go sa/ mthon por phebs nas/ mnga' zhabs sngar yod rnams/ bo zags med pa'i steng du/ rtsa srid byin po'i gtso bor gyur
cing / gdan sa chen po dang / dpal ldan lha rtse/ mdogamus/ chu 'dus man/ gong dkar/ 'phyongs rgyas stag rtse yan/ 'brel chags su zin na'ang / byang phyogs kyi srid po
rnams kyang / de'i bka' lung dang du len cing / de dag thams cad kyi rgyal khrims bdag po/ mthu stobs dang ldan par gyur pas na/ sku lnga'i gzi 'od gsung gis nga ro dang
/ thugs kyis stobs kyi rgyal khrims gnon pa dang / phyag dor gyi sprul pa yin zhes tshig don mthun par grags/ bar pa nang chen rab 'byor 'phags pas/ sa skya nang sor phebs
nas ti shri chen po chos rgyal theg chen chos rgyal gyi thog drangs pa'i/ gdung rgyud khu dbon pa'i zhabs tog dang / sde srid kyis 'dzin skyong rnams kyang / gcen gyis

dgongs pa dang mthun pa'i/ rang phyogs la byang sems dang ldan zhing / gzhan phyogs su non shin tu che zhes phyi nang kun tu bstod cing smon pa'i gnas su gyur to/ /gcung po
dmag dpon bkra shis 'phags pa ni sku gzhon nu nyid nas/ yab mes gong ma rnams kyi mdzad srol dang mthun par/ dgra ri dwags kyi phyogs la zhal bstan pa tsam gyis/ pha rol
pham par nus kyis/ jus dang dgra thabs la shin tu phan pas/ dus kun tu g.yul las rgyal ba kho na byung bas na/ dmag dpon rin chen dang chos mtshungs la/ de'i don gyi gnad
gang che'i rdzong sa bzung du bzhugs pas/ mnga' zhabs yar 'phel du chod pa/ kun gyi mthun snang du grub pa 'dis/ mi dbang sku mched de rnams kyi dbon sras/ drung bkra shis
rab bstan 'phags pa/ dpal bzang po de nyid kyang / chos 'brangs khungs nas byung ba yis/ rje btsun gyi yon tan thams cad tshang bas/ chos rgyal chen po'i zhal nas/ 'di
ni sde srid kyis bstan pa 'dzin pa'i skyes bu dam par 'gyur ro gsungs shing / mdzad 'phrin mthong thos kyi skye bo thams cad kyang mgrin gcig tu bstod cing / snyan grags
brjod cing sku brtan par bzhugs pa lags so/ /chos rgyal sku mched yab sras mnga' thang dang / /blon po sde jus khur gyis mi ngal zhing / /zhi drag thabs lam blo gros bang
mdzod rgyas/ /sdag bsngal nad gsol sman pa'i rgyal po dang / /shes rab spyan ldan 'jam dbyangs dpon btsun dang / /sde jus bya ba mkhas pa sangs rgyas gsum/ /'di 'dra'i
blon rje na rim bsnan pa yis/ /sde pa su lang 'dug pa mthong ma myong / /rje blon shas che sde

jus byung ba rnams/ /shes la 'chol dang bcol bas byed pa ste/ /kun la dkon kyang 'di na 'dzoms pa 'di/ /byang sems sprul pa 'di yi sde bar go /'di la smon rnams 'di 'dra mdzad
par rigs/ /slar yang rje dpon sku tshe brtan pa dang / /zhal ngo 'phel zhing mnga' thang rgyas pa dang / /chab srid dar zhing rgyas par shog/ // dge'o// //

ma sangs sprul pa stag sna rdzong pa'i byung tshul lo/ / 'gro ba'i gtsug rgyan dpal ldan sa skya pas/ /chol kha gsur la kha lo bsgyur pa'i dus/ /de yi 'phrin las sgrub pa'i
dpon chen dang / /slob dpon dge bshes blon rje rim pa rnams/ /mkhas pa mchog stobs grangs las 'das mod kyis/ /thog mar yus po che ba'i mi gsum po/ /grom pa'i sa skya dpon
rje shAka bzang dang / /shar smad tsong kha'i dge bshes rin brtson dang / /mdo stod go 'jo'i hor chen don tshul yin/ /de gsum nang nas rigs mtho blo gsal ba/ /dge bshes
chen po nas brgyud ding sang bar/ /bla ma'i zhabs tog dbus gtsang bya ba dang / /mi mthun dpung 'joms ma sangs bka' babs zhes/ /snyan pa'i grags pas phyogs bcu kun khyab
pa/ /blon chen 'di pa'i byon tshul 'di ltar ro/ /de yang 'di ltar thos te/ sngon bod du chos skyong rgyal po khri srong lde btsan dang / de'i sras bzhi pa/ khri lde srong
btsan rgyal po'i sku ring la/ mtha'i dmag 'gog pa'i bod yul gyi phyogs bzhir/ sgo srung bskos/ khyad par bod dmag khri khrag mang po khyer nas/ bha ta hor gyi sgom grwa
bcom/ g.yul rgyal/ gnang bcad nas phyir byon dus/ de phyogs kyi sgo srung la/ bod dmag gseb nas skyen btus pa'i dpa' bo mi dgu dmag brgya phrag dgu dang bcas pa hor bod
kyi so mtshams su bzhag de dus khong rnams kyi/ nged rnams ji tsam la log

rgyu yin zhus pas/ rgyal po'i lung gi nged kyi bka' ma byung bar la log rgyu med gsungs pas/ de phyin pas dpa' bo mi dgu'i rus ling bka' ma log zer bar chags te/ der yun ring
bas/ bka' ma log gi bod 'brog sde tshan mang po yod/ se chen rgyal po'i blon chen sang gha ching sang zer ba de'ang / rus bka' ma log tshang yin zer ba 'dug de rnams kyi
chad rgyud las chad pa/ shar tsong kha mtsho sngon gyi mthil na/ skad gsar ba bya ba dang / bya rong ba bcu dgu mer bya ba dang / yul khams chen po gsum gyi bdag po yang
zangs ring mo'i sras che ba/ skya ming dbon po rin chen rgyal mtshan zhes pa/ blo gsal zhing skye mched dwangs pa zhig byung ba/ de nyid gzhon nu nas dkar po'i phyogs
la mos pa zhig yod pas/ yul khams rnams mched zla kun 'dzin du bcug nas/ gtsang sa skya bla ma'i snyan grags tshor/ mos gus bcug te/ zhabs la gtug par 'dod nas yar byon te/
mdo stod kyi hor chen ston tshul yang / chos don du gnyer ba la/ sngon la 'bri gung du byon/ der ma bsten/ sa skyar chas pa dang / khong rnam gnyis gya ba lung par mjal/
mdo stod smad kyi phyogs srid dang / sku tshe sngon ma'i 'brel shugs kyis/ spun phu nu ltar thugs shin tu mthun par byung nas/ de'i dbyar gya ba 'brong ngu dgon par bsdad/
ston de 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa gong nas yar phebs dus/ 'brong ngu dgon pa bas gdan drangs/ bsnyen bkur zhus/ de thog tu khong rnam gnyis pas kyang mjal/
rab byung zhus/ dbon po'i mtshan rin chen brtson 'grus bya bar btags/ bdag slob gnyer mthil phyin pa zhig byed 'dod pas/ rjes su bzung du gsol zhus pas/ de bzhin legs/

slob dpon shar pa ye shes rin chen gyi slob gnyer gyi 'go 'don gyis la/ dge bshes chen po zhig mgyogs par yong bar byed do gsungs nas/ dge bshes la snga ba rin chen brtson
'grus zer ba'ang / de dus nas byung bar gda'o/ /de gnyis ka'i phyag phyir byon/ sa skyar phebs/ slob gnyer mdzad pas/ shes rab dang / thugs rus che ba'i tshad thub par byung
nas/ ring por ma lon par sa skya'i dge bshes rnams kyi nang nas/ mkhas grags thon par byung / bar skabs nas bla ma 'phags pa'i phyag phyi zhabs tog mthil bzhugs yun ring
mdzad/ bya ba'i ljid khur chen po mang du gal/ de mtshams sa 'bri 'khrug pa'i 'go tshugs/ gong du khrims kyi gtug bsher la phyogs phyogs nas mi drag pa 'gro dgos pa byung
dus/ dpon chen shAkya bzang po dang / dge bshes rin chen brtson 'grus/ rin po che ston tshul gsum po'i bla ma dang / bstan pa gdan sa chen pos phyis la bsam te/ blos
blangs nas byon/ khrims lugs su song bas/ tshal gung thang nas/ pho brang shang rdo'i bar la/ an khur nas rkang thang la byon/ gong du gtug bsher legs/ sa skya pa'i bya
ba rnams la gang 'dod legs par grub nas/ yar 'khor dus khong rnams sa skya ba la/ yus che ba'i mi gsum du grags par byung zhing / chen por gyur/ spyi sgos su bla ma'i gnang
sbyin/ brgya stong so so'i bya dga' chen po byas/ khyad par dge bshes chen po la/ ja rin la sa skya'i drug cha ma'i 'dab sgo dang / tshong dus khang leb kyi 'go byas/
grwa sa khang ga ra phu'i gyog gzhis ka rnams gtsang mar gnang / skya btsun thams cad kyi bkur sti zhabs tog che bar byung / de'i skabs su mched grogs ston tshul ba'i gros
la slob

gnyer gyi bka' spyad byas/ dge bshes kyi snyan grags ni thob/ sa skyas gsang sngags zab mo'i bdag po yin pas/ da yang gsang sngags dang mthun par mdzad na sku khams kyi 'tsho
skyong du'ang 'gyur la/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su/ bu slob rjes 'dzin sogs la'ang khyad che bar yong zer ba la gsan nas myang stong byed mda' ba/ ma gcig mkha' 'gro 'bum mngon
chung ngus gyog gzhis ka ru bzhagaphyag rgya bsten pa la sras gsum byung ba'i che ba ban rgan blo gros rin chen/ bar pa dharma dkon mchog chung pa dpon kun dga' do rje
rnams byung / bar pa 'di 'gro mgon phyag na'i sras/ dharma pha la rakShi ta dang / lo zla zhag dus mnyam du 'khrungs pa na/ mtshan 'di chos rgyal 'phags pas btags par byed
do/ /de'i dus su rgyal bu chos dpal/ bod 'chos pa la byon pas/ bsu skyel zhabs tog la dge bshes chen po de bas/ 'bad rtsol skyes pas/ nyi ma nub phyogs kyi bya ba rnams
legs par grub nas phyir byon dus/ sog sa mdo bar skyel thung la byon par rgyal bu mnyes nas/ byang re thag phyir than gang 'dug rin chen brtson 'grus mi rgyud dang bcas
pa shes su chug cing / khyed kyi shed mong 'dab pa bzhin du bu tsha bo rnams kyis kyang / gong ma yon mchod la shed mong 'dab chug zer ba'i/ lung ji bzang po gnang / de
nas dge bshes chen po/ sa skya'i tshong dus khang leb tu zhi bar gshegs rting / sras che ba ban rgan pas/ yab kyi rjes su zhugs nas khrims kyi bya ba dang / sa skya pa'i
zhabs tog nang so'i mthil len/ dgos su bla ma bdag nyid chen po'i zhabs la gtug shed mong gdab/ ta tu'i pho brang du byon pas/ bla ma'i sku drin la/ o la ja du rgyal po'i
lung lha

rgod mdung rtse yan nas/ dwangs ra g.yu mtsho man 'di/ blo gros rin chen rgyud pa dang bcas pa shes su bcug pa'i 'ja' sa gtsang ma gnang / gcung gnyis po nye ring med par bskyangs/
gcen la byang gi khri dpon dang / gcung la du dben shI'i las ka zhus nas bskos/ dharma dkon mchog gi gzhis pa la/ ma gcig mkha' 'gro 'bum gyi nye gnas ma zhig dang
/ dpon kun rdor rje la ma gcig bsod 'bum gyi tsha mo zhig blangs nas/ gnyis ka la sras ma byung / ban rgan pas zhal ta mdzad/ zhal ta ma re re 'og tu bzhag pa las/ khri
dpon dharma dkon mchog la sras khri dpon chos rgyal dang / dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po byung / du dben sha kun dga' rdo rje la sras/ khri dpon dkon mchog rgyal mtshan byung
/ khri dpon chos rgyal gyis/ yab kyi shul du byang ru'i khri dpon thog gcig mdzad nas sku gshegs so/ /sras med pas dkon mchog rgyal mtsha khri dpon la bskos/ bla chen
kun blo'i phyag phyir gong la byon/ yar jo mo sreg shing dbon mo bslangs nas/ mthong smon sa cha/ lha khang spang grong grong gi kha 'dzin byed dus/ sras bzhi byung ba'i
che ba dpon po dkon mchog 'od zer dang / dkon mchog rin chen/ mkhan po bsod nams blo gros/ chung ba rgod po rin chen rnams byung ngo / /gcung po 'di ma sangs kyi sprul
pa yin pa'i rgyu mtshan ni/ 'di'i skabs su dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po de nyid/ 'brog khri skor gyi ru thog mtsho mo ru khyung gi skor nas sgar chen bzhugs dus/ chibs pa
ston chen bya ba zhig bor nas/ lha 'dre mi gsum la lca hu bkrams/ rtsad gcod pa phyogs bzhir btang bas/ shar phyogs pa mi gnyis kyis kha ba skya sribs babs pa'i steng la
rta rjes 'dug pa/

mthar ded pas sog la skya bo'i zhol na/ sgar chen zhig 'dug de'i khrod na chibs pa yang 'dug nas/ mgron mnyer ba la rgyu mtshan bshad/ sgar 'di su'i yin bris pas/ ma sangs
gyi sgar yin/ ge sar dang rgu ldi la sogs pa yod zer/ gur nang du khrid/ rgu ldi yin zer ba de na re/ nged kyi kha sing nas byang stong la yong / dpon chen pa dang mjal rtsis
la ma mjal/ da gzod khyed kyi dpon po zhig yod pa de dang / yang yang 'phrad zer ba gyis la/ rta dang mda' rgod sgro ma 'di phul zer nas khyer yong / dpon chen pa la
phul/ der rting dpon po rgod po rin chen 'khrungs so/ /dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po de nyid/ ti shri kun rgyal ba'i zhabs la gtug gong la phyag phyir byon/ bla ma'i sku drin
dang / khrims kyi bya ba la mkhas pas/ sngon la dbon shri dang / der rting du dbus gtsang gi dpon chen sngun ma thob/ yar phebs dus rgan pas zhal ta mdzad/ jo mor bla
ma mus chen po'i dbon mo dang / dpon mo jo mo rim par blangs na'ang / sras ma byung ba/ zhal ta ma 'bum rgyan bya ba la sras grags pa rgyal mtshan pa byung zhing / rting
la sras zur du dbon po hor tsha bya ba zhig yang byung / dpon chen pas dbon po dkon mchog 'od zer byang khri dpon la bskos/ sras po grags pa rgyal mtshan pa sa skya nang
sor bzhag dbus gtsang bde ba la bkod nas/ dbon po dkon mchog rin chen pa phyag phyir khrid te/ yang gong ma yon mchod kyi zhabs drung du byon pa/ sngon rting dril bas lo
bco brgyad tsam gong du bzhugs/ son jing dben gyi rtsa ba'i dpon chen lo zhang lan gsum mdzad/ lung gu ta ha'i zon gnang / yar 'byon khar nga'i sbra ber khyung gsum gyi
tshong pa/ bod la lo re

bzhin yong ba'i 'babs sa'i gnas gzhi zhig brtsigs dgos zhus pas/ gang 'os tshol gsungs pa la/ shangs na e mar sgang rgyud nas sa che bar 'dug pas 'di dgos zhus pas/ gye re
babs la gdong yan/ thag ma ngal gdong / nyang ri shi cig man gyi sa cha/ rgyal ba bzang po'i rta sga 'bogs la byin cing / de khongs gang 'os su gnas gzhi brtsig tu chug gsungs
pa'i lung bzang po gnang bas/ yar phebs nas shangs mthong smon gyi sa cha 'di na/ klu gnas pa'i rdzing zhig 'dug pas/ ming dang gang sa nas rten 'brel la legs pas/
'di khongs su chug pa gyis gsungs lcags ri/ dpe lcog rnams kyi dkyil du khang leb chen mo dang bcas par btab/ der rting gong ma yon mchod kyi sku rim smon lam 'debs shing
/ spos bsregs pa'i lha khang zhig bzhengs su bcug dgos zer ba'i zhu ba gong du btang bas/ de bzhin yin chug gsungs pa'i lung phebs nas/nyug rgyal khang rgyal po'i pho brang
la dpe blangs na bzhengs/ chos sde 'di sngon bod rgyal blon bzhugs dus kyi bka' bstsal rnying pa dang / ram sding ma bas dgon lag rnying pa da cha med pa zhig 'dug pa'ang
/ dpon chen pas rgyal khang bzhengs pa dang mnyam du/ sa paNDi ta 'jigs med grags pa/ chos dpon la gdan drangs/ dgos kyi mnga' zhabs la btsun khral thengs gnyis rgyab
nas bshad grwa btsugs/ chos sde'i shed mong skyed/ chos khrims dar bar mdzad cing / yab yum gyi phyi bstan la/ g.ye mar sgang stod du/ sku 'bum chen mo bzhengs/ zha lu
bu ston rin po che gdan drangs nas/ rab gnas dbus gtsang du rgyas pa'i dpe thub pa mdzad/ lung gi bskos pa'i dpon chen gnyis/ byang sa'i phyag tshab cig

dang bcas pas/ gong du dbus gtsang dang / dpon chen thengs gsum mdzad pas/ de bar la gdan sa chen mo'i zhabs tog bla ma la bkur sti/ mnga' zhabs kyi skyong thar/ phag gru khri
dpon dang / khams pa la sogs khrims 'gal mu med byed mi rnams la/ drag las kyi 'jun 'dul/ gzhan yang rgyal khrims chen po'i bya ba la'ang / nye ring med cing blang dor
ma 'dzol bar byung bas/ kun gyi byang chub sems dpa'i dpon chen du grags shing / gong nas rting ma phebs rjes la/ sras blo gros rgyal mtshan pa byung ba/ gcen dpon chen
