grags rgyal dang / dgung lo bcu bdun bco brgyad kyi khyad yod pas na/ grags rgyal ba'i sras yin par byed pa yang yod la/ khong gnyis kyi bar du dpon po hor tshas dpon thog
tu lo gcig gnyis bzhugs zer ba'ang gleng / dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po bas/ khrims gnyis kyi bya ba dpon chen dbang brtson la 'phrod pa'i skabs su/ lha rtse'i gzims khang
lho mar bde bar gshegs nas/ spur bzhu dus/ thugs ljags dang bcas te byon pa de/ gzims khang gung rigs la/ chos rgyal 'phags pa'i sku 'dra yod pa/ de'i thugs kar thim
pa kun gyi mthun snang du grub bo/ /phyis skor gyi dpon chen la/ 'di nyid bla ma la gus zhing khrims gnyis kyi bya ba la mkhas par byed do/ /dpon chen pa'i sras po grags
pa rgyal mtshan pas/ sngon sa skya nang chen bzung / rting la dpon chen gyi ming thob/ shang mthong smon bzung ba'i skabs der sku gshegs so/ /gcung po dpon po hor tsha'i
sras/ sna dkar ba dpon kun dga' rgyal po rgyud chad/ blo gros rgyal mtshan pas/ si tu'i ming dang las ka thob/ dpon chen pas dbon po 'di dang / mthong

smon sbrags nas ta'i si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan la sprad/ gtsang phyogs kyi sde pa dar lcog dkar po 'dzugs pa'i sngon ma byas zer ba 'dug 'di'i ring la mthong smon pad chen
bzhengs/ sgo pad zur lcog rnams kyi kha sgron/ 'bor lcags chung bzos so/ /de'i sras bzhi pa'i che ba du dben sha byang chub rgyal ba dpal bzang po'ang / ldog thung du
grags pa/ thugs rgod cing rtsal skyen pas/ de'i ring la rdzong shang dang / phyi nang gi sde 'khrug mang / de 'og mkhan po kun dga' blo gros pas/ nyug chos sde'i mkhan po
mdzad/ de 'og tu dben sha kun dga' rgyal mtshan pas/ rgyal mthong bzung kun dang mthun pa'i lugs shas che bar byung / gcung po chung ba dpon po kun dga' rdo rje bas/ du
dban sha kun rgyal bas gdung rgyud lcam mo blangs pa la sras shig 'khrungs pa/ du dben sha rin chen rgyal po sku brtan par bzhugs pa'o/ khri dpon dkon mchog 'od zer bas
byang ru thog gi khri dpon mdzad cing / dpon po dkon mchog rin chen dang / rgod po rin chen pas/ nyug rgyal khang mgo byas/ bres sna la sogs 'dzin/ mkhan po bsod nams blo
gros pas zhang po'i gdan sa sreg shing gi mkhan po mdzad pa'i dus su/ mthong smon na yang/ dpon chen grags rgyal ba yod pas/ dpon skya g.yog rigs kyi dbang du song nas shangs
pa nang ma bde/ dpon po sku mched che ba gnyis sku gshegs rting dpon po rgod po rin chen pas/ stag tshang rdzong khar bla chen bsod blo sku mched pa'i zhabs la gtugs/
rgyab bcol nas rdzong blang sde gzar rgyun ring / dgung lo bco brgyad pa la bla chen gyi phyag phyir mkhan chen g.yas ru pas byas nas/ gong la byon bla ma'i bka' drin
la/ tho

gon thi mur rgyal pos/ phing gcig pa'i mi dpon srid swan jing dben gyi hu shri'i mtshan dang / dam rtags/ ban rgan blo gros rin chen pa'i dus su/ ji ltar gnang ba bzhin gyi
bod 'brog dbang rigs rnams/ rgod po rin chen du hu shri mi rgyud dang bcas pa shes su chug gsungs pa'i lung bzang po dang bcas pa gnang / yar phebs bla ma sku mched pas
zhabs tog sde pa stag tshang rdzong kha'i phyi'i dgra 'dul dmag dpon gyi bya ba gang la'ang / sde pa'i mtshan jus gtso bor ston pas/ dpon sa nas kyang thag rta nag ga gnyer
pa gnang / sna dmar rdzong brtsigs/ shangs pa nang ltar gyi sde gsar 'pho 'jug mang na'ang phyi nang sus kyang rgol bar ma nus pa/ rgod pa'i snyan grags shin tu che zhing
/ me pho stag lo rdzong stag sna don grub rtse bzung ste/ de'i char gtogs pa'i mnga' zhabs bod 'brog mang du chod nas/ da lta'i bar la brtan cing 'phel ba dang bcas pa'o/
/de la yum mi gcig pa'i sras bu gsum byung pa'i che ba/ rta nag pa dpon po shAkya rin chen/ ngam rings pa rgyal ba rin chen/ chung ba skyor mo ba sog po rin chen rnams
te/ shAkya rin chen pas/ yab kyi gnyer las kyi rjes rta nag bzung / de la sras dug tsher rin chen dang / nam mkha' rin chen/ dge sbyong dkar por grags pa rnams so/ /rgyal
ba rin chen la sras/ rnam rgyal rin chen dang / dpal ldan rin chen byung / gnyis ka yab kyi sngon la 'das so/ /sog po rin chen pas/ lha bu rin mkhar zer khong lam rdzong
gsar brtsigs/ sras rgyal bu rin chen pa dang / dge sbyong bsod nams rin chen pa/ grags pa rin chen pa rnams byung ngo / khri dpon dkon mchog 'od zer ba/ sku mched phyogs
gcig

pa'i dus kyi sras po gcig byung ba/ drung chen glang po rin chen de nyid/ yab grongs pa'i rjes la stag tshang rdzong khar 'khrungs/ dpon po dang bla brang dang / mtsho skyong
'go 'don yang dag mdzad/ cher skyes nas dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan pas zhal mthong / dbang rnam sras pa'i zhabs la gtugs/ gzim dpon mdzad/ khu dbon phyogs gcig tu dril
nas dgra 'dul gnyen skyong / dpon po'i zhabs tog buddha'i sog rum skyong thar/ 'jig rten gyi bya ba la shin tu mkhas shing / thugs rtsol che bar grags pas phyogs kun tu
khyab bo/ khyad par dbus pa bdag po grags pa rgyal mtshan pas phag mo gru ba'i srid la gtogs pa'i dbus gtsang gi dmag dpung stobs che ba bsdus nas/ me pho khyi lo'i ston
stag sna rdzong la bskor rgyag yun ring byas/ nang yan 'tshag skyel bred sdig ji snyed cig byung na'ang / yab sras dpon g.yog rnams kyi legs par sra bcas/ phur btsugs/ 'thab
rol sprad pas dbus gtsang du mkhregs pa'i tshad thub pa byung zhing / stag shar gtsang srid du grags pa'i 'go de nas tshugs pa yin/ sa skya pa'i srid jus yar 'phel du
song ba blon chen de nyid kyi thugs zhen dang / 'phrin las la brten pa'o/ /de'i sras lnga'i che ba/ drung chen nam mkha' rin chen pa ni/ sku gzhon nu nas klog yig la sogs
bslab shes kyi yon tan mtha' dgasngon du phyogs nas/ mi dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan pa dang / mes po ho shri chen po'i zhabs la gtugs/ gsol ja bzung / pho rtsal sna dgu
skur skyong 'grogs lam sde srid 'dzin pa'i bya ba la yon tan sgor mor 'dzoms pas kun gyi ma sangs kyi sprul par 'dzin cing / khyad par khyi lo dmag chen gyi lo rdzong
gi dus rtse

zhol bsrung ba gang khag pa thams cad du phebs nas/ sgyogs mda' rdo'i gnad sprad pas shin tu ngo mtshar du gyur te/ phyis nas gdong len gyi mi su yang med pa byung ngo / /gzhan
yang dmag che chung mtha' rogs snga phyi mang po'i 'go ma la byon pa/ dus nam yang gdong phud ngor lang kho na mdzad cing / phyi skor bya ba gang la'ang / brtan lhing
gtso bor 'don pas/ phyi nang kun gyis 'di ni dpa' mdzangs 'dzoms pa'i skyes bu chen po yin zhes grags so/ /de'i gcung po rgya bzang rin chen/ rgya mtsho rin chen/ nor bu
rin chen/ grub pa rin chen rnams yin/ gcung 'di'i rdzong rang 'byon rtse bzung / mtshar zhan bod 'brog kun gsar du chod do/ /gcen gyi khab tu gdung rgyud lcam mo/ byang
sems nam mkha' rgyal po ba byon pa'i sras che ba chos rgyal rin chen mched gsum te/ sku mched khu dbon zhal ngo mang la hrags pa/ sku brtan par bzhugs pa lags so/ /blon
chen che rgyud ma sangs sprul pa'i rigs/ kha drag mi dpung 'dzoms pa 'khor bcas 'dis/ /phas rgol mi mthun phyogs las rgyal ba dang / /dpal 'byor yar ngo'i zla ltar rgyas
gyur cig /dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig /pho rtsal sna dgu ni mtheb kyi sha non pa dang gcig rkyal gyis chu non pa/ yang sor bya lta bu dang gsum la dpa' shed lus kyi rtsal
gsum zer/ lo rgyus kyi dge yon thon pa dang / 'gran shags kyi lce non pa dang / khyom tshos bzhad gad thon pa dang gsum la smra ba ngag gi rtsal gsum zer/ dpa' la brtan
tshugs pa dang gcig mdzangs la blo myur ba dang gnyis/ go gsal la gting sus kyang mi rtogs pa dag gsum la/ blo gros sems kyi rtsal gsum zer/ pho rtsal sna dgu ni/ mda' rdo
mchongs gsum/ sho phras rtsis gsum/ bang shags rkyal gsum dang dgu'o/ /pho rtsal sna dgu 'di 'dzom na ma sangs sprul par byed do/ //

gnod sbyin sprul pa rnam rgyal gling pa'i byon tshul bzhugs so/ /oM swa sti/ 'gro ba'i gtsug rgyan dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /sku ring las byung dpon chen nye gnas sogs/ /rab
dang rim par byung ba mang mod kyi/ /phyi skor bla brang kho na'i bya ba rnams/ /ches lhag phul phyin sgrub pa'i nye gnas mchog / dam tshig gtsang zhing bsod nams dpal gyis
mtho/ /zas nor dbang 'byor gnod sbyin sprul par grags/ /byas pa lag rjes che ba 'di ltar byung / /de'ang sngon spu rgyal bod 'di/ chos skyong ba'i rgyal po khri srong
lde'u btsan gyi sku'i ring la/ za hor kyi yul nas/ mkhan po bo dhi satwa gdan drangs nas/ bla ma'i mchod gnas su bkur/ bod du btsun pa la snga ba/ sad mi mi bdun bya ba
rab tu byung nas/ 'khor mang po dang bcas te/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar bar mdzad/ de dang dus mnyam du nub phyogs u rgyan gyi yul nas/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas gdan
drangs/ bod kyi lha klu gdug pa can dam la btags/ rgya gar o tan ta pu ri'i gtsug lag khang la dpe blangs nas/ ri rab gling bzhi gling phran nyi zla lcags ri mu khyud dang
bcas pa/ dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen po bzhengs/ bod rgyal po'i bla mar mnga' gsol/ de'i dus su u rgyan

pad ma'i dngos slob gnyags dang / 'khon rdo rje rin chen dang / so zur snubs gsum la sogs/ dkyil 'khor gtso brgyad du grags pa byung / de rnams kyi nang nas/ dbas kyi ston
pa a mes mtshan rdo rje rgyal mtshan bya ba/ bdud rtsi yon tan gyi lha tshogs la thugs dam gyi gtso bo mdzad cing / chos skyong tshogs bdag dkar dmar/ bran du 'khol nus pa
gsang sngags rnying ma'i grub thob chen po zhig dang / dbus ru skyi shod kyi lung par/ zul phu 'o ma'i nags 'dabs su byung te/ bla ma de nyid kyi zul phu gnas gsar gyi
dgon pa btab/ sngags pa'i grwa bu slob mang po bskyangs nas/ gsang sngags kyi bstan pa dar bar mdzad/ de nas bzung ste/ rgyud pa bcu tsam gyi bar la/ gnam la rdo rje'i gur
ma zhig pa/ sa la dkyil 'khor gyi bkrag ma yal ba/ bar na rakta'i mtsho ma bskams pa'i/ sngags 'chang grub pa thob pa mang po byung ngo / /de'i skabs su hor sa skya pa
yon mchod du 'brel nas/ bod chol kha gsum po la sa skya pas kha lo bsgyur ba'i dus/ gnas gsar sngags pa'i dbon rgyud/ dbon po dkon mchog skyabs zer ba zhig byung ba des/
dpal ldan sa skyar bla ma bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal ba yab sras kyi zhabs la btugs/ sa skya nang so dang / chu mig khri khang lo 'ga' bzung / nye gnas chen po mgon
po skyabs zhes par grags pa de'i ring la/ gtsang stod lhan lung gi sa cha dang / pa snam phyogs kyi sa phran 'dra bdag tu bzung bar 'dug 'di yan la so sor gyes pa'i rus mtshams
ni/ rta nag phug pa/ dpon dgos pa rin chen pa skor yang yin par byed cing /

zul phu phyogs na'ang da lta yang / sngags rgyud 'dzin pa mang rab yod par snang / nye gnas chen po mgon po skyabs pa la/ sras po mched gsum byung ba'i che ba/ chen po don
grub rgyal mtshan pa de bstan pa'i mnga' bdag ti shri kun blo'i zhabs la gtugs/ bod khams su gdan sa bar ba/ rtse 'od bsam grub kyi nye gnas chen po dang / sho tham kha gnang
/ de nas bzung 'phags pa kun blo gshegs nas/ ti shri kun rgyal ba'i phyag phyi mthil byas/ gong la byon bla mas thugs la btags nas/ pho brang ta'i tur/ rdzong kha bu'i
khrims ra dang / nye gnas chen po la bskos/ bod la 'byon khar gong ma tho gon thi mur rgyal pos/ du dben shri mtshan dang lung lag rtags bzang po gnang zhing / khyad par
yab yum gtsang stod lhan lung gi 'og tu lhan gangs gdong yan/ span smad jo bo rigs gsum mgon po man/ pa rnam gyi gzhis phran rnams dang bcas pa gtsang gzhis su 'jags pa'i/
'ja' sa chen mo gnang / yar phebs nas kyang lha khang bla brang bas gdung rgyud yab sras rnams kyis zhabs tog tshul bzhin sgrub par gda'o/ /de'i gcung chen po/ dpal
ldan rgyal mtshan pa des/ ta dben gu shri kun dga' nyi mas thog drangs 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan pa sku mched pa'i phyag phyir slebs/ rin chen sgang bla brang ba'i
nye gnas chen po mdzad/ rin chen sgang ga lcags ri chen mo dang / sgo spe shar nub/ gar phu'i phyogs bzhis kha khram mo/ /bo dong e'i lcags ri phyi ma/ sgo lcog 'khor ma/
nang du bud rtse gsar ma/ phyi ru mgron khang skar bcas/ gzhan yang bo dong ma

las dga' ba'i bu bzhir grags pa'i gzhis ka bkra shis sgang / rog tshe/ shab dge sding / 'jad mthong smon la sogs/ gzhis che chung mang po'i mkhar las gsar brdungs zhabs su
phyug par bzhengs/ mdor na bla brang gi bya ba kho na la gtso bor ston pa'i nang gi gsog mchog phyis 'dul skyong dgos pa gang la'ang / phyis skor gyi nye gnas chen mo rnams
kyi nang nas/ 'di nyid bya ba lag rjes shin tu che bar grags so/ /gcung chung shos chen po nor bu bzang po pas/ gcen gyi rjes su 'brang ste/ bo dong gi nye gnas chen po
mdzad/ dpal lngan bla ma dam pa dang chos rje bsod rgyal ba/ chos 'khor chen mo skor ba'i mthun rkyen/ brjid khur mthil gzhu sogs rin chen sgang pa'i gdung rgyud zhal ngo
rnams kyi zhabs tog bsgrubs/ gcung po slob dpon chen po bsod nams yon tan pas rab tu byung nas dpal bo dong e'i chos dpon mdzad do/ /gcen po don rgyal du dben shrIs/ jo
mo khams mo la/ sras shig byung ba ni/ dbang hu bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa'o/ /yang jo mo gtsang mo la sras slob dpon don grub rgyal mtshan pa byung nas/ rin chen sgang
dang / bo dong du thog cig bzhugs nas/ chen po grub rgyal du grags so/ /des rtsa ba'i gzhis/ gtsang stod lhan lung gi skor rnams sgos bdag tu bzung / de'i dbon sras kyi rgyud
dang / lhan lung pa yab sras rnams yin no/ /dbang hu chen po de nyid kyis sku gzhon nu'i dus dpal bo dong e'i chos grwa chen por dpang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa'i
drung du/ rab tu byung nas mngon pa mdzod la slob gnyer mdzad pa'i/ dge

bshes su grags/ de'i skabs su/ bla chen bsod blo ba sku mched/ dus mchod bla brang nas/ stag tshang rdzong khar phebs pa'i phyag phyir byon/ gsol gzim mdzad pa gang la'ang
'jug pa'i las tshan mthil bzung / zhabs tog la brtson cing / phyi nang gi bya ba la mkhas pas/ bla chen pa shin tu mnyes nas/ gong la byon pa'i phyag phyir khrid/ bla ma'i
sku drin la/ gong ma thog gan thi mur rgyal pos/ ri tsing dbang gi las 'dzin/ khrims ra brgyad yod pa'i che shos g.yas phyogs kyi dbang hu'i mtshan dang / dam rtags lung
bzang po dang bcas pa gnang / yar phebs nas pa'e len dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan pas bka' lung ji ltar gnang pa bzhin/ las stod mnga' ris kyi phyogs la lam 'phrang dgra
gnyen gang la'ang ma bsam par byon nas/ dgra phyogs 'dul ba dang / rang phyogs bstod pa la sogs bya ba chen po rnams/ dpon po'i dgongs pa dang mthun par grub nas phyir phebs
dus/ dpon sa nas kyang mnga' ral gsum gyi gdan sa/ lha sde mi sde/ ya mi snyan gyis rus sde dang bcas pa bzhengs te/ dpa' zhal la gnang / stag tshang rdzong gong 'og
gi gnyer las nye gnas chen mo la bskos/ mi dbang chen mo rang gi sras mo/ byang sems bsod nams rgyal mo ba khab tu gnang ba la sogs/ gdung rus las chad pa'i dbon sras ngo
bo dang 'dra bar 'jog pa sogs/ thugs 'dogs shin tu che bar mdzad cing / dpon sa'i thugs 'dogs dang / khong rang yang rgyal khrims kyi bya ba la mkhas shing / sku bsod kyi
dpal gyi mngon par mtho bas/ dgra 'dul gnyen skyong sde srid

mdzad 'phrin mtha' dag lhun gyis grub nas/ chu mo phag gi lo hor zla brgyad pa'i tshes bco lnga bza' skar dus tshes 'phrod sbyor kun bzang ba'i nyin nas/ rdzong rnam rgyal
gling chen gyi 'gram bting / ring por ma thogs par zhabs su chug par bzhengs/ mnyam med rgyal ba bzang pos thog drangs/ bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen bzang grags mang pa'i
rdzong la rab gnas gsol/ sbyin bdag rang gi yi dam gyi mtshan dang mthun par byed gsung nas/ rnam rgyal gling chen zhes par ming btags/ son wi pa'i mi dpon chen mo 'di nyid
ni bzang zhing dpa' ba/ mthu stobs zas nor la dbang 'byor pas/ rang gzhan gyi mnga' zhabs thams cad/ bde ba la bkod pa'i snyan grags kyis dbus gtsang thams cad khyab par
gyur cing / gnod sbyin tshogs kyi bdag po'i sprul par grags so/ /de nyid kyi jo mo sngon ma 'bri gung dgung khar dbon mo la/ sras drung chen chos rgyal bzang po ba byung
zhing / gdung rgyud lcam mo la/ thog mar sras gnyis byung ba/ grub chen gong ma 'dra'i sku skyes bzhengs par 'dug na'ang / gzhon nu la sku gshegs/ drung chen chos rgyal
bzang po ba de nyid/ dgung lo brgyad pa la nub chos lung dgon par/ mkhan chen rin po che rgyal bzang pa'i drung du bzhugs nas/ chab klog yig rtsis la sogs sku che ba'i
yon tan mtha' dag la thugs goms par mdzad/ bcu gnyis pa nas ri tsing dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan pas drung du byon/ gsol dpon gyi mthil yun ring bzung / sku dang grib ma
bzhin 'bral ba med par phyag phyir brtson cing /

rdzong gong 'og gi gnyer las kyang yab sras pa'i lo sum cu so bdun mdzad pa'i ring la/ bla brang gi nang du gsol bzang zhing / phyi nas dgra thos skad gcig kyang ma phog pas/
bu rta 'dab rgyas pa dang / mi sde mnga' zhabs bde skyid la longs spyod pa byung / yab bde bar gshegs pa'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs rnams kyang / gtsang g.yas ru'i phyogs
su bzang zhing ngo mtshar che ba'i tshad thub par bsgrubs/ rang gi rdzong mnga' zhabs la/ pha rol gyi dmag dpung stobs chen gyis/ skor rgyag gnod pa yun ring byung dus/
phyi nang kun gyis dpon g.yog thams cad la smon cing / ma khrel sra phur legs par bcas pas/ phyi mi slu brid mgo skor dmag dpung gang gis kyang / rang sde gzhom par ma nus
pa'i steng du/ stag tshang rdzong gi bstan jus zin pa dang / gtsang srid kyi 'go tshugs pa'i skyes bu sde dpon chen por gyur cing / der rting nas sa zugs kyi rdzong gdan
mnga' zhabs gsar du chod pa shin tu mang lags 'di pa yab yum dkar phyogs la mos shing / thugs dge dpa' mdzangs ldan pas/ gong 'og sku nye 'brel chags thams cad la bkur
skyong / 'brog lam zas nor kyi 'dzin tshugs mtshan dag don du ldan pas/ mthun 'jug gang la'ang / sus kyang 'gran du med pa'i snyan grags kyi phyogs kun tu khyab la/ chos
rgyal chen por gda'o/ /drung chen po pa de nyid dang / gdung rgyud lcam mo byang sems bsod nams rgyal mo ba la/ sras po mched gnyis byung ba'i gcen drung rgyal ba dpal bzang
po pa yin cing / gcung po nang so chos skyong rgyal mtshan dpal bzang

po pa 'di bas/ mi dbang nam mkha' legs pa'i gsol dpon bzung / skur skyong 'brog lam/ sde srid chen po dang / yar 'phel la byung ba'i mdzad 'phrin la g.yel mi mnga' zhing /
sku brtan par bzhugs pa lags so/ /sngon chad sku bsod rnam dkar 'phrin las kun/ /rgyu rkyen 'dzoms pas yar 'phel 'byung ba bzhin/ /phyi rabs rgyud 'dzin sku tshe brtan pa
dang / /dpal 'byor mnga' thang che cher dar rgyas shog/ //

bod du bstan pa phyi dar dang / mkhas grub sde dgon byung tshul bzhugs so/ /e ma ho/ chos rgyal mes dbon mkhyen brtse'i nam mkha' la/ /bstan pa'i nyi ma bod kyi yul du gsal/
/sdig chen dar ma'i dgra can gdong pa yis/ /chu mo phag nas drug cu rtsa brgyad bar/ /mun pa'i rgyal khams bzhin du nag por bsgribs/ /bod khams phal cher bstan pa'i sgra
mi grags/ /bstan 'dzin thams cad gab dang bros la rtsol/ /dbus gtsang mthil du chos min sna tshogs dar/ /rgyal khrims chen po'ang rang gi spyod par thal/ /de la rgyal ba
rnams kyis ma bzod par/ /mnga' bdag tsha la na yi thugs rgyud bskul/ /bla chen spyan sngar chos zhu rim par brdzangs/ /bstan pa'i me ro smad nas bslang tshul dang / /phyi
dar rgyas pa byung tshul 'di ltar snang/ zha lu bu ston chos rje'i chos 'byung la/ /bod yul kha ba can gyi yul ljongs 'dir/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa phyi dar byung tshul
ni/ sdig rgyal glang dar mar grags pa de nyid/ chu mo lug lo sum cu so dgu lon pa'i dus/ mnga' bdag khri ral grongs nas/ khong gis rgyal srid bzung / lo gnyis rgyal po tshul
bzhin sgrub/ chu mo phag gi lo gzhug nas thugs la gdon gsol ba dang / blon po rgyal to re stag sna can la sogs pa sdig pa la dga' ba rnams kyis bsgyur nas/ sngar nu bo
la rgyal srid bskos pa'i snying nad

du byas/ bod du sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsnubs/ lo phyed dang bzhir sdig rgyal kho na byas/ zhe bzhi lon pa me pho stag gi lo'i dus/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rjes/ lha sa'i rdo
ring rtsa ru glang dar ma bkrongs so/ /de'i dus su 'jad kyi mi gtsang rab gsal dang / bo dong pa g.yo dge 'byung / stod lung pa dmar shAkya mu ne gsum po/ dpal chu bo
ri la sgom zhing yod pas na btsun pas khyi ra byed pa mthong te/ dris pas rgyal pos bstan pa bsnubs par shes te/ 'dul ba'i po ti drel khal gcig bkal nas mnga' ris stod du
bros/ gar log la lam byas nas hor yul du phyin la/ chos dar bar bya snyam pa la/ skad rigs mi gcig lo tsA med pas dar bar ma nus te/ mdo smad lho dngos kyi be ra tshwa mtsho
na tshur byung nas/ rma lung rdo rje brag ra/ an byung gnam rdzong/ dan tig shel kyi yang dgon du slebs/ sgom zhing yod pa la/ rma chu kha'i phyugs rdzis mthong nas
yul mi la smras pa/ bon po'i grub thob/ mu zu gsal bzang bya ba'i bu lo bco lnga lon pa/ las dang skal ba ldan zhing mos pa la spyod pa'i/ dpal dmu zu gsal 'bar gyi tshor
nas/ ltar phyin pas mthong ba tsam gyi dad nas/ rab tu byung ba zhus pa la/ 'dul ba'i bslab bya'i po ti bstan nas/ 'di la ltos/ 'di ltar rab tu byung na gsungs/ bltas pas
shin du dad te mchi ma byung ngo / /der gtsang gis mkhan po/ g.yos slob dpon byas nas rab tu byung dge tshul gyi ming / mkhan slob dang sbyar nas dge ba rab gsal du btags
so/ /phyis thugs rab che bas/ dgongs pa rab gsal du grags so/ /de nas lo 'ga' song ba dang / bsnyen rdzogs zhus dus/ dge slong lnga ma tshang bas mi yong gsungs/ lha lung
dpal gyi

rdo rje na re/ ngas rgyal po bsad pas byar mi rung gzhan nas btsal gyis rgya nag ha shang ke wang dang / gyi ban bya ba btang byung ba dang / mkhan slob dang dmar gyis gsang
ston/ rgya'i dge song gnyis pos kha skang byas te lnga tshogs kyis bsnyen rdzogs byas so/ /de nas lo lnga lon pa dang / bsam yas na yum brtan gyi rgyal rgyud/ mnga' bdag
tsha la na yab sras kyis/ mdo smad na rab byung yod pa'i rgyu mtshan tshor nas/ dbus gtsang gi mi shes rab dang snying rus che rnams/ chos 'tshol ba la nges par btang dgos
dgongs par shar te/ dbus nas glags pa lam pa/ klu mes shes rab tshul khrims dang / 'bre ye shes yon tan/ rag shi tshul khrims 'byung gnas/ sba tshul khrims blo gros/
sum pa ye shes blo gros dang lnga/ gtsang nas/ mgur mo rab kha ba/ lo ston rdo rje dbang phyugashab sgo mnga' ba'i tshong btsun shes rab seng ge mnga' ris pa 'od rgyal spun
gnyis/ bo dong pa u pa lte dkar ba dang lnga ste/ mi bcu po de khams la brdzangs nas/ gtsang g.yo dmar gsum la/ bka' drin zhus pas/ gtsang na re/ nged rgas pas mkhan po
mi 'khyongs/ bla ma chen po la zhus gsungs/ bla chen gyis bsnyen par rdzogs nas/ lo lnga las ma lon pas na/ mkhan po mi gtub zer ba la/ gtsang na re/ dmigs bsal la gtub
pas gyis gsung nas/ bla chen gyis mkhan po/ gtsang g.yos las slob dang gsang ston byas/ dmar dang ha shang gis kha skong byas te/ thams cad chig rdzogs byas so/ /de nas
bla chen gyi zhal nas da khyed rnams yar song la/ dbus gtsang du bstan pa dar ba zhig gal che'o/ /de'ang lo ston mthu che bas bstan bsrung gyis/ klu mes sku btsun

pas mkhan po gyis/ tshong dge blo rno bas ston pa gyis/ 'bring kha bkod mkhas pas gnas gzhi zung gsungs nas byin po yar yong / klu mes kyis gnubs ye shes rgyal mtshan la 'dul
ba nyan cing bsdad do/ /de nas yar yong ba rnams kyis/ ldan klong thang du slebs dus/ lo ston na re/ khyed tsho 'di khar sdod cig ngas dbus gtsang du phyin la bstan pa
dar nus mi nus brtag ste/ nus na bsdad kyi mi nus na nga yang log yong gis gsungs nas/ ldan ma'i tshong pa dang 'grogs te yar byon/ de'i phyi lo klu mes kyis kyang / slob
dpon la zhus nas yar byon pa dang / lo ston gyi khong rnams la bsu ba la byon pas/ thams cad dbus su 'dzoms nas/ yar byon pa dang / bsam yas su mnga' bdag tsha la na yab
sras dang mjal lo/ /sdig rgyal glang dar mas chu mo phag nas bstan pa bsnubs/ khong rang gi lo mang ma thub kyang / de'i smon lam log pa dang / las ngan shugs ches pas/
lo drug cu rtsa brgyad kyi bar la/ bstan pa'i ming med pa'i dus su/ dbus gtsang gnyis gyi mi bcu po bsam yas su slebs/ rgyal pos bkur sti dang bya dga' chen po mdzad/ bstan
pa'i me ro smad nas bslangs te/ nyin mo ltar gsal zhing / dar rgyas che bar mdzad do/ /de nas rgyal pos bka' gnang / khong rnams gros mthun par dbus gtsang gi sa char/
rten lha khang bzhengs pa dang / dge 'dun gyi sde 'dzugs par chad bsdams te/ klu mes kyis/ sngar sor la mo phyag de'u brtsigs/ gzhu kun dga' ra ba dang / tsha mig brtsigs/
'bring ngan lam spyil mo dang / snye thang brag sna brang ra mo che brtsigs/ sngas kyis gzhung nya mo gyur dang / lan pa spyil bu brtsigs/ rakshi'i

'phrang po lha khang dang / sum pas 'gro swa thang dang / rme ru brtsigs/ khong rnams kyi slob ma yang slob dang bcas pa rnams kyis kyang / gtsug lag khang mang du bzhengs
so/ /gtsang du lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug gis rgyan gong brtsigs/rgya shAkya gzhon nu dang / 'gos g.yag srung la sogs pa bu chen nyi shu rtsa bzhi byung / a mes tshong btsun
shes rab seng ges/ rtsig gi yang dben brtsigs/ zhang ston mtshal 'phags la sogs/ slob ma yang mang dag byung bas/ de rnams kyi dge 'dun gyi sde lha khang tshan che ba
bzhengs/ mgo g.yag gi slob ma/ lce btsun sher 'byung gis zha lu 'a mo bzhengs/ de ltar khams su dbus gtsang gi mi bcus phyin kyang / sum pa dang 'o rgyang spun la mched
pa med cing / 'a 'bring gnyis de rnams la ma gtogs zer ro/ /a mes bla ma chen mo dang / mnga' bdag tsha la na yab sras/ dbus gtsang gi mi bcu po dang bcas pa de rnams/ bod
kha ba can pa la shin tu nas kyang sku drin che'o/ /der rting bod rgyal 'od srung rgyud/ lha bla ma ye shes khu dbon rnams kyis rje btsun gha ya dha ra dang / jo bo rje
dpal ldan a ti sha pha dam pa/ paN chen shAkya shri la sogs/ rgya bal gyi lo paN mang po gdan drangs pa dang / bod yul du 'khrungs pa'i bla ma sa skya khu dbon/ lo chen
rin bzang / /khu rngog 'brom gsum/ dwags po dang shangs pa bka' rgyud pa la sogs/ lo paN mkhas grub bzang la mang ba/ rim par byon pa rnams bshad nyan sgom sgrub kyis bya
ba rgya chen po mdzad pas/ bstan pa rin po che gangs la nyi ma shar ba lta bu gsal zhing dwangsdngas par bzhugs pa lags so/ /bstan pa phyi dar dar tshul 'di bris pas/ /bstan
pa'i chu rgyun rgyun ring gnas pa dang / /bstan 'dzin skyes mchog mchog tu yar 'phel nas/ / bstan zhugs 'gro kun kun mkhyen thob par shog/ //

jo bo rje'i slob rgyud dang / bka' gdams pa'i byon tshul bzhugs so/ / na mo ratna gu ru bhyaH gangs chen ljongs 'dir thub bstan gsal ba dang / /snyigs dus 'gro rnams smin grol
'god pa'i phyir/ /jo bo yab sras bka' gdams rgyud pa rnams/ /byon pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar 'di ltar snang/ /bod du bka' gdams pa'i rgyud pa byung tshul ni/ dang po rgya
gar gyi mkhan po zhi ba 'tsho bzang po'i gdung rus las chad pa/ jo bo di paM ka ra shrI dznyA na zhes pa de'i yab ni/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi za hor rgyal po dge ba'i
dpal gyis sras gsum gyi 'bring po mtshan zla ba'i snying po/ gzhon nu nas dge 'dun phal chen sde pa la rab tu byung nas/ bi kra ma la shI la'i gnas brtan mdzad pa/ jo bo
rje dpal ldan a ti sha zhes pa mtshan yongs su grags pa des rgya gar du 'gro don rgya chen po mdzad cing / chu pho rta lo la dgung la drug cu re gnyis bzhes pa/ bod la
byon nas bal por lo gcig mnga' ris stod du lo gnyis/ gtsang du lo gcig dbus su lo bdun zla ba lnga'i bar la bzhugs/ bstan pa nyin mo ltar cher gsal bar mdzad nas/ don gsum
pa shing pho rta lo dbyug pa zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad la/ snye thang 'or nas dga' ldan du sku gshegs so/ /de nyid la rgya bod na slob ma mang du yod cing / bod du thugs
sras kyi mchog khu rngog 'brom gsum/

de'i nang nas kyang bka' gdams pa'i mes po/ 'brom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas de/ stod lung snam kyi bye ma lung pa/ rten dge bsnyen yin/ jo bo rje dang mnga' ris su mjal/
rwa sgreng dgon pa btab/ de'i sras thu bo mched gsum ni / phu chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan dang / pu to rin chen gsal/ spyan mnga' ba rin chen 'bar te/ khams pa lung pa
dang / bzhir yang grags so/ /pu to ba'i sras kyi mthu bo bu chen bzhir grags pa'i nang nas/ dbur stod kyi zhang sha ra ba yon tan rgya mtsho/ de'i sras bka' babs bzhir grags
pa'i nang nas/ byang sems kyi bka' babs/ bya 'chad ka ba/ de'i slob ma se spyil bu pa/ des spyil bu btab/ de na slob rgyud rim pa bzhin/ lha rin po che 'gro ba'i mgon
po/ lha lung gi dbang phyug lha zur khang pa/ rnal 'byor byang seng / des gro sa dgon pa btab/ de'i slob ma sangs rgyas dar des mkha' ru dgon pa btab/ pu to ba'i slob ma
gtum ston blo gros grags kyis/ snar thang btab ste/ chos lung sku gshegs su grags so/ /de'i gdan sa sding dkar sku gshegs/ shes rab grags kyis snar thang zhes pa'i ming
btags/ de nas zhang btsun rdo rje 'od/ de gsum ga'i slob ma gro bdud rtsi grags/ de la bla ma yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs shing / sangs rgyas stong gi ya gyal du grags/
de nas zhang ston chos kyi bla ma/ sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ de'i ring la dha na shI la'i slob ma/ skyi nag grags seng gis mtshan nyid kyi grwa sa btsugs/ bcom
ldan ral gri la sogs byung / byang chen btab/ de nas mchims nam mkha' grags/ chos rgyal 'phags pa'i bla ma dang / chu mig chos 'khor chen mo'i tshogs dpon mdzad/ lha

khang rnying ma bzhengs/ de nas skyo ston smon lam tshul khrims/ des gtsug lag khang chen mo dang / lcags ri bzhengs/ de nas chos rje nyi ma rgyal mtshan pas/ tshul khrims
stag brgyad bskos/ chos khrims dag ther cher mdzad/ der rting 'dul 'dzin grags brtson ze'u bas/ se chen dang ol ja du rgyal po'i dus/ bstan pa dang gdan sa la phan thogs/
der rting grags che ba/ mchims blo bzang grags pa/ 'dis sha khrims dang / khams pa mi bsten pa'i khrims mdzad de/ de la sogs pa gzhung 'chad nyan mdzad pa rnams/ pu to ba'i
rgyud sde bka' gdams gzhung par grags so/ /	pu to ba'i bu chen spyan lnga tshul khrims 'bar gyis/ lo pa'i gnas brtan bgres po zhig 'dug pa la/ brid skol byas/ tshogs
pa nam tshogs dus bsngo ba ster ba'i dam bcas nas/ lo dgon pa btab/ de slob ma stod lung pa rin chen snying gis/ btsan gro dgon pa btab nas/ de'i dbon po gzhon nu 'od kyis/
bya yul btab/ de la slob ma chen po bcu bzhir grags pa'i nang nas/ mal gro sprul pa chen po'i rgyal po stengs btab/ khrom zher ba chen pos kam kam btab/ dum bu ri ba chen
pos/ dum ri btab sgyer sgom chen pos/ /rgya ma'i mchod khang rnying ma dang / rin chen sgang btab bo/ /bya yul du der rting mkhan rab bcu gcig song ba'i rjes la/ spyan
mnga' tshul khrims mgon po bya ba'i/ gdan sa 'di pa chos gang bzang re ma gtogs/ dbon rgyud kyis 'dzin pa'i srol med do/ /rgya ma sgyer sgom chen po'i rjes la/ sa skya
dbon gyi lha khang gsar ma btab/ de nas dbon rgyud rim pa bzhin gyi/ drug pa slob dpon bkra shis rgyal mtshan 'dis gdan sa/ sgyer gyi gdung rgyud kyi gdan sa 'dzin pa'i srol
yin no/ /yang

jo bo rje'i slob ma'i bla mchod bzhir grags pa slob rgyud/ /kha rag sne zur ba/ gtsang na grags po lung / spyi bo lhas pa la sogs/ gdams ngag gtso bor ston pas/ bka' gdams
gdams ngag par grags so/ /yang chos rje pa'i slob ma lo tsA ba/ de'i slob ma rong pa phyag sor ba'i dgon pa bcom chung bya ba/ rwa sgreng gi 'og na yod pa'i/ bka' gdams 'og
mar grags/ de dang rwa sgreng gnyis la bka' gdams gong 'og zer ro/ /rong pa'i bu bzhir grags pa'i/ rnam par ba chen pos rnam thar dang / ram pa lha sdings btab/ gsang
phu ne'u thog gi gdan sa'ang lo bdun mdzad/ de dag ni rong pa'i bka' brgyud dar lags so/ /bka' gdams rgyud 'di bris pas rgyal ba'i bka'/ /bka' bsdu gsum nas ma 'chugs rgyud
pa'i bka'/ /bka' yis zab don gdams pa bstan pa yis/ /rgyun mi 'chad cing 'gro kun smin grol shog/ /dge legs 'phel bar shog/ //

rngog lo khu dbon gyi slob rgyud dang / bshad grwa dar tshul bzhugs so/ / na mo manydzu gho sha ya/ kha ba can ljong dbus gtsang gangs ri'i rtser/ /bshes gnyen bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan legs 'dzin pa/ /mtshan nyid ldan pa'i lo chen khu dbon gyis/ /mtshan nyid sde btsugs bstan pa 'di ltar spel/ /de'ang ston pa sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas/
lo sum stong nyis brgya dang brgyad 'das nas/ bod yul kha ba can gyi ljongs yar 'brog tsho dang nye ba'i phyogs su/ gsang sngags rnying ma'i dge bshes rdo rje gzhon nu
zhes pa'i sras lnga'i che shos rngog legs pa'i shes rab kyis/ jo bo rje la sogs pa'i mkhas grub du ma bsten cing / gsang phu ne'u thog gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs te/ bstan
pa'i bya ba rgya che bar mdzad/ de'i gcung tha lhag chos bkras/ chos skyabs kyis dpal mo bya ba khab tu bzhes pa la sras sems dpa' chen po blo ldan shes rab lcags mo phag
lo la sku 'khrungs te/ de nyid gzhon nu nas/ lo bcu bdun gyi bar la khu bo dang / rno tshul khrims shes rab la sogs pa'i drung du/ klog yig skad rigs bstan bcos phal che
ba la legs par sbyangs/ zhabs tog gi mnyes par mdzad/ de nas khu dbon pas kyang / bstan pa'i khur khur cing byin gyisabarlabs nas/ bal po dang rgya gar dbus phyogs kha
che la sogs par byon/ paNDi ta pra dznyA na dang / 'bum phrag gsum pa la sogs/ mkhas grub mang du bsten/

lo bcu bdun gyi bar du/ rgya gar dang / bal por bka' mdo rgyud man ngag bstan bcos lung dang rigs par sbyangs zhing / mnga' brnyes par mdzad/ mthar bod du byon/ de dag thams
cad ma lus par bsgyur/ bstan pa nyi ma shar ba ltar du gsal bar mdzad/ dbus gtsang / lho bal/ mdo stod smad/ shar tsong kha/ rgya mi nyag la sogs su grub mtha' 'dzin pa'i
slob ma/ ring slob tu ma gyur pa med cing / dbus gtsang du lo bcu bdun gyi bar du 'gro don mdzad do//de'i thugs kyi sras/ zhang tshe spong chos kyi bla ma la sogs thu
bo bzhir grags pa dang / gzhan yang gangs pa shi'u la sogs/ bu slob bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin par mdzad pa'i nang nas/ zhang tshe spong chos kyi bla mas/ ne'u thog gi gdan
sa lo sum cu so gnyis mdzad/ de'i rjes su gnyal pa ril lus la gnyis mdzad/ rnam par bas lo brgyad mdzad do/ /bla ma de gsum gyi slob ma/ phywa pa chos kyi seng ges gdan
sa lo bco brgyad kyi bar la mdzad do/ /'dzam bu gling thams cad snyan grags dang bu slob kyi khyab par mdzad/ de'i sras kyi gtso bo gtsang nag pa brtson 'grus seng ge la
sogs seng chen brgyad dang / jo sras rtse mo la sogs/ jo sras bzhi dang / gzhan yang 'jad pa ston skyabs/ khams pa rdor rgyal la sogs dbus gtsang khams gsum lho gnyal gyi
slob ma dpag tu med pa smin par mdzad de/ bstan pa che cher 'phel bar mdzad do/ /de'i thugs sras brgyad po'i nang nas/ brtsegs dbang phyug seng ges gdan sa lo lnga/ de
gnyis kyi slob ma/ gnyal pa dad pa bzang pos lo bdun/ 'dzam tsan nes lo bdun/ bzad pa dar ma 'od dang / bzad pa don grub gnyis kyis lo sum cu mdzad do/ /

yang 'bre shes rab 'bar gyis myang stod skyegs gnas rnying du chos bshad/ las stod pa dkon mchog mkhar gyis gdan sa mdzad/ ding sang gi bar du de'i mi rgyud kyis 'dzin no/
/gtsang pa 'bre sgur gyis dga' ba gdong dang / khu sher brtson gyis thang po cher chos bshad grwa pa khri lhag 'dus/ ar byang yes/ gnam rtse lding sogs dang / dkar chung
ring mo/ zhang e pa gnyis kyis/ 'u shang rdo la sogs su/ mdo smad tsho bzhir grags pa la chos gsungs/ mkhas pa bsod rin dang / gnyal zhig la sogs pa/ dpag tu med pa smin
par mdzad/ gral stan za 'og la byed pa dang / dus chos re la ja sig chen lnga bcu tsam re skol ba la sogs pa/ longs spyod kyang de dus kho na che bar grags/ der rting mkhan
po bsod rin gyi gdan sa byas/ chos blo bshad byed pa de nas byung / der rting 'gral sher rgyal gyis gdan sa mdzad/ gnyal zhig gi slob ma bu dgur grags pa'i nang nas gtsang
drug gis zha lu'i gdan sa dang / bo dong rin po ches/ grags ram gyi bshad grwa btsugs/ 'gral gyi lo bco lnga gdan sa mdzad pa'i rjes la/ rog gis zla ba drug mdzad do/
/de nas slob dpon shAkya gzhon nu dang / tshad ma'i skyes bu mang po smin par mdzad/ slob dpon shAkya gzhon gyis/ tshal gung thang du bshad grwa btsugs/ ne' thog gi gdan
sa lo nyi shu rtsa bdun mdzad cing / blo gros mtshungs med dang / phyogs las rnam rgyal sogs du ma smin par mdzad do/ /de rjes rgya ma pas lo brgyad gdan sa mdzad/ der
rting phyogs las rnam rgyal pas lo brgyad mdzad do/ /yar 'brog pa mkhan po rgyal gyis zla ba gcig slob dpon gzhon seng gis lo brgyad/ gtsang dkar gyis lo

gsum/ slob dpon blo gros seng ges lo lnga'i bar du/ gsang bu gling smad kyi gdan sa mdzad do/ /gsang phu ne'u thog gi gdan sa 'jam can nas mdzad pa'i dus/ gtsang pa 'jam seng
gis bshad pa mdzad pas/ gling stod pa gyes ste/ dbon po jo yun zhes pas/ bdag rkyen byas nas/ 'jam ston/ zhus ston/ blo gros 'bar gsum gyis rim par bshad/ de'i dus su
gnyal zhig gis lo brgyad/ de nas rgyal ba lo ston gyis byas/ khong bros nas/ rgya 'ching ru bas mdzad/ de'i rjes khong gi slob ma/ chu mig pa seng ge dpal gyis/ lo bco brgyad
mdzad cing / ldan ma grags rin dang / la stod pa grags rgyal la sogs/ slob ma mkhas pa mang du byon/ ldan ma grags rin gyis gdan sa lo brgyad mdzad/ de nas lho brag
pas sngon rting dril bas lo nyer gnyis mdzad cing / thog ston dang / myang stod pa ye shes mgon la sogs mang du smin par mdzad/ myang stod pas lo bdun bla chos bshad/ yang
lho brag pa rang gi mdzad/ de'i rting btsan dgon pa gzhon nu bsam gtan gyis/ lo nyi shu'i bar la gdan sa mdzad/ chos grags gsar ma dang / bla brang dbon po la sogs slob
ma mang du byung / der rjes bla brang pa dang / chos grags gsar ma/ ya rtse ba/ lha yul ba/ rin chen grags pa/ yon tan rgya mtsho rnams kyis rim pa bzhin byas/ yang rgya
'ching gi dus su/ bde ba can du gnyags grags tshul gyis bshad cing / rgya ston bsod rin la sogs slob ma mang du byung / de'i rting rgya ston bsod rin gyis bshad/ dge brag
pa la sogs pa'i slob ma mang du byung / de rjes su dge grags pas byas/ de'i rjes la snye thang ba bkra shis seng ges gling stod gdan sa

byas pa'o/ /spre'u'i lo slob dpon shAkya gzhon nu dang / slob dpon don grub dpal/ dpon slob kyi gung thang gi bshad grwa btsugs nas/ lo drug na slob dpon shAg gzhon ne'u thog
tu byon/ gung thang du slob dpon don grub dpal gyis/ stag lo nas rta lo'i bar lo zhe gcig gi ring la/ bstan pa'i bya ba mdzad/ kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan dang /
mkhas btsun blo gros bzang po/ skyes mchog bsod dpal la sogs/ slob ma mkhas grub bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin par mdzad/ de'i rting kun mkhyen sher rgyal ba rta lo la/ rgyal
tshab tu dbang skur te/ des lo bcu bzhi gdan sa mdzad/ yos lo nas mkhas btsun jo bzang pas/ lo bcu gcig mdzad/ de'i rjes su skyes mchog bsod dpal ba bskos so/ /yang bzad
ring gis khro phur bshad grwa btsugs nas/ stag ston spyil bu la sogs slob ma mang du byon/ ldong gis gdan sa byas/ de'i rting slob ma lho pa grub seng gi byas/ rong pa
dang rigs thigs pa la sogs/ slob ma mang du byon/ rigs thigs pa'i slob ma zha lu bu ston las phyi ba yin no/ /yang skyel nag grags seng gis snar thang du bshad grwa la tshad
ma bshad pas/ skyi ston grags 'bum/ de nas slob rgyud rim pa bzhin/ bcom ldan ral gri/ mkhan po zi dbon/ gra ring gra thung / rtsed ring rtsed thung la sogs mkhas pa
mang du byon/ de'i rting dpon po rin chen 'byung gis bshad/ de'i slob ma ldong ston yin no/ /bshad brgyud rim pa rim par byon tshul 'di/ /'di phyi gnyis phan phan bde 'byung
phyir bris/ /bris pa'i nus mthu mthu chen bstan pa'i rgyun/ /rgyun chags ring du ring du gnas par shog /dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig/ / /

smad 'dul gyi bshad rgyud bzhugs so/ /na mo gu ru bhya/ smad 'dul du grags pa'i bshad rgyud ni/ ston pa sangs rgyas te/ nye bar 'khor/ kun dga' bo dang / sha na'i gos can/
nyer sbas dhi dhi ka nag po legs mthong / blo gros mi 'bebs/ yon tan 'od/ shAkya 'od/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ che chung gnyis/ de gnyis kas seng ge gdong can/ des dha na shI
la dang / dzI na mi tra/ des lcog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan/ des g.yo dge 'byung dang / gtsang rab gsal/ dmar shAkya mu ne gsum la bshad/ de gsum mdo smad du byon nas/ a mes
bla chen dgong pa rab gsal la bshad/ des slob ma la snga ba khams kyi zog po mi drug bya ba byung te/ spang gong ye shes g.yung drung / par rin chen gsal/ 'al rdo rje dbang
phyug snubs rakshi ta/ jo bo ye shes seng ge lcog ro shes rab byang chub rnams yin pa/ dang po mkhan slob cha ma tshang bas/ bsnyen rdzogs ma grub/ dge tshul yin/ 'dul
ba la sogs chos rnams ni gnang / bla chen gyi bon po'i thugs zhen du byas nas/ zhwa theb kyi mu thugs sngon por byed pa sogs kyi/ bka' rtags kyi phyag rgya bzhi bya ba
yang khong drug po la gnang bar byed do/ /spang par gnyis kyi slob ma/ grum ye shes rgyal mtshan/ des grum g.yung drung rgyal mtshan shing lag can la/ des dbus gtsang gi
mi bcu'i nang nas/ klu mes tshul khrims shes rab la 'dul ba bshad/ des

gzus rdo rje rgyal mtshan la/ de nas rim pa bzhin du/ snel bo grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rgya dbang rdor/ bya brtson 'grus 'bar/ rtsis pa gzhon seng / snyer chung bzang ston/ de
la shAkya'i dge slong thub pa shes rab bdag gi 'dul ba'i chos skor rnams tshang mar zhus pa legs so/ /yang grum shing lag can gyis/ lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug dang / tshong
btsun shes rab seng ge sum pa ye shes blo gros/ a btsun shAkya rgyal mtshan/ 'bre ston tshul khrims gzhon nu rnams la/ 'dul ba bshad nas dbus gtsang du dar bar mdzad
pa rnams la'ang / smad 'dul zer cing / bshad rgyud rang rang na gsal lo/ /smad 'dul bshad rgyud 'di bris dge ba yis/ /'dul khrims gtsang zhing 'chad nyan dar bar shog /dge
legs 'phel bar gyur cig/ //

bod du bla chen mkhan rgyud dang / spu tsho mkhan rgyud/ paN chen mkhan rgyud rnams kyi byon tshul bzhugs so/ /na mo buddha ya/ thub bstan gangs ri'i khrod du gsal mdzad pa'i/
/smad 'dul byung khung mkhan rgyud rim pa ni/ /kun mkhyen rgyal po thugs sras sha ri'i bu/ /sras mchog sgra gcan bram ze sgra gcan 'dzin/ /klu sgrub skyes mchog legs
ldan dpal sbas dang / /ye shes snying po zhi ba 'tsho la 'dud/ /sbas ston ratna gtsang ston rab gsal dang / /bla chen dgongs gsal shes rab seng ge dang / /byang chub gzhon
nu byang chub rgyal mtshan te/ 'jad pa ston skyabs byang ston gzhon nu zhabs/ /rtsis 'dul chen po mkhan po bde ba dpal/ /byang sems rin mgon thogs med bzang po dpal/ /yon
tan 'od sogs bla chen mkhan rgyud kyi/ /sdom brtson dam pa rnams la gus pas 'dud/ /bla chen mkhan rgyud ni/ rgyal sras thogs med pa nas rgyud pa 'di dag par byed par yod
do/ / na mo dharma ya/ thub bstan gsal zhing stod 'dul rgyas mdzad pa'i/ /spu tsho mkhan rgyud byon pa'i rim pa ni/ thub dbang sha ra'i bu dang sgra gcan 'dzin/ /legs
'dom nag po pa dang dha ri ka/ grags mchog legs skyong rgyal ba shes rab ste/ /mu gro 'dul 'dzin chen po'i zhabs la 'dud/ /byang sems zla rgyal

dharma rgyal mtshan dang / /mnga' ris dgra bcom mkhan chen dbang phyug mdzes/ /mdzes pa 'od zer mdzes pa bzang po dang / /seng dpal kun mkhyen mdzes pa'i zhabs la 'dud/ /nam
mkha' dpal bzang tshul khrims rgyal mtshan dang / /shAkya rgyal mtshan spu tsho mkhan rgyud kyi/ /bslab gsum rgyan ldan rnams la gus pas 'dud/ /spu tsho mkhan rgyud stod
'dul gyi byung khungs 'di/ gtsang g.yas ru 'u yug zam tshe ba la rgyud pa 'di dag par byed do// //

tshogs pa sde bzhir gyes tshul bzhugs so/ /na mo sangga ya/ thub bstan rtsod ldan dus 'dir gsal mdzad pa'i/ /paN chen mkhan rgyud tshogs pa sde bzhi'i khungs/ /ston pa sangs
rgyas dngos slob shA ri'i bu/ /sgra gcan 'dzin gnyis klu sgrub ghu ma ti/ /ratna mi tra dharma pha la dang / /ghu na pa ti chos 'phreng 'byung gnas sbas/ /des slob paN
chen shAkya shri zhes pa/ /ston pa sku 'das sum stong nyi brgya dang / /lnga bcu rtsa brgyad chu pho stag la bltams/ /brgyad cu lnga bzhes me stag dbus su phebs/ /lo grangs
bcu gnyis bod du 'gro don mdzad/ /dgu bcu bdun la rgya gar yul la byon/ /go dgu lcags pho 'brug la mya ngan 'das/ /paN chen thegs nas lo dgur tsam song bas/ /gdan gcig
srol bskyangs de rting rdo rje dpal/ /sangs rgyas dpal nas gzhung pa dpon rgyal gyes/ /bye rdzing par grags de nas thugs rje dpal/ /dar ma dpal bzang gzhon nu bzang tshul
dpal/ /sangs gzhon dar bzang tshul khrims mgon po pa/ /bsod 'od rin tshul bsod shes shes rab mgon/ /grags bsod sher 'phags sher tshul rin shes pa/ /chos dpal sher 'od kun
dga' shes rab yun/ /rdor dpal man la mkhan rab nyer gnyis byon/ /paN chen me stag phebs nas ding sang gis/ /shing stag brgyad dkar dbus gnas yar chod la/ /lo grangs nyis
brgya bzhi bcu rtsa bdun song / /tshal mig pa la

mkhan po sangs rgyas dpal/ /'od dpal chos kyi rgyal mtshan sangs rin pa/ /'od dpal sher mgon seng rgyal bsod dbang dang / /dran tshul tshul rin dpang blo rgyal dbang dang /
/sras seng yon rin byang chub bzang po yan/ /bcu phrag phyed dang gnyis po ding sang dus/ /tshogs chen par grags thub bstan dri med kyis/ /srog 'dzin mkhan rgyud rnams la
phyag 'tshal lo/ /chos lung thog ma lho brag byang chub dpal/ /bsod stobs sde dpal grags gzhon bsod nams grags/ /bsod bzang gzhon mgon mkhan chen grags rgyal dang / /grags
tshul grags pa bshes gnyen rnam rgyal ba/ /'jam dbyangs rin rgyal rgyal mchog grags dbang rgyal/ /zla blo rgyal ba phyag na ding sang yan/ /bcu phrag gcig dang drug cu
byung bar grags/ /slab gsum rnam dag shAkya'i bstan pa yi/ /gsal byed mkhan rgyud rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dge 'dun sgang pa byang chub dpal nas gyes/ /dbang grags gzhon
rgyal 'dul tsha don grub dpal/ /yon tan rgya mtsho dpal grub yon blo ba/ brtson rgyal seng ge dpal dang chos grub yan/ /bcu dang gcig gis 'gro kun smin grol la/ /'god
mdzad mkhan rgyud rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /snyigs ma'i dus 'dir 'gro mang padmo'i gnyen/ /bod yul mun pa sel bar mdzad pa yis/ /paN chen mkhan rgyud rim pa'i 'od zer gyis/
/sangs rgyas bstan pa dar mdzad 'phrin las pa/ kha che paN chen slob rgyud 'di bris pas/ kha ba can 'dir thub bstan seng ge'i sgras/ kha na ma tho chos kun zil mnan
nas/ kha TwaM gyis mtshon sku gsum myur thob shog/// dge legs 'phel// //

dwags po bka' brgyud byon tshul bzhugs/na mo ratna gu ru/ rdo rje 'chang gis byin brlabs pa/ /te lo na ro rgyud 'dzin cing / /gtum mo'i chos la dbang 'byor pa/ /dwags po bka'
rgyud 'di ltar byon/ /thub bstan lnga brgya tha ma'i dus su/ bod gangs can gyi khrod 'dir/ theg chen gsang sngags zab mo/ 'dzin skyong spel bar mdzad pa/ dwags po bka'
rgyud du grags pa 'di ltar byung te/ de'ang rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang chen pos/dngos su byin gyis brlabs pa'i grub thob chen po/ te lo shes rab bzang po de la sangs rgyas
dngos kyi mos gus thob nas/ dus thabs bstan pas sa lam bgrod de/ mchog thun mong gi dngos grub thob pa ni/ jo bo na ro pa ye shes dngos grub te/ dpal nA lendra'i byang sgo
bsrung ba'i/ paNDi ta chen po/ des smin cing grol bar mdzad pa'i dngos slob/ lho bod pa/ sgra bsgyur gyi rgyal po mar pa lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros zhes mtshan yongs su
grags pa de nyid/ dang po mar yul gyi mar she lugs rtse'i sras/ mar pa khri 'jam/ lho phu chu skyer gyi shab steng su byon/ de'i sras gsum gyi 'bring po/ mar ston dbang
phyug de'i sras lnga'i mtha' rtag tu jo mo la sku 'khrungs/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes dang / se lo tsA ba la lo tsA bslabs/ rgya gar du lan gsum byon/ rje 'gran gyi do med
rnams gnyis dang / khyad par grub thob zhal mnga' chos kyi 'brel ba'i/ bla ma bcu gsum

rnams bsten cing / de rnams kyi dbang bskur byin gyis brlabs pas bka' bstan bcos lung man ngag du ma thob/ yi dam gyis zhal gzigs/ chos kyi mnga' bdag chen por gyur te/ mthar
'pho ba grongs 'jug ga gdams pa zhu ru byon dus/ bla ma na ro pa chen pos/ bu khyod la bod na gdul bya snod ldan yod cing / rigs rgyud nam mkha'i me tog ltar yal kyang
/ chos rgyud chu bo'i rgyun ltar ring / lo tsA ba 'di'i 'og rol tu/ mchog gi dngos grub thob par 'gyur zhing / khyod kyi slob rgyud bdun yan yan la/ bla mas byin gyis brlabs
de'ang mchog gi dngos grub ster ces lung bstan/ rgyal tshab tu bskos nas bod du phebs/sgrub rgyud kyi bstan pa nam lang la nyi ma shar ba ltar du mdzad 'dug lho brag
tu sku mkhar skya bo dgu theg brtsigs nas 'gro don bskyangs/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa brgyad pa la/ mkha' spyod du gshegs so/ /des sku sras bdun gyi che ba| dar ma mdo sde
'bum sku yon tan phun sum tshogs na'ang / bar chad byung nas gzhon nu la sku gshegs/ phug ron gyi ro la 'pho ba grongs 'jug mdzad/ rgya gar la 'phur nas dur khrod du bram
ze gzhon nu la 'phos te/ de ti phu par gyur pa yin zer/ gcung dar ma bsam gtan la sogs drug byung / thugs kyi sras ni byang gi mar pa mgo legs pa dang / sgyer bu'i dge
bshes klog skya jo sras la sogs pa dang / khyad par ka chen bzhir grags pa/ gzhung gi rngog ston chos rdor/ dol gyi tshul ston dbang nge / gtsang rong gi mes ston tshon
po/ gung thang gi mi la ras pa rnams yin/ sngon ma gsum gyi ni bshad rgyud gtso che/ phyi ma gcig bu sgrub rgyud gtso che'o/ /gzhan yang gnyal gyi shud bu sgom dpal/ skyi
ston skyar rgyal/ ba

rang sba ba can la sogs slob ma mkhas grub bzang la mang ba byon no/ /gzhung gi rngog ston chos rdor ni/ gdung rus ldong gi sde tshan rngog bod rgyud pa'i slob brgyud/ rngog
ban chen bya ba/ sngags rnying ma'i dge bshes chen po zhig gis ltas dang / gzhung gi ri bor 'khrungs/ rang gi yab dang / rje mar pa la dbang bshad sgrub mtha' dag thos/
rje mar pa la 'bul mo che lan gsum bgyis pa la sogs kyi zhabs tog che bar byas shing / thugs rab kyi bla ma'i thugs zin par byed/ gzhan yang / rwa rdo rje grags la sogs
mkhas grub du ma bsten/ raM rtsa can dang / can drug gi mi la mthu chen la sogs pa'i slob ma mang du bskyangs/ bshad sgrub mthar phyin nas/ dgung lo drug cu rtsa brgyad la/
gdan sa thel nas sku dngos su mkha' spyod du gshegs so/ /de'i sras rngog mdo sde las stod pa spug ston ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis skye ba yin/ chung ba'i dus rje mar pa
dang mjal/ chag lo sogs lo tsA ba brgyad bsten/ thos bsam mthar phyin/ yab kyi gdan sa mdzad/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i zhal gzigs/ nya mo gur du rje mar pa'i sras mo zhig
la/ gral dpon zhus nas brgya 'bul byas/ mchims chen po dge bshes chen po phywa pa dang / mkhan po bsod nams rtse mo la sogs/ dbus gtsang gi dge bshes lnga brgya bos/
des zla ba phyed gnyis chos 'khor mdzad/ de'i bzang lan la/ sras mo des mar pa'i sku gdung phul/ ldum chung btab/ chos gzhis mang du btsugs/ dgung lo bdun cu rtsa bdun la
gshegs so/ /de'i slob ma brtsegs dharma rwa dza gra ston/ 'thab bral lho nag la sogs mang du byon/ bla ma'i sras/ jo sras tshul khrims shes rab/ thogs med grags pa la

sogs/ mched lnga byung ba thams cad yon tan dang ldan yang / yab bzhugs ring la/ snga rim gyi 'das so/ /thogs med grags pa'i sras rgyal sa ra mo dang / rdor seng ra mo/ ston
chung dbang mo'i skye ba yin/ gdan sa lo bdun bskyangs/ mar pa yab sras kyi sku gdung bzhengs/ rab gnas zhang rin po che la zhus/ gcen jo tshul gyi sras bla ma kun dga'
rdo rje'o/ /des dpal zhang gi gzims khang lho ma btab/ gdan sa mdzad/ lo bdun cu rtsa bdun la 'das so/ /de'i sras slob dpon dge slong dang / bla ma gzi brjid/ slob dpon
rgyal po dga'/ bla ma gzi brjid kyis gzims khang byang ma btab/ gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ gdung khang yang der spyan drangs/ gdan sa mdzad/ lo brgyad cu la gshegs/ slob dpon
rgyal po dga'i sras seng ge sgra/ ri bong pa rin chen bzang po/ slob dpon chos rdor 'od/ ri bong pa'i dgung lo bcu pa la/ bshad pa mdzad/ bco brgyad la zul phur dge tshul
dang / de nas la gsum la bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ nyi shu rtsa bdun pa'i dus khu bo 'das nas gdan sa mdzad/ bco lnga pa la khams su byon nas/ lo gnyis la 'khor nas tshal
pa'i yang dgon du sgom sde dang / dpon rgyud kyi bla mar skur/ gser gyi bka' 'gyur bzhengs/ lha khang dang rgyal sa rgya chen bskyed/ spel zhing dang / zul skyor gyi thog
drangs/ dbus gtsang gi dgon sde 'brel yod kun la/ tshogs gsog rgya chen mdzad/ jo bo nA ro pa dang /mar pa'i sprul par grags/ 'gro don dpag med mdzad nas/ bdun cu rtsa bdun
pa la gshegs so/ /slob dpon seng ge sgra'i sras/ slob dpon rin rgyal spun gsum mo/ /slob dpon chos sbyor gyi sras gsum gyi che shos/ bla ma chos kyi

rgyal mtshan gyi gdan sa mdzad do/ /rgyal tsha ra mo'i rgyud/ ltums chung pa rnams sa so/ /'di'i mtshams su dol gyi tshur ston dbang nge de'i rnam thar bri'o/ /'di chad/ gtsang
rong gi mes ston tshon po ni/ gtsang myang stod stag tshal du 'khrungs/ mtshan bsod nams rgyal mtshan rje mar pa bsten/ zhabs tog gis thugs zin/ rong po do'i gnas bzhengs/
gdung rgyud med/ mar pa dang / mes ston gnyis ka'i slob ma/ zhang bsod nams mkhar/ de nas sras rgyud lnga song ba'i/ zhang ston grags 'byor te/ chos lugs rgyud pa'o/
/gung thang gi mi la ras pa ni/ sngon nA ro pas mar pa la lung bstan pa'i/ bod na gdul bya snod ldan yod gsungs pa de yin cing / mar pa'i bu chen gyi mchog gam/ de'i gdung
rus ni/ khyung po/ yab mi la sher rgyal dang / yum myang bza' dkar rgyan gyi sras su/ la stod gung thang smad kyi/ skya rnga rtsa'i ko ron du 'khrungs/ mtshan thos pa
dga'/ pha tshan gyis yul du sdod du ma ster ba/ rong du lha rje snubs chung dang / dbus su gnyags g.yung ston khro rgyal gyi sar byon/ dgra thams cad tshar bcad/ rong ston
lha dga' la/ rdzogs chen zhus de'i sar/ rje mar pa'i snyan grags gsan nas/ lho brag tu byon/ bla ma dang mjal/ khong gi dgra mar pa nag po btul/ sngar kyi sdig sbyongs
la/ bla mas sras mkhar dgu thog la 'gyel gyin brtsig bcug pas/ sgal rma drug byung na'ang / rgal tshigs bcos gin brtsigs pas/ lo re la thog re zin/ gdam ngag re gnang /
dbang re bskur/ thog lnga pa la rgyud gsungs/ drug pa la yi dam lha'i zhal gzigs/ skabs der rngog ston chos rdor gyi phyag phyir byon/ mi la phug tu sgrub pa mdzad/ khong
gi dgra dol yab pho yas mo ba btul/ mar pa la yum bdag med mas zhu rogs mdzad pa dang /

mos gus la thugs mnyes nas/ chos ma lus par gnang / byin gyis brlabs/ mar pa rgya gar la rting ma byon dus/ mi la sras kyi mthu bor mnga' gsol/ lung bstan nas/ la stod la brdzangs/
'jig rten spangs zhing / la phyi'i gangs kyi dang / rdzongs drug sogs su dka' ba spyad/ sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad/ lo dgu'i bar la nyams rtogs ci yang ma byung
kyang 'bad pas zla ba phyed nas/ nyams rtogs dus gcig la rdol nas/ mchong lung dang / la phyi chu bzang / drin chu bar rnams su/ 'dre dmag theng gsum gyis bar chad brtsams
kyang / rnal 'byor spros bral ro gcig rim par rdzogs/ bar chad re sel ba dang / bogs re thon/ tshe ring ma spun lnga dam la btags/ dogs med kyi rnal 'byor la mngon du
phyogs zhing / rdzu 'phrul du mas gdul bya mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad btul/ rgya gar ngharma pha la dang / dam pa sangs rgyas la sogs dang rdzu 'phrul 'gran/ bod du byon
pa'i grub thob la grub rtags bzang zhing ngo mtshar che bar grags so/ /dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa bzhi pa la/ mya ngan las 'das so/ /de la bu chen dpag tu med pa yod pa'i
nang nas/ sras kyi mthu bo brgyad ni/ gung thang gi gnyan chung ras pa/ lcim lung gi ngan rdzong ras pa/ nya ma'i 'bri sgom ras pa/ mdo sgra'i se ban ras pa/ snyi shang
gi khyi ra ras pa/ ras pa zhi ba 'od/ sde ba skyong / mnyam med dwags po lha rje rnams so/ /dang por che ba'i sras bzhi/ bar du nye ba'i sras brgyad/ tha mar sku bgres khar
'khrungs pa'i jo bo bka' gdams pa gsum yod ces grags so/ /gnyan chung ras pa ni/ mtshan rdo rje grags/ thog mar mi la dang mjal/ thugs zin rgya gar la lan lnga byon/
wa la tsandra/ pham thing pa/ ti phu pa/ ma gcig grub pa'i rgyal mo la sogs pa mang du bsten/

chos skor tshan che ba thob/ phyag rdor sgrub pas mdze thon/ phyis bod du bla ma la zhus nas/ dbus su byon/ bye chung rtsad po'i mdze gsos/ mag pa mdzad/ pho brang skyegs ldan
du/ lha lcam ldem bu'i dam tshig nyams nas bral/ gnyal la sogs par bzhugs/ de la slob ma/ nye gnas rin chen grags/ bur sgom nag po/ sum ston chos dar/ dge bshes khyung
tshang ba la sogs pa mang du byon/ sngon mtsho lnga bre chung du/ rje mi la dang mjal ba'i bu mo dbul mo de/ ras chung ba la gtad nas bsgoms pas/ se mo dor lus ma spangs
pa la/ mkha' spyod du gshegs pa'i grub thob ma zhig kyang byung ngo / /ras chung ba dgung lo gya gnyis pa la gshegs so/ /ras pa zhi ba 'od ni/ brag skye chur sgrub pa rtse
gcig tu mdzad pas/ brag phug spyi bu brtol nas mkha' spyod la gshegs so/ /'bri sgom ras pa ni/ gang pa she'u dang / rngog lo/ lcal lo la sogs bla ma mang du bsten/ rje
mi la rtsa ba'i bla mar gyur nas/ mi lo sum cur sgrub pa mdzad/ yi dam zhal gzigs dngos grub brnyes/ mal yer pa la sogs slob ma mang du byon gda'/ mnyam med dwags po lha
rje ni/ mdo ting nge 'dzin rgyal po dang / snying rje pad dkar du/ sangs rgyas kyis 'di dge slong 'tsho byed du gyur nas/ bstan pa 'dzin pa la bkod cing / mthar rgyal ba
dri ma med pa ces su sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' zla 'od gzhon nur gyur pa yin la/ de dang lhan gcig tu bstan pa 'dzin par khas blangs pas/
byang chub sems pa stong lnga brgya yang / 'dis 'khor da nga rgyud pa 'dzin pa rnams yin par/ mdo sde nyid las gsal bas/ rnam thar bsam gyis mi khyab mod kyi/ gdul bya'i
snang ngor yang / rje mi la'i thugs sras kun gyi mchog tu mar pa dang / mi la gnyis

ka'i lung bstan pa yin no/ /'khrungs yul ni gnyal rus snyi ba/ yab nyi ma lha rje'i/ sras gsum gyi bar pa/ mtshan snying po kun dga'/ lha rje mdzad cing / dgung lo bcu gnyis
pa la/ dge bshes sha ba gling pa la rab tu byung / bsod nams rin chen du mtshan gsol/ mkhan po dang bya 'dul ba la 'dul ba lung skor zhus/ mar yul bsam gtan la gsang sngags
gsan/ dbu ru byang du dge bshes snyug rum pa/ lcags ri gong kha ba byang chub dpal/ dge bshes bya yul ba rnams la/ bka' gdams zhus/ zhag bcu gsum tsam mi 'chor ba'i
gnas pa bzang po byung / rtogs pa gong du 'phel/ sa bcu non pa'i rmi ltas byung / yab mes kyis brtsigs pa'i gser chung lha khang du bzhugs dus/ sprang po gsum las rje mi
la'i snyan pa thos ma thag mos pa skyes/ byin brlabs zhugs pas yid phrogs nas/ la stod la byon pa sprang po zhig la lam sna bcol bas/ tshong dus nas khong 'gro ma nyan par/
khong rang gi byon/ mjal ma thag bla ma mnyes nas sa sna lan gyi mgur gsungs/ sngags kyi nyams zhus pas bzhad nas/ bye ma btsir bas mar khu gang la yong / /yungs dkar
btsir na yong pa yin/ /thabs lam sgoms gsungs nas/ gdams pa rnams rim gyis gnang / bsgoms pas zhag bdun nas/ bde stong rang 'bar la song / rtags snang nyams myong khyad par
can skyes/ ring por ma thogs par sprul sku/ longs sku dang mjal/ chos sku myur du mthong bar lung bstan/ byin gyis brlabs shing rgyal tshab tu dbang bskur nas/ lcags ri
gong khar byon te se ba lung du/ bka' gdams pa'i gseb tu bzhugs pas/ thugs dam cung zhig 'grib/ yar byon/ mi la bsten pas/ dran pa sor chug zer ba yang 'dug 'ol kha nas
sgam po zangs lung du

byon/ sgom pa sor chud/ sgam po mthong ba'i la khar bla ma'i lung bstan bzhin/ chos nyid bden pa dngos su rtogs/ bla ma la sangs rgyas kyi 'du shes skyes/ 'o de gung rgyal
gyi bu/ dwags la sgam pos sbyin bdag byas nas/ sgam po'i ri khrod btab ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs dang / mngon shes rdzu 'phrul du ma thob/ snang sems 'dres shing dbang du
'dus/ nyams rtogs mthar phyin/ dgung lo bdun cu rtsa bdun pa la/ mya ngan las 'das so/ /bla ma des don gnyis kyi gter kha phye bas/ 'gro don dpag med mdzad cing / bu chen
gdugs thogs lnga brgya byung ba'i/ snga tshar la dwags po sgom pa dang / rgyal ba khyung tshang ba la sogs/ bar tshar la grub thob dbu se/ khams pa rdor rgyal/ zhang sum
thog pa la sogs/ phyi tshar la byang gi 'bab rom pa chen po/ shangs pa rmog cog pa la sogs kyi thog drangs pa'i gnam gyi skar ma tsam byon/ bstan pa dar zhing rgyas par
mdzad do/ /dwags po rin po che'i gcung po/ lha rje rdor 'bar gyi sras po dwags po sgom pa ni/thog ma'i mtshan la zla rgyal gling / dgung lo bcu gcig pa la bla ma'i drung
du yong / chos ma lus par thob/ bcu gsum pa la spros bral gyi rtogs pa shar/ bcu drug pa la mkhan po mnga' ris pa sher snying la/ dge tshul zhus/ mtshan tshul khrims snying
por btags/ bco brgyad pa la/ sgom ro gcig tu rtogs/ nyi shu rtsa lnga pa la/ sngags kyi mkhan po dang slob dpon/ shab rtse yon tan blo gros la sogs las/ bsnyen rdzogs
mdzad/ sum cu rtsa lnga nas gdan sa bskyangs pa'i lo gnyis nas bla ma gshegs/ bkra shis sgo mang bzhengs nas/ dbus su byon/ lha sa'i jo bo rin po che'i thugs rje dang /
srung mas bskul nas lha sa'i gso thabs mdzad/ rgya 'bri'i sde 'khrug bsdums/ zhang rin po che la gnas gzhi

bstan nas/ sgam por byon/ mkhyen rtogs dang thugs rje mdzad pa'i rnam thar dpag yas mnga' ba de/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa bzhi pa/ glang lo dbyug pa zla ba'i tshes nyi shu la
mya ngan las 'das so/ /de'i slob ma grub thob dbu se/ zhang rin po che/ zhang ston ka lo ka dung ston la sogs mang du byon/ bde gshegs khams pa rdor rgyal gyi gdung rus
ni/ rme 'dor ba'i nang tshan dbas/ de'i nang tshan dbe na/ yab dbe na a dar gyi sras su/ me pho rta lo la/ mdo khams yor khrims su 'khrungs/ ldong yan byang chub kyi bu/
tshul khrims la rab tu byung / u ring rgyal 'bar la chos gsan/ nyi shu rtsa lnga lon pa la dbus su phebs/ zul phur bya 'dul ba 'dzin pa'i drung du bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ dge
bshes g.yor gnyan/ dbar tsang bu kha pa/ byang sems dpa'i dam pa snyal chung ba/ bla ma 'dzim/ 'khon sa skya pa chen po/ nyang sgo mkhan po/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/
bla ma brag dkar po ba la sogs/ sngags mtshan nyid kyi bka' lung gdams pa rnams zhus/ dgung lo bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis pa/ dge bshes zhang sum thog pa dang 'grogs nas/ sgam
por byon nas/ mnyam med dwags po lha rje dang mjal/ rtogs pa 'khrungs/ lo ngo gsum bsten/ yar byon tsha rang btsan po'i sbyin bdag mdzad nas/ lcags pho khyi lo la/ phag
mo grur 'jag spyil dgon pa btab/ chos khrims bcas/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa lnga nas 'gro don bskyangs/ drug cu re gcig pa me mo phag ston zla tha chung gi nyi shu lnga
la phag mo gru'i mthar tsar mya ngan las 'das so/ /de'i thugs kyi sras yin te/ bsod nams mthar phyin 'bri khung pa/ mos gus mthar phyin stag lung pa/ shes rab mthar phyin
par bu ba/ rtogs pa mthar phyin sna bu ba rnams so/ /nye ba'i sras bzhi ni/

skal ldan ye shes seng ge kun ldan gtsang pa ras chung pa/ rtogs ldan mi nyag sgom rin/ grub thob nyag re se bo'o/ /gzhan yang mkhan po zhang sum thog pa dang / khro phu ba'i
rgyal tsha rin chen/ chos rje ldum/ rlangs seng ge rgyal mtshan/ smon ston chos blo/ seng ge sding pa/ nyan shan grong pa/ zhang shi ri ba/ sras po dge ba dpal/ dge bshes
ston 'jam/ rgyal tsha/ me sgom la sogs te/ sku 'da' ba'i lo grwa pa mkhas grags thon pa brgyad brgya tsam byung ngo / /sgrub rgyud bstan pa'i srog shing mkhas grub rnams/
/byon tshul rnam thar ba dan cher g.yos pas/ /zab don nor bu'i tog 'dzin mkhas rnams kyi/ /sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan rgyun ring 'dzugs par shog / //

phag mo gru pa'i chos rgyud dang / bla rabs byon tshul bzhugs so/ / na mo gu ru dpal phag mo gru pa'i chos rgyud/ bla rabs byon tshul ni/ bde gshegs rin po che/ khams pa rdor
rgyal mya ngan las 'das rting / thugs sras kyi thu bo ni/ bsod nams mthar phyin/ 'bri khung skyu ra chos rje/ phag gru dang / 'bri khung gnyis ka'i gdan sa lo mang bskyangs/
sku bgres khar 'bri phag gdan sa gnyis su 'byon bzhud dka' bar byung / shas cher 'bri khung du bzhugs dus/ pag gru mthar brtsigs grwa slob rnams gros bsdur/ rje rin
po che sku gnas bgres/ gdan sa khag gnyis skyong dgos pa/ da rang re rnams kyi mgo sdud/ gdan sa zhig bsko bar zhu zhus pa/ drag zer ba la kha 'cham/ ri pa che bgres 'ga'
'bri khung du btang / rje dang mjal nas rgyu mtshan zhus pas/ de bzhin cis kyang 'thad pas de'i 'os su 'dug khyed rang rnams kyi ltos gsungs khong rnams na re/ rje rin
po che rang gi spyan mnga' na bzhugs pa'i/ gsol ja ba 'di 'dra ba zhig bsko bar zhu zhus pas/ 'o de yin de bzhin legs so gsungs/ ngas kyang byin gyis brlabs/ gdan drongs
la song zhig khong gdan sar bskos rjes spyan lam nas byon pas/ de phyin spyan mnga' bar grags pa 'di byung ba yin/ de'i gdung rus rlangs lha gzigs yin/ mtshan lha rgyal
ba byang chub kyang

zer la/ spyan mnga' grags pa byang chub par grags so/ /des phag gru'i lha khang rnying ma bzhengs/ bstan pa dang gdan sa'i bya ba cher mdzad/ phyis khong pas kyang / 'bri khung
gdan sa yang bskyangs shing / shas che ba 'bri khung du bzhugs/ phag gru'i gdan sa la/ khong rang gi dbon po/ lha rgyal ba ye shes pa bskos nas btang bas/ mal gro la
thog tu phebs pa dang / mal gro gzi chen la sogs/ phar tshur gyi gzhi bdag gdug pa can 'ga' ga' res/ bla ma'i nyams sad pa'i phyir du/ glo bur du sprin bsdus/ 'brug bsgrags/
thog ser phabs byung ba dang / bla mas chos gos thu ba bar snang la bzed pa dang / thog mda' lnga thu ba nang sran ma rgyug pa bzhin/ phar ril tshur ril du byed kyin
'dug ste/ bla ma dpon slob mi nor gang la'ang / thog gi gnod pa ma nus pas/ rgyal ba thog gdugs par grags shing / gdul bya dang snyan grags shin du che bar grags so/ /de'i
sku tshe'i smad la/ stod hor rgyal po hu la hu'i brgya 'bul/ nyi shu rtsa gcig gis thog drangs pa'i 'bul mo che blangs/ de nas zhag bcu bdun song ba dang / rgyal ba rin
po che grongs/ de'i dbon po rin po che bcu gnyis pas gdan sa mdzad nas/ rgyal ba rin po che'i nang rten la/ gser gyi sgo mang bzhengs/ gdan sa mthil gyi sgo mang snga ma
yin no/ /de'i slob ma la/ spu rtogs zer/ khong grongs nas/ spu rtogs tshos bla ma'i nang rten la sgo mang zhig bzhengs/ gdan sa bcu gnyis pa'i dbon po che ba/ gcen grags
ye bskos/ de'i slob ma la ldol spu zer/ spu ldol gyi chags sdang de nas byung / rin po che grags pas/ sa skya pa'i bla ma 'phags pa la/ rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa
zhus/ bla ma shar pa ye

shes rin chen pa la/ khong rang gi snag tsha/ dbon po grags le ba phul/ des sa skya pas phag gru'i gdan sa bsko grab byas pas/ gcung rgyal pos bkrongs/ de mtshams rin po che
grags ye grongs nas/ gcung rgyal po grags rin pas gdan sa mdzad/ sa skya'i grags le dbon pos 'kham gcung bsko grab byas pa la / gcung rgyal po'i rting 'bri khung pas mnan
nas/ sa 'bri 'thab pa'i 'go tshugs/ phag gru rang la skyon cher ma byung na'ang / sa 'bri yun ring po 'khrug phyi'i gcung rgya bos bla dpon sbrel nas mdzad/ de grongs
nas khong gi dbon po grags pa rgyal mtshan pa sa pho byi ba lo la gdan sa la bskos pa yin/ khong rang grongs nas de'i dbon po rigs rgyud/ spyan mnga' grags byang pa gdan
sar bskos/ lo 'ga' sne gdong khri thog dang / slob dpon sbrags pa mdzad/ de gshegs rting / gcung po grags pa rin chen pa phag gru'i gdan sar bskos/ de'i rjes la/ khri dpon
shAka rin gyi sras po/ spyan mnga' bsod nams dpal ba dang / bsod nams bzang po ba/ bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa sku mched rnams kyi rim par gdan sa mdzad/ chu mo glang gi
lo'i gsham la/ spyan snga chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa sku mched gshegs/ de'i gshegs rdzongs kyi skabs shing pho stag gi lo/ srog sme brgyad dkar dbus su shar ston
nas/ phag gru nang zing la bstan pas/ dbus gtsang bde dog chen mo langs pa yin/ bde gshegs bla ma rnams kyi thugs rje yi/ /dbus gtsang bde zhing thub bstan gsal ba dang /
/bstan 'dzin skyes bu'i gdan sa ma stong bar/ /sgrub rgyud nyi ma'i 'od ltar gsal bar shog/mdo rgyud nas bshad pa'i spyan lnga ni/ sha'i spyan/ lha'i spyan/ shes rab kyi
spyan/ chos kyi spyan/ sangs rgyas kyi spyan dang lnga'o/ /dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig/ //

dpal phag mo gru pa'i dpon rabs byon tshul bzhugs so/ /oM swa sti/ dpal phag mo gru pa'i dpon rabs ni/ dang po spyan snga chos rje'i dus na/ 'bri khung nas sgom pa shAka rin
gyis spyi'i kha ta byed/ spyan snga ba'i nye gnas sgom brtson gyis rkang yangs dang / smad hor la ngo lta byas/ rting la mdo khams nas/ dpon rdo rje dpal bya ba'i mi gzhon
cig byung / rus pa lha gzigs yin byas pas spyan snga ba'i drung dru bzhag sngon la gsol ja ba bcol/ rting du rgya yul la brdzangs pas/ phag khru khri skor du stag mgo
blang / khri dpon yun ring du byas/ shing pho stag lo la sne gdong rdzong brtsigs/ de 'das nas/ de'i nu bo gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gyi dpon byas/ de 'das rting khong gi dbon
skya yar 'brog pa/ byang gzhon gyis khri dpon byas/ skabs der sa 'bri 'khrug pa la| byang gzhon gyis/ sa skya pa gang gsungs byas/ dpon chen a glen gyis/ phag gru bsreg
par byung ba la/ byang gzhon gyi zhus pas 'tsheng / byang gzhon shi nas/ gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gyi tsha bo/ gzhon nu yon tan gyis khri dpon byas/ hor rgyal bu thi mur bho
kha yum sras bod du bzhugs pa'i zhabs tog dang / dmag gi phyag phyi cung ma 'grub/ phyi go ma chod kyang / nang du zhing pa ya gsum la sogs pa la gzan po byas pas/ rin
po che gcung rgya bo ma mnyes pa ra/ rgyal po

yum sras la zhus pas/ gzhon nu yon tan phab/ gong du zhu ba btang / de ma 'khor bar la rgyal po'i ma ma go cha/ sa skya ba'i chos khrims pa rin chen bkra shis/ rin po che'i
nye gnas brtson 'grus dpal/ gzhon nu yon tan gyi dpon 'og ma/ grags pa 'od zer/ sngags hu la hu'i bskos pa'i yul bsrung ba/ go bo chu'i bu rdo rje/ yar klungs jo bo brag
rin rnams 'dzoms kyin/ khri skor gyi bya ba bsgrubs/ de mtshams gong du bla ma ti shri grags 'od pa'i bdag mdzad nas/ rin po che'i gcung rgyal po la khri dpon gyi 'ja' sa
bsgrubs nas/ bla dpon sbrags/ gzhon nu yon tan la rten sor/ 'phyongs rgyas smon mkhar byin/ gcung rgya bo grongs rting / rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan pa'i gcen po/
rgyal mtshan dpal gyis gong du byon/ lha rje phag mo gru pas zhus nas/ lung gis rgyal mtshan dpal bskos/ de'i lag nas khong rang gi nu bo/ grags bzang sa skya pas zhus nas
bskos de'i lag nas/ gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gyi bu rgyal mtshan skyabs kyi 'ja' sa blangs/ rin po che grags rgyal ba'i gcung po/ byang chub rgyal mtshan/ shing pho stag lo
la bla ma bdag nyid chen po'i drung dru/ lo bcu bzhi lon pa yos lo la phyin nas/ phyag phyir bsdad dam gnyer byas/ bla ma'i gsungs nas/ khyod rin po che byed dam/ khri
dpon byed gsungs nas/ rin po che byed lags zhus pas/ de mi yong bar 'dug khri dpon byed dgos pas/ g.yul rgyal dang / legs bshad la ltos gsungs/ thugs mkhyen mnga' bar 'dug
de'i rjes bdag nyid chen pos sprad nas/ bla ma mnyam med pa la slob gnyer zhus/ brtag gnyis bslabs/ 'brug lo ston gzhug la/ khong gi bshad gsar gyi ja dang /

gcen po slob dpon grags pa bzang pa/ phag gru'i khri dpon la/ sa skya nas khyon bskos byas pa'i/ tshogs ja mnyam du bkol/ ti shri kun blo'i gong du byon dus/ rgyal mtshan skyabs
phab nas/ khong gi khri dpon du bskos/ tsang dbang rgyal po'i 'ja' sa dang / si tu'i ming thob/ rgyal mtshan skyabs kyi tsha bo bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis lung gis
brtsad cing / khyon gyi bsko bzhag dang / mtho sman gang du byung yang / sus kyang ma thub par/ rgyal khams dbang du bsdus pa'i mi de 'di yin no/ /ta'i si tu byang chub
rgyal mtshan pa 'di nyid sku na gzhon dus/ phyi nang gi sde gzar dka' dgu sbyongs brjod che na'ang / dgung lo nga lnga pa'i thog chu pho spre lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes lnga
la/ dpon chen rgyal ba bzang po lha rtser skong / de 'don phyir khri skor rnams kyi dmag bsdus pa'i dpon thob nas/ zla ba lnga pa'i tshes lnga'i nyin/ sa skyar bca' ho
btang / khrims bcas pa nas/ bstan pa'i 'go tshugs te/ mtshan jus dang mnga' thang yar 'phel du byung / khong gi ring la/ rang re lha gzigs kyi rgyud pa 'dis/ mis mi go
chod cing / chos kyi chos go chod pa zhig dgos pa 'dug gsungs/ rtsed thang gi dgon pa gsar du btab/ bshad grwa btsugs/ sne gdong dang srol gcig par byas/ chos rje bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ba gdan drangs/ chos sde'i rab gnas dang khong rang gi dbon po/ slob dpon shAkya rgyal mtshan chos dpon la bskos pa'i tshogs dpon
zhus/ chos 'jig rten gyi bya ba la'ang / mkhyen rab dang rtsol shin tu che bar grag cing / phag mo gru pa'i sde srid kyi bya ba byas pa/ phyag rjes dpon rab sngon rting
/ du gzhan las kyang 'di nyid mchog tu che bar

byed do/ /ta'i si tu de dgung lo re gsum pa/ me pho 'brug gi lo la bde bar gshegs so/ /de nas dbon po slob dpon shAkya rgyal mtshan pas/ sne gdong khri thog tu bzhugs/ bla
dpon sbrags nas mdzad pa'i rigs la/ rgyal khrims 'jags shing / chos khrims dar/ dbus gtsang bde ba dang / mnga' zhabs skyid par byung na dgongs pa'i thugs dge ba kho na bzung
bas/ kun gyi 'jam dbyangs shAkya rgyal mtshan zhes bstod cing bsngags pa'i snyan grags cher byung shing / tshul de dang mthun par gyur to/ /hor tho gan the mur rgyal
pos kyang / chang gu'i gung gi mtshan dang / las ka gnang / khong gshegs rting gcung po khri dpon shAkya rin chen pa/ sne gdong du bskos nas/ dbus gtsang gi gzhis bskor
la 'byon par chas/ gzhung skyid mo gshong du phebs nub/ khang skor byin la me stobs chen shor/ dpon g.yog rnams nyen can la gtad pas/ rtog bcas kyi phyir log nas/ mkhar thog
dgon gsar du bzhugs su bcugathugs ma bde nas mu med mang rab mdzad pas/ khrims bdag smyon par grags pa'ang byung la/ spyan mnga' grags byang pas lo shas bla dpon sbrags
nas bzung /de'i rting de'i gcung po grags pa rin chen pa sne gdong du lo 'ga' bskos/ de mtshams rdzong ji rgyal mtshan bzang po ba khu dbon gyi/ dam byas nas/ bdag po
grags rin pa/ glo bur du gong dkar nas gzhung ko la gdan drangs/ spyan mnga' grags pa'i gdan sar bskyal/ sne gdong khri thog tu/ khri dpon shAg rin gyi sras che ba/ grags
pa rgyal mtshan pa dgung lo bcu gcig lon pa'i dus/ shing pho byi ba'i lo la/ dpon sar bton/ sku tshe'i stod la/ dbon zhang gi 'khon

rtsod dang / e gnyal gyi sde gzar la sogs/ dka' dgu mang po byung na'ang / rting la sde pa nang 'jags/ dbus gtsang gi khri stong phal che ba/ srid dbang du 'dus/ rgya nag ta
ming rgyal pos/ kon ting gu shri dang / tshan hi dbang gi mtshan / dam kha lung lag rtags bzang po'i rim pa gnang / stobs dang dpal 'byor mnga' thang phun sum tshogs pa
byung shing / dgung lo bcu gcig nas/ lnga bcu rtsa dgu'i bar la/ mtshan go sa mthon por bzhugs nas/ sde srid yar 'phel du byung bas/ phag mo gru pa'i dpon rgyud/ khri thog
tu bzhugs pa la/ 'di pa yun ring cing / sku bsod che bar grags/ lnga bcu nga dgu bzhes pa/ chu pho byi ba'i lo la sne gdong rtser sku gshegs so/ /dge legs 'phel bar gyur
cig/ //

lha pa'i bla rabs dang / chos rgyud byon tshul bzhugs so/ /oM swa sti/ lha pa'i thog ma/ gnyos lo tsA ba rin chen grags pas/ rgya gar du byon nas/ slob dpon chen po bha ling
ta a tsarya la/ chos don thog tu dril la/ kha zin che ba zhig zhu byas pas/ gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs kyi skor gnang / las kha tshar tshang ba zhig zhu byas pas/ gshin rje
dgra nag gnang / la chung zhig gi tsa na dgra yod pas/ bka' bsrung zhig yang zhu byas pas/ 'jigs byed la Taka shad sbrel nas gnang / phag rgyud skor gsum zhes grags te/
dar zhing rgyas par mdzad/ de'i sras slob dpon rdo rje bla ma/ pha rgyud skor gsum la mkhas zhing / bod kyi mi chen bzhir grags pa'i/ ya ba zhig yin/ de'i sras/ dpal seng
ge'i sras/ gnyos nag grags pa dpal/ chos rgyal mya ngan med kyi sku skye yin par zhang rin po che'i lung bstan/ khong gis sras/ ras chen gnyos lha nang ba de/ rgya gar
gyi nag po spyod pa chung ba yin par zhang rin po che'i lung bstan 'dug cing / tsa rir byon dus mkha' 'gro mas kyang lung bstan to/ /zhang gi drung du bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/
'bri khung chos rje'i drung du/ nA ro chos drug gsan/ tsa ri ti se sogs la byon/ sgrub pa nan tan che bar mdzad/ mon gyi pa gro bcal kha la sogs par/ tshogs pa yang thog
re bskyangs/ byang du lha nang btab/ lha pa nyis stong brgyad brgyar grags pa yang de nas byung / khong

gi dbon po/ lha rin chen rgyal de nyid/ lha sras mu ne btsan po'i sku skye yin skad/skyor mo lung du rab byung mdzad/ pha rgyud skor gsum la mkhas/ bcal kha sa g.yos kyi sgyel
ba'i tshab/ phag ri rin chen sgang brtsigs/ lha nang du gdan sar bzhugs pas/ rgyal khrims che ba'i dmag sna'i gnod pa byung bas/ skyid smad du byon nas/ rab gong brtsigs
lha nang du/ khu'u'i bla ma grub thob 'dam seng gdan sa la brdzangs/ 'dam pa rigs pas nye gnas byas/ gye re dgon pa btab cing / gye re lha khang gi gtsug lag khang brtsigs/
de'i dbon rgyud/ bla ma dar ma rgyal po dang / de'i dbon po lha gzi brjid rgyal po/ chos kyi rgyud pa ni/ lha rin chen rgyal po khu dbon la/ mkhas pa dge brag pa tshul
gzhon gyi thug de'i slob ma mkhas pa byang dar/ de'i slob ma 'jam dbyangs gzi rjid rgyal po la sogs/ lha rabs bris pas lha mi kun/ /kun mkhyen rgyal po myur thob shog
/dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig/ //

shangs pa bka' brgyud rin chen bdun byon tshul bzhugs so/ / na mo ratna gu ru/ zab don thar lam nye ba mkha' 'gro'i chos/ /sgyu lam rmi lam sprul sgyur dbang 'byor zhing /
/chos skyong mgon po'i 'phrin las legs bsgrubs pa/ /shangs pa bka' rgyud byon tshul zur tsam 'bri/ /de'ang shangs pa'i chos skor zhes bya ba/ rgyud thag nye zhing / rgyud
pa bka' babs dang ldan pa/ gdams ngag nus pa dang ldan pa/ mkha' 'gro'i byin rlabs dang ldan pa/ 'di'i byung tshul bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar zur tsam bstan pa ni/ thog
mar sangs rgyas ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma ni gu ma dang / su ga siddhi la gsungs shing / de gnyis kyi zhal dngos su bstan nas gsung ba ni/ mkhas grub chen po khyung po
rnal 'byor gyi 'khrung yul ni/ snye mo ra mangs/ rigs ni bon po/ rus ni khyung po/ yab khyung po stag skyes dang / yum bkra shis skyid kyi sras su 'khrungs ma thag tu/ grub
thob a mo gha pas lung bstan/ yig rtsis la sogs mkhas par mkhyen/ bon dang / phyag rgya chen po zhus pa la the tshom re tsam 'khrungs nas/ rgya gar la chos 'tshol du byon/
paNDi ta ma thu badzra dang / bla ma rdo rje gdan pa'i drung du mjal/ ma ga dhar dge tshul zhus/ mtshan tshul khrims mgon por btags pas/ bla mas shangs khrag shor nas/
khyung po rnal 'byor la mtshan dpod ma thub/ de

nas bzung ste spyir rgya gar dang bal por theng bdun byon zhing / rje btsun shrI dznyA na dang / bai ro tsa na rakShi ta la sogs pa/ khyad par can gyi bla ma brgya lnga bcu
dang / rtsa ba'i bla ma rnam bzhi/ 'gran gyi zla med ye shes kyi DA ki ma/ zhal gnyis rnams/ mos gus dang gser srang mang pos mnyes par byas nas gang la gang 'dod kyi zab
chos/ bka' lung man ngag bsam gyis mi khyab pa gnang zhing / khyad par du rgyal sras mi tri pa dang / dpal sha ba ri pas chos skyong phyag drug pa'i skor tshang ma dang
/ mkha' 'gro rnam gnyis kyis byin gyis brlabs/ gsang yum mdzad/ chos drug gi khrid tshang ma gnang / khyod nas mi rabs lnga'i bar la chig rgyud las ma spel cig gsungs/ bka'
rgya bsdams/ chos kyi mnga' bdag chen por gyur nas/ bod la byon/ mnga' ris su jo bo rje dang mjal/ gdams pa zhus/ glang ri thang pa'i drung du bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ 'jog
po'i ri la sgrub pa mdzad/ cha dkar dgon pa btab/ mkha' 'gro'i lung bstan byung nas/ dpon slob sum stong gi yan byon/ shangs su zhong zhong dgon pas 'go byas/ gnas dgon
brgya rtsa btab/ grwa slob mang dus khri tsho bdun brgyad 'tshogs/ de thams cad chos kyis tshim par mdzad/ de skabs DA ki ma kun tu bzang mo byon nas/ tshogs pa'i mthar
thug khri tsho brgyad/ /slob ma'i mthar thug lnga brgya dang / /tshe yi mthar thug brgya lnga bcu/ / zhing khams mthar thug bde ba can/ /zhes gsungs pa de rnams 'dzoms shing
dus la babs par mkhyen nas/ slob ma'i thu bo rmi'u ston pa dang / g.yor po rgya mo che sngul ston rin dbang / zhang sgom chos seng / las stod pa dkon mchog mkhar dang
lnga/ chig rgyud kyi bka' babs pa/

rmog cog pa rin chen brtson 'grus/ rnams kyis thog drangs pa'i/ grwa slob dbu che ba rnams la chos kyi phyi ma gsungs/ chos rgyud dar zhing rgyas par yong cing / nga'i phung
po 'di ril bur gzhug su bcug nas/ gsol ba btab na/ gnas zhong zhong 'di rdo rje gdan dang mnyam pa zhig yong ngo / /gsungs pa la sogs kyi lung bstan mang po mdzad nas/
bde ba can du gshegs so/ /de'i thugs kyi sras mchog rmog cog pa rin chen brtson 'grus ni/ 'khrungs yul lha phug spangs rtsa ba/ rus she yab shor rgan sman chung dang / yum
'be mo padma sgron gyi sras su 'khrungs te/ dgung lo bcu bdun pa la/ mkhas grub khyung po'i drung du rab tu byung / bla ma'i zhal nas slob gnyer cig sngon la gyis gsungs
nas/ blo mos dang / dmigs rkyen sgrub pa la che bar byung nas/ slob dpon la ching ba dang / grub thob / khams pa a seng / bur sgom nag po/ dge bshes dkon mchog mkhar pa
la sogs/ mkhas grub mang po la/ sgom 'khrid zhus/ slar zhong zhong bla ma'i drung du byon nas/ nyams rtogs re tsam phul bas/ sngon ma bla mas bkyon par byung na'ang / rting
du nga'i chig rgyud kyi gdams pa zab mo 'di/ khyod la byin gsungs pa DA ki ma'i lung bstan yin gsungs nas/ bum pa gang byo gnang / ne gu'i thugs dam thang sku/ dgyes
rdor gyi thang sku/ ka pa li dang / thod pa mtshan ldan/ dbang bum dang bcas pa gnang / rgyal tshab tu dbang bskur/ bla ma'i gsung bzhin bsgoms pas/ sgyu lus rmi lam 'byongs/
sprul sgyur la dbang thob/ chos skyong bran bzhin nyan/ gnas chen dang yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs/ rje dwags po lha rje sogs dang mjal/ byin rlabs zhus/ rmog cog gi

brag la lo bcu gnyis kyi bar la lto gos 'phri ba bcad nas/ rtse gcig tu sgrub pa mdzad/ zad sar gyi sprul sgyur/ nam mkha' la skyil krung du bzhugs/ slob ma mkhas pa dran don/
dbus pa rdo seng la sogs pa mang du byung zhing / de rnams kyi nang nas/ chig rgyud kyi gdams pa dbon ston skyer sgang pa la phog grwa slob mang nas rmog cog tu ma shong
bar/ skung lung dgon pa btab/ bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don dar zhing rgyas par mdzad/ bde ba can du gdan 'dren byung na'ang ma byon par/ der rting lo gsum gyi bar la chos
gsungs nas/ nga 'das pa dang mngon dgar gsol ba thob gsungs nas/ tshes bco brgyad kyi srod la/ 'gro rus btsan gyi snyon dris/ lan gnang / tho rangs bde bar gshegs so/
/de'i thugs sras dam pa skyer sgang pa/ dbon ston thugs rje chen po ni/ 'khrungs yul nang gong rnams pa/ rus pa 'bal/ dgung lo bcu bdun la/ khu bo 'bal thams cad mkhyen
pa'i drung du rab tu byung / mtshan chos kyi seng ge btags/ des gdan sa byed dgos pas/ thos pa gyis zer na'ang / lha sa'i brag lha klu phug tu lce sgom rdzong pa la/ thugs
rje chen po'i chos skor zhus/ rtse gcig sgrub pas/ zla ba phyed dang bzhi nas/ gtso 'khor gsum po zhal mthong / bla ma tsa ri ras pa dang / rtogs ldan zhang la sogs/ bla
ma mang du bsten/ rmi lam bzung nas/ blo dpon padma la sogs rgya bod kyi grub chen rnams la chos zhus/ yi dam mkha' 'gro mang po'i zhal mthong / zhing khams gnas chen mang
du bstan/ bha ru nas sbyin bdag byas/ smyon pa brgyad cu btul/ mchog tu sku drin che bas/ bla ma rmog cog pas/ mkha' 'gro'i zab chos chig rgyud kyi thog drangs pa'i/
gdams

pa thams cad ma lus par/ dbus snyung bzhes nas gnang / chos skyong dran bzhin nyan pa'i bka' bsgo mdzad/ byin gyis brlabs sku drin dran pa'i 'bul mo che thengs gsum phul/ bla
ma skyer sgang du byon dus/ nyams bsdur mdzad pas/mnyes nas dbon ston/ pa la mdzo skyes zer ba'i skad thongs shig gsung zhing / sngar rgya gar gyi grub thob phal che ba
las/ mkhas grub khyung po thugs dam bzang bar 'dug de las nga dge sbyor bzang bar 'dug gsung zhing yod/ nga las khyed nyams rtogs bzang bar 'dug go/ ngo mtshar che gsungs
ngo / /grwa slob yon bdag ni/ rgya thang rgya'i rgyal po/ bla ma sog pa/ dkar chung btsad po/ rgyal tsha la sogs/ skya btsun mang po chos kyi tshim zhing / nad gdon las
grol nas/ thugs rje chen po'i zhal mthong ba sha stag byung ngo / /chos rgyud 'di/ g.yor po stod pa zhig gis 'dzin cing / rdo rje 'chang gis lung bstan pa bzhin/ brgyud
pa bdun thims nas/ chig rgyud kyi zab chos/ mkha' 'gro'i zhal gdams 'dis/ phyogs kun du khyab nas/ gdul bya snod ldan yang / mang du 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /nga ni 'di nas
