mngon dgar 'gro bas/ gsol ba der thob cig gsungs pa la sogs lung bstan mang du gnang zhing / bstan pa dang 'gro ba mang po'i don rgya che la yun ring bar mdzad nas/ dgung
lo don gsum bzhes pa/ston zla ra ba'i tshes bcu gsum la/ skyer sgang du bde bar gshegs so/ /	yol bu ri gong gnyan ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor ni/ 'khrungs yul yol bu'i mda'/
rus gnyan de nyid ni/ sku gzhon nu nas/ chos kho na'i gtam dang /spyod lam la brtson pa zhig byung ste/ dgung lo bcu gcig pa la gung po mkhar du/

slob dpon ston yes la/ chos sgor zhugs/ bcu bdun pa la/ mkhan po byang sems pa la dge tshul zhus/ mtshan chos kyi shes rab tu btags/ nyi shu pa la mkhan po bzod pa'i drung
du bsnyen par rdzogs nas/ g.yor slob dpon e pa sogs la/ 'dul ba bslabs/ slob gnyer thog cig byed dgos dgongs pa la/ mched grogs las stod 'khyams pos blo sgul nas/ sgom sgrub
pa la mos te/ skyer sgang du byon/ dbon ston pas shangs pa'i chos skor dang / chig rgyud kyi gdams pa zab mo thams cad bum pa gang byo gnang / chos skyong la bka' bsgo
dang / ri gong dgon pa 'debs pa/ skabs 'di tsam nas spyod pa'i tshul bzung /slob ma snod ldan bcu phrag cig yod pa de/ skye bo 'bum phrag cig las lhag go gsungs pa la sogs
kyi lung bstan mdzad/ bla ma dang nam mjal dus/ thugs rje chen por rgyun par mthong / bla ma las stod pa mgon po chos sgo skyel la byung /rmi lam bzung nas/ yi dam dang
zhing khams mang po mthong / khyad par grub chen brgyad cu la sogs/ DA ki ma mang po 'dzoms nas/ chos kyi bzang bdun mdzad par byon/ ye shes kyi bdud rtsi'i skal ba gsol/
lha klu bdud btsan mang po btul/ bla ma 'dis dus gsum gyi skye 'gag gnas gsum mkhyen na'ang / blo dman gyi blor mi shong bas/ log rtog gi rgyur song dogs bka' rgya bsdams
pas na/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor chen por grags zhing / sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan btsugs nas/ 'gro ba'i don rgya chen po mdzad do/ /bde bar gshegs dus/ nga ni 'di nas shar
phyogs me tog bkram pa'i zhing du/ sangs rgyas padmo'i dpal zhes par 'gyur bas/ gsol ba der thob cig gsungs so/ /

brag dgon pa ba chos rje sangs rgyas ston pa ni/ 'khrungs yul kha rag sil ma/ rus ya ngal dkar po/ rigs bon po yin na'ang / bon la thugs ma song / gzhon nu nas/ mi rtag pa
kho na rgyud la skye ba byung zhing / dgung lo bcu pa la sprul sku'i dbang bskur lung bstan/ bcu gsum pa la bla ma tsA ri ras pa la rab tu byung / mtshan brtson 'grus seng
ger btags/ slob dpon sdigs [sregs]dang / sum pa ras pa/ bla ma sa skya pa/ bla ma khro phu pa la sogs/ mkhas grub mang du bsten/ gdams pa dpag med zhus/ bcu dgu pa la/
slob dpon chos rgyal ba la bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ der rting slob dpon rngog ston gyi lung bstan pa bzhin yol bu ri gong du byon pas/ bla ma gnyan ston mnyes nas/ dbang bskur
shangs pa'i chos skor thams cad/ chig rgyud kyi gdams pa dang bcas pa bum pa gang byo dbus snyung bzhes nas gnang / chos skyong lcam dral la mi lab pa bzhin du ngo sprad/
bka' bsgo mdzad/ de nas chos drug gi 'khrid bskyangs pas/ zhag nyi shu rtsa lnga la/ sprul sgyur sbyongs spel thub pa byung bas/ bla ma'i zhal nas/ sngar rgya gar gyi grub
thob rnams las/ bla ma khyung po nyams rtogs bzang bar grags/ de las rim gyi bzang du song zer/ nga las ni khyed dge sbyor bzang bar 'dug pa/ 'di 'dra'i dge sbyor skye
lugs da lta rgya bod gang na'ang med/ khyed kyi 'gro don rgya chen po 'grub pa 'dug gsungs shing / lung bstan zhal gdams mang po gnang ngo / /de ltar bsgoms pas bla ma
yi dam mkha' 'gro mang po'i zhal mthong / chos gnang / brag dgon du lo gcig dbu sngas la ma bzhag par sgom pas zad par gyi ting nge 'dzin rnams rgya chen po dang /

sangs rgyas zhing khams gang mos su/ rmi lam bzung nas phyin chog pa byung / gnod byed mang po rmi lam du btul/ chos skyong 'khor la sdig ma gsog zer ba'i kha mnan gang thub
byas/ sman lung su snyung nas grongs la thug pa'i dus/ tsha drags brag ring gi btsan gyi/ bal yul nas sman blangs nas phul ba dang / thugs dam rtse gcig mdzad pas/ snyung
ba las grol cing / sgrub rgyud kyi bstan pa dar bar mdzad do/ /bla ma 'di'i rjes la/ chig rgyud kyi bka' rgya khrol te/ khong gi slob ma chos rje shangs ston dang / mkhas

rgyas par mdzad pa lags so/ /rgyud pa rin chen bdun ma 'di bris pas/ /dge tshogs rin chen phyogs bcu kun khyab ste/ dal 'byor rin chen thob pa'i mi rnams dang / 'gro
kun rin chen brtson 'grus nyid gyur cig/ //

chos rgyal 'phags pa'i shes bya rab gsal las/ snod bcud kyi chags tshul mdor bsdus pa bzhugs so/ / oM swa sti/ bsam 'phel bla ma kun mkhyen zas gtsang sras/ /smra ba'i seng
ge 'jam dbyangs zhabs btud nas/ /de yi rnam 'phrul chos rgyal 'phags pa yis/ /mdo rgyud don bsdus shes bya'i gnas rnams kun/ /rab tu gsal byed bstan bcos brtsams pa las/
/mdor tsam bsdus pa 'di dag bdag gis bri/ /dang po rdul grangs 'gyur khyad brtsi ba ni/ bcang bzung gzhig tu med pa'i phra rab rdul/ /bdun 'gyur rdul phran lcags chu ri
bong lug /glang rdul nyi zer sro ma shig nas rdul/ /de bzhin re re bzhin du bdun 'gyur te/ /nas bdun sor tshigs bcu gnyis mtho gang la/ /mtho do khru gang khru bzhi 'dom
pa gang / /de dag lnga brgya rgyang grags de brgyad la/ /dpag tshad gcig tu brtsi ba rab gsal lugs/ /snod kyi chags tshul dang po stong pa la/ /phyogs bcu'i rlung g.yos dkyil
'khor rgya gram gyi/ /rngams su dpag tshad 'bum phrag bcu drug dang / /rgya khyon grangs med de yis brten pa'i steng / /chu yi dkyil 'khor zlum po mthug rngams la/ /chig
'bum rags chen thad kar sa ya gcig /gnyis 'bum gsum stong brgya phrag phyed dang lnga/ /de dag 'og gi rgya mtsho brgyad ldan chu/ /de bsrubs

spris ma gser gyi sa gzhi ni/ /rngams su dpag tshad sum 'bum nyis khri dang / /thad ka'i tshad ni 'og gi tshad dang mnyam/ /gnyis ka'i mthas skor thad la gsum 'gyur ro/ /rlung
gi dkyil 'khor mi mjed 'jig rten khams/ /sa chu'i dkyil 'khor gling bzhi ri rab gdan/ /gser gyi sa steng char phab rgya mtshor gyur/ /rlung gis bsrubs pa'i khams rab
'dus ri rab/ /'bring 'dus pa la gser gyi ri bdun dang / /tha ma'i lcags ri sna tshogs 'dus pa'i gling / /rim par chags zhing lhun po'i shar phyogs dngul/ /lho bai DUrya nub
la shel dmar po/ /byang phyogs gser dang ri bdun gser 'ba' zhig /gling bzhi gling phran dang brgyad phal cher ba/ khor yug lcags ri lcags la ri rab gyi/ /dpangs la dpag
tshad dag ni chig 'bum dang / /drug khri yod pa mtsho mtshams yar mar phyed/ /ri bdun mtho shos gnya' shing 'dzin gyi dpangs/ /dpag tshad bzhi khri de nas shol mda' 'dzin/
/seng ldeng 'dzin dang rta sna sdug ri dang / /rta sna rnam bdud mu khyud 'dzin rnams la/ /rim bzhin phyed mar phyi ma lcags ris dpangs/ /dpag tshad sum brgya phyed dang
bcu gsum yod/ /thad ka'i tshad rnams dpangs dang mnyam pa'o/ /ri bdun bar gyi mtsho bdun kha zheng la/ /nang ma dpag tshad brgyad khri de'i phyi mar/ /rim bzhin phyed
'phri ri rab ri bdun po/ /mtshor bcas gru bzhi lcags ri sgor mor gnas/ /mu khyud 'dzin dang lcags ri bar gyi tshad/ /dpag tshad sum 'bum nyi khri nyis stong yod/ /lcags
ri'i nang na ba tshwa can gyi mtsho/ /mtsho gcig rgya mtsho chen po bzhir grags pa/ /lhun po'i phyogs bzhi'i ngos kyi kha dog bzhin/ /mtsho dang gling rnams de dang mthun
pa'i

phyir/ /rgya mtsho de yi mtha' skor dpag tshad ni/ /sa ya phrag gsum drug 'bum bdun brgya dang / /lnga bcu yod cing de yi phyi rol gyi/ khor yug lcags ri mtha' skor sa ya gsum/
drug 'bum nyis stong drug brgya nyer lnga yod/ /ri rab lho phyogs 'dzam gling shing rta'i dbyibs/ /sog kha'i yu ba chu ngos bstan pa la/ /dpag tshad phyed dang bzhi
gzhan phyogs gsum la/ /stong phrag gnyis gnyis shar na rnga yab dang / /nub na rnga yab gzhan yod 'dzam gling dbus/ /ma ga dha nas byang du ri nag po/ /dgur rgyud gangs ri
spos ngad de yi phyir/ /spos ri ngad lngan de gnyis bar gyi mtsho/ /ma dros gru bzhi zab dang ngos de'i tshad/ /dpag tshad lnga bcu re re de yi chu/ /gtsang dang 'jam dang
snyog ma med mngar dang / dri zhim mgrin pa lto la mi gnod pa/ /yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i chu yin no/ /de la chu bo bzhi 'bab si ta dang / /ganggA sindhu pakShu zhes
pa'o/ /ma dros rtsa ba'i brag gi bya skyibs na/ /'dzam bu tri sha'i dpag bsam sdong bu las/ /'bras bu cher smin mtsho nang lhung ba'i sgra/ /'dzam bu zhes bya'i mtshon
pas 'dzam gling grags/ /shar gyi lus 'phags gling ni zla gam la/ /ri rab ngos bstan spyad kha dpag tshad ni/ /sum brgya lnga bcu grangs gzhan gsum drug re/ /byang na lus
dang lho na lus 'phags yod/ /de gsum gling gzhan rnams las rta la bdun/ /gyen du 'phags dang mi rnams gzugs bzang bas/ /lus 'phags po zhes grags pa de nas yin/ /byang na
sgra mi snyan ni gru bzhi la/ /ngos rer dpag tshad nyis stong nub phyogs na/ /sgra mi snyan dang shar na de'i zla ba/ /shing dang sha za'i skad kyis zhag bdun nas/ /'chi
'pho sgra 'byung de phyir sgra mi snyan/ /nub kyi ba glang spyod ni

zlum po yin/ /mtha' skor dag la dpag tshad bdun stong dang / /lnga brgya yod cing lho na g.yo ldan dang / /byang na lam mchog 'gro yod de yi ming / /phal cher ba glang rin
chen longs spyod pas/ /ba glang spyod zhes grags pa de yi phyir/ /ri bdun gling rnams ri bo thams cad kyang / /ri rab dang mtshungs thur du brgyad khri zug /ri rab mtsho
steng yan la bang rim bzhi/ /'og ma'i ngos der dpag tshad khri drug stong / /gong ma'i rim bzhin phyed de zhum pa'o/ /steng phyogs dpag tshad bzhi khri me shel la'ang / /nyi
ma'i dkyil 'khor thad kar dpag tshad grangs/ /lnga bcu rtsa gcig mtha' skor chig brgya dang / /lnga bcu rtsa gsum dpangs la dpag tshad drug /bco brgyad cha gcig yod pa
bar snang gnas/ /mthug rngams de bzhin chu shel las grub pa/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor thad kar lnga bcu dang / /mtha' skor dpag tshad phyed dang nyis brgya'o/ /skar ma rin
chen sna tshogs las grub mang / /zlum po chung tshad rgyang grags gcig dang ni/ /'bring gsum che ba la drug mtha' skor la/ /rang rang thad ka'i gsum 'gyur dag tu 'dod/ /'di
nas dpag tshad lnga yan ri rab kyi/ /rtse man gnas shing grangs ka dung phyur gnyis/ /bye ba phrag brgyad sa ya lnga ru bzhed/ /bcud kyi sems can smin tshul stong gsum
'di/ /bskal ba mes bshig rjes la 'od gsal gyi/ /lha nas rim gyis tshe 'phos tshangs ris slebs/ /'jig rten spyi las tshangs pa bya ba byung / /de ni lha nas rim rgyud sgra
mi snyan/ /ba glang spyod dang lus 'phags 'dzam gling skyes/ /dud 'gro yi dwags dmyal ba mthar thug te/ /dmyal ba zhes bya 'jam gling 'di'i 'og tu/ /dpag tshad stong phrag
nyi shu gru bzhir gnas/ /yi dwags gnas

pa rgyal po'i khab kyi 'og /dpag tshad lnga brgyar grong khyer ser skya na/ /yi dwags gtso bo gshin rje chos rgyal yod/ /dud 'gro phal cher phyi yi rgya mtshor gnas/ kha 'thor
ba rnams lha mi'i yul na'ang yod/ /mi rnams gling bzhi gling g.yog brgyad po dang / /gser gling la sogs gling phran gzhan na'ang gnas/ /lha min gnas pa ri rab mtshor
bying ba'i/ khong seng la yod mthur la rim pa bzhin/ /gnas bzang chang gi ltung ba med pa tsam/ /ma rtogs lha dang lo ngo mnyam 'drar bshad/khams gsum sems can dbye ba 'di
lta te/ /mnar med dmyal ba yi dwags dud 'gro dang / /mi dang lha min 'dod pa'i lha drug man/ /'khrig pa zas nor chags pas 'dod khams zer/ /lha drug 'og ma rgyal chen rigs
bzhi'i 'khor/ /ri rab bang rim dang por gzhong thogs dang / /gnyis par 'phreng thogs gsum par stag nyos gnas/ /bzhi pa'i lha dang gnya' shing 'dzin ri yi/ /shar phyogs
yul 'khor srung na yul 'khor srung/ /byang phyogs lcang lo can na rnam thos sras/ /nub phyogs sna tshogs gzugs na mig mi bzang / /lho phyogs 'phags skyes po na 'phags skyes
rgyal/ /nyi zla skar ma lcags ri 'dzam gling gi/ ri dang ljon shing la gnas lha tshogs rnams/ /rgyal chen rigs bzhir cha stong sde tshan gcig/der rting ri rab zur bzhi'i
lcog de la/ /'phang du dpag tshad phyed dang lnga de 'phags/ /chu zheng brgya dang nyi shu rtsa lnga re/ /mtha' skor dpag tshad lnga brgyas skor ba na/ /gnod sbyin gsang
ba pa rnams gnas par bshad/ /de yi dbus na sum cu rtsa gsum ni/ /gser las grub pa'i grong khyer lta na sdug /dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis 'phags ngos re la/ /nyis stong
lnga brgya mtha' ma khris 'khor

ba'i/ /lcags ri dang bcas de dbus lha'i gnas/ /rnam rgyal khang bzangs gru bzhi gyen phyogs la/ /dpag tshad phyed dang lnga 'phags ngos re la/ /nyi brgya lnga bcu re yod de
dag na/ /nor lha mched brgyad drag po bcu gcig dang / /nyi ma bcu gnyis mtha' skar bu gnyis te/ /dbang po nyer dbang sum cu rtsa gsum dag /yod phyir lha gnas sum cu rtsa
gsum zer/ /brgya byin btsun mo'i sde sogs lha dbang ni/ /lha min bu mo rnams dang rnam par rol/ /de steng dpag tshad brgyad khri 'thab bral gnas/ /tshad ni ri rab ngos las
nyis 'gyur che/ /de yan 'thab rtsod dang bral 'thab bral zhes/ /de nas dpag tshad drug khri 'phags pa na/ /dga' ldan lha gnas 'thab bral gnyis 'gyur che/ /byams mgon theg
chen skyong bas dga' ldan zer/ /der steng dpag tshad gsum 'bum nyi khri na/ /'phrul dga'i lha gnas dga' ldan nyis 'gyur che/ /rang gi sprul nas spyod pas 'phrul dga'
zer/ /der steng dpag tshad drug 'bum bzhi khri na/ /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed 'phrul dga'i nyis 'gyur che/ /gzhan gyi sprul pa'i longs spyod dpag med la/ /bde bar spyod pas
gzhan 'phrul dbang byed zer/ /de man 'dod pa'i lha drug 'dod khams yin/ /der steng gzugs khams lha rigs bcu bdun ni/ /bsam gtan bzhis bsdus dang po tshangs ris dang / /'dun
na 'don dang tshangs pa chen po'o/ /gnyis pa 'od chung tshad med 'od gsal lo/ /gsur pa dge chung tshad med dge rgyas so/ /bzhi pa dag la rnam pa brgyad du 'byed/ /sprin
med bsod nams skyes dang 'bras bu che/ /de man so so skye bo'i gnas gzhan yin/ /mi che mi gdung gya nom snang ba dang / /shin tu mtho ba 'og min gnas dang lnga/ /

'phags pa'i gnas yin gtsang rigs lha lnga zer/ /bar khyad rgya khyon gnyis 'gyur yar yar che/ /bcu bdun pa de 'dod lha 'dod chags bral/ /gzugs la chags pas gzugs khams pa zhes
zer/ /de yi steng na gzugs med lha gnas bzhi/ /lus med ting 'dzin bye brag bzhi 'gyur te/ /nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched rnam shes dang / /ci yang med dang 'du shes
med min rnams/ /gzugs med 'dod pa'i 'dod chags bcas pa'i phyir/ /gzugs med khams kyi lha ni bzhi zer ro/ /e ma srid pa'i rtser phyin lha thob kyang / /sems kyi gnas lugs
ma rtogs 'khrul ba spyod/ /zo chun 'khyud mo ji bzhin 'khor ba rnams/ /dal 'byor thob dus btsan sa 'dzin pa rigs/ /bskal ba dang lo zla zhag dus kyi thung mtha'i skad cig
ma la thug te/ de'ang / phra ba'i skad gcig ma'i tshad ni/ gyad kyis se gol gtogs pa gcig gi yun nam/ bud med 'bring po'i bal 'dab 'then nas 'phang la/ dkris pa'i yun de
brgya nyi shur bgos pa'i cha gcig yin par 'dod do/ /phra ba'i skad gcig ma de brgya nyi shu la rags pa'i skad gcig go /de drug cu la thang gcig go/ de sum cu la yud tsam
gcig de sum cu la nyin zhag gcig de sum cu la zla ba gcig zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig lo de/ bcu/ brgya/ stong / khri/ 'bum/ sa ya/ bye ba/ dung phyur/ ther 'bum rnams bcu
'gyur yin/ der rting zla bo dang bcas pa'i grangs kyi rnam grangs ni dpag tu med de/ mthar thug brjod du med pa'o/ /bskal ba drug zhes pa ni/ bar gyi bskal ba dang / chags
pa'i bskal ba dang / gnas pa'i bskal ba dang / 'jig pa'i bskal ba dang / stong pa'i bskal ba dang / bskal ba chen

po'o/ /bar bskal ces pa ni/ mi lo ther 'bum bcu la ther 'bum chen po gcig yong ba/ de la bar bskal gcig zer te/ de 'dra ba nyi shu'i yun la snod bcud 'jig nyi shu'i yun la
stong / nyi shu'i yun du chags/ nyi shu'i yun du gnas pa/ bar bskal brgyad cu po de rdzogs pa la/ bskal ba chen po gcig zer ro/ /dang por chags pa la bar bskal gcig 'gro
ba'i tshad ni/ rlung gi dkyil 'khor brtsams pa nas/ dmyal ba mnar med du sems can gcig skyes pa'i bar de yin cing / 'jig pa'i 'go brtsams pa nas/ mnar med du sems can gcig
kyang med pa'i dus de'ang / bar bskal gcig yin no/ /snod 'jig pa'i tshe mes 'jig pa dang / chus 'jig pa dang / rlung gis 'jig pa dag gsum las/ mthar rlung gis 'jig pa'i
dus su/ bsam gtan gsum pa'i gnas man 'jig te/ rlung chen pos ri rab kyang gtor nas yang du stong la/ gzhan rnams lta smos kyang ci dgos/ de ltar du thams cad zhig tshar
ba'i rjes la/ phyogs bcu'i rlung 'dus nas/ sra zhing brtan pa'i dkyil 'khor chags pa la brten nas/ chu'i dkyil 'khor dang / gser gyi sa gzhi la sogs snod kyi 'jig rten dang
/ bcud kyi sems can sngon ma ltar yar mar/ rim pa bzhin legs par chags so/ /chos rgyal 'phags pas mdo rgyud mtha' dag gis/ khyad par 'phags pa'i don bsdus bstan bcos ming
/ /shes bya rab gsal grags pa'i nyi ma yis/ /bdag blo'i mun pa bsal phyir snod bcud kyi/ /chags 'jig khams sum dbye ba mdor bsdus 'dis/ /dge bas 'gro rnams kun mkhyen
thob par shog/ //

yig tshang mkhas pa dga' byed kyi mdzad byang dang / smon lam bzhugs so/ oM swa sti/ rgyal ba'i bka' dang bstan 'dzin skyes bu yis/ /dgongs bzhed dang mthun 'dzam gling shas
che ba'i/ /lo paN mkhas grub chos rgyal rim pa dang / /stobs ldan rnams kyi thub bstan rgyas pa'i thabs/ /sna tshogs spel mdzad rnam thar bsgrigs pa yis/ /legs bshad mkhas
pa dga' byed yig tshang 'di/ /yig mkhan shAkya'i dge sten shri bhu ti/ /bha dra'i ming can g.yas ru stag tshang pa'i/ /shing pho stag la stag sna don rtser bkod/ /'di
yi dge ba rab dkar dri med des/ /rgyal ba'i bstan pa yun ring gnas pa dang / /'gro kun bla med byang chub myur thob shog /sngon chad bod 'dir mkhas mang gis bsdebs pa'i/
/yig tshang yig tshogs rgyas pa mang mod kyi/ /de dag kun kyang rin chen gser dang mtshungs/ /tshig gi nor bu rdog bsdus yi ge'i 'bru/ /dag gsal srad bur brgyus pa'i yig
tshang mchog /mdor bsdus don gsal 'dzam bu chu bo'i gser/ ji bzhin mkhas pa'i khyad nor 'di 'dra dkon/ /skal ldan dga' spro spel ba'i rgyur gyur cig /'di don mthong thos
dran pa'i skyes bu kun/ /chos rgyal yon mchod rnams la sems dad cing / /sangs rgyas bstan la

mchog tu mos pa dang / /rang gzhan dge la bskul ba'i rgyur gyur cig /mkhas mang rgyu skar dbus na nyi ma bzhin/ /gzhan phan 'od stong 'gyed pa'i yig tshang 'dis/ /blo ngan
mun nag rab rib phyir bsal nas/ /blo gros pad tshal rgyas pa'i rgyur gyur cig /blo gsal ri dwags gtso bo gdong lnga bzhin/ /smra ba'i phyogs la mi 'jigs yig tshang 'dis/
/ltas ngan wa skyes tshogs rnams zil mnan nas/ /phas rgol spobs pa 'joms pa'i rgyur gyur cig /zab yangs rgya mtsho'i skye bo'i khrod na ded dpon bzhin/ /gang la ci 'dod ster
ba'i yig tshang 'dis/ /blun rmongs dbul ba'i sdug bsngal kun bsal nas/ /'dod dgu'i gter kha 'byed pa'i rgyur gyur cig /nor 'tshol skye bo'i khrod na ded dpon bzhin/ /thabs
mkhas gru chen ldan pa'i yig tshang 'dis/ /'gro mang phan bde'i rlung gis rab bskyod nas/ /thar pa'i lam mchog stsol ba'i rgyur gyur cig /dge ba'i bsam pas phyogs kun
mtha' dag nas/ /zab bsdus legs par bsgrigs pa'i yig tshang 'dis/ /mkha' ltar khyab nas bstan pa'i bya ba kun/ /sgrub pa'i dmigs rkyen byed pa'i rgyur gyur cig /phyogs
gcig 'dus na 'dod dgu'i gter mdzod dang / /so sor 'thor na'ang rin chen ras ma bzhin/ /gang ltar gyur kyang phan byed yig tshang 'dis/ /'gro mang dge la bskul ba'i rgyur
gyur cig /'dod dgu'i bang mdzod legs bshad rgyan gyi spras/ /ngo mtshar gtam rgyud 'phreng ba'i drwa phyed 'phyangs/ /sangs rgyas byon tshul tog gi nyer mdzes pa'i/ /khang
bzangs kun 'dzoms de yi phyogs bzhi ru/ /da

lta'i skabs na bstan pa'i srog shing 'dzin/ /snyigs dus 'gro mgon chos rgyal rab brtan gyis/ /rnam thar nor bu'i rgyal mtshan cher btsugs nas/ /snyan grags ba dan g.yo ba'i
rgyur gyur cig /mdor na bstan dang 'gro la phan phyir du/ /lhag bsam rnam par dag pas bkod pa dang / /bla med dkon mchog gsum gyi bden pa'i mthus/ /ji ltar smon pa yid bzhin
'grub gyur cig /smra ba'i seng ge 'jam dbyangs mgon po'i sku/ /mtshan dpe'i gzi 'od 'khor tshogs sku tshe'i tshad/ /zhing khams 'phrin las bzang po ci 'dra ba/ /de 'dra
kho nar bdag sogs 'jug gyur cig /phyogs dus gnas skabs thams cad du dge legs chen po'i dpal gyis kun nas kun tu 'byor cing khyab gyur cig bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ smon lam thams cad yongs su grub pa'i rgyal po phyag 'tshal lo/ /tadya thA/ oM dha ra dha ra bhan dha re swA hA/
zhes pa lan gcig brjod pas/ rang dang gzhan gyi don du/ smon lam btab pa thams cad gdon mi za bar 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /zhes mdo sde nas gsal bar gsungs so/ /dge legs 'phel
bar gyur cig rgya gar rgya nag li yul kha ba can/ /zas gtsang la sogs rgyal rabs mang po dang / /sa skya'i gdung rabs la sogs gangs can du/ /bla rabs byon tshul mdzad 'phrin
deb gter 'di/ /bstan la rab 'byams bo dhi dhwa dza yis/ /lhag bsam rnam par dag pas myur bar bris/ /'di bris pa las dge ba gang thob des/ /'gro la 'khor ba'i g.yang
sa rab bkan nas/ /sa dang lam gyi spangs rtogs myur rdzogs te/ /bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa thob phyir bsngo// dge'o/ /bkra shis// //
